good leue yll aſke nothynge agayne loue thy ſouerayne ſkyll vnto takeſt thou none entente thou tourneſt fro full vnkyndly loues vnlefull thy loue lente thy herte beholdeth heuen ſo hye goodes haue gaue thy goodnes withouten cauſe thoughe haue greued yet thy benefaytes thou nought withdrawſe haue deſerued haue hell pytte haue lyued ayenſt thy lawſe lorde thou knoweſt mannes febleneſſe frayle hath ben aye thoughe ſoule haue thy lykeneſſe man fulſome erthe claye ſynne conceyued wretchedneſſe ſoule rebell alwaye fyrſt man groweth dooth greſſe waſteth floures haye syth man ſo frayle thynge thy power ſo grete kynde worlde twynkelynge thou mayſt deſtroye myght fynde thy ryght lorde mercy mynge ſore ſalue thou ſende sore repenteth ſlyuynge mercy lorde wyll amende deus man gaue bodyly hele thou ſholde ſpende ſeruyce fayrenes alſo fetures fele man dooſt thou thyſe thou delytes deuyll dooſt dele whiche great deſpyſe thou lyueſt lecherous lyfe vnlele fro yere yere thou lyſt ryſe thou ſtudyeſt nyce araye makeſt great coſt thy clothynge make ſemely ſholde ſaye thou coudeſt amende makynge thou purpoſed daye daye ſet people ſynnynge thy wretched wyll thou foloweſt alwaye ende ſynne hathe yu thynkeſt nothynge no tyme bycauſe ſynne lecherye eſpecyall vengeaūce came mānes kynne saue viii perſones drowned sodome gomor men wtin made fyre brymſtone fall fro heuen bode therin ſynne dyomedes noble worthy knyght whan troye falle toures fayre reygne caſte repayre lyeges began feyne quarell agaynſt hym ſhope rebell malys conſpiracy owne hym withhelde bothe ſceptre crowne theyr deuty olde lygeaunce hym denye trouthe obeyſſaunce wherfore anone ſo bokes telle • l folke went dwelle vnto calabre began poſſede knyghtes dyomede tro troye haue hym thyder ſewed fourme byrdes anone trāſmewed circe crafte doughter ſonne eyre flee one gonne called ben yſydre rede amonge grekes brydes dyomede ſome bokes bere wytneſſe chaunge made venus y• goddeſſe wrathe yt ſhe hadde worthy knyght oonly ſawe hym one fyght eneas hir owne ſone dere whiche tyme faughte yfere dyomede darte grounde ame hym deedly mortall wounde ¶this moder venus began anone hym ſhroude vnder ſkye myſtye cloude ſaue hym tyme fro myſchaunce ſkyl venus toke vengaunce byrdes tourne meyne fourme yere yere fle vnto tombe graue vpon hym mynde haue cuſtome remembraunce aryte holde obſeruaunce exequyes thyſe brydes euerychone dayes ſpace thennys nat ne gone ouer dewe loue grekes platly eſchewe latynes nought may betyde preſent anone fice aſyde eche bokes v aſſure theſe byrdes knowe oonly nature grekes latynes kyndely aſſonder whan ſe ſuch wonder vnto wyt nat aſpye cauſes hydde ſuche ſorcerye well wote though wyt blent roote fals enchauntement faythe ought defye suche apparences ſhewed eye whiche fende illuſion thereof thus whan troye towne euerſed y• brought nought full many cyte ybyld wrought ¶and many lande many ryche towne edefyed occaſiowne werre ye haue herde telle whiche declare nowe maye nat dwelle poynt poynt lyke bokes ſayne iaſon wyll reſorte agayne landyd worthy hercules symeounte hauen ches haue tolde reſte comforte nat elles oonly diſporte kynge reygnynge troye towne tyme called lamedowne fals enuye reported tolde certayne grekes herte bolde entrete lande y• whiche nat knewe well arayed veſſell newe whiche aryue hadde lycence purpoſe done offence lyklyheed lande greue pryde without leue ſauf conduyte haue ſtronde ytake ſuche mayſtryes lande make theyr power maner thynge hauynge regarde playnely kynge ¶of eſtate take none hede ſuche ſtraungers great drede men laches outher neclygent fully wete theyr entent forthe prolonge peryll caſte suche ſodayne thynge wolde wyſt faſte nat differred tyll harme wyſdom ſe men may longe ſuffre abyde neclygence lete ſlyde enquere theyr gouernaunce ſpeche dalyaunce eueryche reuelaciowne euery ſtrete thorugh troye towne rownynge ſome ſpake brode ſpeche ſo longe bode one another ſothely ſowne reported kynge lamedowne ye haue herde whiche wylfulneſſe without counſayle vyſyneſſe haſtely maked hath ſonde wyt hardy londe beſyde leue preſumpcion wherfore bad concluſion without bode ſoone remewe fynally ſhulde nat eſchewe compelled maugre ſayth nay ſo kynge vpon certayne day haſte hath ſent embaſſatoure vnto jaſon grekes gouernoure nouther thoughte harme villanye innocent companye diſportyd hym endlonge ſtronde euer hath ſythe came londe charge hym layde worde worde iaſon ſayde effect euery circumſtaunce ſōme playnely ſubſtaunce ¶how kyng lamedone troyeſent meſſenger vnto iaſon byd hym auoyde countre theyr langage betwene capitulo v wyſe worthy famous renown myghty kȳg ye noble lamedown hath vnto meſſage ſent whiche theffect ſentement ſothe hath meruayle lande aryuayle bryngynge grekes nat afewe haue conduyte ſhewe proteccion playnly lycence preiudyce magnyfycence wherfore hath charge layde wyll platly ſayde ye anone without delaye without noyſe affraye troye lande bondes ye leue youres caſteth greue better eaſe departe folye lyues ieoparte wyſe lacke prouydence agaynſt wyll make reſyſtence outher pryde wylfulneſſe bolde without vyſyneſſe interrupte felycyte deſyreth tranquyllyte holde reygne without perturbaunce whoſe parſone made ſuche allyaunce wene manhode royall mageſte wyll nat ſuffre none degre enpugne quyete maner wyſe wherfore counſayle ye ſeme wyſe take hede vnto ſeye byddynge nat diſobeye ¶leſte ye offende knyghtly excellence ye ſhall fynde experyence without feynynge ſothe telle take hede therfore may lenger dwelle poynt poynt ſyth ye wyſe ſage hool effect meſſage whan iaſon herde meſſagere thyſe wordꝭ gan chaūge kepte hym cloſe ſobre coūtenaunce nat haſty irene greuaunce rancoure caughte tale saue face began wex pale longe abydynge aughte wolde ſayne ſpake worde agayne vnto hym fro kynge ſent began diſcloſe ſōme entent vnto folke ſtondynge rounde aboute vnto diſcured oute meſſage hool firſte whan abreyde worde worde thus ſeyde syres ſayth knowe take hede praye bothe hye lowe lamedone kynge troye hath ſent v wonderfull enuoye chargynge haſte hye londe axeth vpon ſtronde aryue hadde hardyneſſe without leue ſe gentylneſſe fredom whiche nat alyte lyke kynge hym quyte vnto ſtraungers entre yle nought god wote lytell whyle refreſſhe departe anoon lyke ye recorde euerychon bere wytneſſe ſome ala fredom become ¶where manhode gentylneſſe alſo whiche kynge togyder bothe two shulde cuſtome haue theyr reſtyng place honour ſhuld alſo embrace alordes herte whiche kyngly ryght manly fredome full myght shulde ſtraungers refreſſhe recomforte afterwarde myght hym reporte ¶larges experte manhode gentylleſſe haue founde worthyneſſe nobleſſe allye fredom eke knyt regallye longeth honoure kynge ſhulde haue charged firſte thynge worthy lyeges myght pleaſe haue ſhewed comforte eaſe theyr myght theyr beſy cure vnto ſtraungers venture ſee dryuen diſmayed comforte nat euyll apayed caas ſemblable outher fortune varyable ſort hap may nat withſtande aryued hadde grekes lande honeſtly lyke degre ſholde v haue receyued lyke longeth vnto gentrye ſyth ought eſpy • hath fredom honoure humanyte one made courte fle choſe dyſhonour let worſhyp gone ſhall euery chone hath choſe helpe fulfyll whan power ſhall nat belyke wyll ſaye ſothe ſhalbe founde dede ſhall hym ſelfe rebounde syth malys hath werke begonne perauenture ſomer ſonne ſodyak hath thryes gone aboute lete hym truſte thynge doute ſhall hym ſerue wt ſuche hath ſought lyue ſhalbe dere bought therof ſette tyde lande wyll lenger byde tyll haue leyſer better ſoiourne yt worde gan anone tourne manly face ſterne chere sodaynly vnto meſſagere fro kynge vnto hym ſent wyſe ſheweth entent frende quod haue well vnderſtande meſſage hool thou toke hande thy kynge brynge vnto v right vnwarely ſyth ſtondeth thus haue menynge euerydele poynt poynt vnderſtonde wele word word haue playnly cōteyned gyftes haue receyued behalfe great nede wyll remembre take right good hede euery thynge thou haſte v brought truſte well forgete nought emprente well ſuerly mynde goodly fynde great bounte maner thynge within lande lamedone kynge welcomynge great chere goodly ſonde thou bryngeſt nat accordynge nat entent god well wote neuer ment harme vnto hym playnly damage none maner age vpon goddes inmortall kynde ben celeſtyall vnto recorde myn herte take touching borowes make wytneſſynge ment none offence ne toke nat violence within realme woman childe man ſo thou mayſte reporte thou dryuen ſee compelled neceſſyte aryue thou haſte harde ſayne oonly reſte v vpon playne without vnto certayne daye afterwarde holde forthe waye vpon iourney make taryenge lyke thou mayſte recorde thy kynge ſaye hym eke ſhall tyme • e paraunter ſhall mowe thanked whan tyme cometh v ſome go forthe thy way ſay hym thus brother anone ialon pe manly knyght worthy hercules whā herd thyng fro poȳt poynt anone brought ſuche diſioynt haſty rancoure ſodayne ire whiche herte almoſte ſette fyre ſodaynly abreyde bake hye diſdeyne euen thus ſpake chere aſkoyne vnto meſſagere ſayde felawe thynge abydynge right well certayne tytan bemes reyſe agayne ſhall departe ſhyp gone men ſhall nat leue one within lande god toforne morowe vpon haue fayth borowe lenger ſhall holde ſoioure elles ſhall make retoure morowe erely dawnynge vpon payne repref ſo go ſay thy kynge thre yere god v graunt lyfe maugre grutcheth make ſtryfe vnto lande ſhall agayne retourne caſte anker whyle ſoiourne take hede therof note well tyme newe chaunge ſhall folowe pryme power ſhall nat ſo large ſtreche ſauf conduyte lytell ſhall reche ſaye platly entent wyll nat haue vnto maundement lytell regarde day abyde takynge leue ſhalbe ſette ſyde bycauſe hath begonne playe whiche ſhall quyte god maye tourne ſhall owne ſhame ſpare nat ſaye thy kynge ſame meſſager gan agayne replye ſayde ſyr ye maye nat denye honeſte meſſage declare auyſe wyll nat ſpare kynges ſonde playnely telle ſo ye lyſte go dwelle ye may yet cheſe ſo leef lothe ye haue cauſe wrothe ſyt nat vnto worthyneſſe ye take hede waye gentylleſſe manaſſynge ſuche arowes ſhete honeſte thretynge lete kepe ſecrete tyll ye large certaynely parcell charge ſtryue debate better tymes late ye beware harme myght falle parte ſay vnto alle pytee ye deſtroyed man hyndre ſhulde dere worthy parſones maner wyſe whiche ben lykly diſcrete wyſe leſt wordes greue ſaye take leue nyght ypaſſed ſprīgyng y• daye whan • arke bleſſed laye began ſalue luſty rowes rede phebus chare freſſhely ſprede vpon bordure oryente aurora herte hool entente ſwetneſſe hir ſyluer ſhoures bedewed hadde freſſhe ſomer floures made roſe newe bawme flete ſoote lylye margarete vncloſe theyr tendre leues whyte oppreſſed hertes gladneſſe delyte drery afore myghtes tene hony ſouklys amonge buſſhes grene enbawmed hadde enuyron eyre longe tytan began make repeyre bryghtneſſe bemys merye reioyſe emyſperye longe aforne dyde aryſe worthy iaſon full haſty wyſe felowe hercules alſo chargyd haue theyr ſhypmen haue ado hale vp anker redy make bad haſte euery man take right waye vnto ſhyp anoon ſotheneſſe manly man iaſon thought nat ſtuffed meyne begyn werre troye cyte nat ſhortly conclude egall noumbre multitude tyme werre begynne nat lykly ſhulde wynne victorye tho fewe nat holſome man hewe aboue heed whan ouer hye leſte chyppes wyll falle eye wherfore frygye leue coſtes blyue drewe vp ſayle ſhyp began dryue wynde good goddes fauorable fortune theyr frende though ſhe varyable thus colchos ſauf ben come vnto lande bothe ſome ben aryued lytell ſpace ſee haue founde grace neptunus cauſed blyue ſayde ere colchos aryue yle lytell lande y• colchos hyghte ye ſhall vnderſtande ryall cheyf cyte reygne mooſt dignyte worthyneſſe rycheſſe fame iachonytes tyme bare name cheueſt ſpeke buyldynge ſtretes large coryous houſynge therwith dyched well withoute stronge walled toured rounde aboute huge heyght aboue batayled magecolde alſo leſte aſſayled many paleys ſtately royall ſete mooſt pryncypall kynge abyde better elles tyme happed hym called cethes rede full renōmed knyghode manhede aboute hym well beſene meyne lyke ſyttynge vnto degre euery landes enuyrowne ſame ſpradde hye renowne aboute myghty cheyfcytee cethes helde royall ſee freſſhe ryuers water clene lyke criſtall ſhone agayne ſonne ſhene fayre playnes guydo bereth wytneſſe holſom hylles full luſtyneſſe many lay many luſty welle eke myn aucto • r telle full many parke full fayre freſſhe ſene many wode many medowe grene ſondry floures amonge y• herbes meynt whiche theyr ſtalke nature hath depeynt ſondry hewes within withoute ſeaſon yt ſomer came aboute fyſſhynge foulynge haukynge alſo venerye huatynge bothe two place • ly delytable corne greyne paſſyngly greable plenteuous maner thynge men herde byrdes freſſhely ſynge tyme yere theyr armonye noyſe ſoote melodye freſſhe braunches full delycyous reioyſe wolde theſe folkes amerous loues bronde fyred herte adawen theyr paynes ſinerte certaynely whan grene vere ypaſſed aye fro yere yere may come monthe gladneſſe freſſhe flora floures empereſſe hadde cladde ſoyle newe hir deuyſe noble place lyke paradyſe cere goddeſſe largeſſe foyſon suche plente gaue vnto regyon fleſſhe fyſſhe wyne vytayle corne lycoure hir full horne vpon lande ſo began rayne ſnowe aſtates bothe hyghe lowe lad theyr lyfe ſoueraygne ſuffyſaunce nature cowde myght auaunce lytell yle hir gyftes greate lyke toforne ye haue herde treate plente habundaūce myght pleaſaunce herte cōmodytee ſo beſell cytee iaſon come hym hercules foloweth pres full well arayed ryally ſayne army sencloſyd togyder twayne twayne people choſe none therwith brawnes bone eueryche makynge facyon full well complete proporcyon yonge age good ſtature countenaunce ſad full demure euery wyghte hadde great pleſaunce ſe maner theyr gouernaunce yonge ſo freſſhe hardy meke alſo one paleys go ſuche chere eueryche hath diſporte ſe maner theyr noble porte gentylmanly demenyd people gan preſe euery toſe thyſe ſtraungers lyke grekes gyſe demene ſelfe ſo thryfty wyſe deſyre people ne wolde ceeſſe aboute gader empreeſſe enquere myght newe ſuche ryalte ben ſodenly entred towne thus eueryche wolde felawe rowne ſo rude ſtare gaſe gape loke maſe townyſſhe folke ſo comonly euery thynge falleth ſodeynly cethes lyke worthy kynge whan herde firſte theyr comynge receyueth hooly matere ye lyſte one ye ſhall whan y• ye kyng hath ſothly vnderſtāde grekes come lande iaſon alſo therwith borne dyſſent blode royall theſalye lykly heyre grace haue agayne repeyre auentures achyeued colchos kynge anone ſee aroos gentylleſſe haſte may goodly wyſe mete way receyueth chere full benynge vnto one dothe aſſygne offycers awayte nyght daye chargynge maner waye ſo euer may eſe thynge may queme pleſe haue foyſon plente eueryche lyke degre thus cōmaunded maner thynge anone noble worthy kynge fredom myroure thorughe many halle many ryche toure many tourne many dyuers waye many gree made marbyll graye hath conueyed full eaſy pa tyll brought • hambre helde dalyaunce anone euery circumſtaunce manly fredom made chere chambre englaſed bryght clere ſhone full ſhene golde aſure many ymage pycture hath cōmaunded offycers oonly honour ſtraūgers sp • ce wyne anoon yonge freſſhe luſty man iaſon faſte gan lycence kynge declare cauſe cōmynge firſte kynge great tyaltee aſſendyd royall ſee clothes golde hanged enuyron cuſtome regyon beholde noble ſyght stondynge aboute many worthy knyght many ſquyre many gentylman full well beſene kynge right vnto iaſon ſtondynge preſence cōmaundyd hath magnyfycence hercules ſytte downe beſyde iaſon lenger lyſte abyde cōmynge cauſe ſhewe effect whiche wordes fewe saue iaſon tale began full well auyſed chered lyke man conceyued hath noted wonder well poynt poynt mater euerydell nat forgat worde ſpeche euen lyke rethoryk dothe teche gan tale ſo crafte conueye make kynge wolde ſeye condeſcende rather enclyne aſſente myght fyne cōmynge knyghtly hye empryſe thus worde worde ſhal deuyſe right worthy prynce preſent ī place oonly ſupporte hye grace goodneſſe moſte excellent dygne pacyence fauour benyngne diſpleaſe nat may ſaye ſhewe declare wordes fewe fynall grounde cauſe cōmynge ye lyſte whiche ben ſo noble kynge goodly wyſe without offence benyngly gyue audyence requeſt ye nat diſdeyne goodly graunte may atteyne y•le may auayle ſlees golde frely aſſayle goddes auenture lyſte ordayne fatall eure lyeth playnly fortune gouerne thynges comune pea conqueſt victorye army renowne glorye diſcomfyture bryngynge outraunce lyeth hyndre auaunte ayen whoſe myght mortal man may cheſ • wynne leſe lyfe deth befyne labour ye lyſte fauour gyue leue delaye accorded fully aſſaye lyke ſtatute maketh mencyon lyſte make none excepcyon vpon ſyde fauour fynde rytys playnly make mynde euer falle ſhall vnder fonge lowly beſechynge ye nat prolonge purpoſe make delaye grace ſette daye myne empryſe may achyeue myne abode ſtant vpon leue seyth one worde grauntynge y• leſte haue fyne requeſte whan kynge herde ceryouſly entent iaſon ſayde ſo manfully ſtynt alyte kepte hym cloſe whyle tyll laſte goodly gan ſmyle towardes iaſon ſayde vnto hym thus iaſon quod though thou deſyrous vnderfonge paſſynge hye empryſe counſayle lyke ſhall deuyſe full prudently caſte aforne mortal peryle thou lorne thynge lawe ſette bychauntement may nat belette remedyed fauour mede deth ſothe ſo taketh hede guerdon platly twynne fall yt caſte flees golde wynne helpe none manhode fortune ſtreyghte waye ſo importune dredfull eke ſo full rage ſaue deth paſſage victorye palme conquere ſothly iaſon ſhall lere founded olde meruaylous workynge ſtatutes mortall thynge ſore bounde vnder regalye rygour may nat modefye wherfore iaſon thou thynge tame leſte afterwarde layde blame thy leſynge deſtruccion feythfull herte trewe entencion warne ſelfe quyte man iuſtely ſhall wyte though thou youthe wylfulneſſe thy lyfe deſtroye without vyſyneſſe syth iaſon perylous caas poynt poynt haue tolde y• caas auyſed put faute ſurplus frely lyeth thynge ſythe thou mayſt cheſe ſo thou wynne leſe man iuſtly may arecte lawe mar hym ſelfe ſette mortall man dewe right may paſſe hye lowe gette noon grace goddes lyſte hym ordeyne euer caſte hym darreyne dyuers thynge moſte furyous drede wherfore iaſon euer thou ſpede haue openly declared hooly peryle fauour ſpared fer ſothe reaſon wyll ryght thou woteſt well lyeth myght declare man lette manhode knyghtly caſte ſette vpon thynge thou haſte herde tell ſhulde ilenger mater dwell vayne thou knoweſt beware hir tourneth ball tyme thou getteſt thou lyſte put choys worde kynge roſe vp anone vpon tyme whan ſhulde gone vnto mete iaſon ſyde ye ſhall ye lyſte abyde tyme aprocheth gan neygh faſt offycers full beſely caſt make redy theyr full cure halle bordes cure dyall hour began marke phebus ſhouthward reyſed ī arke hye lofte drewe noone tyme kynge gone vnto mete entre halle cethes lordes alle knyghtꝭ hym euerychon hercules alſo iaſon ſette mete royall ſee euery lorde lyke degree firſte worthy man iaſon aſſygned kynge anoon ſytte owne borde hercules ſo great lorde ſet alſo faſte ſyde marſhall lenger lyſte abyde aſſygne eſtates ſhulde lyke hye lowe degree ſcaffolde hye lofte noyſe gan loude thynge ſof • e bothe trompers claryoners noble offycers full thryftely ſerued haue halle lyke ſeaſon tyme dyde falle deyntes may rekened ſothfaſtly foyſon plente kyngly fredom vnto hye lowe fulſomly gan reygne ſnowe thorugh y• hall y• manhode preyſed kynge renowne reyſed geſtes ſothely ſye whan hym lyſte chere feſ • ey lyke kynge ſo thryfty wyſe deynte man deuyſe feſte ſolempnyte grekes myght great nobley ſee kyng cethes worthyneſſe reporte therof bere wytneſſe ſo come theyr lyue wante connynge ordre diſcryue euery cours dyuerſytees ſtraunge ſewes ſotyltees day ſerued place haue excuſed thoughe lyghtly paſſe though nat ordre ſayne myn englyſſhe rude eke playne endyte ſo hye thynge forthe wyll reherſe kynge ſhewe geſtes nobley ouer hathe doughter ſent ſpecyall bad ſhe ſhulde forth anoon brought whiche ſothe though men ſought world thrugh playn aſſure men myght founde fayrer creature womanly porte manere demure ſadder hir chere whoſe beaute nat lykely fade whan ſhe came grekes glade halle ſooth ſhe walketh vp downe woman hede pure affeccy owne make chere vnto theſe geſtes newe
