one ioyned longe endure empereſſe called nature ſhe hir made lyke hir deuyſe beholde paradyſe ſothe bothe one olde yonge ſyttynge hall therto ſhe ſucceſſyon borne heyre regyon hir fader diſcent lyne ſhe abyde dure fyne syth • e right ſuccede noon heyre male rede alſo boke maketh mencyon vnto yeres diſcrecyon able age maryed withſtondynge alſo eke ſhe beaute womanheed one fayreſt reed yet none bothe haue hir youthe let clergye hir deſyre ſet paſſyngly ſpecyall artes called lyberall expert knowynge beſte hir vre konne hir leſte ſuche woman herde neuer telle elycon ſhe dranke ſo welle hir tyme none ſemblable founde ſothe ne none ſo able conceyue ſtudye doctryne nature diſpute termyne koude alſo cauſes fynde thynges formed kynde lernynge ſo hir tyme ſpent ſhe knewe fyrmament trewe cours ſterres theyr meuynge ſhulde fall expert ſhe aſtronomye moſte ſhe wrought nygromanyce exorſiſmes coniuriſons vſed alſo make illuſions hir charmes ſayde ſondry wyſe rytes dyuers ſacrifyſe encens rechelys caſte fyre ſhewe thynges lyke hir deſyre gootes horne mylke blode whan mone equat ſtode fyfthe ſyxte hous fortuned lokynge gracious cheſe houre conuenyent fortunat enchauntement make werke ſondry apparences well ſhe knewe heuenly influence aſpectes bothe wrothe glade ſhe hir thynges made appartene ſuche experymentes whan hir lyſte hir enchauntementes cowde make wyndes blowe thondre lyghte hayle ſnowe freſe alſo greue men payne ſodeynly ſhe cowde make rayne shewe weder hir lyſte haue gaſten men ſodeyne erthe quaue turne daye vnwarely vnto nyght anone make ſonne bryght shewe bemes full perſynge full ſhene golden horne voyde nyghtes tene reyſe floodes many dredfull wawe whan hir lyſt ſhe cowde eft wtdrawe eke yonge tree ſere roote rynde afterwarde make ageyne kynde luſty braunches bloſme budde newe alſo wynter floures flreſſhe hewe aray erthe tappte hym grene beholde ioye ſene many coloure ſhewynge full dyuers whyte rede grene ynde pers dayeſye hir ryche crowne floures wynter made frown • vpon theyr ſtalke freſſhely appere ſodeynly dedely chere cowde ſomer wynter tourne cauſynge daye myſtes morne olde men ſhe cowde make yonge eft agayne ſpronge cowde ſhewe bothe heed berde full hore graye crafte ſhe ſo lerede tree wt fruyte ſhe cowde eke make bare rynde leef men ſtare clypſe mone bryght ſonne naturelly hadde theyr cours yronne apropred whiche may nat paſſe tytan cours kynde traſe whan meueth vnder clyptyk lyne clypſe nat folowe auctours lyſt diffyne theyr diſcripcion bothe twayne full coniunccion ſonne bemes reed haue dwellynge dragon heed mone ſet eke tayle nature may nat fayle muſt falle eclips nede ſondry bokes lyke ye may rede bycauſe certayne interſecacions dyuers clerkes reuolucions maked ben heuen lofte whiche cauſe v fayle ofte freſſhe comfortable ſtremes v ſhadde phebus bemes mone hath made dyuyſion ſodayne interpoſicion ſyght ſtremes viſuall may nat beholde ſene luſte fully comprehende appollo chare chyuende wonte aforehande ſe great tholome kynge egypt telleth great cauſes within boke full compendyouſly bothe eclyps coniunccion falle naturell mocion medee though clerke ſuyde encreaſe hir name vpon euery ſyde leſt fable ſuche thynges telle thoughe poetes ſprynge welle yet god forbede ye ſhulde gyue credence ſuche feynynge ſo hygh offence syth nature muſte denyed ſuche affermynge alſo diffyed euery criſten ſtedfaſt byleue certaynly wolde hyghly greue conſcience wyſe wene agaynſt kynde whiche ſo hye quene wyght orlyuynge creature shulde haue power playne ••• ure curſyd thynges ſuperſticious werke kynde contraryous ¶for god almyghty iuge iuges alle hath ſet lawe whiche may nat falle amonge planettes perpetuelly endure afore ordeyned eternall cure whiche may nat clerkes lyſt termyne vpon ſyde bowe declyne diſcorde debate eternally yformed create thorugh fynger ſapyence alway meue theyr intellygence lyke lordſhyp bounde neuer yet ne eclyps yfounde mone nat beynge coniunccion haue tolde ſaue paſſyon whiche eclips agaynſt kynde nature hir knot tyme dyde vnbynde whan goddes ſone ſtarfe vpon roode ſonne lyfe dyrked goode whan heuen erthe wt hye compunccion haue ſygnes ſhewed lamentacion erthe quaues lyght tourned dyrkeneſſe deed bodyes vpwarde gan dreſſe theyr tombes agayne deth lyue stone rocke ſonder ganne ryue temple veyll kut two ſygnes many yſhewed tho wonder token meruaylous great worthy dyonyſyous whiche athene clerkes hym wryte called ſcolys ariopagyte whan ſawe noble famous clerke bryght daye ſodaynly ſo derke though apaynym tho dayes infect rightꝭ theyr layes mooſt cheyf pryncypall phyloſophers reken yet tyme aſtoned mynde sayde platly outher god kynde suffreth dethe outher doute rounde worlde whiche ſo large aboute shalbe diſſolued ybrought nought ſodayne chaunge haſty thought ¶by clergye knewe better ſkyll god may chaunge wyll hath power ſuche coaccion vnder whoſe myght diſpoſicion lawe kynde conſtreyned ſothe ſeye poynt poynt lowely obeye euery thynge hym lyſt ordeyne elementꝭ may cours reſtreyne hooly wryt wytneſſeth ye may ſe requeſte worthy ioſue bryght ſonne ſtode gabaon adayes ſpace one degre ſhon shewynge token trewe knyght fynally gyue hym lyght myght hye proweſſe cruell foon manfully oppreſſe whan faught knyght ioſue kynges fyue reygnynge amoree longe laſte purſute chaas tyll take theyr treſpaas dempt dede bible telle ſyth god thus hyghly lyſt fulfylle knyght requeſt oriſon wonder though paſſion criſte iheſu incarnat ſake ſonne bemes though wex blake syth hath lordſhyp planettes alle hym lyſt nedes muſt falle medea though ouydius fable reherſeth wryte thus lyſt hir name exalte yet trouthe ſome whyle doth alte ſhe paſſynge ſorcereſſe fertheſt name chauntereſſe 〈◊〉 wyll paſſe ouer agayne matere ſhe came mete ye ſhall whan hir fader hadde hir ſent came anone cōmaundement ſhe came fynde tofore make hir beaute ſeme hir cloſet ſhe toke hir beſte araye encreaſe euer ſhe maye nature werke royall apparayle woman gladly wyll nat fayle whā beaute haue plenteuous largeſſe embellyſſhe theyr beſyneſſe ryche tyre vpon euery ſyde fought myſſe cloſe hyde foule ſhall couertly wryed defaute outwarde eſpyed ¶but ſhe bothe fayre well beſayne hir porte ſo womanly certayne hir comynge gladeth halle ioye vnto one alle ſe maner tho hir entree hir fader bad take hir ſee beſyde iaſon hym diſporte womanhode recomforte ¶but oo ala lacked hye prudence diſcrete auyſe inwarde prouydence wyſdome alſo perell caſte afore truſte mayde tendre yeres bore vnhappy fonde wylfulneſſe kynge gentylneſſe cōmaunded hath confuſion diſhonour deſtruccion owne donghter borne heyre alſo ſo womanly feyre ſodaynly downe diſcende conſydred nat myſcheif ende ala durſt hir affye make hir ſytte curteſye ſhe myght caſuell mocion full lyghtly catche haue occaſion amyſſe ala dyde ſo lyſt hym nat take hede therto auerte diſcrecion wyſely caſte afore reaſon vnware chaunge womanhede whiche euery wyſe man oughte drede euer yet ſo mad wood ought reaſon konne ryght good gyue fayth haſtely credence woman without experyence nouther truſte ſykerneſſe ben ſo double full brytylneſſe harde aſſure vnto longeth nature theyr byrthe haue allyaunce doubleneſſe varyaunce theyr hertes ſo freell vnſtable namely youthe ſo meuynge mutable ſo clerkes lyſt endyte ſory wryte ſaye chaunge mutabylyte apropred ben femynyte affermed full ſage ſpecyally whyle tendre age theyr wexynge whan yt yonge whoſe herte accordeth full ſelde wt tonge trouthe inwardely ſought y• ſurplus remenaunt theyr thought men may trewe patron fynde inconſtaunce whoſe flaſkyſable kynde fro meuynge wynde hercules nat ſtronge bynde nouther sampſon ſo beleue woman herte make nat remeue blaſe whyrleth afyre fro flee theyr deſyre tyll accomplyſſhe fully theyr delyte matere naturell appetyte kyndely deſyreth fourme tyll cours proceſſe may perfourme woman refrayne ne ſewe theyr luſte fro man man wyll nat ceaſe tyll aſſayed wolde god matere apayed one fourme holdeth hym content whan boundes hath terme went nat deſyre ferther procede ſtyll abyte wyll nat excede example woman wolde reſte one dewely ſholde holde payde ſtylle abyde vnſure fotynge dothe ofte ſlyde nat content vnytee purſue aye pluralytee nature meuynge thewed though amōge ſignes outward ſhewed pretende maner ſtabylneſſe vnder hyd doublenſſe ſecrely outwarde eye full harde treaſon eſpye vnder curtyn veyle honeſte cloſed chaunge mutabylyte theyr deſyre kepte full cloſe mewe thynge hadde leueſt ſewe outwarde haue lawde declyne wt faynynge frawde ¶wherfore cethes thy wyt barayne thou afore prudence naddyſt ſayne ſhulde folowe vnhappy ca thou bolde ſuffre ala thyn owne doughter ſo fayre freſſhe hewe ſtraunge geſtys entred newe folylye lete hir dele wher thrugh thy hono • thy worſhip thy hele loſte haſte ſhe myſcheif brought ſtraunge lande wt ſorowe moche thought ſhe great ſclaundre great myſerye aduerſyte ende made thou lefte ſole thou myghteſt wel complayne make dole ala whyle thy prudent ſyght thou haddeſt grace remembre ryght haue caſt diſcrete purueaunce weyed wyſely meſure balaunce fraude woman freelte full ſelde ſykerte latyn guydo doth expreſſe wherfore thou cethes recheleſneſſe thou haſte one augment thy wo without recure bothe two forgo firſte thy treaſoure thy doughter dere ſo paſſyngly entere eke thyne heyre whan yt ſhe gone ſayth myn auctour none thy daye occupye thy royall ceptre thy lande gye ¶but worthe y• great prouydence waker kepynge beſy dylygence myghty mar god batayle myght helpe diffende auayle agayne wyt woman ſleyghte whoſe fraudes ſo huge aweyghte lyſte aye game gothe theyr purpoſe holde ſo lyef lothe ſlye ſo prudent ſo wyſe ſtorye playnly doth deuyſe medea hir engyne crafte hir fader treaſour hath berafte thorugh worchynge hir ſleyght gyle ye ſhall within lytell whyle ſhe ſat mete tyde next hir fader iaſon hir ſyde ſodaynly hir freſſhe roſen hewe full ofte tyme gan chaunge renewe hondreth fythe alytell ſpace blood hir goodly face vnto hir herte vnwarely gan bale therwithall ſhe wexeth dede pale efte anone take hede hir hewe chaungeth goodly rede euer amonge ennewe hir coloure roſe meynt lylye f • oure though roſe ſome delegan pace yet lylye abydeth place tyll nature made efte mete thus colde ſodayne hete medea hir ſelfe aſſayled paſſyngly bexed trauayled ſhe brent ſhe gan colde aye ſhe gan beholde yonge iaſon ſhe gan deſyr • loke hym ſo ſhe ſet afyre beaute ſemelyneſſe euery thynge ſhe inly gan inpreſſe y• ſhe ſawe bothe mynde thought emprenteth forgat right nought ſhe conſidereth euery circumſtaunce bothe porte gouernaunce ſonnyſſhe heer criſped lyke golde knyghtly loke manly chere countenaunce many noble ſygne face alſo moſte gracious benygne moſte acceptable vnto hir pleſaunce ſhe thought ſuffiſaunce without vnto hir alone conſyder loke parſone tyme without drede mete drynke ſhe toke lytell hede ſhe foode hath loſte hir appetyte loke hym ſhe hath ſo great delyte ſo prynted hir remembraunce loue hathe hir caught ſo newly traunce marked fury bronde ſhe may nat eſcape honde noreſchewe ſtroke ſpeciall ſhe yolde body herte vnto iaſon platly ſeye euer amonge hym ſhe caſt hir eye whan ſhe fonde aleyſer opportune wyſdom ſhe woldenat contune hir loke longe leſt men dempte amys maner theſe woman kepte hir cloſe wonderly ſecree hir chere man myght ſee ſhe mente none occaſion put ſuſpeccion openly token ſene caſte rather men ſhulde wene encheſon hir abſtynence ſhe ſat ſo ſylence oonly womanhede honeſte ſhame chaſte drede togyder hir herte mette whiche twayne ſo mayde lette fro mete drynke wolde ſeme thus wyſdome ſhe made deme ſo caſte theyr oppynyon thus ſhe blent diſcrecion hir chere cowde euery thynge excuſe gaue mater fooles muſe ¶no chere vnbrydeled tyme hir aſterte one encloſed hir herte another hir chere declared maydens hath ofte ſythes ſpared ſhewe deſyre dede falleth ſo take hede whyle flouren virgynyte youthe haue lyberte ſpecefye theyr herte wolde kepe cloſe nat bolde ſhewe ſūme theyr ſentence thus medea kepynge aye ſylence ne lette worde hir lyppes pace couertly • obre chere face ſhe mente ſheweth hir eye ſecretly man cowde eſpye hote fyre hir breſt yreke hir ſelfe right thus ſhe gan ſpeke ſhe ſothe ſo moche wolde god yonge luſty man whiche ſo fayre ſemely ſyght aſſured myn owne kynght whiche moſte pleſaunt enteer berde yſpronge ſhynynge lyke gold weer well ilymed compact meaſure well growe heyght good ſtature lyketh euery parte ſo wele aſſent fortune hir whele iewred ſtonde grace ſemeth vpon knyghtly face heuen beholde therwith herte fele colde yet ſothe may none ala ne hath wopyte leſte knewe entente moche trouthe hym mente whiche ala taketh maner hede hym brenne dothe glede deed dare nat diſcure ala pytous wofull auenture rewefull mortall payne murdred dare complayn • frende foo chaunce ala fynde helpe ſocour ca trewely yet ſhall deuyſe thynge mene honeſt wyſe lyke ſhall openly founde deſyre knyt bounde hym wedlok neuer hym twyn menynge withouten ſyn grounded ſette vpon clenlyneſſe without fraude doubylneſſe clene pure myne entencion lo aye maner condycion theſe woman ſo well fayne ſhewe one though thynke twayne couertly thynge ſayne humble chere face playn • encloſe theyr luſtes ſuche ſotylte vnder boundes honeſte theyr entent though trecherye withall ſurplus vnder iurye though fayth afore pretende fraude wt floriſſhing wel defēde flaterye oonly worlde blende doubylneſſe encloſed ende yet aye deceyt benethe ment vnder ſugre fayned clene entent ſothe exiſtence truſte well apparence ſhewe one another mene whoſe blewe lyghtly dyed grene vnder floures depeynt ſtabylneſſe ſerpent dareth newfangelneſſe playne ſeme wt wordes fayre gloſed vnderneth theyr couert wyles cloſed thyngr moſte theyr paye wyll denye ratheſt ſwere naye lyketh guydo womē endyte ala wolde ſo curſydly wryte agaynſt debate right ſory englyſſhe tranſlate repreef euyll ſeye leuer theyr loue deye wherfore praye take pacyence purpoſe nat offence ſo good parfyte euerychone reken trowe nat one wyll herte trewe though amonge cheſe thē loues newe conſydereth thynge blame ofte tyme ſe men ſame muſt puruaye whā mē refuſe cowde wolde excuſe ſytteth nat woman lyue alone ſtore haue mo one prayeng grace hope treſpace though makynge ſame guydo wryte origynall myſſayth lete hym bere wyte ſyt well vengaunce byte hym ſo theſe woman hath offended myght ſhulde amended ſhulde receyue duely penaunce deyed without repentaunce diſpeyred ſauacion ſhulde euer haue remyſſion contryte ſynne redreſſe may nat ben clerkes bere wytneſſe ¶and trouthe alyue mene guydo ſhulde hym ſhryue bytter penaunce playnly ſhulde haue tyme ygraue ſhulde remembre platly nat ſterte repente hym hole herte ſo ſpake confuſion wyll lenger make diſgreſſion matere lete gnydo tell forthe workynge medee hath lycence hir fader nome hir chaumbre alone come whan halle withdrawen pres whan iaſon alſo hercules lyke kynge mete hadde theyr chambres conueyed ladde full royally arayed beſayne euery walle couered certayne clothe golde full ſtately wyſe whyle ye haue herde deuyſe medea hir chaumbre gone wherby ſelfe complaynynge euer one gaue yſſue hir paynes ſmerte hir ſo ſore haue wounded herte loue hath brought hir ſodayne rage nat lykly ſoone aſwage sotheneſſe furyous god cupyde hath ſuche fyre kynled hir ſyde neuer lykly lete violent feruent hete encreaſe gan hir payne hir breſt wixe twayne great debate ſtronge batayle feruently eche dyde aſſayle contek erne game inparted betwyxt loue ſhame metynge togydre vnſet ſteuen felde nat parted euen loue ſothe full hye renowne bolde hardy lyke fyerſe lyowne nat ferefull ſpere ſwerde knyfe hote haſty auntre lyfe eke ſurquydous ſtoute full pryde chefe champyon god cupyde cauſeth ofte bothe f • e bonde full many peryll take honde cauſed hath full many man deth many one yelde vp breth made theyr woundes largely blede peryll loue taketh none hede gete hym honour excellence fame ¶but contrary enmye called ſhame lyke cowarde faynt hertles neuer dare put hymſelfe pres lacke manhode draweth hȳ euer bake ſo dredfull ferefull wrake lyke childe yonge tendre age hath nouther herte corage aſſayle ſo febyll myght yet full ofte hath ſtonde ſyght many louer lete hym ſpede thorugh falſe cōſpyrynge brother drede drede ſhame whan allyed one aſſent haue pytouſly denyed vnto loue herte hardyneſſe ne durſt worde expreſſe whan loue manhode wolde ſpeke woode fyre breſt vnreke vpon poynt whan ſhulde aſſay cometh ſhame anone vtterly fayth nay cauſeth loue horne ſhrynke abaſſhe chere pytouſly wynke cowardely cauſe appayre thus ſhame frowarde contrayre thorugh helpe drede louers folke fere doutleſſe ſhame nought ne kouthe bothe nyghe ferre loue lawes often ſhulde erre wynde honeſtes cheyne bondes brydell breke reyne right hors tray large lytell nought louers wolde charge folowe theyr wyll theyr luſt ſewe whyle ſhame kept mewe within breſt ſo none knowe outwarde porte loue bereth hym lowe ne ſhame clerkes haue compyled theyr hertes daunger exyled ſtraungeneſſe feyned fals diſdayne ne ſhame playnly wardayne theſe woman wrytynge theſe olde without aſſaute caſtell yolde nede ſege layne ſuche caas longe tretye vayne nature loue proceſſe ¶but ala drede ſhamefaſtneſſe haue daunted loue full lowe manere made hym full humble porte chere haue eke theyr vyolence manhode put hym ſylence ben great cauſe mornyng payne amyddes ylke twayne loue ſhame euen vpon poynt stode medea full great diſioynt ſhe ne may payne nat endure hoote ſhe brente wofull creature betwyxe bothe mene loue ſhame whan loue wolde thynge attame deſyres declare oute came ſhame anone put hym doute drede redy luſt denye thus ſhe ſtode iupardye loue ſhame maner traunce vn euenly hanged balaunce ſhame great loue yet ſhe well knewe hir ſyghes ſore hir ſtormy cruell auenture drede ſhame durſte nat diſcure fyre loue hath hir breſt encloſed whiche full harde depoſed thus ſhe henge euen wixe two ſhene wyſte beſte tyll fortune hir double face vnhappely hath wrought gete hir grace whyrlynge hir whele aboute cauſeth wretch ful lowe dowe loute whan beſte wene ſytte hye lofte experyence men may ſe full ofte hir gery reuolucion lady tranſmutacion full ofte tyme fals full vnſtable enhaſteth thynges foolys full greable whiche ende theyr confuſion vndre ſugre ſhrowde hir poyſon aye fortune hir maner wretch ſheweth fayre chere face flaterye ſhe benyngne eye fully foolys parfourme thentent thorugh great myſcheif ſhent ende crafte eſchewe vnware harme hir tayle doth ſewe right fell whylome medee gynnyge grounde hir aduerſyte ¶for lady called fortune graunted hath leyſer opportune ſhewe iaſon hooly hir herte whiche made hir full ſore wepe ſmerte daye merydyene whan appollo bemes ſhene ſouthe plage gan weſtre faſte cethes hir fader hath ſent haſte medea come hym anone bad hir ſhe ſhulde gone vnto iaſon hercules make chere amonge pres whan ſhe kaught oportune ſpace hir deſyre ſawe eke place hir fader mooſt occupyed ſhe thought nat eſpyed apparceyuynge great beſyneſſe towarde iaſon anone ſhe gan hir dreſſe haſte full knyghtly chere curteys wyſe gan drawe nere towardes hir ſawe let whan togyder met medea ſyghynge firſte abrayde iaſon euen thus ſhe ſayde ¶howe medea ſhewed iaſon maner conqueſt golden flees wan ca vi iaſon quod ſhe thyne hye nobleſſe thy manhode thy gentylneſſe bothe aſſembled thy parſone yfere knyghthode firſte requere thy conceyte oppynyon nat arecte preſumpcyon doubylneſſe inconſtaunce womanhede varyaunce bolde thynge ſpare menynge clerely declare without • eynynge wordes plat playne beſechynge firſte ſhall ſayne without goodlyhede benyngnely take hede pacyently wordes leſte ſaye take beſte entent thynge greue thynges two myne herte ſore meue ſaye loue gentylneſſe mene clerely expreſſe perſone thynge counſele parte lyke ye ſhall fele ſemeth firſte curteſye ſoth faſtneſſe genterye ſtraungers euery maner wyght bounde holde due ryght make chere trewely bycauſe iaſon ſe moche manhode ſo great worthyneſſe wyll nat fayne beſyneſſe helpe al may lyke worde herte ſhe gan ſyke ſake ſayde ouer fele full great anoy ſore meued without auyſeneſſe oonly youthe wylfull hardyneſſe flees golde gete ye may whiche empryſe euer aſſay peryllous playnly achyeue ſothe ye cowdelyeue douteles well aſſure fynall mede auenture nat deth ſaue report ſhame ye wene gete name ende playnly ſhall tourne contrarye gynnynge ſo fyne ſhall varye wyt man nouther engyne myght though neuer ſo expert fyght haue armes paſſynge excerſyſe ſleyghtes olde newe empryſe though beſte brethed endure deuyſe armure wepen alſo brynge harded ſtele trenchaunt perſynge yet laſte whan hath ſought without vayle may right nought ¶wherfore iaſon haue compaſſion youthe pure affeccion wylfulneſſe ye ſhall thus lorne ben blood lyne ſo hygh yborne certaynly may none ye counſayle take none may helpe eſe ala iaſon wyll ye nat appeſe manly corage caas yblent counſayle ben obedyent durſt ſwere ye ſhulde haue victory ben remembred put memorye perpetuelly thorugh knyghthod wyn flees golde whiche yonde within yle ſtandes beſyde whiche mar gouernour gyde wherfore one ſelfe aſſente counſayle fully conſente fewe wordes ye lyſte ſpede leue luſt worke rede iaſon wt full humble chere anſwered ſayd myn owne lady dere thanke beſt wyſe right fet forthe may ſuffyſe power platly may attayne myne hertes quene lady ſouerayne ye may hooly enſure whyle lyfe may dure truſte right well lyſt nat fayne lyue dye luſte reſtrayne hym owne trewe man obeye euer without chaunge doubylneſſe whyle lyue ſothfaſtneſſe lyſte trewe affeccion vpon lyfe haue compaſſion gentylleſſe ye lyſte haue suche cherte body ſaue good fayth due ryght ybounde owne knyght vnto myn ende ſpecially grace ſo benyngnely ye lyſt ſelfe counſayle neuer afore degre ne dyde ſeruyſe womanhede wordes full goodlyhede owne man lyſteth recomforte whiche ſothe ſo reporte thouſande folde pleſaunt neuer afore meryte gat hym graunt ne deſert requeſt prayere frely herte full entere lyſt vnrequyred wo rewe vndiſſerued ſo trewe enſure vpon fayth faſte ſeruyſe ſhall vnto laſte parſeuer ſothely ſhalbe ſlouthe varyaunce therto trouthe fynally withouten wene fewe wordes ſaye right mene lyſte nat fayne flatre delude beheſte dethe ſhall conclude whan parcas lyues threde rende ſome thus make ende quod ſhe ful wyſely herte ye muſte afore conſydre aud aduerte aduenture ye take hande prudently peryll vnderſtande full warely caſte haue mynde mortall harme tayle behynde well credyble leue well impoſſyble gynne honour alſo fyne thylke flees hye power dyuyne preſerued eke marcys myght ſo entreth therfore fyght full harde hym eſcape fyrye flawme whan bulles gape ben braſſe trapped leuen drede lyghtnynge y• heuen tofore dynt great thonder ſeuered hath many toure aſonder aſſhes muſt man conſume wherfore rede ye nat preſume ram aſſayle leſte ye labour leſe withdrawe foote yet ſythe ye may cheſe good aduyſe diſcreciowne honour ſauf hye renowne ſo ye lyſte wylfulneſſe oonly folye haſtyneſſe empryſe heed procede ye lyſt lyke rede saue ſelfe wo myſchaunce lyke ye ſhall myn ordenaunce ye commytte lowely lyſte obeye without fraude ſeye iaſon ſyttynge borde medea emprentynge euery worde waxe ire almoſte vnpacyent ſayde ala entent counſayle leue empryſe certes foule cowardyſe gynne thynge myght nat cheue euery man wolde repreue reporte confuſion pryde preſumpcion toke whan large hye thynge ſo great charge durſt doute myſchefe accomplyſſhe whan cam prefe leuer myn owne lady dere iuparte put ſelfe one wordes fewe ſmale pecys hewe ſhulde cowardely forſake thylke empryſe haue vndertake ye well knowe leue thus ala let counſayle playnely ca ſo euer happe falle truſteth right well ſhall none cowarde herte fro purpoſe ſhulde dyuerte without lawde lyfe ſhulde lede ſhame eternall ſhulde mede worlde noted ouer euery lande ſpoke ſpeciall iaſon hath ſo hyghly vndertake fere dare none ende make thynketh right well ſhall betyde lyfe dethe myſcheif abyde vpon trouthe enſure ferforthe lyfe may endure ſhall parfourme haue begonne though ſo may nat wonne muſte deth beye wyll nat leue leuer haue deye lyue aſhamed cowardyſe ſlouthe ſemeth hygh routhe man appere dare ſhewe hede whan hath honour vyllanede tyme whan name ſlayne eueryman ſhulde rather fayne dye honour lyue wretche though thynge deth ſtretche welcome ſhall well abyde ſome ſo betyde quod ſhe ſythe ſo ye algates deſyre haue ado ther nomore ought eſpy ye leuer ſhortly dye rather lyue haue ſhame yet erneſt game ſuche monſtres vnwarely dele lyke dede ye ſhall fele wherfore meued pyte greatly ſtered ye volunte without aduyſe diſcrecion counſayle good delyberacion lyſte take meruaylous vyage youthe alſo corage gouerned ben matere luſte bothe two yfere inparded ben ye purpoſe ſewe unpoſſyble eſchewe ſodayne dethe nouther fre bonde crafte man hath power withſtonde ¶wherfore thynke herte good entent caſte awaye yet ye ſhent tourne ſhape remedye suche routhe haue ye ſhulde dye fader loue moſte rather ye ſhulde thus loſte ſhall offende vtterly diſpleaſe frendes ſo may eaſe ſhall fynde ſuche amene weye leſte ye ſhall nat deye caas thynke gyde ſhall ſette aſyde byrthe firſte ſtok royall ¶and ouer myn heritage withall myn honour ſhalbe put backe helpe ſhalbe lacke founde ſo ye wyll kynde ye lyſte haue mynde diſſerne goodly quyte conſyderynge firſte nat alyte ſaue lyfe ſtande ieopardye peryllouſ • ye eſpye ſhall ſo ordayne thorugh crafte oonly wyxe v twayne parte hope ſhalbe wele vpon poynt ſo may fele faythfully ioye wo ſmerte full accorde body wyll herte deſyre ye condecende vndertake make good ende ſothly lady ſayde iaſon tho aſſented without wordes mo fulfyll euery circumſtaunce euer may pleaſaunce quod ſhe ſayne firſte wt fayth herte playne myght beſy cure menynge hole ye meaſſure ye hereafter ſhall take wyfe holde kepe lyfe dede accorde heſt • fyne ſūme requeſte excepte oonly ye ſhall ordeyne repayre faders reygne faythfully ye ſhall led • whan ye ſuccede daye herytage herte aye one one corage ye ſhall lyke trewe cheryſſhe chaunge newe lyke myn eſtate without varyaunce whyle ye lyue haue remembraunce kyndeneſſe great nede none lyue may ſpede creature mortall aſſayle force marcy dragon bulles bothe fere ſo lere hooly manere ſhall hym gye lyke thynke ſpecifye whan happeth mete agayne none may helpe certayne caas platly ye ſhall fynde nat aſke ye kynde sothly quod iaſon ſhalbe ye deuyſe wyll ſo fayth aſſure goodlyeſt creature euer yet ſawe vnto paye fayreſt eke ſothe naye bounte ye ben comparable dethe ye ben ſo merciable whyle lyue ſaye fayth myn herte meneth tunge • ayth wyll founde owne trewe man lyfe deth euer grace pleaſaunt parfourme heſtes graunnt worke fully ſauacion ye haue ſayde full concluſion trewely ye bere lyfe beaute haue prerogatyfe paſſynge echone lyſt nat gloſe amonges floures dothe rede roſe whiche ſomer amyd leuys ſoote veer hath made roote humydyte kyndly aſcende barayne foyle clothe amende braunches wynter made bare ſote bloſmes freſſhely repare medowes many ſondry hewe tapited ben dyuers floures newe ſondry motlees moſte luſty ſene holſome bawme ſhad amonge ye grene ¶right roſe fayreſt echone right ſo nature ſette alone whan ſhe made firſte hir deuyſe aboue haue pryſe ye ben bounte ſprynge welle therto beuute ſothly ye excelle lyue compariſon ne may made diſcrecion ye paſſe euery man may ſe fynde vnto moſte goodly euer yet borne without lorne helpe ſocour fully deſtitute ne founde refute fro al fredō mewarde doth haboūde ſomoche euer bounde fer forthe lyue may ſtreche ſake deth ne reche therwithall myght agrene helpe ſo goodly lyſte ſene neclygence ſholde thynge refuſe ye wolde myght reaſon full well merked noted eke wylfull nycetee folylye voyde away grace arage man hym chace wylfull fortune whan ſhe benyngne wherfore hooly reſygne herte body lyfe eke dethe hande whyle laſteth brethe othes afferme may perſeruer myn endynge day youre trewe ſpouſe haue ſayd ſworne beheſted playnly toforne vpon euery thynge obeye may pleaſe tyll tyme deye ſome ſhuld lenger tarye beheſte ſhall neuer varye whan ſhe ſawe great ſtedefaſtneſſe • uppryſed ſo hye gladneſſe ſo great ioye pleynly hir herte ſhe voyde euery wo ſmerte ſo lowly hir luſt obeyde ſhe wente thus hym ſhe ſeyde iaſon quod ſhe ſhall ordayne amene waye bothe twayne may efte agayne leyſer mete ſone parfourme done matere lyke entent ſhalbe made fynall ſacrament deſyre man ſhall vnbynde though therto may leyſer fynde towarde eue ſhall nat eſcape truſte right well tyme ſhape secretly may mete yfere ſhall ſende pryue chambrere myne whiche ſhall conueye vnto chamber pryue weye certayne houre without fable entent moſte greable vpon poynt whan phebus wt lyght weſtryd eke derke nyght hath dymneſſe ſhadowes blake emyſperye fully ouer take ofte gyueth fauour fortune vnto louers leyſer opportune parfourme theyr luſtes achyeue right anone draweth eue ſhall cloſet ſende euery thynge make ende ſhall good leyſer ſpeke eueryche hertes breke declare ſūme wylle whan haue ſpoken fylle good leyſer fully byhete ſhall ordayne whan ſo v luſt mete ſette tyme euer ſaye nay alway nyght whan paſſed day myghty ioue wyſely ſocoure hence forth wyll hooly youre whyle lyue wakynge ſlepe ſo ye heſtys kepe ioſan lowly gan enclyne ſaid fer man may ymagyne wyght may clerely comprehende wyll lyues ende ſeruaunt faythfully quyte though nat ſay lyte trewe herte wyll nat neuerthelaſſe though nat peynte compaſſe gay proceſſe ſoueraygne hertes quene tyll deed trewely ſhall mene haue trouth whyle haue lyf mȳde ende trewely ye ſhall fynde theyr ſpeche ende thus make medea ſhope hir take hir leue anone amonges pres firſt hir fader hercules bode lenger forth anone vnto hir chambre haſte ſhe gone vp downe ſhe made many wente none hir meyne wetynge ſhe mente caſtynge wayes hir purpoſe chyeue hir wyttes gan beſyly meue ſhe rometh hir habytacle ſyde obſtacle lettynge whiche wolde hir ſore greue hir ſtudye tyll drewe eue hir leue complaynynge hir wo many thought walkynge fro ¶the myddaye houre gone ouer ſlyde tytan ſo faſte hath chare ryde dayes arke eſt weſt compaſſed fyry ſtedes haue almoſte paſſed oryzonte drawe downe full lowe golden wayne man myght knowe hydde fyry bemes bryght deſcence full fer ſyght ¶and herynes hir cope myrke euenynge begonne dyrke twylyght whan day gan fade eſperus ſtremes glade ben ſo freſſhe ſo luſty ſo merye gan recomforte emyſperye ¶whan medea hir ſelfe alone hygh deſyre gan make hir mone ſhe ſo longe abode hir knyght alway accountynge houres nyght full trouble full thought whiche hath full ſtreytly ſerched ſought redy waye vnto hir purpoſe ſhe kept full cloſe amyd hir herte quappynge awawe drede fere tyll hope gan adawe bad ſhe ſhulde right merye gladde tyll drede agaynward made hir ſobre ſadde leſt hir deſyre troubled lette thus ſhe abay yſette amyd hope drede alſo ſhe ne wyſte beſte ¶for hir deſyre hye affeccion ſobre brente hir oppynyon luſte ſhe hadde mete iaſon agaynſt drede came anoon made hir ferefull leſt ſhe eſpyed hir ſorowe holpe remedyed oonly fortune dyrke nyght whiche ſhe made full glade lyght recomforted oonly thyſe two good hope made hir glade alſo began anone caſte deuyſe whan mone heuen wolde ryſe whan ſhe hir horne pale wolde ſhede hir lyght vpon hylle vale gan acounte caſte well tyme founde quarter paſſed pryme ſhe well knowynge art ſawe ſothe fourth part mone ſhadde newe lyght paſſed hir cours full ryght tyme coniunccion thre ſygnes full computacion complet ſeuen dayes hir age ¶at whiche tyme ſhe brennynge hir rage thorugh darted cupides arowe gan loke beholde narowe euery dore lyſten beſely ony wyght ſhe myghteſpy court outher walke go man romyn fro ſore ſhedradde goynge vp downe whan ſhe herde noyſe ſowne whan ſhe hereth ſprynge venym ſothly hir ere wyſſhed hadde ben bedde pytouslyfe longe nyght ſhe ledde wtout reſpyte though wyght coude knowe tyll hye mydnyght cokkes crowe whiche tyme whan huſte ſtylle accomplyſſhe ye remenaunt hir wylle euery made ſylence clepyd anone vnto hir preſence aged vecke fer yeres ronne ſuche crafte moche helpe konne thriftely bryng • thynge aboute afore caſte euery doute ¶of yeres paſſed olde experyence hath gyue ſo paſſynge hye prudence loue ſleyghtes knowe ſhe made dogge bowe medea diſcureth hir thought poynt poynt forgat right nought charged hir reles hir ſmerte recomforte hir troubled herte haſte hir anone vpon hir waye vnto hir chaumbre iaſon conuaye ſhe anone nat rekles caas gone hym full ſofte paas ſhe newe nat lere brought hym anone ye ſhall whan cok comon aſtrologere y• mydnyght hour wt voyce ful clere began ſowne dyde beſy payne bete breſte wynges twayne tyme mynute wyll nat pace warne place tydes ſeaſon nyght medea awayte vpon hir knyght full redy entre kepe ſhe lyſte full lytell ſlepe ne parcell hir thought whā iaſon hir chambre brought without eſpyeng maner wyght ſhe anone conueyeth hym full right hir cloſet haſte ſhe maye full well beſene great ryche arraye hir ſyde ſhe made hym take ſee firſte ylke lee three hir moſte expert caas ſodeynly tourned braas vecke ſtare vpon mone walked hath lefte alone whan medea dores ſhette downe iaſon anone ſhe hath hir ſette firſte fynde hir beſy myght aboute chambre ſhe ſet vp lyght great torch cyerges full ryall aboute pyllers euery wall whiche gaue alyght lyke ſonne ſhene cheſte wrought cryſtall clene firſte ſhe taketh hir paſſage whiche ſhe toke aryche ymage pure golde full luſty beholde cuſtome rytes olde myghty ioue eterne creat halowed alſo conſecrat whiche ymage deuoutly ſhe ought humble herte iaſon firſt ſhe brought made hym lowly theron take othe vnto laſte outher lyef orlothe hir ſhulde take vnto wyfe fro daye forthe durynge lyfe herte vnfayned fayth inuyolate cheryſſhe hir lyke hir eſtate fro tyme fynde ſhe hadde euer floured virgynyte myn auctour well reherce aye kept hir clene touche man thought dede neuer dyde amys ſhe herte ſo holly gyuen vnto iaſon euer mo anone hath put hande vnto ſwore fully ye haue herde ſaye hir requeſtes without delaye kepe whyle lyfe may laſte ala ſoone ouer caſte heſt fayth wt whiche aſſured hadde fraude flaterye yeured couertly hir innocence hir trewe menynge hir dylygence euer ſhe deuyſe deceyued falſhede man though yt trouthe apparent aboue doubylneſſe ſo ſlyghly ſhoue though ſothly allyed trewe menyng ſo thynge eſpyed vnder fayre chere faynynge failas myght ſhe wrought ī ca thy ſake ceptre regalye lordes eke hir alye forſoke one toke hede pyte goodlyhede loſte hir frendes hir good fame oonly iaſon ſaue froſhame yet moreouer forſoke hir herytage borne ſo hye parage ſhulde haue ſucceſſyon heyre diſſent regyon womanly ſhe wolde hir quyte yfere ſhe ſet nat amyte one hour ſhe hath forſake vnto ſhe hath hir holly take oonly truſte thou ſhuldeſt haue kynde rycheſſe honour ſhe hath lefte behynde ches exyle gone hir kynne cely mayde alone ala wepe thyne vnkyndneſſe hath ſhe nat fro deth fro diſtreſſe preſerued yet thou takeſt none hede ſhulde haue deyed ne ſhe thy rede thy conqueſt ſhe cauſe may nat ſhortly clauſe wryte hir bounte breifly comprehende effectuelly parfourmed ende wordes fewe may nat tolde thorugh y• haſt ryche f • ee golde manly conquered whiche without doute vnlyaly brought aboute whan thou helpe deſtytute thy comforte ſynguler refute thou mayſt nat denye erthely honour ſhe gan defye conſerue heuyneſſe hir fader ſhe hath • rycheſſe emperyſſhed pyte enſample whiche woman myght lere ſhulde truſte man ala medea ſo moche bothe ſterres aſtronomye yet ſawe ſhe nat afore hir deſten ye loue hath hir put ſo gouernayle hir crafte ne myght hir natauayle ſlowe calculacion caſte afore conſtellacion hir byrthe hir wofull fate rekleſhed ſhe ſawe late ſuppoſe hir connynge fallyble doutles ſemeth nat credyble ſhe hadde wyſte toforne pytouſly ſhe hadde nat lorne ye ſhall ſe haſtely ſtorye reherſeth befell iaſon medee firſte ye ſhall ordre maner ſe ſhe wrought ſwore ſame nyght ala ſhe hathe forbore hir mayden hede y• great pyte yet ſhe mente nat honeſte ſuppoſe ſhe went haue wyfe touchynge holde ſtryfe yet one thynge dare aferme fayne menynge ylke twayne ne nat one wonder fer atwene ſhe trewely gan mene honeſte thynkynge outrage lyke mayde innocent age accomplyſſhe fleſſhely falſe appetyte parfourme foule appetyte wrought euery thynge hir entent contrayre ala ſhe ſo debonayre truſte vpon curteſye quyte hir hir genterye haſtely rewe vpon ſinerte woman ſo tendre herte wyll gladly routhe pyte whan man aduerſyte saue lyfe rather ſhulde deye ſo medea ſhortly ſeye caſtynge peryll ſhall fall deſyres luſtes hooly obeyeth hir full myght ſo longe almoſte nyght hath courſe rounde aboute gon whiche tyme hir ſpake iaſon lowly ſayde lady tyme aryſe ſoone wyll pryme ye may ſe well daye begynneth ſprynge may byrdes ſynge prayenge beſte wyſe ſhall werke ye lyſte deuyſe ceryouſly euery thynge diſpoſe beſeche goodly freſſhe roſe myne empryſe brynge ende erſt henſe wyll wynde saue thynke firſte wt trete wyſe countre ye ſhall lete grece repayre agayne whiche lande great felycyte truſte well thynge drede reyne ſhall lede conqueſt ſo wynne wherfore praye goodly begynne ſhall werke haſte ye maye good fayth anone wyll daye ſhe ſpake fayeng ye ſhall myn owne iaſon vnto dere myſelfe concluſion aſſented full affeccion wyttes hole herte enfourme ye ſhall aſterte euery daunger lytell yle ſo ye lyſte abyde whyle vp ſhe roſe haſte ſhe maye cofre hir treaſour laye went anone brought hym hir honde ryche ymage ſyluer ſhe fonde whiche ſothely meruaylous entayle whoſe power vertue auayle effectuelly hir bothe entent agayne magyk enchauntement ſytte force sorcerye made aſtronomye houre choſe equat none clerkes olde full longe agone whylom whā flouryng ī age vſed make ſuche ymages dyde kynge called tholomee ſo iaſon cōmaunded hath medee bere ymage hym pryuely ye haue herde worke effectuelly euery thynge ſhe dyde aſſygne ſhe toke hym medecyne made maner oynement ennoynte hym nat brent ryche precious bawme agayne malys euery fyre flawme ſhe toke hym anone ryche rynge ſette ſtone vertue hadde venym deſtroye ſyde myght hym noye whiche ſtone alſo myght man cowde bere ryght within hande next ſkyn encloſed ſtrengthe ſyght ſhulde depoſed wolde gaſe beholde ſo euer hande holde vertue infallyble ſtorye ſayth ſhulde vyſyble whiche ſtone wyſe clerkes calle achates moſte vertuous alle founde ſothely cecyle whiche ſtone whylom wrote virgyle venus eneas ſente firſte whan cartage wente ſhe iaſon toke certayne bylle wryten lyke boke iourney myght moche auayle bad hym wyſely nat ne fayle caſte hym graciouſly ſpede firſte ſcripture rede ram touche wyſe hym chargynge eke afore hye empryſe humble herte deuocyon knelynge ſaye oryſon vp downe wryten bylle prayenge goddes lowely fulfylle requeſte mercy haue pyte myſcheif hym ſaue cheif ſocoure toke hym vyoll lycoure bad hym manly without fere drede whan come vnto bully rede hym ſhape knyghtly eſcape faſte ſeeth gape theyr goles lycour caſte hym nat lytell gaſte theyr iowes togyder ſhall glyewe ſyde ſhall nat eſchewe beye luſte hym lyſte cōſtreyne doutles maugre theyr peyne ſhall ſo daunte make tame hym lyſte erneſt game myght make louten enclyne bowe bothe backe chyne lycour ſhall chawles ſo coharte ſonder ſhall nat departe offende noye wyght whan ſhe thus vnto hir knyght euery thynge gaue inſtruccion playne doctryne informacion ſhall ſcape daungers take hede werke auyſely accorded thought ye beſt parte men theyr reſt waked drewe daye well ſawe morowe graye leſte men hadde ſuſpecion hye prudence diſcrecion twene twelyght rody morowe toke theyr leue wt ſeynt iohn̄ ye borowe oft kyſſynge louers whā twynne ſo wente ſhe lefte withinne beynge hope mete agayne ſome daye iaſon faſte euer maye gan ordayne hym iourney acheue thought wolde anone go take leue wyſe within lytell whyle maner rude ſtyle purpoſe ſothely nat ſpare ſupporte playnly declare whan rowes rayes rede eſtwarde v full erely gonne ſprede euen twelyght ye damnynge whan larke cuſtome gynneth ſynge ſalue hir heuenly laye luſty goddeſſe morowe graye mene aurora whiche afore ſonne wonte enchaſe blacke ſkyes donne derkeneſſe dymme nyght freſſhe phebus cōforte lyght bryghtneſſe bemes ſhene hadde ouer gylte hye hylles grene floures eke agayne morowe tyde vpon theyr ſtalkꝭ gan playn leues wyde whan iaſon companye towarde kynge full faſte gan hym hye fonde lyke eſtate ſceptre hande full pompous elate hye ſee regalye syttynge full kyngly amyd chyualrye lordes aboute enuyron whiche tyme yonge champyon vnder vowe ſtondyng ram ſterne face tofore kynge cam beſechynge hym magnyfycence ſame day graunte hym lycence armes make delayes concludynge playnly aſſayes wyll daye felde founde achieue lyke bounde olde byheſte nat poynt declyne lyfe deth tyll parfourme fyne hooly auntres vnto flees longe kynge requeryng lenger hym prolonge goodly graunte fyn empryſe kynge full ſobre wyſe conſyderynge ſūme demaunde iaſon ſpake ſayde ſhall cōmaunde requeſte parfourmed haſte quod full ſore gaſte wylfulneſſe thou ſhuldeſt deſtruyde leſte men thy deth arected vnto therupon wolde blame ſette ryall power nat ne lette thy manly youthe ſuche iupartye whiche ſothe great vylanye preiudyce myn eſtate name afterwarde men put blame thorugh fals reporte wronge opynyon withſtode nat thy deſtruccion ¶wherfore rede yet thou auyſed counſayle lete nat diſpyſed better honoure certayne thy countre repayre agayne wylfully take honde mortall thynge man may wtſtonde rede fully myn aduyſe take hede therto fythe thou art wyſe leſte thou repente whan late ſo thou wylt algate thy purpoſe holde nat rede almyghty mar praye ſpede gyde ſo euer falle eke praye goddes alle saufe ſounde thy body reſtore ſome thou getteſt whan iaſon herde kynge nat diſmayed ſtoned thynge knyghtly wyſe dyde hym reuerence thankynge hyghly royall excellence grace benyngnyte vpon deth hym lyſte haue pyte fully concludynge touchynge batayle nouther rede counſayle wyſe purpoſe ſhulde withdrawe lyke ſtatute playnly lawe right fer forthe fortune wyll hym eure ſo tyde auenture settynge aſyde euery feer drede sayde platly wyll procede parfourme hath vndertake ydell mo ſkylles make allegge agayne iaſon full openly playne touchynge y• ſurplus dredfull thynge departynge ſayde kynge audyence lordes alle ſo euer falle ſo euer malys theron muſe worlde firſte excuſe goddes platly quyte though deye ye nothynge wyte ne man ſhall arecte ſkylle werke frely wylle agayne aduyſe hye prudence lyfe deth preſence hooly herte neuer f • ytte goddes fortune cōmytte lyſte ordayne agayne whoſe wyll ſhall neuer playne put blame ſo betyde honour ioye ſhame thynge thus ende make tyme leue take tho aboute ſtonde one one toke honde wyſe forthe gan hym dreſſe anone thynke expreſſe whan tytan wt feruent hete drawe vp ye dewe leues wete towarde myd morowe diffyne vpon houre whan clocke nyne iaſon full manly full lyke knyght armed ſtele chere full glad lyght ganoreſſe hym forth hap euer fall ſayde dieu vnto feres boote vpon ſtronde alone whan came londe water hadde veſſell lafte firſte remembrynge crafte medea circumſtaunces ſhulde kepe obſeruaunces euery thynge hadde well mynde anone full manly fynde ſhope hym forth went knyghtly pa towarde bulles forged bra poynt whan iourney gan hym medea wexed full pale wan • ore agaſt thynge myght hir glade routhe ſe woſhe made teres hir chekes twayne full pyteouſly diſtylle • ayne fordewed hir wedes blake aye ſorowe ſhe made ſake lyke woman ferefull doute whyle armes ful māly brought aboute ſobbe ſyghe ſhe nat pe leſte haſte oughte rekles poynt poynt lyke ſhe badde lyfe ſhe hym hath ladde ¶and ſe ſhulde hym defende gan anone grecys aſſende toure hye pynacle ſhe myght haue none obſtacle lettynge nouther haue ſyght hym hir owne choſen knyght euer amonge wordes ſhe brake ſtoundemell thus hir ſelfe ſhe ſpake thou iaſo • ſouerayne hertes hele thou knewe wo forthe fele sothly trowe ſhulde nat aſterte trewe thy hole herte god praye iourney leſte may tyme tourne beſte kepe ſaufe ſounde euery membre yefe myght fully remembre taughte ſame fourme euery thynge fully parfourme oonly daye thyn honoure auaunce whiche ſe hole pleaſaunce certes iaſon fylle ought amyſſe fare well helthe worldly blyſſe fare well myrthe ſolace welfare fortune grace one hertely ſuffyſaunce ¶lo hym hir gouernaunce tyme lande hath • ome firſte whan come bulles fell diſpytous caſte theyr fyre frawme f • ryous theyr mouthes wonder large huge agayne whiche chefe refuge hym ſaue nat brent enoynted oyntement body kept hym damage thylke fyre ſo full rage ſmokes derke full horryble whiche eſcape almoſte impoſſyble man eſtate without comforte counſayle medee whoſe doctryne iaſon ſo werke ſcaped myſtes derke fyre blaſes blake eyer ſo cludy dyde make hadde hym made ſo diſcret ſage oonly vertue thylke ymage whiche aboute necke bare wherby ſo prudent ſo ware whan ye bulles haue moſt feerſly gaped hath theyr malys auyſely eſcaped enfeccion theyr troubled eyre hath venquyſſhed diſſpeyre effecte agayne foule fume wolde man vnto deth conſume ymage preſeruatyfe hym diffende ſaue lyfe ſurely kepe hym drede full ofte ſythe wrytte dyde rede vertue oryſon vnto hym full proteccion nat fell diſtreſſe ſykerneſſe hym preſerue mortall ca toke lycour vyell therwithall full lyke manly man one toke bulles forgat nat ſo warely caſt therwithal chawes made faſt vertue ſo myghtely englewed thorugh hath vtterly eſchewed enfeccion ſinoky leuen whan eyre gan clere heuen myſtes waſted hym toforne manly herte raughte horne ſterne bulles vyolence drewe forth defence yoketh ſo maner ploughe made go pa vp n • w downe eere londe lyſte ſo buxom fonde ſoyle ſmothe bare playne made redy bere grayne renges tourned vp ſo downe th • rebellyowne humble meke redy wylle deſyres playnly fulfylle ¶and iaſon lyke champyon gan hym enhaſte towarde dragon beeſt great monſtruous foule horryble ryght venymous enarmed ſcales large thycke brethe peryllous wycke heyre peſtylence venym ſuche vyolence full deedly mortall throte yſſued flawme fyre fournes mouthe lyke leuene downe ſouthe geſt wont tempeſt ſmyte right ſo dragon ſothely wryte mouthe hadde flawme blaſed wherof iaſon fyrſte lytell maſed herte dredefull thynge whan remembred rynge fere drede layde aſyde gone rynge ſette ſtone full ryche noble ryght vertuous whiche techeth great y•ſydorus myn auctor alſo fynde moſte comenly comyth ynde muſt kept chaſte wonder clene colour ſurmounteth euery grene whoſe vertue venym deſtroye withſtande may nat anoye dragon ſerpent adder ſnake ſpecially take holden oppoſyte worme euen agayne ſyte without abode ſothe may nat cheſe venym force muſte leſe ſtronge vyolent rage ſtone dothe full great damage whan hath vertue blyue pecys ſmale gynneth ryue ſelfe hole abydes whyle lande called cecyle worme bufo bereth name whā men wyll malys make hym tame venym vtterly expreſſe take quyll myn auctor bereth wytneſſe whan wyll worke large ende ſtone lette lyne right agayne wromes hede holde tyll dede ſothly vertue nature venym may laſte endure preſence ryche ſtone fynde bufo right anone thorugh myght therof breſteth euen twayn oonly kynde whiche man may reſtrayn goddeſſe called nature whiche next hir lorde thynge cure hath vertue gyue herhe gras ſtone whiche man knoweth hir ſelfe alone cauſes hyd cloſed hir hande wytte man nat vnderſtande openly myght hir workynge ſo iaſon vertue rynge thrugh ſtone yt might hȳ moſt auaūce hath dragon brought vnto vttraunce fonde maner reſyſtence hym withſtande force diffence nouther venym none ſtryfe wherfore hath berafte hym lyfe manly wyſe felde outrayed iaſon full glad well apayed hath wt ſwerde ſpent hȳ many ſtroke layde hym men hewe oke bryght ſkales ſo harde dur • well vnneth ne myght endure hym diſmembre ſmyte hede anone ſtede ſede gan tethe hede arace ryght forthwith ſelfe place gan ſowe ryght men corne vpon lande ered aforne whiche ſede ſprange wonder grayne bryght armed knyght ſtondinge y• playne whiche anone wt ſharpe ſwerdes grounde eueryche gan hurte wounde tyll eche felowe hath cruelly ſlawe theyr fate fynall lawe none ſhulde victorye dethe reioyſe memorye yfere thus made ende iaſon gan wende vnto ram dylygence whiche fonde power diffence maner ſtryfe rebellyowne myghtely ram draweth downe ſette honde vpon eueryche horne ſlewe firſte hath ſhorne flees golde ſo paſſynge ryche world treſour lyche made delay take boote haſte may roweth forthe tother yle hercules mene whyle vpon brynke many nother mo • ode iaſon tyll euerychone fynde blyue oonly ioye whan dyde aryue gan thanke cheyr goddes graciouſly hath fall flees hath ſo knyghtly wonne ſhone clere ſomer ſonne whiche brought wt hym vnto londe feres abydynge ſtronde whan appollo dayes arke ye weſt almoſt ronne marke faſte gan downwarde declyne wawes full watrye gan ſhyne yet paſſed occian iaſon come many manly man feres preſence kynge hadde acheued euery thynge whiche longeth conqueſt ram cethes ſoone euer cam make hym chere outward hath hȳ payned herte fayned ſory without drede expleyte good ſpede iaſon flees hath wonne lyke ſothe theſe feyners konne whan lyſte craftly compace ſhewe outwarde faythfull trewe face venym encloſed hole within menynge maner ſyn ryght ſo kynge loke forheed clere made vnto iaſon outward ryght good chere gan hym ſpeke wordes fewe frendlyhede many ſygnes ſhewe though conqueſt euery dele poynt poynt lyked wonder wele befull glad ſo fortuned vnto ende hath contuned reioyſeth ſpeche countenaunce fortune lyſte hym ſo auaunce paleys gan goodly hym conueye daye daye full rychely feſteye thynge done herte le felte full great ſmerte treaſour deſpoyled ſo hath ryche flees forgo damage confucion thus great dyuyſion twixe chere menynge thought fareth ofte well ſought many man menynge fals double calme couer ſo trouble hye malys hyd deſyre rake falſly wycked couert fyre full hoote brennynge inwarde enuye well hym cowde eſpye knewe theyr menynge fals fraudelent thorugh ala full many innocent deceyued wote nat mene namely ſuche nat trouthe wene euery chere men make innocence beſte take wyſe thynke nat wele ryght ſo certayne iaſon euery dele hath take gre ye kynge hath wrought nat aduertynge ye grutchynge thought doutles ſat kynge full ſore ram hath loſte euermore whan hath vtterly ſayne though grutche gayne fynally neceſſyte tyme myght none outher playnely ſawe may nat cheſe algate flees muſt leſe whether lefe lothe fayneth chere nat wrothe oonly gentylneſſe ſygne outward grutchyng dyd expreſſe daye daye curteſye chereth iaſon companye whiche tyme aboute enuyrowne euery partye regyowne people came ſtare gaſe vpon ram maſe loke wondre deme lyſte whoſe dome lytell tryſte ofte vary tourne fro wyſely taketh hede therto comon people chaungeth phane daye wexe morowe wane dothe mone ſo flaſkyſable truſteth ſhal fynde thē ful vnſtable ſome glad iaſon hath ſped wele ſome ſory lyke neuer adele ſome ſayde wonder myght agayne dragon bulles fyght agayne force marte ile alyue myght parte another ſayde parauenture crafte wrought diſcomfyture outher charme ſome ſorcerye thus eche theyr fantaſye gan deme hym longe day laſte makynge delay full glad lyght medea downe deſcendeth hir chambre outwarde pretendeth sadneſſe chere ſhe thynge ne knewe men coude nat conceyue hir hewe hir ſecrete menynge ſhe ſo womanly • mened hir ſo prudently ſhe auoyded diſcrecion fantaſye ſuſpeccion man coude hir workynge deme thynge well dyde ſeme porte chere cauſe ſo proceſſe ſhe drewe hir pryuely towarde iaſon ſhe nat lere ſecretly badde hym ere alwyſe nat ne leue hir chambre come eue mater hadde trete ſhal know leyſer whan mete ſo anone whan entred nyght sool hym ſelfe without torche lyght medea hath way take ſhe abode ſlepeles ſake wonder deuoutly deſyrynge geſſe hym trete ſome holyneſſe touchynge materes contemplacion ſhe ſmytte deuocion freſhe venus holde memorye hym alone hir oratorye nat openly ypocrytes praye dyuers angle ioynge waye people comended nat ſo hath nyght diſpended vayneglorye none laude themſelfe thynkyng fraude secretly ylke twayne alone without lyght outher ſonne mone longe nyght haue ladde without reſte thought nat beſte ſpeke ſlepe tyll pryme caſte leſe tho tyme thus nyght togyder diſpende dull comprehende obſeruaunces ſuche relygyous prolix werkynge compendyous deme ſelfe ye gete nomore well ye wote euery faculte hath knowynge experyence men wyll hym rather gyue credence wherfore ſaye ye wyſe axe nat whiche ſo rude man deme thynge namely whan paſſeth knowynge alſo wit dulled myn ymagenatyfe deme practyke ſpeculatyfe wherfore paſſe lete ouer ſlyde forthe thynke ye lyſte abyde playnely tell iaſon • ee whiche accorded aſſented ſhe hym ſhall grece wende whan gothe ſhortly ende vnwyſte hir fader euery wyght saue alone hath trouthe plyght trewe bothe well woo▪ vnto laſte hir moo ⸫ ⸫ ⸫ ¶howe iaſon toke ſhyppynge loue medea ſayled awaye hir ca vij whan iaſon iournee full rychely lyke degree refreſſhed colchos kynge withall myght lykynge amoneth paſſed gone grekes aſſented one purpoſed hath ſhortly myght medea ſtele awaye nyght moche treaſour ryche flees full accorde alſo herculees medea thou haſteſt faſte thou ſlowe wyſely caſte ſhulde falle whan yu thy iourney toke myſcheif forſoke falſe eke vnkynde othes fynde thou bothe eue morowe thy fatall chaunce thy pytous ſorowe wepteſt gan thy ſelfe rende tyll dethe made wofull ende vayne make reherſayle wote thynge myght auayle iaſon vnkynde none receyued hath penam talliones goddes diſnaturelneſſe myſcheif wretchedneſſe made eke ende thorugh cruell hate felle mar loo mortall fate theſe twayne made theyr ende ſo trowe lyke wryte guydo theyr gynnynge nat vertuous ende foloweth full contagyous ala hadde take hede aforne nat myſcheif lorne wyll nat afore myſcheif ſe may nat eſchewe haue aduerſyte ende platly deuyne euen lyke ryght medecyne auayleth nat whan ſyke deed may helpe ſtomake heed letuarye emplayſtre pocyon reſſeyt confeccyon herbe ſtone lech knowe whan corp layde erthe lowe ¶or whan beeſt tourned careyne myne auctor ſayth veyne recure vpon halowe ere leyne ſalowe veryly fantaſye helpeth nat doth remedye thynge parfourmed due date vertue hath whan cometh late rightſom caſe veryly ſemblable worldly truſte falſe full mutable caſte peryll tyll falle ſtede ſugre ofte caſteth galle blended luſte whiche preſent future ſlouthe neclygent ne lyſte afore myſcheif caſte tyll ſnare englued faſte prouyde graceles full vnprudent wylfull recheles caſte peryll tyde ſewe theyr luſte reaſon goth aſyde befelle whylom two medea iaſon alſo ¶but ſo euer iaſon • ynde playnly harme alone ſhe great damage fynall ſmerte lacke wyſdome y• ſhe ne wolde aduerte ſhulde falle whan ſhe hir iourney toke hir fader folyly forſoke ſythe ſhe wrought oonly wylfulneſſe without counſayle auyſeneſſe lyſte hir harmes bewayle lytell nought myght auayle lete hir alone complayne hir damage well wote touchynge hir paſſage nat take good plyte moone haſtyneſſe ſhe began ſoone cheſynge houre nat fortunat ſhe alone frendes deſolat colchos forſoke ſhyp gon haſte byddynge iaſon hercules companye hym came theſalye without taryeng one worde yentred ben within ſhyppes borde oonly cauſe wynde gode euery thynge theyr luſte tho ſtode ſo aſſent ſtale awaye nyght treaſoure catche myght ladde plente vytayle forthe anone began ſayle many coſte many ſondry ile towardes grece mene whyle medea glad good chere iaſon ſyttynge bothe yfere hercules gentylneſſe comforte dyde beſyneſſe faynyngly maner ſake theſe louers full queynte make tyll haue hadde hooly theyr pleaſaunce theyr luſte fulfylled vttreth varyaunce preued iaſon vtterly hath forſake full vnkyndely medea payne ſorowe wo hir guydo ne wryte wordes mo maketh hir none mencyon bycauſe trowe myn opynyon hir ſorowes ende euery dele reherſed full openly wele methamorphoſeos wryte full playne naſo recordeth certayne hir deth nat oonly hir heuyneſſe parcell eke vnkyndeneſſe iaſon telleth playnely howe medea hir bothe ſones ſlowe lyke theyr fader vyſage telleth eke put hir moſte rage falſly hym nat excuſe loued nother called ceruſe eke pyſteles ſo taketh hede hir deedly ſorowe may beholde rede ſhe hir trouthe boughte ſore medea ye gete boke hir auenture wyll beſy cure hooly tourne ſtyle iaſon werre made lamedon lyke guydo openly deſcryued grece aryued fi rſte whan iaſon hercules alſo londed many nother mo lande reygne theſalye kynge pelleus cheualrye caſte hym playnely wyll nat fayle mete neuewe aryuayle whan mette countenaunce • made outwarde hole entere hadde ſoueraygne gladneſſe kynghthode heyproweſſe renowne manly hede expleyte good ſpede fortune encreaſe name hath cauſed hym ſo noble fame colchos honour repayre chere vtterly contrayre entent euer came agayne face hole playne welcomed hym agaynſt herte full ſore aſtoned euer aſterte auentures colchos peryllous retourned ſo victoryous couertly treaſon hyde delaye gan ſette aſyde iaſon chere full benyngne herytage firſte gan reſygne septre crowne kyngdome leſte parfourme ſūme beheſte lyke aſſured bonde iaſon toke honde gan vncle full lowe manere firſte thanke herte entere ful knyghtly gan hym praye goodly wolde ſaye matere fret herte ſore daye daye encreſynge euer beſechynge hym graunte hym audyence tochynge wronge vyolence done vnto hym whan harme ne mente torye lande colchos wente ſaye kynge troye towne within bondes regyon whan myne great aduerſyte wynde weder dryue ſee v refreſſhe lande dyde aryue purpoſe hym ſtryue reſt v wo lytell whyle forth anone go ſothe maner harme ne thought vnkyngly malys ſought agaynſt v firſte occaſion byddynge haſte voyde regyon nat withſtondynge come pe lyke brother knoweth hercules vnto myght doynge diſtreſſe wherfore praye hye nobleſſe purpoſe condeſcende whiche platly fynall ende ſette full concluſion hooly werke deſtruccion lyke auowe whan thenſe went ſo ye goodly lyſte aſſent one ſtrongly nat ſpare maugre myght troye fare may fynde fauoure v refreſſhe golde creaſoure oonly eke curteſye v ſtrengthe alſo cheualrye pelleus without abode anone mater vnderſtode aſſented herte wyll alſo vyage go worthy regyowne kynges duke lordes renowne accorded nat one ſayth nay go helpe may iourney chyeue ſolycytour hercules worthy conquerour haſte retenewe make towarde ſparthos hath way take whiche yle grekes pertynent fully obeyeng theyr cōmaundement whiche pollux caſtor eke alſo worthy kyngꝭ myghty brother two wereas fynde tyme gouernours bare theyr crowne lyke noble werreours brothren alſo eleyne poetes lyketh feyne iubiter deyte vpon dyane begat thre beaute dyde excelle eleyne lyke bokes telle conceyued tyndarys yle vnto londe ioynynge cecyle therfore ſome fynde ſhe yle called tyndarys theyr byrthe lyſte endyte forthe thynke hercules wryte hath beſought theſe noble k • gꝭ twayne myghty hande theyr beſy payne oonly graunte hym wende troye warde ſhortly ende aſſente ſaye nat one nay power catche may agayne tyme hym lyſte aſſygne hercules cherefull benyngne thanked hym behyght forthe wente haſte myght towarwe meſſene ſtronge myghty londe within whiche noble kynge fonde knyghtly man worthy thelamon lorde prynce regyon armes one manlyeſt lyue egall beſte whan knewe hercules come • oye hath hym armes • e receyued maner thynge lyke ſat worthy kynge whan wyſte ſothely mente without anone dyde aſſente hym gone troyens greue hercules goodly toke leue hym enhaſteth theſalye agayne pelleus telleth hym certayne hath ſpedde beſechynge hym alſo haſte may ſende letter lordes call aſſemble worthy knyghtes thorugh lande nygh ferre suche knewe expert werre alſo counſayle ſage wyt ronne age force without experyence whan manhode mente ſapyence conſydereth may double auayle longe haue vſed trauayle lyke playnely ſuppoſe may helpe moſte iourney diſpoſe vnto age experyence wytte youthe force hardyneſſe ſytte whan bothe one entent fully accorded worke aſſent quarell grounded vpon ryght thorugh helpe grace y• hath treble myght nat drede ſpere wt ſhelde knyghtly wyſe holde felde knyghthode fame glorye armes conqueſt victorye nat aſſured vpon multytude manhode ſo grace lyſte conclude therfore lete v auenge wronge firſte ryght make ſelfe ſtronge force manly ſhewe knyghtes choſe taken fewe deuoyde encombraunce nombre ſo ſhall foe beſte encombre hercules hath ſayde kynge pelleus right well apayde hym thought coūſayle right gode hercules without abode great haſte meyne gon aprouynce called phylon whiche duke noble fame fynde neſtor name full renowmed ſtronge chyualrye eke full nye allye hercules ſame blode whan playnely vnderſtode purpoſe hole cauſe comynge graunted hym without tariynge go hymſelfe hym vyage worthy baronage redy agayne certayne daye hercules faſte euer maye repayred home theſalye gadred hooly nauye lordes full redy apparayled well enarmed rychely vytayled pelleus hath taken firſte ſee euery lorde lyke degree ſhypped redy gon hercules alſo iaſon theyr beheſtes manly fulfylle towardes troye cyte ſpylle ſothely fynde nat abyde vpon wynde ¶how iaſon hercules prynces grece toke theyr ſhyppynge go deſtroye cyte troye ca viii whan y• ſote ſtormes aprylle vnto roote full lowe gan diſtylle luſty lycoure many holſome ſhoure reyſe vertue vpon floure phebus aſcendynge ſpere breſt ſmote bemes clere ram full coleryke halowynge veer equynoxiall whan may kalendes entre ſothe zephyrus full ageable ſmothe tendre braūches enſpyreth doth ſprynge euery buſſhe luſty bloſſomynge hylle water reuolued ſnowes whyte y• phebus hath diſſolued bawme vapoureth vp lofte eyre herbes ſofte rote vertue wt colde wynter hydde hath hole myght forſe kydde erthe herbe euery tree shade braunches humydytee areyſed oonly ſonnes hete moyſture raynes ſwete whan ſyluer welles ſhedeth theyr ſtremes ryuers gylte ſonne bemes hadde newe grene agayne hir lyner ſhad vpon euery playne nyghtyngalys wooed ronge full amorouſly welcomed ſonge luſty ſeaſon freſſhe deſyrous namely hertes amerous ſee calour blaundyſſhynge trouble wynde wawy bollynge tempeſt ſure eſcape ſame ſeaſon grekes forth ſhape towardes troye erles▪ dukes▪ kynges ſhyppes ſtuffed al maner thynges werre myght moſte auayle right anone began ſayle whan redy without abode eche ſhyppe water rode whan wynde theyr luſte gan blowe ioye ſe go rowe whiche made faſte haſt theyr waye ſhorte tyme come ben troye hauen called symeonte whan phebus fer vnder theyr oryſonte weſtred men ne myght hym ſe grekes eſcaped peryll ſee caſte theyr ancres thought beſte theyr ſhyppes ſame nyght reſte y• morowe whan y• larke ſonge worthy grekꝭ ſo māly ſo ſtronge began lande haſte myghte troye grounde theyr tentys pyght • afore towne great dylygence ne founde maner reſyſtence whyle ſette good awayte euery ſyde leſte deceyte tyll houre ſonne bryghte hadde morowe ſhade rody lyghte amyd felde vpon euery tente whiche tyme one aſſente grekes aſſembled euerychon • byddynge kynge anone iaſon firſte hym hercules many worthy beynge pres ben ten • e pelleus come whan lordes ſome • ogyder place met eche degre ſet pelleus whan al whyſte ſtyll began ryght thus declare wyll noble worthy hye eſtate lowe whoſe knyghtly fame thrugh y• world yknow reported fer ſhyneth ſonne grekes yet neuer thynge begonne ne hadde victorye ende lawrer fer men may wende crowned ben toke hande suche theyr happe ſe lande ¶wherfore ye lordꝭ moſte worthy renowne ye remembre kynge lameoow • e wronge y• vpon • rought whan harme hym none ne thought whiche muſte quyt ſhortly ende come ſtroye ſhende wherfore anone haſte may lete v ſet without delay firſte rede take hede thynges thre moſte helpynge nede ¶firſte aduyſe good diſcrecion defence ſauacion prudently wardes make none oures myſcheif take ylke daye lacke prouydence ſeconde dylygence myght hole entencion laboure full deſtruccion four foe owne glorye thirde may victorye reioyſe platly laſte ye maye afore well caſte knyghthod thorugh hardyneſſe may venquyſſhe ſhal ſo hyerycheſſe conquere poſſeſſiowne knowen troye towne plente ſhalbe founde golde treaſour paſſyngly habounde ſhyppes ſothly wene receyue ne ſhall nat mow ſuſtene habundaunce yonder within ſo cyte wyn god v graunte wyll ¶and alſo faſte kynge ſtyll noble knyght ſtronge hercules preſence worthy pres sayd counſayle hyghly cōmende wyſe begynnynge preyſed ende effect purpoſe brynge counſayle mornynge tofore diſcured ben daye v arme haſte maye felde payne deuyde mayne twayne tone ſhall kynge thelamowne gouernour hye renowne kynge pelleus ſhall haue gouernaunce wyſely ſaue myſelfe iaſon brother shall ſecretly go vnder cyte ſonneſhynes buſſhayle thycke vynes ſhall v hyde kepe v full koye lamedon kynge troye anone may eſpye grekes chyualrye cyte wyll iſſue anone fyghte venge hym fone whan cometh ſhyppes warde neſtor duke ſhall firſte warde mete hym caſtor ſhall alſo whan ſeeth tyme knyghtly haue ado helpe neſtor nede thirde warde pelleus ſhall lede whyles ye thus hym occupye iaſon ſhall v faſte hye cyte vnwyſt echone doute nat ſhall wynne anone dothe counſayle wyll auayle trouthe ye may nat fayle conquere cyte yonder afore ſome ye gete accorde wt al theyr ſtrēgth myght arme ſtele y• ſhone full bryght agayne ſonne morowe whan ryſeth wrought fully hercules deuyſeth ¶how grekes armed vpon morowe fought troyens diſcomfyte toke theyr cyte diſtroyed capitulo ix lamedon whan herde tell comyng h • lyſt lēger dwell went many noble knyght flourynge youthe deſyrous fyght tho myght armes bere coude ſho • e durſte handell ſpere whan aſſembled felde eueryche armes depeynt vpon ſhelde brouded bete vpon coote armure lamedone beſy cure set inordre wardes maketh felde forthe way taketh towarde grekes lyneryght fully purpoſynge abyde fyght nat ware behynde nat aduerteth caſteth mynde great ſleyghte trecherye hym ſhape coude nat eſpye forthe went wardes ſet grekes anone hym hath met herte bolde aſtoned nat alle duke neſtor firſte ſturdy walle whoſe manhod neuer founde lacke full knyghtly vpon hors backe herte men knyghtes eke gan preſe many worthy greke lamedon ſturdely mete whiche tyme felte full vnſwete ¶and frountell ful many manly man ſharpe ſperes firſte togyder ran ſwerdes ſharpe kene grounde thylke daye gyuen many wounde mette vpon euery ſyde thrugh plate mayle theyr woūdꝭ bled wyde baſenettes ryue crowne noyſe ſtrokes eyre gan ſowne blode ſhad newe grene ſoyle chaunged hath dyed playnly reed vpon whiche full many man lay deed many worthy loſt lyfe certaynly mortall ſtryfe grekes hadde diſcomfyted echone ne caſtor ſocoured anone troye ſo manly haue bore many knyght grekes lore whan caſtor entreth batayle knyghtes ſo ſore dyde aſſayle worthy troyans y• ſpere ſhelde grekes agayne recouerde haue felde many one lyeth ſlayne grene gyrt thorugh body wt ſharpe ſperes kene troye mortall ſtoure dryue backe tyll came ſocoure haſte worthy lamedowne whiche entrede lyke wood lyowne made waye vpon euery ſyde made ſwerde glyd • deth ſo manly hym bare well vnneth none dare abyde ſtroke rydynge vp downe made waye aboute hym enuyrowne renges hath foen ſought day armes meruailes hath wrought manhod worthyneſſe grekes hath brought ſuche diſtreſſe ſwerde fledde deth mercyles ſo many ſleeth whiche ſlaughter grekes confuſe tyll pelleus came theyr reſcuſe irous wood fall rage thought wolde great pompe aſwage troye ſo dyde one vnhorſeth many one felly ſlough ſtode hym aforne many harneys hath day torne made ſheldes ryue ſondre beholde wondre tyll lamedone people ſawe go backe pelleus brought ſo wracke wherof herte felte full great payne beſechynge repayre agayne kythe theyr myght lyke men endure ſo felde made recure tyll duke neſtor knewe lamedowne amyd felde kynge troye towne right anone without abode agaynſt hym full great paſe rode whan kynge dyde hym firſte eſpye hye diſpyte rancour enuye knyghtly wyſe gan tourne agayne thynge agaſt hye diſdayne irous herte enbolled pryde hor • fyerſly gan take ſyde tyll ranne rede blode neſtor lyke woode rode anone ſpere brake full knyghtly kept hors bake full delyue • ly hym agayne quyte w • th ſpere full ſharpe whette byte thorugh ſheld breſt gaue hym ſuch woūde fro hors felde h • downe groūde whiche falle kynge thynge ferde ro • e hym vp drewe ſwerde angre fret hym herte rote vnhorſed fyghte muſte fote wherof party full confuſe tyll one cedar came reſcuſe made knyght ſelfe ſame yere yonge freſſhe luſty noble chere syttynge tyme noble ſtede whan gan take hede ſawe kynge fote myſcheif fyght gan pryke haſte myght towarde neſtor ſpere hymhytte ſadell made hym f • ytte downe grounde afore kynge lamedon anone lyke champion recured vp hym ſelfe diffendeth many ſtroke eche ſpendeth ſharpe ſwerdes kene byte eueryche gan foyne ſmyte tyll lamedone diſpytous chere face raſed viſer force one ſmet ryche cercle baſenet large perle goynge enuyrowne creſte fyerſly bete downe whyles neſtor thus afore hym ſtode face depeynt blode certaynly ſothe conclude hadde nat grekes great multytude reſcued hym lamedowne beſlayne faſte bore downe vnto erthe amonge hors f • te caſtor thought ne wolde lete helpe byhelde fere irouſly toke myghty ſpere cedar ſpake late gan ryde prycke great hate came toke hym douteles troyan knyght called segnerides coſyn cedar whan hath ſene courſer rode anone bytwene ſpere ſmote caſtor ſo ſtroke brake euen two caſtor without areſte hath ſpere amyddes breſte segnerides gyue mortall wounde lykly neuer ſounde wherfore cedar caughte ſuche enuye anone melancolye deſpyte boylynge herte segnerides whan ſawe ſo ſmerte maugre grutcheth amyddes felde myght caſtor toke ſhelde thorugh vyſer rancour rage wounded hym amyddes vyſage hors fro hym alſo caughte ſquyer manfully raughte certaynly ſtode ſuche diſioynt worthy caſtor poynt haue taken troye tho fote hym muſt haue go ne hadde pollux many manly knyght mo vii hondred ſtele armed bryght rather come caſtor reſcewe whiche ſo ſoregan ſewe maugre caſtor whan fonde force toke hym fro theyr honde hors reſtored hym agayne pollux certayne anger feruent ire agayne troyens rancour ſet fyre one vpon ſette mode fortune mette troyan knyght called elyatus armes yonge freſſhe deſyrous wonder ſemely tendre age kynges ſone alſo cartage neuewe eke vnto lamedon whan pollux hath lyke fyers lyon without routhe pyte mercy renges ſlayne cruelly lamedone whan gan take hede inwarde dole felte herte blede whan hym ſawe euen vpon dethe full pytouſly yelde vp brethe vpon playne lay hym beforne whiche anone made ſowne horne whiche tyme came full ryche araye seuen knyghtꝭ haſte maye vpon dethe auenged whiche mercyles great cruelte grekes haue grounded lyeth one dede another wounded myght haue take mortally made go abake gan tourne theyr confuſion fynally day lamedon tryumphe hadde felde gone saue ala towne anone vnto kynge came meſſangere hath hym tolde full pytous chere grekes haue cyte take ¶than ſe wo dyde make wolde haue made pytous herte blyue dole ſondre ryue ſore gan within hym ſelfe morne wyſte nat partye may torne weer abydynge longe afore hym ſawe myghty grekes ſtronge cyte another hooſt behynde almoſte wo went mynde ſodeynly bakwarde behelde towarde cyte ſawe come felde firſte hercules hym iaſon theyr ſleyghte wonne towne ¶and haſte cruell hercules myghty gyaunt force pereles lyke lyon wood deſpytous tygre rage furyous gan newe troye aſſayle ſwerde perce plate mayle whiche labour full mate feynt longe fyghte weryneſſe atteynt came luſty freſſhe grene force myght nat ſuſtene rode amonge yonder cruell wyſe ſeuered ſonder put hooly hye myſchaunce reule gouernaunce kynge oppreſſed dole wardes deſtytute ſole myſcheif left infortunat comforte fully diſconſolat hercules deſpytous loke ſharp ſpores ſtede felly toke cruelly rode lamedowne erthe fyerſly bare hym downe vpon hym haſte myght downe hors ſodeynly lyghte myghtely rent baſenette ſwerde ſharp grounde whette smote hede none grace caſte forthe ſelfe place amonge hors cruell vyolence without pyte reuerence arage raughte hors agayne lyke alyon rennynge playne baredowne ſloughe came weye many troyan day made deye lyke ſhepe ſkatered wyde deſtytute gouernour guyde ne rede ſhortly conclude grekes double multytude gan enchace amonges nede many day bleſſydfull lyfe lede frome yere yere reuoluciowne theyr manhode theyr hye renowne theyr honour ran rounde worlde aboute offende many lande hath doute theyr knyghthode ſo wyſe ¶and tyll ſtorye lyſte agayne deuyſe manere ferther procede fauour goodlyhede wyll reſte lytell ſpace vp borne wt ſupporte grace accomplyſſhe vndertoke ende firſte boke make quakynge hande drede 〈◊〉 fere ſhall rede lyſte ye ala haſty mocyon ne wyll nat haue compaſſyon pyte routhe vpon rudeneſſe lowly beſechynge gentylneſſe mercy oonly bothe nyghe ferre ye fynde fayle erre correcte ye ferther flytte grace hooly commytte lydgate complayneth hym fortune firſte dyſtruccyon cyte troye begynneth ſeconde boke folowynge mater ſayde ſtorye capitulo x enuyous ordre fortunat meuȳge worldly thynge falſe flykerynge ne wyll nat ſuffre v ī p̄ſent lyfe 〈…〉 reſte without werre ſtryfe ſhe blynde fykell vnſtable hir courſe falſe full mutable ſytte hyeſt ſhe downe hym enclyne 〈…〉 leeſt weneth brynge hym ruyne 〈…〉 •• ay • e gladly ben ſodayne hir face parted twayne shewe mooſt hole whan ſhe leeſt tryſte tha • well hym hir diſceytes wyſte 〈…〉 engynes hir trappes knewe euery daye hir courte newe whiche ſothe well afferme dare mortall man may lyfe beware ſhe vneuen peyſynge balaunce countrefete fayned countenaunce lokynge playne chere flaterye vnwarely blere mannes eye hym begyle ſothe face blandyſſhynge ſmothe whā ſhe hath hym fro hye degre brought lowe full falſly ſmyle make hym mowe yet ſomwhyle mooſt varyaunt hewe vnto ſome pretendeth trewe ſhe whylom ſome fauourable ſome falſe deceyuable reyſe one brynge another downe falſe lady tranſmutaciowne ſome ſhe gyueth renowne victorye dothe floure honour glorye ſome ſhe apayre falſe fame gyltles put man blame ſome ſhe goodly benyngne diſdayne ſhe alſo malygne agayne another make hym lowte lowe theyr ſees ſhe kynges throwe auayle theyr hye toures ſhe plonge worthy emperours hylle hye proſperyte vale aduerſyte ryche emporyſſhe rancoure diſdayne pore ſhe enhaunce agayne falſe goddeſſe hir eyen blynde set one afore nother gothe behynde dothe one renne nother halte one ſhe rycheſſe hye exalte nother plonge pouerte man may haue ſykerte ſome ſugre hony ſhe diſtylleth ſome ſhe botell fylleth bytter galle myrre ale thus lady wylfull recheles ſhe frowarde peruers hath hir ſeler drynkes dyuers ſhe ſome fraude falla mynyſtreth pyment bawme ypocras ſodaynly whan ſoote paſte cuſtome gyue hym caſte conclude falſly fyne bytter eyſell egre wyne corroſynes fret perce depe narcotykes cauſe men ſlepe thus ſhe hir approche ſwete bytter broche hir reygne quene varyaunce whoſe ioye fyneth alway myſchaunce truſteth hir ſhe wyll hym ouer caſte hym deceyue playnly laſte eſtate ſo euer double lady mut abylyte se example kynge lamedon ſhe hath brought confuſion lytell cauſe athynge nouthe hir cruelte hath dere bought wherfore rede euery man take hede gynne quarell nede lytell fyre vnder aſſhes reke may kyndled wyll breke ſuche flawme men may nat peaſe beſte ſuffre moſt ſhall haue eaſe therfore ye kynges lordes euerychone make myrour lamedone well ware vyolence vnto ſtraungers whan none offence whan come fer regyon ne ſuffre nat none oppreſſyon boundes haue wronge owne though ye ſtronge myghty eke amonge lyeges alle nother daye perauenture may falle whan ye full lytell thynke ſodayne caſe ye may quyt thanked nother place auenture ye happe pace therfore whan ye may ſuche eſpye doo good chere curteſye prudently conſyder wyt lorde gentylleſſe ſyt euery ſtraunger goodly hym haue thyng may honour ſaue refreſſhe frely diſporte may good hym reporte whoſe cōtrarye hath moch wo wrought afore tyme well ſought firſte troy vtterly deſtroyed people ſorowe wo cloyed lad exyle fer fro theyr cyte lyuynge thraldome captyuyte exyone ye haue herde telle lad grece thelamon dwelle guydo teche take ſo great vengaunce wreche eyther parte trouthe moche routhe boke ye maye rede ceryouſly ye lyſte take hede gladly aye reuoluſion fatall thynge diſpoſicion ſo enuyous alway meynt wo worlde ſo go truely may aduerte thought value thynge nought mortall cauſes werres firſte begonne ſtryfe debate vnder ſonne meued firſte ſmale occaſion cauſed great confuſion noman harmes halfe endyte cauſe dere inough myte eche redy deſtroye man lytell wyll ſtryue brother blode vnkynde whiche greatly drede ala ne wyll take better hede olde troye newe thorugh ſmall encheſon y• trouthe knewe fynally brought diſtruccion olde bokes make mencion many worthy many noble knyght slayne felde dute •• e fyght kynges prynces ſege dede whan attropos breke theyr lyues threde tell myſcheif wo wante connynge fele alſo penne quake tremble honde lyſte lorde dradde ſee londe whoſe worthynes thrugh ye world doth ſprede makynge rude ſhall beholde rede whiche colour full naked bare grace ſpare diſdayne lyſte haue pyte fere tremble ſhulde ſe ¶but onely mercy yt doth herte enbrace byd preſume fully grace seynge hym moſte vertuous gode mercy anexed vnto royall blode prynce longeth nyghe ferre aye tofore right pyte preferre thorugh ſupporte hye nobleſſe sowpowayled wyll ſtyle dreſſe wryte forth ſtorye newe troye ordre ceryouſly myn auctour latyn guydo wryt prayeng reder worde myſſyt cauſynge metre halte lame correcte ſaue fro blame lete hym wayte curyoſyte syth ryme englyſſhe hath ſcarſte ſo dull certayne ne folowe guy clerke coryous man whiche latyn hath rethoryke set ſo wordes nat lyke ſewe ſtyle tranſlacion worde worde lyke conſtruccion maner gramaryens lyke ſtyle rethorycyens toke nat ſtorye tranſlate clyo came late ſuche crafte hath great experyence leue theſe wordes folowe ſentence trouthe metre ſette alſo ſyde art hadde tho guyde reduce whan went wronge toke none hede nouther ſhorte longe trouthe lefte euryoſyte bothe makynge metre nat purpoſynge moche varye dyuers contrarye vnto guydo diſcordaunce conforme fully ſubſtaunce oonly menynge conclude one ne way gone ſewe floures eloquence peyntynge haue none excellence ſondry hewes noble freſſhe gay ryche colour byggen ne may muſte procede ſable blacke ennewynge ye fynde lacke axe mercy fro twynne fauour wyll anone begynne haſte ſtyle forth dyrecte erre praye correcte ſame tyme whan yt troye towne deſtroyed kyng lamedowne alſo ſlayne thorugh cruelte hercules vnder eyte ſone ſtorye telleth v whiche heyce called pryamus wonder manly diſcrete prudente whiche tyme troye abſent whan fader loſte lyfe tyme ecuba wyfe ſones aboute caſtell lay knyghtes gete may hath myghtely werreyed fader haue falſly diſobeyed vnto hym rebell wonder longe pryam wt ſautes huge ſtronge hadde aſſayled ofte many ſythe ſtrengthe lyke knyght kythe gete armes worſhyp honour daunte lyke conquerour caſte hym fully departe day day lyfe gan iuparte theyr walles preue myght many baron many worthy knyght yet hadde yonge luſty blode age flowrynge knyghthode aſſautes ſuche maner ſtryfe firſte auntre lyfe herte men hym lyſte nat behynde drede dethe ſothly fynde afore caſtell hye thycke walled wyfe ecuba called pryam full worthy degree fyue ſones yonge doughters three whiche eldeſt ector called whiche alſo fer phebus compas naturell daye goth cercle aboute fer hym without doute reported renowne name worthyneſſe noble fame lyke bokes hym ſpecefye roote ſtocke chyualrye knyghthod ſoueraygne floure ſours welle worſhyp honoure manhod dare well expreſſe example myroure hye proweſſe gynnynge grounde yfere wonder benygne lowely chere diſcrete alſo prudent vertuous dedes actes meruaylous remembred ben ſo longe gone alone excelled euerychone olde auctours rede ye may fynde knyghthod yet make mynde nexte brother called parys nature gaue herdeuys ſhap fourme beaute ſemelyneſſe remembre excellent fayreneſſe tyme without drede paſſed rede eke full manly knyght mooſt vſed whan ſhulde fyght hande bere abowe ſuche archer man coude knowe ſeke bothe fer nere ſhotynge myght pere founde whan hadde alyſaundre called alſo thirde ſone hyghte dephebus worthy knyght chyualrous hadde armes full great renowne man hye diſcreciowne wyſe coūſayle myn auctor telleth thus ¶the fourth brother called helenus sad diſcrete hye prudence alſo man great ſcyente renōmed therwith ſpecyall artes called lyberall expert ryght fyfte ſone worthy knyght freſſhe luſty yongeſt ſayth guydo troylus men hym call manly man founde barayle deſyrous fomen aſſayle
