one beſte tyme founde called ector ſecounde manhode thorugh troye boke within werre full ofte vpon hym toke knyghthod many hye empryſe ſtorye hereafter ſhall deuyſe boke lyke wryte virgyle poete olde full ſouerayneſtyle kynge pryam hadde alſo ecuba ſones two recorde virgilius one called pollyodorus pryamus grene youthe whan comynge grekes kouthe troye warde haſte anone golde treaſour many ryche ſtone sent hym forth beſyde vnto kynge full great truſte haue hym kepynge tyll tyme ſawe concluſiowne ſhulde falle towne eke fyne werre wolde take vpon grekes dyde make ¶but thylke kynge falſe couetyſe treaſour ye haue herde deuyſe whan ſawe fortune varyaunce towward pryam vnhappy chaunce lyke tyraunt murdrer alſo childes throte made cutte two full cruelly made men burye hym pryuely man myght treſon vnderſtonde beſyde ſee depe vnder ſtronde ſone alſo irede virgyle called ganymede iubyter foreſt hente gpon daye huntynge wente bare hym vp aboue ſterres clere made hym heuen botelere eternally hym wone ſtede hebe owne dere ſone firſte doughter kynge pryamus hyght creuſa ſayth virgilius eneydos ſothly ſhe wedded vnto eneas ſayth ſtorye eke ylke enee wonderfull natyuyte fader fynde doutles tyme called anchyſes hym begat venus goddeſſe hir hadde ſuche fayreneſſe neuer wyght ne coude yet ſe man paſſynge beaute ſtorye touchyng workynge shall declare many wonder thynge ſo great los virgyle gaue eneydos boke worſhyp enee compyled hath lyke ye may ſe knyghthod many ſtronge batayle hym acheued wan itayle full longe royall towne troye brought confuſiowne conqueſt ye lyſte take hede poete ye may ordre rede armes wrought age comynge alſo cartage fro troyewarde lytell whyle ye may beholde virgyle another doughter alſo founde kynge pryam hadde byrthe ſeconde called caſſandra full great ſadneſſe maner dyuynereſſe eche art hadde experyence thynges futur fully preſcyence tell afore ſhall betyde fame ſprange coſtes wyde whiche kepte hirchaſte virgynyte aye prayer honeſte ladde hir lyfe deuocion rytes relygyon paganyſme vſed tho ſayes obſeruaunces kepynge theyrlayes thirde doughter hyght pollycene yongeſt euer maydeclene kepte hir ſelfe honeſt hir lawe vnto tyme pirrus hath hir ſlawe ſhap fortune neuer nature wrought ſhap fayrer creature eke fynde noble kynge alſo hadde thyrty ſones boke ſayth mo hardy armes noble founde called ſones naturall excepte none worthy knyghtes manly men echone theyr name ſo lyſte knowe ſhall fynde wryte vpon arowe ſtorye eueryche begynnynge firſte eldeſt brother whyles pryam ſege laye tofore caſtell gete maye theraboute hath many way ſought wofull tydynges vnto hym brought grekes haue take troye towne ſlayne fader worthy lamedowne cyte olde foundaciowne full pytouſly tourned vp ſo downe worthy lordes gentyll men echone taken ſlayne lefte nat one lyue thorugh grekes cruelte ruyne ala theyr cyte exion owne ſuſter dere lad exyle hir eyen clere ¶wherfore kynge herte ſtoned ſo ſorowe ne wyſte ſodayne wo gan hym ſo conſtrayne ſobbeth wepeth mortall payne thought herte wolde ſonder breſte hye diſtreſſe myght haue reſte teeres gan hymſelfe diſlylle deye fynally wylle ¶and fortune ſo falſly varye drery herte gan warye ſhe hym ſo deceyuable inly cruell vnmercyable diſpytous ſo ſterne face vengeable deuoyde grace enuy rage thought hath hir wreſte malys hȳ wrought felly ſhewed ſhe myght worlde neuer wyght ſo wo ſuppoſe maner age reken hir harmes damage whiche anone euer maye faſte chaungeth ryche araye tryſte heuy deedly face pale aſtoned mortall tale deſyre haue dede countenaunce enclyned hede lyfe ladde cladde hym blacke ſodaynely ſege bracke wolde tho lenger abyde folke anone gan ryde pyteouſly gan hym morne towarde troye attones retourne whan hath cyte founde playne ſoyle euen wt grounde hye walles whylom thycke longe vere downe made ſo ſtronge toures paleys pryncypall byldynge ſo excellent royall famous ryche great nobylneſſe fonde tourned wylderneſſe people ſlayne ſuſter ladde awaye wo ne wyſte ſaye conſtreynt aduerſyte harmes wyll recured tyme fully ſure vpon ſyde recure wherfore nat ſobbe wepe breſt wt ſyghes ſought full depe broken deed vyſage thus ala furyous rage full pyteouſly hooſte without reſpyte contynewe dayes thre tyll laſte derke ſkyes blacke gan theyr wo partye ſlacke tempeſt ſome delegan withdrawe theyr wepynge blādyſſhe gan y• wawe whan floode wo ouer paſte ebbe ioye folowe muſte haſte ſorowe euer wolde theyr hertes ſhende terme euery wo muſte ende though frendes men aye wepe wayle theyr deth may recure vayle wherfore kynge care hath ſought waye cyte repare caſte hym fully wolde make reuerture neceſſyte manfully tene whan eyre gan wexe clene myſtes cloudy ſorowe ſomedele adawe gan morowe heuyneſſe derke nyght chaced awaye ſonne bryght newe ioye aye fyne wo muſte gladneſſe whan ſorowe go ſo pryam certayne ſpace whan ſorowe gan lyte aud lyte pace wyſdome pytous ſmerte gan prudently plucke vp herte eyen wawes gan clere anone wrought right ye ſhall ¶how kynge pryamus ſone vnto kynge la medone buylded troye newe agayne ca xi ſorowe aſwaged ſyghes olde longe proceſſe lyke tolde worthy kynge called pryamus herte ſo deſyrous vpon playne ſo waſte wylde ſtronge towne newe bylde deuyſe cyte edefye ſhall aſſautes vtterly defye enmyes mortall foone ryche toures walles harde ſtoone aboute countres enuyron made ſeke euery regyon ſuche workemen curyous wyt inuentyfe caſtynge meruaylous ſuche coude crafte gemetrye ſotyll theyr fantaſye eueryche good deuyſous maſon hewer crafty quarreour euery wryghte paſſynge carpenter may founde ferre nere ſuche coude graue groupe kerue ſuche able ſerue lyme ſtone reyſe walle bataylynge creſtes marcyalle ſuche hadde konnynge theyr hede alabaſtre outher whyte rede marbyll graye pullyſſhe playne make ſmothe vaynes grayne ſente alſo euery ymagour bothe entayle euery portreyour coude drawe coloure peynte hewes freſſhe yt werke nat feynte ſuche coude wt countenaunce glade make image wyll neuer fade countrefete metall tree ſtoon ſotyll werke pygmaleon appollo whiche bokes telle ymagerye dyde excelle crafty workynge curyous tombe made kynge daryous whiche alyſaundre dyde heyght reyſe oonly men ſhulde fame preyſe conqueſt perce whan went thus pryam euery mayſter ſent eche keruere paſſynge ioygnyour make knottes many curyous floure ſette creſtes within withoute vpon wall cyte rounde aboute excellynge practyke arte called mecanyke hadde name flowrynge famous ſent come pryamus ¶for purpoſeth noble worthy kynge make cyte mooſt royall byloynge brode large wyde lyſt aſſayled werre proudely aboute enbatayled firſte grounde made ſought full depe lowe fayle nought make ſure foundaciowne place olde towne firſte ybylded walles ſette lande many myle mette aboute compaſſe make large mayſtres toke charge deuyſed haue ſettynge ſyte holſome eyre delyte whan ſoyle defouled ruyne walles olde made playne lyne workemen gan cyte founde full myghtely ſtones ſquare rounde worlde none lyche workemanſhyp byldynge ryche crafte curyous maſonrye termes ſpeke gemetrye wherfore muſte ſette aſyde douteles radde neuer enclyde mayſter foundour worke quare compas kepe theyr meaſure leuell lyne rude clerely diffyne diſcryue werke euery part lacke termes longynge arte dare well trouthe afferme world ne neuer pere vnto cyte wryte ſothe boke mayſter guydo dothe myght proſperyte hye honour felycyte aſſaute perpetuelly contune reyſed worſhyp neptune named troye forne lyke firſte thorugh grekes lorne lengthe ſhortly conclude thre dayes iourne lyke latytude neuer herde make mencion ſuche nother foundacion huge compaſe ſuche largeſſe counte ſo paſſynge fayreneſſe edefyed iuſty ſyghte rede walles hyghte two hondred cubytes marbyll graye magecolled without lautes aſſaye make pleaſaunt delyte amonge marbyll alabaſtre whyte meynt walles rounde y• towne make ſhewe within without freſſhe ſo ryche ſo delectable alone comparable cytes mortall man sawe euer yet ſythe worlde began corner euery walle ſette crowne golde ryche ſtones frette ſhone full bryght agayne y• ſonne ſhene euery toure bretexed ſo clene choſe ſtone nat fer ſondre beholde wondre therto cyte compaſſed enuyrowne hadde gate vi entre towne firſte ſtrengeſt eke largeſt alſo moſte pryncypall myghty byldynge alone pereles kynge called dardanydes ſtorye lyke founde tymbria named ſeconde thirde called helyas fourthe gate hyghte alſo cetheas fyfte troiana ſyxth anthonydes stronge myghty bothe werre pe ſquare toures ſet euery ſyde whoſe corner pompe pryde workemen haue ſterne fell vyſages ryche entayle ſette vp great ymages wrought ſtone yt neuer lyke fayle full curyouſly enarmed batayle thorugh walle theyr fomen lette euery toure great gonne ſette aſſautes ſodayne auentures tourette reyſed vp fygures wylde beeſtes beres lyon tygres bore ſerpentes dragon hertes eke theyr brode horne olyfauntes large vnycornes bugle bulles many great gryf • forged braſſe coper laton cruelly ſygnes theyr face vpon theyr foon made felle menace barbycans bul werkes huge afore towne made hye refuge nede erely eke late portekoles ſtronge euery gate nede nat none aſſaylynge charge locke thycke brode large gate bryght bra within myghty ſhyttynge ſtronge iren barres ſquare rounde great barres pytched grounde huge cheynes forged diffence whiche ne wolde breke vyolence harde thorugh wynne euery hous bylded within euery paleys euery manſtowne marbell thorughout towne crafty byldynge workynge moſte royall hyghte euery walle sixty cubytes grounde accounted none yt hath ſurmounted cyte one heyghte alyche ſothe bothe pore ryche harde hye eſtate lowe hous paleys ſonder knowe egally tymbre ſtone theyr houſes reyſed euerychone ſhulde reherſe korue knottes craſte maſonry freſſhe enbowȳge wt verge right lynes houſynge full bakewynes ryche koynynge luſty tablementes vynettes rennynge caſementes though termes englyſſhe wolde ryme reken haue tyme ne langage pycked none ſotyll ioynynge tell ſtones put ſtede mortere ioyntoures coper gylte full clere make ioyne leuell lyne amonge marbyll freſſhely ſhyne agaynſt ſonne whan ſhene lyght smote golde burned bryght make werke glyſtre euery ſyde towne ſtretes large wyde crafte ſo prudently prouyded werkmen ſette ſo deuyded holſome eyre amyddes myght enſpyre erely morowe deſyre zephyrus ſo comfortable noryſſhe thynges vegetable tyme yere thorughe euery ſtrete ſugred flauour ſo luſty ſo ſwete moſte pleſauntly eyre gan ſmyte cytezeynes oonly delyte brethe recomforte whan lyſte walke themſelfe diſporte thrugh ye towne wt crafty purueaunce great auyſe diſcrete ordenaunce compaſe caſte ſquared ſquyers polyſſhed marble vpon ſtronge pyllers deuyſed longe large wyde frontell euery ſtretes ſyde freſſhe alures luſty hye pynacles mouſtrynge outwarde ryche tabernacle vouted aboue lyke reclynatoryes called deambulatoryes men walke togyders twayne twayne kepe drye whan dyde rayne ſaue fro tempeſt wynde thundre lyſt ſhroude themſelf ther vndre euery hous couered leede many gargoyle many hydous heede ſpoutes thorugh pypes aughte ſtone werke canell taughte voydynge fylthes lowe grounde thorugh grate perced yron perced tounde ſtretes paued bothe lengthe brede cheker wyſe ſtones whyte rede euery crafte maner man lande deuyſe reken kynge pryamus hye diſcreciowne ordeyned hath dwelle towne ſtretes ſeuered yonder eueryche ſet ſonder myght cōmodyte eche hymſelfe werke lyberte goldſmythes firſte ryche iewelleres themfelfe crafty browdereres weuers alſo wollen lyn clothe golde damaſke ſatyn veluet ſendell dowble ſamyt eke eueryche clothe men lyſte ſeke smythes alſo coude forge wele pollaxes ſwerdes ſperes ſharpe ſtele dartes dagger mayme wounde quarethedes ſharpe ſquare ygrounde alſo crafty armerers bowyers faſte fletcher ſuche coude make ſhaftes playne eke dyde theyr beſy payne werre make alſo trappures bete baners royall cote armures deuyſe standardes penounſe felde freſſhe gay getounſe euery crafte may rekened tell ſhortly cyte thorughe towne ſoryche excellent myddes large ryuer went cauſynge full great cōmodyte whiche twayne hath parted cyte ofcours full ſwyfte wt freſſhe ſtremes clere hyghte xamtus guydo doth v lere rede vpon flode eche ſyde many mylle ſtode whā nede theyr grayne corne grynde ſuſteyne ſtorye fynde ryuer eke fyſſhe full plenteous deuyded werkmen curyous craftely thorugh caſtynge ſouerayne cours ſtremes myght attayne areche guydo doth comecte archys ſtronge cours reflecte thorugh condyte pypes large wyde withall certayne meanes artyficiall made full purgacion ordure fylthes towne waſſhynge ſtretes ſtode arowe gutter erthe lowe cyte fylthe ſene canell ſcoured ſo clene deuoyded ſo ſecrete wyſe man myght eſpye deuyſe engyne ſylthes fer nere borne awaye cours ryuere couertly euery thynge couered wherby towne vtterly aſſured engendrynge corrupcion wycked eyre infexion cauſe ofte theyr vyolence mortalyte great peſtylence example flode made cybre rome wrought eneas whiche alſo departeth rome two myn auctour ſayth note ſo enhabyte royall chefe cyte kynge pryam hath aboute countre made ſerche hole entent prouynces adiacent borowes townes ſmale vyllages ygadred maner age thropes folkes full dyuers ſuche vacaunt dyſpers aboute troye regiowne made hath entre towne great multitude yonge olde enhabyte ye haue herde tolde afore hym foreynes hath troye made cyteſeynes full diſcretly lyke founde whan gan people abounde ¶kynge pryamus hye affecciowne buyldynge myghty towne hath herte caught fantaſye newe cyte magnefye put remembraunce caſte fully ſome obſeruaunce myghty mar ſterne ferſe hewe ſpecially certayne playes newe hors foote many ſondry wyſe gyue men knyghthode excerſyſe eueryche put aſſay iuſtes boordes alſo tournay preue theyr force whan happe mete whiche playes foūded firſte crete lande hye lowe eſtate martys honoure dedycate paleſte wake nyght playes men aſſaye myght oonly foote many ſotyll poynt ſome naked enioynt wynne pryſe dyde full entent founde clerkes full prudent cheſſe playe moſte gloryous whiche ſo ſotyll ſo meruaylous harde mater diſcryue though man ſtudyed lyue ſhall aye fynde dyuerſe fantaſyes wardes makynge newe iupartyes ſo great dyuerſyte firſte founde cyte durynge ſege lyke ſayth guydo iacobus de vitriaco coutrarye oppynyon lyke maketh mencyon affermeth fully aduyſe philometer phyloſopher wyſe vnto kynge ſtynte crueltee fonde firſte play made caldee grece then ſent alſo troye great auyſement playe founde firſte dyce table caſtynge chaunces deceyuables haue cauſe ofte great debate one nowe founde fortunate wynne whyle fauoure chaunce ware ſodayne varyaunce vnhappely put backe nother ſtode vpon wracke loſſe plonged diſtreſſe reyſed haue vnto hye rycheſſe gladneſſe one nother rage deuaunt haſarde paſſage one haue ioye another ſuffreth wo lyke bone ronne fro hondred ſythe daye varye blandyſſhynge contrarye man aſſured ioye firſte alſo rede troye ſonge red many freſſhe comedyes dytees called tragedyes declare ſhortly ſentence bothe two fynall difference ¶a comedye hath gynnynge pryme face maner complaynynge afterwarde endeth gladneſſe dedes oonly doth expreſſe ſuche pouerte plonged lowe tragedye ſo lyſte knowe begynneth proſperyte endeth euer aduerſyte alſo doth conqueſte treate ryche kynges lordes greate myghty men olde conqueroures whiche fraude fortune ſhoures ouer caſte whelmed theyr glorye whylom thus halowed y• memorye tragedyes bokes make mynde whan red ſonge fynde ¶in theatre ſmale auter amyddes ſette halfe circuler whiche eſt cuſtome directe vpon whiche pulpet erecte therin ſtode auncyent poete reherſe rethorykes ſwete noble dedes hyſtoryall kynges prynces memoryall theſe olde worthy emperours great empryſe eke conquerours gate martes hye honoure lawrer grene fyne theyr laboure palme knighthod diſſerued olde date parchas made paſſe fate ¶and chere face pale ſtyle enclyned gan tourne tale ſynge theyr loo full mortally ſtroke antropos tell alſo theyr worthy hede ſodayne brekynge theyr lyues threde pytouſly made theyr mortall ende thrugh falſe fortune yt y• world wyll ſhende fyne theyr worthyneſſe endede ſorowe hye tryſteſſe compaſſynge fraude falſe treaſon ſodayne murdre vengeaunce poyſon conſpyrynge fretynge falſe enuye vnwarly dyde dye theyr renowne theyr hye fame hatrede ſodaynly made lame theyr honour drough vnto declyne myſchefe theyr vnhappy fyne fortune vnſwete tolde red poete whyle pulpet ſtode dedely face deuoyde blode syngynge dytees muſes rent amyd theatre ſhrowded tent cam men gaſtfull theyr cheres diffygured theyr face vyſeres playeng ſygnes people ſyght poete ſonge hath heyght maner diſcordaunce wene dytees theyr countenauce ¶for lyke lofte dyde expreſſe wordes ioye heuyneſſe menynge benethe playeng poynt poynt alway anſweryng triſte glade heuy lyght face chaunged ſodayne ſyght craftely coude tranſfygure conformynge chaunce plure ſynge ſodaynly wepe well coude theyr obſeruaunces kepe done apryll may whan bloſmes newe bothe buſſhe hay floures freſſhe gynne ſprynge byrdes wood ſynge luſte ſuppryſed ſomer ſonne whan theſe playes troye begonne theatre halowed yholde thus ryte tragedyes olde pryamus worthy kynge began mater tell bvt wyll forth ſtorye wryte mater boyſtouſly endyte pryamus paſſynge dylygent right deſirous wardly feruent myght amonge werkes alle bylde paleys ryche halle whiche ſhulde choſe chefe dungyon royall ſee ſouerayne manſyon whan gan werke approche made bylde hye vpon roche aſſure foundacion called noble ylion ſyght whiche iuſtly circuler compaſe caſt rounde ſper wold content ye grounde truely acounte place rounde theatre firſte muſte entre takynge ye lyne yt kerueth thorugh centre gemetrye longeth art trebled ſeuenthe part fynde myght experyence meaſure hole circumference lande alſo playnly eke conteyned within ſtronge wall creſte whiche loweſt hadde heyghte full ſyxe hondred pa bylded marbyll full royall full ſtronge many ryche ſtone amonge whoſe toures reyſed vp ſo hye raughte almoſte lkye werke whiche man myght amende lyſte greces vp aſſende myght ſe inſpeccyon boundes many regyon prouynces ſtode rounde aboute walles within withoute endlonge knottes grauen clene depeynt aſure golde cynopre grene veryly whan ſonne ſhone vpon golde meynt amonge ſtone gaue lyght withouten phebus doth mydday ſpere worke wyndowe eke feneſtrall wrought beryle clere cryſtall ¶and amyddes ylyon freſſhe ſo ryche foundacyon whiche clerkes yet theyr bokes prayſe kynge pryam made halle rayſe excellynge beaute ſtrengthe latytude accordynge lengthe marbyll outwarde walle tymbre moſte noble ſpecialle halfe cedre reherſe remenaunt ryche eban whiche moſte able dare ſpecefye ſtone ioyne crafte carpentrye tymber haue ſoueraynte tell eban tree lyke bokes ſothely fynde cometh ethyope ynde blacke geete wyll wexe anone whan korue harde ſtone euermore laſte endure nat corrupte water moyſture halle diffyne ſtones ſquare leuell lyne paued great dilygence maſonrye paſſynge excellence aboue reyſed ſee full curyouſly ſtones perre called chefe pryncipall reygne ſete moſte royall fore whiche ſette great delyte borde eban yuery whyte egally yioyned ſo clene werke ryfte ſene ſeſſyouns made euery ſyde oonly eſtates ordre deuyde eke halle couenable eche partye dormaunt table yuery eke eban tree euen agayne kynges royall ſe partye therto contrayre reyſed many crafty ſtayre hye halle ſyte right lyne oppoſyte pured metall ſtones clere brede lengthe full ryche autere whiche ſtode fygure vyſage maſſy fe golde wonderfull ymage honoured hye ſete oonly honour iubyter grete ¶and ſtatute huge heyghte fyftene cubytes complet heyghte crowne golde hye vpon heede heuenly ſaphyres many ruby rede fret enuyron ſtones ynde amonges medled fynde whyte perles maſſyfe large rounde moſt chefe dirkeneſſe confounde carbuncle kynge ſtones alle recomforte glade halle enlumyne blacke nyght freſſheneſſe rody lyght value therof ineſtymable rycheſſe playnly comparable ymage dyuyſion ſhap proporcion heed fote ſo mayſterly entayled apoynt y• workman hath nat fayled parfourme crafty excellence pryamus drede reuerence honoured hath aboue goddes alle myſchefe hym clepe calle hym hole affeccion ſoueraygne truſte deuocion hope alſo affyaunce helthe ioye aſſuraunce welfare proſperyte hath cōmytted deyte wenynge herte wonder ſykerly aſſured myſchefe therby diffended eche aduerſyte holde reygne hye felycyte honour contynuelly ſhyne whyle iubyter thorugh power dyuyne hym hath proteccion truſte full opynyon thus werke fynally achyeued wherof pryam ioye full releued cyte noble ylyon hath fully brought vnto perfeccyon lyke entent whan began thus pryam kyge worthy man full many day newe troye lyeges lad lyfe ioye hym leue royall ſete soueraygnely reygnynge quyete procedynge forthe ye lyſte vnto effect anone matere ¶how kȳg pryamus ſent anthenor īto grece haue ſuſter exyone agayne ca xij hateful harme moſt dred kyndled ſolonge oſparke old hatred roote debate grounde enuy • newe flawme hertes fyre grayne malys cauſer offence francour ruſted impacience whiche haſt newe made feſtred ſores ſinerte whan thou art one raked herte whiche diſdayne mercy mayſt lete man whyle lyue equyte delueſt vp malys many folde debate newe buryed olde falſly quykeſt ſtryues reſtore enuyous ſerpent y• ſlayne yore whiche felly hath addre enuyous reſte awaked pryamus venym ſo perſynge ſo ylle made hym wery lyue tranquylle meued hym iniquyte vpon grekes auenged pea helde reygne lyeges ioy ſouereygne without anoye perturbaunce ſerpent hath newe remembraunce without aduyſe diſcrete areſte hoote flawme kyndled breſte olde enuye freſſhe rancour meynte lykly neuer queynte pryam nowe entenciowne caſte compaſſeth reuoluynge vp downe howe ſtronge rycheſſe meyne howe noble myghty alſo cyte habundaunt ſhortly conclude bothe plente multytude men armes chyualrye whiche ſtered hym haue fantaſye ala whyle vnhappy chaunce deed take wyll vengeaunce vpon foon fyre hoote enuye brent hym warde malencolye stondynge purpoſe yt man chaūge may damage auenged ſome day miuryes yt hym haue wrought whan tyme ſought purpoſe moſte conuenyent anone hath lordes ſent knyghtes called euerychone come haſte excuſed nat one namely hye degre obeyeng humylyte byddynge hooly made delay come echeone agayne certayne day ſones alſo preſent ector except tyme abſent ſtronge myghty regyon panomye whiche ſubieccyon kynge pryam helde thorugh worthyneſſe amende thynges redreſſe ector gone panomye certayne cauſes iuſtefye reaſon thought beſte ſette quyete reſte aye ſo iuſte ſo prudent well aduyſed ſo pacyent ſo demened gouernaunce hym lothe vengeaunce myght eaſy wyſe treate reforme thynges ſmale greate lothe noble worthy knyght haſte execute ryght cauſeles rygour condempne whyle full worthy ſolempne kynge pryamus lordes great ſmall within troye helde court royall lyſte coſte ſpare ceryouſly menynge declare ſee lordes enuyron gan thus ſhewe hertes mocyon worthy lordes preſent faythfull trewe herte entent nat vnknowen diſcrecyon great damage oppreſſyon whiche grekes haue vpon v wrought without cauſe thynge nought daye ſayth late trowe ſo newe yet date freſſhe remēbred mynde vnto blode ye kynde ſuppoſe foryetylneſſe may put awaye mortall heuyneſſe harmes olde whiche aye renewe agayne memorye ſaye certayne trowe playnly thought euer grene ne dyeth nought haue ſlayne progenytours whylom ſo noble werreours cyte brente brought vnto ruyne robbed falſly rauyne tourned wylderneſſe grece caryed rycheſſe fader ſlayne hyghte lamedon without cauſe occaſyon raught hym golde treſour whiche ſemeth foule errour myght right amendes well chalenge deſyre v iuſtly reuenge afore goddes ſo hye offence oonly reaſon conſcyence paſſynge theyr mortall cruelte one thynge moſte greueth vngoodly agaynſt gentylleſſe rewarde hauynge worthyneſſe byrthe ne royall blode hir ſo fayre eke ſo gode meane ſuſter called exyon ala theyr confuſyon difuſe kepe nat lyke hir degre day day diſhoneſte thorugh hir honour hir name lorne conſyderynge nat ſtok ſhe borne blynde take hede aduerte roote hir kynrede ſurquyde ſo indu rate ſythe ſhe ſo hye eſtate ytreted • lyke ye may ſe ſuppoſe lowe degre eouerned full diſhoneſtly ye may thynke demetruely wyues maydens companye eke allye ynaunted vſed theyr luſte grekes haue better truſte ne ſpare nother blode age thus lyue turment ſeruage without touthe mercy pyte whiche toucheth well ſemeth equyte ryght ye oughte echone full myght wronges whiche ye offended ſeke awaye myght amended worke one aſſent procede lyke oure entent theyr malys curſed cruelte one auenged herte wyll thought one accorde ne vary nought force dowbled pouſte right reaſon good equyte requyre vengeaunce hym y• doth y• wronge though ſo abyde longe truſte alſo goddes rightwyſeneſſe ſhall helpe harmes redreſſe fauour v innocence chaſtyſe wrought offence alſo ye knowe cyte ſtronge myghty great ſuerte toures hye walled werre alſo fer ſhyneth ſonne ſterre none lyke reken may force therto perygall ye knowe alſo ſhalbe founde chyualrye habounde expert armes olde aſſayed drede neuer diſmayed haue plente alſo vytayle frendſhyp eke ne wyll v nat fayle theyr myght v ſocour wherfore rede without ſoiour ſette vpon ſythe able tyme nowe ſemeth couenable manhode byd make delay venge wronge hap may differynge ofte great damage worke tyme double auauntage purpoſe lacketh neuer adele thorugh manhod aſſured wele lyſte nat holde haſty rakell worke wylfully werre alſo ſtande auenture aye mart doutous eure rede firſte grekes ſende wyt harmes wyll amende without ſtryfe werre debate may ſayne fortunate contrarye reaſon condyſcende concluſion graunte aſkynge equyte ryght haue cauſe preue myght procede rygour ſhall offer meaſour fer right reaſon eke requere diſdayne lyſt nat quarell deuoyde wylfulneſſe yrooted vpon ſykerneſſe theyr great offence axe amendes firſte pacyence god fortune hope wyll nat aſſente ende ſhall v nat repente better pea haue redreſſe gynne werre without auyſeneſſe therfore lete v wofull auenture pacyently ſuffre endure porte humble playne vpon anſwere wyll ſayn • though ſo myne entencion ymeued iuſte occaſion procede yre vengeaunce wyll put remembraunce lete ſlyde foryetfulneſſe wronges voyde heuyneſſe towarde grekes axe wyll exyona reſtore v agayne whiche moſte derre oonly ſtynte debate werre ſurplus mortall eure ſhall diſſymule prudently endure harmes olde forth pacyence ye accorde vnto ſentence saye vpon ye auyſed ſonde deſpyſed lyſte reaſon obeye may iuſtely ſeke nother weye haue redreſſe saue purpoſe ſende anthenore whiche man diſcrete auyſee ſpecyally mater treate bothe wyſe eloquente ye well knowe paſſyngly prudente whan kynge tolde tale anone counſayle conſent euerychone anthenor iourney vndertake haſte gan hym redy make without abode wyll nat denye take hym embaſſetrye well auyſed diſcrecion toke wente informacion poynt poynt great charge hym caſte ſtande large without errour coude gode effect full playnly vnderſtode euery thynge prynted thought went forgate right nought worde caſte hym nat fayle ſhyppe gothe began ſayle ſhort tyme companye aryued vp theſalye cyte called mynuſyus fortune kynge pelleus ſame tyme anthenor anone vnto kynge right waye gone guydo hath conceyued pryme face benyngnely receyued whan knewe cauſe comynge haſte without taryenge authenor felle vyſage shortly ſaye effecte meſſage troyā knyght aſtoned neuer adel full demure auyſed wel nat haſty rakell ſayne abydynge loke face playne pelleus manly chere sayde effecte right thus ye ſhall worthy kynge called pryamus wyſe ſo noble ſo manly famous knyghthod paſſynge excellent hath firſte goodly wyſe ſent torye royall chefe cyte full entent meſſage ſhall ſaye wordes playne ſo ye nat diſdayne pacyently gyue audyence remembrynge firſte aduertence harmes nat full longe ago wronges ye wroughte alſo full cruelly eke youres troye lande progenytoures iniuryes deſtruccion cauſeles without occaſion ye ſhewed haue cruelte mercyles deſtroyed cyte slayne fader named lamedowne cyte brent bete downe nouther lefte paleys hous toure ladde awaye rycheſſe treaſoure nouther ſpared reherſe ſlaughter woman childe man myght none ſwerde aſterte yet one thynge moſt hath herte ſuſter called exyon holde kept kynge thelamon diſhoneſtly agayne gentrye great diſhonour great vyllanye hir kynred lyke ye may ſe treated cheryſſhed lyke hir degre wherfore ſythe ye ſo wyſe knyght ye oughte aduerte haue ſyght ſuche thynges iuſte affeccyon conſydre diſcrecyon gentylleſſe equyte ſuche wronges myght amended wherfore pryam great auyſeneſſe fully beſyneſſe herte wyll deſyreth pea reſte sendeth beſechynge beſte ye wyll beſy dylygence make hym lytell recompence may haue reſtytucyon thorugh knyghtly medyaryon ſuſter without lenger ſpace remenaunt wyll lete pace stryfe werre oonly eſchewe deſyreth fully ſewe pea quyete hole affeccyon purſue meaſour reaſon fynally lyke ye may ſe occaſyon werre fle conſyder holde ſo ſage fyne fully meſſage ¶whan pelleus hym playnly vnderſtode ſodayne yre wexe herte wode loke fell furyous rancour right melancolyous ne myght attempre appeaſe haſty fyre gan herte ſeaſe anone full deſpytous wyſe gan pryamus threten deſpyſe malys ſette ſonde nought meanes yt anthenor hath ſought gan alſo troyan knyght menace bad haſte ſhulde voyde place vpon peryll falle myght anone wente ſyght haſte meynee without abode taken haue ſee began ſayle theſalye theyr waye ſo faſte hye ſhorte tyme aryued vp salempne myghty ſtronge cyte fortune royall towne anthenor fonde kynge thelamowne paleys hath waye nome firſte fynde whan come accepted vnto preſence benynguely without offence exyone preſent tyde auenture ſtondynge ſyde reuerence hir woman hede anthenor toke better hede cuſtome kynge thelamon hye deſpyte indignacyon euery troyan coude eſpye ſpecially hadde enuye rancour oonly thorugh bytter rag • whiche herte myght neuer aſwage pacyence anthenor hath gyuen audyence whiche anone full ſobre wyſe tale gan ſhall deuyſe syr quod ſupport grace ye graunte opportune ſpace declare cauſe comynge wyll reherſe without taryenge mater hole breefly ſentence make kouthe magnyfycence signefyeng without diſpleaſaunce pryamus hath gouernaunce troye towne hath vnto ſent faythfull menynge clene entent beſechynge firſte goodlyhede wronges forgete eke dede ye oonly hye nobleſſe equyte gentylneſſe ye wyll reſtore exyona agayne whiche ye holde ſpeke wordꝭ playne ſothe nat lyke hir eſtate wherfore prayeth ſtynte debate euery harme put memorye knyghtly honour owne glorye ſende hir home make delyueraunce goodly hir without varyaunce ye haue holde ſo many longe dayes ne taryeth natnor ſetteth delayes ne lete founde nowe ſlouthe ſothfaſtlye great routhe recorde ye haue hir vſed may trouthe nat goodly excuſed ſhall lete lyghtly ouer ſlyde ye benyngnely prouyde ſende hir home lyke haue ſayde lo charge layde without abydynge certayne goodly anſwere ye wyll ſende agayne ¶whan thelamon herkened tale haſty yre gan wexe pale fyry coke hath hym made ſo wode face aualed blode within herte gan frete byte loke aſkoye tourned vp whyte hye diſdayne face deſpytous pale ſmylynge laughter furyous gan rake feble mortall fyre fretynge hate brent deſyre ſhortly made concluſyon anthenor obieccyon ſayde frende euer thou wonder greatly meruayle auenture ſodayne newe thynge vnprudently meueth thy kynge vnto make ſuche ſonde thou fole whan thou toke honde oather vnhappy infortunat brynge embaſſat hym haue thynge ado loke thou ſay hym ſo ne aqueynted alyte thynge platly delyte ſhorte wordes thou lyſt hym prayere ne haue ioye nouther feſte right nought ſothly requeſte wote well whyle go troye myſelfe mo reforme thynge amys thorugh offence ſhortly thus certayne thynge wrought lamedowne manhod wonne ye towne ſlewe kynge yt hym helde knyghtly wyſe hym metynge felde eueryche myght ſe dyde entre firſte cyte graunted memorye ſygne oonly myne hye victorye without contradiccyon grekes haue poſſeſſyon hir moſte entere exyona thou claymeſt well ſyker thyne aſkynge vayne truſte well ſyker right well certayne thou geteſt hir nat one worde may ſhall firſte made full great affray hir leue durynge lyue euer grutche agaynſt ſtryue nat ſyttynge leue hir ſo whylom ſo great ado hir gat ſpendynge blode wrothe therwith wode wyll hir kepe ſhalbe founde hadde ſo many mortall wounde troye towne hir wan good fayth ferforth ſhall nat lyghtly fro handes pace ſhe alone ſtandeth ſo grace hir beaute hir ſemelyhede hir bounte hir goodlyhede ſhall reaſon ſhortly fyne ſothe moſte femynyne euer ſawe without drede porte connynge womanhede hath alone exiſtence ſouereynte excellence pryamus ought y• thou canſt ſayne whyle lyue gete hir nat agayne hir bye many dedely wounde ſharpe ſwerdes ſquare ſperes grounde ſhall firſte reyſed ſuche ſtryfe ſhall coſte many mannes lyfe ſhe agayne reſtored take forſothe thou getteſt whan hym lyſte may well begynne ſuppoſe ſhall lytell wynne none wyſe tolde woteſt great role holde put ſo ferre iupartye execute embaſſetrye manly grekes ſo boldly offende beware therfore ſende vpon thy lyfe rancour pryde go thy way thou abyde lenger ſothly ſyght thou woteſt ye pryſe yt haue hyght thou ſcapeſt nat lefe lothe anthenor anone ſhyp gothe ſayle hym lyſte nat delaye towarde yle called achaye whan taken hath londe ryuayle auenture fonde worthy kynges pollux caſtor right anone troyan anthenor without abode courte fare vnto meſſage declare togydre whan preſent ryght thus ſayde ſentement noble kynge troye ryte hath vnto ſent wyll beſechynge full lowe maner ye lyſte vnto prayer equyte condeſcende goodly helpe certayne wronge mende touchynge ſuſter called exyon may haue reſtytucyon hir agayne diſcrete aduyſe ſythe ye ſo manly ſo wyſe lykly oppynyon 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 good medyacyon shelyghtly may agayne reſtored cheryſſhe pea vnyte wherfore prayeth wt herte entere goodly wyſe deuere holde ben ſo knyghtly ſo ſage wyll playnely ſurpluſage wronges olde put ſuſpence deſyreth knyghtly hye prudence ſtynte werre noryll pe nouther rakell rekles auyſed werkes caſte afore ſhalbe fall thynges futur aduertynge ferre ſeeth perell werre wyll hym conforme vnto pea reſte conceyueth beſte euery man vnyte ſewe prudently alſo eſchewe debate eche occacyon lo fyne entencyon whiche cōmytte iugement caſtor yre inpacyent haſtyneſſe ne myght nat abyde cruell herte ſo ſwolle pryde brake anone deſpytous face ſayde frende knowe treſpace grekes dyde euer vnto thy kynge axe amendes wonder • ynge v neuer dyde hym •• offence saue made maner recompence wronge wrought lamedon whiche firſte ſought occacyon agaynſt grekes vngoodly wyſe cauſed v vpon hym ryſe one manly hym ſette due right quyr • dette lyke decrete haue hym playnly ſerued nothȳg wrought hath diſſerued amendes gynneth late coueyte mortall hate vtter malys enmyte outher pea accorde vnyte effecte hereafter ſhall fele happe v dele bargeyn ſhall full dere ben abought frendſhyp ſothly ſette nought ouer ſpeke lykly ſemeth vnto pryamus loued alyte nat value ſuppoſe myte whan ſent vpon meſſage thou folye dydeſt great outrage take ſo hye peryllous thynge vnto grekes brynge ſuche tydynge thorugh thy lyfe put iupartye counſayle faſt thou hye ſyght lyſt thou repente ¶and anthenor forthe ſhyp wente wynde gan ſayle anon towarde yle called pyllyon haſte whan dyde aryue ſhope hym forth court blyue duke neſtor maner thynge houſholde helde royall kynge anthenor full ſad auyſee tofore neſtor ſyttynge ſee whan amytted ſayne tale tolde full openly playne poynt poynt ye herde afore vayne reherſe alway concluded hath one lyke ye herde touchynge exyone duke neſtor face thynge rede hewe aſſhes dede fret coloure ſo inwardly blode eche extremyte drawen downe vnto herte whiche yre ſo ſore made hym ſmerte gan quake euery ioynt vayne hande vnnethe may reſtrayne melancolye venged lyke lyon ſo wood wrothe fer hymſelfe ſo alyenat inwardly rancour paſſyonat loke reuerſed furyous ſyght tempre hymſelfe vnnethes ne myght felte angre ſo great aduerſyte amyddes cruelte ſodayne haſte one brake euen thus anthenor ſpake thou quod thy wordes whyte ſuppoſe thou wyſte full lyte vnto fore thou haſte thy tale tolde meruayle thou arte ſo bolde preſume myne eres offende pryam ſo proudely pretende maner tytle thy kynges name worthy grekes put blame vniuſtly foule hardyneſſe requere haue redreſſe iniuryes wrought • amedon boldely affermynge falſe preſumpcion vpon grekes wronges outragyous whiche myneres ſo odyous fretynge eke ſo bytynge ſokene lyſte may nat ſuſtene herynge lo hatefull ſowne ner honour hyerenowne refrayned ſhulde cruell wyſe execute full haſtely iuſtyce thorugh rygour mortall lawe beſtes wylde firſte drawe therupon thy fayned tale diſmembre peces ſmale deſpyte pryamus kynge teche brynge tydynge preſumptuouſly talys newe lorde better y• hym knewe ſhulde thy preſumpcyon thy laſte mede fynall guerdon without mercy lyke haue behyght haſte bego ſyght vtterly dothe great offence vnto myn eye hauethe preſence thorugh diſdayne cauſeth myn vnreſte anthenor thought beſte nat holſom lenger abyde caſte wyſely rancour pryde beſte bere hym fayre ſhyppe gan anone repayre haſte poſſybylytee without abode taken hath ſee gan ſayle homewarde faſte drawe ſodaynly boyle gan wawe ſee ryſe cloudes blake appere wynde wake wonder gaſtfull alſo heuene dredfull fyre bryght leuene thonder ſmote tempeſt gan dryue maſte gan ſoder ryue alofre poynt drowne felle weder gan ſo frowne awayte nat vpon dethe euen poynt yeldynge vp brethe ne ſawe none remedye euer amonge gan clepe crye theyr goddes auowes make deuoutly vndertake eche lyke age eſcape go pylgrymage lyke rytes theyr paynem wyſe goddes theyr ſacryfyſe ſubſtaunce myght ſodaynly weder derke nyght newe lyght grace gan adawe ſee waxe calme ſmothe gan wawe happe amonge euerychone tempeſt peryſſhed nat one tofore troye within ſytell ſpace aryued euerychone grace eſcaped ſafe euery ieopardye bothe anthenor companye temple toke right way prayer full longe lay many another alſo ſake thākyng goddes yt made ſo eſkape euery peryll tempeſt ſee vnto kynge gothe lordes aboute hym full royall paleys dongyon pryncypall sat abode full ſolempnelye trewe reporte embaſſatrye knyght hath hym falle hath tolde kynge tofore lordes alle anthenor hath firſt made mēcion tofore kynge iuſte relacyon expleyt ordre wyſe vncurteyſly receyued kynge pelleus thretes wordes deſpytous ſuffred kynge thelamon beynge ferſe wood lyon afterwarde gan alſo complayne deſpyte bretherne twayne rebuke great drede neſtor dyde ſpede lyfe myght vnneth ſkape tolde gan ende make iourney eke repayre pryam fully deſpayre outher forte aduenture euer agayne ſuſter recure conceyueth aduertence clere reporte experte euydence aye benygne vngoodly ayen hym malygne moſt hym ſheweth debonayre fonde thē agaynward moſt cōtrayre frowardly euer quyte shewynge ſygnes ſette lyte frenſhyp ought coude aduerte wherof pure ſorym herte conſtrayned right nede compelled iuſtly procede haue redreſſe oonly rygour profre pea myght haue fauour admytted tytle ryghtwyſeneſſe thorugh hye deſpyte haſty wylfulneſſe euery mene meaſour vayne saue oonly werre engendred diſdayne begonne cauſed olde hatrede whiche gan anone ſuche bronde brede newe enuye kynges breſte pryamus without areſte ſo iuly yre rancour fret diſdayne ſo ſore grounde whet ſo leſe wynne vpon grekes wyll werre begynne iuparte manly knyght lyfe deth bycauſe hadde ryght caſte hym firſte nauee ſende grece fomen fende lyke knyght force haunte knyghtly wyſe caſte hym daunte pompe grekes ſturdyneſſe fynally theyr pryde oppreſſe ¶but ſaye pryam infelycyte newe trouble hap deſtyne aboue hatefull influence deſcended vnware vyolence • ue thou canſte nat lyue pee ſodayne ſorte fortune gracelees chaunce vnhappy without auyſeneſſe wylfull luſte fonned hardyneſſe haue put thy ſoule tranquyllyte make werye thy proſperyte haſt y• fauour bytter ſwete canſte nat lyue pea quyete thou art trauayled wylfull mocyons ouer mayſtred thy paſſyons lacke reaſon hye prudence derked blynde prouydence full barayne caſt afore ſe harmes folowynge thyne aduerſyte thou ſlowe wyſely conſydere wante ſyght made ſlydere thorugh myſte errour falſly forueye pathys wronge right weye voyde reaſon wylfull haſtyneſſe wher thy guyde wher thy maiſtreſſe deſcrecyon ſo prudent ſo ladde vyſelye ſhulde haue ladde trace ſenſualyte though full ſelde mannes power ſuffraunce hymſelfe refrayne whan ſodayne yre doth herte ſtrayne thou ſhuldeſt afore better caſt thy chaunce wrought counſayle nat put balaunce thy ſykerneſſe ala dydeſt thou ſo haue ſymuled ſome dele thy wo caſte thy chaunge well afore pryme haue forgoten wronges olde tyme thought afore thyn aduertence ofte falleth experyence whyles men moſte beſyneſſe vengeably theyr wronges redreſſe double harme ware falle agayne newe ſnare damage forgete clene falſe reporte rumoure freſſhe grene renewed thorugh ſwyfte fame fleeth ſo fer hyndre alordes name namely whan purpoſe wende oonly hede ſe nat ende pryde ſodayne heete voyde themſelfe quyete aduertynge nat worke auyſelye prouerbe techeth comonlye ſtande ſure enhaſte hym nat meue ſhall hym greue walketh ſurely playne ſtumble vayne ſo helyſte folye neclygent put hym wylfullye auenture hymſelfe reche eſchewe peryll holde wreche ſothly pryam thou rechelees cōmytte thy quyete pee dredefully durynge date cruell fortune fykell fate whoſe maner cuſtome comonly whan man truſteth moſte ſoueraynely goddeſſe blynde full vnſtable ſhe hym moſte deceyuable hym abate royall ſtalle ſodaynly make hym downe falle tryp throwe hym bake gayne ſtryueth ſhall haue lytell take ſo ſlyely hir gynne ſnare ſhe make man fro welfare hir pantre fraude englewed whan leſt weneth remewed therfore man haue none affyaunce fortune hir vary aunce ne lete wyght eaſe iuparte lyſt thou playe wyll afterwarde departe tourne chaunce outher well wo ſelde one ſhe doth game go ye may ſe example pryamus folye ſo deſyrous werke hede folowe owne wylle trouble ala calme tranquylle boke ſhalbe founde hym cyte platly confounde vtterly confuſyon afterwarde longe ſucceſſyon ſhalbe red ſtorye fable remembred dytees delytable pleaſaunce ſhall example may beware lere haſty luſte volunte begyn thynge wherin ſuerte dependeth aye ſtryfe werre debate ſuch playe vnwarely cometh chek mate harme done late amende whoſe fyne ofte wende ſtorye ye ſhall ſe lete pryam alwaye myrour haſty errour tymes correcte anone poyntell wyll directe maner trace rude ſtorye remenaunt conclude worthy kyng euer one ſentence aye fyred feruence hath breuettes letter ſente lordes holde parlemente cōmaunded al haſt may come anone theyr aſſygned day euery warde partye towne aſſemble noble ilyowne chefe reygne whan echone hym preſent noble kynge anone tofore ſhortly wyll declareth thus began syres quod bycauſe ye wyſe nedeth nat longe proceſſe deuyſe reherſe comynge cauſe tell ſhortly clauſe meane make delay ye wot day sent grece counſayle knyght myne anthenor men call haue recured exyona agayne whoſe meſſage nat vayne grekes full vncurteyſly receyued diſpytouſly threte rebuked poynt haue dede vnneth myght eſcape hede put hym ſuche offence blame reboundeth alderſhame day day muſt encreaſe ordayne ſome remedye therfore meſour haue offred haue v werre ſtryfe yprof • ed hye deſpyte rancour hete malys cruelly v threte wolde pea purchace wronges done fellyvs manace y• harmes haue v wrought nat purpoſe playnly theyr thought redreſſe amendes make vtterly werre v awake whoſe ioye fully encreaſe greuaunce wolde god repentaunce contryte herte ſtynte myſchefe lykly falle grefe outher parte myght ouer ſlyde ala rancour pryde ar ſwolle newe threte god diffende halfe dele ſore infortune euer ſhulde fall purpoſe v ſythe haue ſhape thus v muſt reſyſte theyr wyll malycyous thorugh myght god neceſſyte diffence wyll none beſte holde vnto oure entent worke one aſſent purpoſe ſoneſt ſhall acheue diſcorde may quarell preue parte hertes nat one victorye may wyſe gone chefe conqueſt pea vnyte right diſcorde aduerſyte ouyde hertes maketh rewmes ſure dyuyſyon cauſeth diſcomfyture wherfore rede wyll herte lette v ſet grekes ſmerte ſothfaſtly ye lyſt ſe dare afferme ſtrenger grekes vpon euery parte haue armes parfytely arte coūted knyghthod crop roote plente haue men hors foote arrayed well eueryche degre therwith alſo ſtronge cyte withſtonde fomen euerychone counſaylynge ordayne anone firſte aſſemble hooly nauye ſtuffe ſtrongly wt chyualrye grece haſtely ſende proude grekes manly offende iuſte cauſe tytle ryght oa werre full myght theyr townes brenne theyr feldes waſte herte vnfayned alſo v enhaſte quyte deſerued haue rede ſhall none ſaue cruelly take vengeaunce ne hath fere ne let greuaunce though afore fortune victoures • lee auncetres progenytoures vnhap firſte put downe remounteth ofte full hye renowne chaunge varyaunce werre ſtryfe euer balaunce day aſſured wele tomorowe caſte downe whele victor ofte put aduenture vanquyſſhed diſcomfyture hym hadde afore victorye vp downe armes ſtande y• glorye martes chaunce man hym aſſure cometh let hym take eure gery mar influence gyue man whylom excellence wynne pryſe lyke conqueroure ſodaynly ſomer floure honour make fade whan aſpectis glade man lyſteth wrythe renowne olde goth awaye blythe floode ebbe foloweth aye men deſerue prayſe daye thoughe phebus day mery ſhyne tomorowe may bemes downe declyne thorugh thyckneſſe myſtes trouble ryght ſo mar chaunces double vp downe lowe alofte fortune whiche chaungeth ofte lyſt hir whele make man aſſende vnwarely downe agayne deſcende stoundemele honoure auaunce aſweygh throwe hym myſchaūce nowe fauour ſet hym vp full hye eſt auale hym twynclynge eye hir playe vnſtable tourneth balle whyle one gothe vp nother hath falle reyſeth one doth nother loute euery man whan cometh aboute muſt take tourne hir play requereth experte hir fraudes lereth shall hir ſugre fynde galle meynt hir hony aye bytter ſpreynt pea werre honour fame dignytes renowne ſhame hi • lykynge hir lyſt graunte therfore man hap moche auaunte ¶for though grekes whylom alofte may hereafter happe full vnſofte wherfore echone ſhewe worthyneſſe ſo named ſtrengthe hardyneſſe fortune playnely comytte let fer manly hertes f • ytte ſtande hole menynge playne therupon let ſe ye wyll ſayne atones theyr voyſe gan reyſe ſentence hyghly preyſe one herte manly gan expreſſe wyll diſpende goodes rycheſſe theyr bodyes put iupardye nat one wolde tho denye graunte thanketh echone gaue leue lyſt gone diſſolued hath parlement euery man waye went repayred manſyowne kynge alone lefte ylyowne sole hymſelfe inwardely muſynge purpoſe myght aboute brynge ſoth thynge elles thought therupon euen thus wrought byng pryamus makyng thus mone tolde chambre alone many wayes caſtynge vp downe parfourme concluſyowne fulfyll fyne entent firſte prudently hath ſent ſones come hym haſte well borne baſte tother aſſemble yfere purpoſe lyke ye ſhall haue counſayle nedefull purueaunce agaynſt grekes make ordenaunce firſte themſelfe alone pryuely whan ordre eueryche ſet dewe ſee lyke age degree ector firſte floure chyualrye repayred home panomye moſt acceptable euery wyghtes grace nexte fader taken hathe place ¶and whan pryam leyſer dyde eſpye ſyghes ſore caſtynge vp eye echone ſyttynge enuyron gan declare hertes mocion ¶but firſte myght wyll expowne teres gan hymſelfe drowne hertely wo ſo outragyous wepynge ſobbynge furyous vnneth myght worde breke vnto diſtreſſe ſpeke openly inwarde menynge ſhewe tyll laſte wordes fewe gan abrade pytous fare euen thus menynge declare ¶my dere ſones ſo louynge ſo kynde ſuppoſe ye haue mynde remembre diſcretly aduerte emprente full freſſhely herte grekes agayne right lawe cruell ſwerde murdred haue ſlawe worthy auncetres full hye renowne deſtroyed brent bete downe firſte troye walles olde vngoodly alſo holde myn owne ſuſter called exyon full great ſhame confuſyon hye reprefe worthyneſſe ſemeth kyndeneſſe nature ye oughte agreued inwardly herte ſore meued ſuffre hyndrynge hir name treated alder ſhame ala nyl ye beſyneſſe hye deſpyte knyghtly redreſſe auenge vpon theyr cruelte recure fynde iniquyte syth ye ſo myghty ſo ſtronge certes ſemeth ye byde longe fro day day ye ſo differre knyghtly wyſe gynne werre force myght manly aſſaye pure ſorye ye lyſte delaye comforte vnto deſyre theyr hate brenne hote fyre vpon lyke ye may ſe fretynge yre auenged lyke theyr decrete quyte theyr mede ye ala take lyſt hede whyle renowne doth ſo freſſhely ſhyne vnto luſte hertes declyne conſyderynge lyke kouthe haue grene youthe yfoſtred brought forth echone frothylke day ye coude gone tenderly coude myght whiche thynge inwarde ſyght ye ſhulde aduerte alway new newe nature ſores rewe remedye myn aduerſyte whiche toucheth alſo well syth ye wote ſore doth greue ye ſhulde ſhape myn harmes releue ſodaynly thus ganmourne towardes ector gan face tourne ſayde ector truſte ioye myn heyre alſo lyke reygne troye day ſucceſſoure named arte ſouerayne floure worthyneſſe manhod welle thy brother knyghthod doſt excelle armes lyke conquerour called ſtocke worſhyp honour hertely praye though thou ſytte ſtylle wyllynge purpoſe fulfylle execute deſyre ſo fynally nomo full fayth brynge aboute take thynge doute chefe prynce alſo gouernour purpoſe vtterly ſocour thyn honde iourney cōmytte hooly herte ſo thou ne flytte confourme good aduyſement parfourme vp fyne myne entent reaſon beſt ſyt whiche art ſo prudent ſo full wyt stronge delyuer flouryng eke youthe fame thorugh y• world kouthe yonge yeres olde diſcreciowne eurous loue paſſynge renowne vnto whoſe wyll thy bretherne ſhall obeye ſto • de bothe lyue deye cōdeſcende accomphyſſhe requeſte thou feleſt anſwere leſte ¶and whā y• kyng hath ſhewed ſentence demure chere humble reuerence worthy ector example gentrye ſofte ſpeche techeth cutteſye anſwere gaue ſobre countenaunce effecte whiche ſubſtaunce myne owne lorde fader dere benyngnely ye lyſte force great myght ſ • nature ryght whiche euery thyng kynde doth conſtrayne bondes hir large chayne ſyttynge doth enſpyre accordynge euery man deſyre wronges done haue amendement hir lawe right conuenyent namely ſuche nobylte kynde hath endewed ſette hye degre ſuche great reprefe ſhame whan wronge vnto theyr name echetreſpaſſe muſt conſydered iuſtly meſured qualyte hym offended alſo parſone y• wronge werre contek debate gretter grefe hye eſtate ſuffre harme caſe auenture wronge vniuſtly endure iniuryes compaſſed malys offence diſcrete aduyſe famous manhode renōmed borne gentyll blode ſuche one holde wretche wherfore muſt greatly charge retche oonly knyghthode worſhyp eke wronges done amendes ſeke ſtate conſydered hye nobleſſe plyte ſtoude worthyneſſe whan beſtes reaſon rude blynde deſyre ſame inſtuyt kynde ¶and parte truſte certayne ye haue ſone wolde halfe ſo fayne vpon grekes auenged trouthe ſay faythfully yre brenne doth glede thurſte theyr blode mede right eldeſt age amonge ſones ſo moſte wt rage fret within iuſtly knyghthode right hande ſhede y• grekes blode ſhall fynde paraunter wene whan tyme cometh ſothe ſhalbe ſene ¶but firſte rede wyſely mynde caſte afore leue nat behynde ye begynne diſcretely aduerte prudently conſydre herte oonly nat gynnynge ende myddes way wyll wende fyne fortune wyll lede ye thus amyſſe ye may ſpede counſayle myne opynyon worthy lytell diſcrecyon haue pryſe caſt nat courſe thynges ordre ceryouſly way trace wo delyte though gynnynge haue appetyte yet ende playnly fable ther may thȳg folow nat cōmēdable worthe agynnynge fortunate cauſeth ſtryfe great debate wherfor ſothe pryncyples drede men well knowe fyne ſhall ſuccede gynnynge grace well fortuned whan ende myddes lyke contuned whan wele ne may contene well better betymes abſtene put doute ſtandeth inſuerte ſo doth hath aduerſyte humbly eſtate royall herte praye let nat offende bolde ſay mocion good fayth none entencion thynge meue offence oonly magnyfycence procede nat hede wylfully ne ſpyryte meue folylye begyn thyng wyll ſhende lacke ye ſe nat ende take hede aduertence conſydre good prouydence grekes haue theyr ſubieccion europe aufryk many region ful large wyde knyghthod moſt famous rycheſſe wonder plenteuous right renōmed alſo worthyneſſe ſupporte dare well expreſſe full peryllous diſpleſe diſturbe quyete parturbe whiche ſtandeth pea greatly drede though aſye helpe v nede loked euery parte aryght nat egall vnto grekes myght ¶and though alſo myn aunte exyon agayne right holde thelamon nat good hir redempcion put v deſtruccion rede nat beye hir halfe ſo dere many v hap ſytte mo myght hir ſake deth vnder • onge ende make whiche wyſedome lyke ſemeth may happe alſo ſhe ſhort tyme hir fatall cours ſhall fyne whan antropos threde two ſhall twyne wonne ſhe go enmyte thought ſorowe wo slaughter men deth confuſion wherfore rede without diſſymylacion without wo endure nat put ſelfe auenture holde beſte werke wyſe douteles cowardyſe ſaye nat hye preſence forcauſe holde prudence fortune full doubylneſſe syth ſure put ſykerneſſe thus ſome effecte wylle worde ector helde hym ſtylle whan y• ector full hye prudence concluded hath y• fyne ſentence full demurely kepte lyppes cloſe therwithall parys vp aroſe gan tale thus afore kynge lorde quod ſo lykynge hyghneſſe take hede ſemeth ſhulde lytell drede knyghtly wyſe vndertake vpon grekes werre make atones theyr pryde confounde syth paſſyngly habounde chyua • rye within towne haue plente poſſeſſiowne eche thynge may werre auayle stuffe ſelfe royall apparayle longeth aſſautes marcyall ſpecyal helpe ſocoure many regyon vsto werke theyr deſtruccyon pompe pryde manly abate grekes malys mate herte ſo ſtoute ſemeth ſhortly nede nat doute parte diſmayde wherfore rede let nat delayde ſhyppes firſte redy make myſelfe wyll fully vndertake lykynge pleaſaunce empryſe hooly gouernaunce aſſure put certayne exyona recure agayne fourme ſhalbe wrought haue awaye founde thought lykely done whiche vnto wyll declare anone firſte haue caſt wt ſtronge myghty hande rauyſſhe ſome lady lande hye eſtate make taryenge myghtely troye hir brynge maugce hir myght concluſion ye may haue teſtytucion eſchaunge hir ye deſyre ſo therupon ſhall nat longe behete grekes ſtronge ſhall nat prolonge wyll ſayne excludynge euery doute aduyſe ſhalbe brought firſte ſhall purpoſe fyne goddes haue thorugh power dyuy • e shewed reuelacion therupon hadde auyſion late gone lay ſlepe vnto whiche ye take kepe ye may nat fayle diſpayre haue recure hir ſo fayre ye haue ſo moche care ¶and maner hole wyll declare dreme magnyfycence ſo ye gyue wyll credence tale ſhall nat dwelle ceryouſly ordre telle trouthe playne fable fayne lorde moſte ſouerayne ¶firſte ye remembre mynde day whan laſt ynde aduyſe cōmaundement mater whiche yourentent ſpecyally hadde cherte knowen betwene whiche toke vpon charge bondes lande full large ¶the ſame tyme deſyre ſpede whan tytan bemes rede gemyny droue chare golde towarde crabbe take holde whiche named paleys dyane bente moone wex wane whan halowed ſonnes ſtacyon nygh myddes moneth iuyn whiche ſeaſon erely morowe whan phebus voyde nyghtes ſorowe doth pirrous wayne agayne vp drawe aurora eſtwarde doth adawe water hir teres rounde ſyluer dewe cauſeth habounde vpon herbes floures ſoote kyndely noryſſhynge crop roote vp roſe bedde anone full deſyrous huntynge gone prycked herte luſty freſſhe pleaſaunce loue ſome dewe obſeruaunce lucyna day magnefye whiche called lady venerye dewely rytes obſerue cythera hir ſerue feres hertes releue caſt v fully tyll drewe eue foreſt playe v diſporte pleaſauntly v recomforte longeth loue luſtyneſſe thylke day venus goddeſſe ſacred full great excellence great honour dewe reuerence unto hir bothe one fryday aduenture fall whan gan haſt v wodes grene hope day ſome game ſene great labour rydynge fro tyll hadde full many bucke doo ſtrengthe ſlayne myght fynde herte chaced wt houndes hynde thorugh downes dale lowe tyll phebus dayes bowe amyd arke meridyen whan bemes full hote ſhene moſte beſy vpon chaas befell wonder dyuerſe caas fortune happed ſodaynly whyle ſeuered fro companye sole ſelfe amonge holtes hore fynde game deſyrous euermore ware thorow thycke thorow thyn full great harte ſawe afore meryn downe lande vale grene ſothe myght nat ſuſtene ſo ſwyfte nygh hym nere albe prycked courſere nyghe y• deth thorugh many ſondry ſhawe ſyght ſo fer gan withdrawe euer ſewe myght anone loſte hym ſyght woode yda bare name ſo faynt gan wexe game myn hors whiche dyde ryde fomynge full whyte vpon euery ſyde flankes blode diſtayned purſute ſo ſore conſtrayned ſpores ſharp dyed rede harte ſo prycked ſtede vp downe full beſy thought laboure auayled right nought tyll laſte amonge bowes glade aduenture caughte pleſaunt ſhade full ſmothe playne luſty ſene ſofte veluet yonge grene fro hors dyd lyght faſte bowe reyne caſte faynte mate weryneſſe layde downe vpon gras vpon brynke ſhortly telle beſyde aryuer criſtalle welle water ireherſe lyke quycke ſyluer ſtremes ran whiche grauell bryght ſtone golde agayne ſonne ſhone ¶where right anone weryneſſe ſondayne ſlepe gan ſo oppreſſe fro tyme firſte borne neuer aſleped ſo toforne lay wonder ſweuen thought hye downe fro heuen wynged god wonderfull chere mercuryous dyde appere ſomedele firſte aferde gyrde croked ſwerde hym brought alſo honde ſlepy yerde plyaunt wonde ſerpent goynge enuyrowne foot alſo lowe downe ſemeth alſo ſtode cocke syngynge houres trewe clocke mouthe god mercurye pypes ſette longe wonder merye whiche ſwete ſugred armonye made myn eres ſuche melodye ſemed tho myn aduyſe rauyſſhed paradyſe thus god dyuerſe lykneſſe wonderfull expreſſe shewed hymſelfe apparence lyke diſcryued fulgence boke methologyes reherſed many poeſyes many lykneſſe lyke ye may ſe take moralyte longe yerde right lyne whiche ſyde wrongly may declyne signefyeth prudent gouernaunce diſcrete folke y• thorugh theyr purueyaunce caſt peryll fall pypes loude ſhall thorugh muſyke entuned trewe betokeneth eke many luſty hewe ſugred dytees great excellence rethoryke eloquence whiche god ſoueraygne patrowne cocke ſwete luſty ſowne iuſtly kepeth houres nyght vtterly aduyſe warde ſyght ſuche voyde waker dylygence theyr court ſlouthe neclygence ſwerde whiche croketh ſo agayne nat forged ymade vayne reuoke right weye suche wrongly trouthe forueye ſerpent whiche tolde whiche wryncled ye may beholde vpon yerde aboute gothe signefyeth falſhode wode wrothe lyeth awayte many ſleyghty weye gynne trouthe werreye god eloquence kynge brought hym eke comynge cythera louers ſerue iuno pallas called mynerue ven u hir lyeges delyte aboute hir hede hadde douues whyte loke benyngne eyen debonayre aye flykerynge ſnowy wynges fayre declare ſothly ſentence douues innocence loue trouthe mene theyr groūde ſhulde honeſt clene ytokened clerely wytneſſe without ſoylynge vnclenneſſe freſſheneſſe roſes rede ſomer ſo luſty ſprede wynter theyr colour fade signefyeth hertely thoughtes glade yonge folkes amerous feruent hope inly deſyrous whan loue gynneth theyr hertes floure tyll longe proceſſe maketh loure wynter vnweldy age luſt palled dulled rage febylneſſe whan ſomer gone folkes knowe trowe mo one therfore venus fleteth ſee ſhewe trouble aduerſytee loue hir ſtormy lawe whiche byſet many ſturdy wawe nowe calme rough ſo taketh hede hope aſſayled aye ſodayne drede next venus pallas behelde hir ſpere hir criſtall ſhelde raynebowe rounde aboute hir hede colour grene blewe rede afore hir deſcryue growynge grene freſſhe olyue therupon browes fowle braunches ſawe ſytte lyke nowle firſte ſhylde pallas goddeſſe signefyed expreſſe vertue force manly hye diffence agayne vyces make reſyſtence hir ſpere ſharpe kene grounde iuſte rygour forged confounde falſe put backe mercy ſhall medle wt wracke ſhafte ſothe ſhauen full playne leſt mercyles right ne wrought vayne werre make full releas olyue betokeneth pea owle alſo ſo odyous ſonges ſyngeth feſtes funerall declareth playnly fyne euery glorye oonly deth hath memorye raynebowe grene rede perſe sygnefyeth chaunges full dyuerſe ofte falleth werre batayle wynne ſodaynly fayle ſtable blewe chaūgyng grene pallas playe alway meynt tene alder laſt haue mynde hir nynphes iuno came behynde whiche cuſtome fulgence telles abyde floodes depe welles iuno poetes ſayne amayden fruyte barayne pecok freſſhe quene yſacred fethers ſhene splayed abrode large ſayle argus eyen emprynted tayle ¶the water rennynge ryuer flode labour men haue gode great trouble beſyneſſe day nyght ſuffre rycheſſe ſo euer theſe flodes rowe lete hym beware aye flowe nature right dewe folowynge moone muſt ebbeſewe moſte drede aye vpon fulle lyſte fortune freſſhe fethers pulle ryche folke ſhyne golde ſo ſhene sythe ſhe chaunge lady quene ¶and argus eyen ſet behynde nygardes hertes ofte ſythes blynde whiche nat aduerte goodes ende lyke ebbe ſodaynly wyll wende whiche nothyng conſydre theyr ſyght fayre luſty fethers bryght pecok vnwarely fall away right ſo rycheſſe ſhortly day wyll theyr mayſter ſodaynly forſake saynge dewe theyr leue take iuno barayne fruyte right ſo naked bare diſtytuyte theſe gredy hertes couetous whiche gadre ſo deſyrous thynge haue ſuffyſaunce fret drede put ſuche myſchaūce ymagenynge worlde wyll fayle theyr fere agayne wynde ſayle tyll atones muſt go fro thus good aye fyne wo namely ſo pynche ſpare drede clarkes declare fruyte good ſpende large man full ſet lytell charge parte frely treaſour comune whan diſcretly ſethe tyme oportune hath ioye put good mewe herte fredome lyſte ſewe gentylneſſe taketh hede therto ¶and wyſe pallas iuno freſſhe venus downe deſcended lyke haue ſhortly comprehended vnder guyynge mercurius whiche vnto gan tale thus parys quod lyfte vp thyne eyen ſe lo theſe goddeſſes nombre thre whiche fro heuen theyr eyen clere dyuerſly vnto appere feſte tell ſhall goddes aboue celeſtyall iubyter helde owne borde none abſent oonly ſaue diſcorde deſpyte ſhe nat preſent auenged ſhe ſette hir entent hir wyttes many wayes ſought tyll laſte euen thus ſhe wrought poetes lyke tolde toke appel rounde pure golde greke letter grauen vp downe whiche ſayde thus concluſy owne without ſtryfe gyue anoon fayreſt euerychone diſcorde lady goddeſſe ſhe debate mayſtreſſe hath appell paſſynge delyte brought feſte malys deſpyte caſte downe amonge borde deynous chere ſpekynge nat worde hir waye faſte gan hir hye ſodaynly ſo preuy great enuye courte appell hath brought great werre ſuche contek wrought hertes theſe ylke thre longe may nat ſtaunchedbe amonge themſelfe ſo gan diſdayne whiche beaute moſte ſoueraygne whiche hath beſte tytle ryght conquere burned appell bryght firſte gan thus beaute ſtryue rancour theyr hertes almoſt ryue wyte right ſhulde firſte poſſede • yet enuye reygneth womanhede one fayrer holde eche woman hir kynde wolde haue ſome parte pry aboue another eche eſtate ſothe none eche hir owne aduys hath ioye beaute haue pry none ſo foule doth myrour prye ſhe fayre hir owne eye lyke fole hymfelfe doth quyte aumber yelowe cheſeth whyte goundy eye deceyued ſoone colour cheſeth moone ſome colour fyre made fyne ſome encreaſed ſpyces wyne oyntementes confeccions nyght falſe illuſions appere wonder freſſhe fayre loke derke day lyght ayre prefe erely morowe ſuche nede beaute borowe nature hath hir ſelfe diſpoſed therfore faſtynge boyſtes vncloſed make thy choyſe byd ouyde whan euery drugge pot ſet aſyde lyſt thou ſentence deceyued lyghtly falſe apparence dayes ſuche crafte full ryue wyſe thus began ſtryue betwyxe iuno venus pallas deſcended ſodaynecas one aſſent touchynge theyr beaute dome therof cōmytted vnto ſpeke called art parys holde art right prudent right wy auyſed thy dome ſhall fyne ne may fro declyne obeye one aſſent without ſtryfe thy iugement herke firſte thou procede eche ſhalbe thy mede conſydre right take good hede therto thou appell graunt vnto iuno ſhall gyue plente rycheſſe hye renowne fame eke worthyneſſe haboundaunce golde treſour ryſe ſo hye honour thou alone ſhalt excelle thy guerdon lyke telle pallas goddeſſe prudence lyſt fyne conclude thy ſentence ſhe may lady appell thy mede ſhe ſhall aſſure wyt ofſapyence thou ſhalt hooly haue excellence wyſdome diſcrecion dyſcerne clereneſſe reaſon alſo fer phebus caſte lyght ſhall nat prudent knyght worlde ſythe began iuſte reporte manlyer man thy name none equypollent venus trewe clene entent lyſte graunt concluſion appell haue poſſeſſion freſſhe goddeſſe ſyt ſo hye aboue shall enſure haue vnto thy loue fayreſt lady tofore worlde euer ſhalbe bore grece thou ſhalt hir knyghtly wynne aduyſed thou begynne iuſtly deme thynge ſpare ¶and anone gan loke vp ſtare greatly aſtoned beſt tyll laſte ſpake mercurye ſayde certayne ne wolde gyue dome naked myghty haue fully lyberte eueryche vyſelye ſe conſydre euery circumſtaunce fayreſt vnto pleſaunce goodlyeſt ſpeke womanhede dome procede anone ye haue herde ſeye deſyre mekely gan obeye haſte theyr beſy cure diſpoyle clothynge veſture lyche ſtatute dome bonde poynt ne wolde nat withſtonde myght haue full inſpexion fourme ſhap eche proporſion diſcerne remembre vyſely ordre euery membre erſt iuge ryght whan eche hadde ſyght gaue venus appell right anone bycauſe ſhe fayreſt echone moſte excellynge ſothly beaute moſte womanly goodly ſe deme playnly ſyght ſtremes hir eyen bryght ilyche glade egall euen lyght y• ſterre y• ſheweth towarde nyght whiche called eſperus ſo ſhene venus hir ſelfe freſſhe luſty quene whiche anone heuenly empereſſe dome hertely hye gladneſſe appell ſhe hooly hath glorye wonne iuſtly victorye reioyſed hir tell ſhe hir feres beaute dyde excell ſhe haſte trewe affeccion concluded hath fully guerdon full demurely lowe nat lofte mercurye ſobre wordes ſofte deuoyde bothe doubylneſſe ſlouthe lyke beheſte holde wyll hir trouthe ſodaynly without iniurye diſapered god mercurye streyghte heuen right way toke anone ſlepe woke ¶wherof lord moſt loue drede ye aduerte wyſely take hede beheſte affermed certayne vnto aſſured nat vayne goodly venus lyke haue tolde wherfore rede ye herte bolde ſende ſtronge myghty hande without abode grekes lande fourme haue ſayde hope ye ſhalbe well apayde whan haue ſpede venus hath behyghte home retourne lady bryghte ſhall ye beſte lyſte nat ſpeke vayne echaunge hir ſuſter wyn agayne thelamon withholde hath yore lo ſay nomore touchynge effect hooly myn aduyſe ſtylle ſat parys fully hymſelfe aquyte ſaye pryam ala thy wyte neclygence take kepe thy truſte ſette dremes ſlepe full thynne thy diſcrecyon take grounde falſe illuſyon procede lyke fantaſye vpon ſweuen meynt flaterye ala reaſon thynge thy guyde pallas wrongly ſette aſyde nat receyued dewe reuerence iuuo eke hir ſapyence hir good lokynge debonayre hir treaſour hir heſtes fayre refuſed ala wylfulneſſe ſhe loue goddeſſe eke alſo vulcanus wyfe whoſe ſeruyce euer werre ſtryfe preferred appell procede agayne right parys toke none hede saue vnto luſte ſette ſyde trouthe thorugh ala yt full great routhe myghty ryche noble towne troye brought confuſyowne oonly knyghthode hath forſake prudence golde choyſe ytake oonly woman holde hym therto roote theyr woo ſtorye ceryouſly ſhall telle dremes wyll lenger dwelle wryte forthe dephebus thyrde ſone kynge pryamus tale gan open audyence kynge ſhortly ſentence lyſte trouthe nat ſpare euen thus conceyte declare lorde quod euery wyght aduerte ſhulde caſte ſyght future thynge peryll doute cerche within withoute poynt poynt alwaye reaſon caſte doutes tourne vp ſo downe wyght ſhulde purpoſe wende matere make ende preſume manhod thought caſte perylles acheueth lytell nought plowman alway caſte aforne many graynes felde corne shalbe deuoured foules rauynous doth ſowe feldes plenteuous ſhulde neuer vale playne cowardſhyp throwe abrode grayne lete ſuche drede nowe layde aſyde holde folye lenger abyde y• parys brother make hym ſtronge ſhyppes venge wronge vpon grekes payne myght preue ſhortly knyght reaſon ye conſydre may man iuſtly may ſay nay parys hath counſayled wele trouthe fer fele errour purpoſe contrarye wherfore let hym lenger tarye holde waye ſtronge nauye auenge great velanye grekes haue ye take hede done heretofore v kynrede fynall execucyon recure touchynge exyon treate diſhoneſt wyſe agaynſt right tytle iuſtyſe thynke gyueth herte wounde ſhame whiche ſo newe doth rebounde vpon hir allye wherfore beſte eſpye parys take vyage ſuche freſſhe luſty age manly wende grekes lande force theyr myghty hande maugre grekes proude moſt elate rauyſſhe ſome lady eſtate ye may knyghthod brother ye lyſte chaunge hir moſte redy ſhort concluſion ſe reſtytucion exyone parys wende counſayle ſhortly thus ende faſte full diſcrete ſage helenus fourth ſone age roſe ſete great reuerence prayeng fader graunte hym audyence may ſay preſence openly ſhalbe fall moſt ſecrete thynges ſoberly thus tale began clene entent trewe affeccion lorde quod ſupportacion grace wherin moſt truſte let none offence vnto luſte diſpleaſe though ſay conceyte syth ye knowe mene deceyte neuer yet fayled ſentence fyll experyence lyke tolde partye pryue treate generall without menynge doubylneſſe folowed dyde expreſſe remembre ye ſhall fynde trewe god wyll ſhall nat newe spare ſay lyke conceyue dede fraude deceyue declarynge firſte trewe entencion ſhall folowe concluſion parys grece wende truſte well wyll v ſhende goddes haue reuelacion made vnto demonſtracion eke knowe aſtronomye neuer yet prophecye ne deceyued ſhulde falle none lyſte counſayle calle taught thynge yt ſhall betyde wherfore praye rancour pryde enuye none olde hatrede take vengaunce ye nat procede aduyſe lyke ye purpoſe ſay playnly lyſte nat gloſe ye ſhall repente ye parys ſende grece whiche god defende wytte well concluſion shall fully tourne deſtruccion fynally ruyne lyke gan afore deuyne fyne folowe ſhall subuercion bothe towne wall paleys houſe cyte goth nought ye get ſemeth ought ynough ſuffyſe haue ſayde ſythe ye wyſe ye aduerte ſawe doute nat ye wyll withdrawe hande tyme damage aſſayle conſtraynte rage better betymes abſtene purpoſe whiche yet grene hede haſtely aſſente thynge whiche ſhall echone repente plenerly ſhall thynge ſocoure ſhall folowe youre deſpytefull deth without excepciowne one abydynge towne firſte ſelfe playnly endyte shall vengaunce grekes byte thorugh furye theyr mortall tene wyfe cuba quene shall lede hir lyfe thorugh grekes cruelte ſorowe wo captyuyte lyeges ſwerde ſhall pace cruell de • h without grace innocentes mercyles ſhall blede auyſe ye procede wylfulneſſe werre make folylye vndertake parturbe quyete reſte whiche ſhall tourne thynge beſte ruyne v • myſchefe fall counſayle afore prouyde wylfulneſſe ſette aſyde specially whan deth tolde muſte fyne ye purpoſe holde lo without wordes mo grece parys go ¶and wyſe whan helenus playnly ſayde guydo telleth v tryſte heuy pale face agayne reſorteth ſyttynge place whoſe ſentence aſtoned euerychone sat ſylence ſtylle ſtone powerles theyr hertes reſume ſpeke worde man dare preſume preſe kept theyr lyppes cloſe laſte troylous vp aroſe yonge freſſhe luſty courageous alſo aye deſyrous haue armes manly longeth knyght whan full glad lyght sawe fader bretherne euerychone inly troubled thus ſpake anone noble worthy ſyttynge enuyron hye prudence great diſcrecyon manfull alſo hye courage ſodayn fere hath brought ī rage new trouble cropen breſte ſentence cowarde preſte syth echone ye ſhall euer fynde deſyre veryly kynde lyue luſte voyde away trauayle dedely hate batayle theyr wyt fynally applye ſewe theyr luſte lyue glotonye fyll theyr ſtomacke reſtore theyr mawe reſte eaſe euer drawe ſewe theyr inwarde appetyte thus theyr ioye thus theyr delyte etynge drynkynge couetyſe theyr ſtudye fully deuyſe may folow luſt without right nought elles ſet ſtore ala ſhame ye ſo diſmayde ſytte mate aſtoned afrayde wordes helenus ferefull drede lytell mous quaketh ſpeke fyght ouer agayne ſkylle ryght preiudyce goddes alle taketh hym ſay ſhall befalle thynge futur ſpecefye ſpyryte prophecye graunted hym alone ſpeciall though connynge perygall goddes hauynge preſcience ſhewe afore thorugh ſapyence ſhall betyde outher euyll gode let let wyght ſo wode hath wyt gyue therto credence man crafte ſcyence mortall hath connynge deuyne fortune courſe fate termyne suche cauſes hyd conceled ſecree reſerued goddes preuytee men may dyuyne folye take hede lye wherfore rede matere one lorde moſt dere exclude drede may diſturbe herte let thynge perturbe hye courage helenus hath tolde herte nat bolde manhode wold helpe venge wronge let hym go hyde hym temple ſtronge kepe hym cloſe contemplacion wake praye deuocion without ſocour dayes nyghtes ſuffre ſuche luſty knyghtes haunte theyr youthe grene luſtyneſſe manly armes preue theyr hardyneſſe may haue better acqueyntaūce tyme comynge vengeaunce theyr enmyes theyr cruell • oon cōmaunde parys may forth goon execute fyne entent afore purpoſed parlament vpon grekes theyr offencyon parfourme vp payne talyon wronges olde whiche yet fame reherſed vnto alder ſhame thorugh worlde ye wote le therwithall troylus helde pe ſodaynly preſent began atones one aſſent troylus counſayle greatly preyſe manhode heuen reyſe freſſhe courage hye proweſſe feruent zele hardyneſſe one herte greatly hym cōmende right anone made ende pryamus whan done vpon tyme houre noone mete goth within ilyon ſones ſyttynge enuyron mete called hath parys dephebus alſo full wy ſecretly bad ſhulde go ſame day lordes mo panomye haſte may make redy agayne certayne day aray worthy chyualrye may gete theyr companye towardes grece ſayle haſtely kynge ſodaynely nexte day made counſayle calle euen thus ſayde afore alle ¶o noble lyeges beynge preſent purpoſe ſay myn entent without abode ye lyſte ſuppoſe nat vnwyſte grekes pryde tyrannye malys olde compaſſed enuye many wyſe haue agayne v wrought whiche ſo grene foryete nought day day encreaſynge euer mo remembraunce renewed wo whan recorde caſte vp downe greues exyowne ſeruytude amonge doth ſoiourne whiche ofte day cauſeth mourne herte almoſt aſonder ryue conſyder ſe lyue whoſe cruelte haue dere bought natwithſtandynge yt haue meanes ſought haue reſte without whan grece ſent anthenore peaſybly ſuſter recure ſurplus pacyently endure nought toke hede offred goodlyhede nat herde lacke gentylleſſe recorde whiche doubleth diſtreſſe ¶wherfore muſte techeth suxgerye ſharpe yrons ſeke remedye cutte away roote rounde proude fleſſhe yt groweth grounde whiche wyll nat voyde wt oyntementes ſofte albe layde therto full ofte right ſo example muſt dureſſe gette recure whan fayreneſſe may none haue wherfore aduyſe purpoſe ſende forthe paryſe grece ſome lady wyn brynge hir home ſhall within kepe hir ſtronge maugre ſayth nay tyll ſe ſome agreable day fayne lyke myn oppynyon haue eſchaunge hir exyon dere ſuſter loue ſo may nat fayle ſhall goddes v fauourable counſayle alſo acceptable echone whan kynge toucheth comonte wyſe men affermed comon ought confermed thynge touchynge ſhulde apreued echone acheued wherfore caſte aduyſe echone playnly werke worde anone noble pryam ſodaynly peaſe amonges preaſe whan whyſte theyr aller ſyght knyght vp roſe pentheus hyght ſone euforbyus de tranſformatis ſayth ouydius fayneth whylom ſoule pictagoras hooly tranſſumed ſo wryte ouyde touchynge wyll lenger byde tell forth pentheus afore kynge whiche gan tale thus lyege lorde vnto hye nobleſſe diſpleaſe nat worthyneſſe preſence mageſte ſhall ſay acquyte towardes fayth trouthe ſoth faſtly may ſlouthe touchynge honour without drede zele faythe brenne doth glede harmes bydde beware douteleſſe afferme well dare ye ſtande firſte aduyſe ye purpoſe ſende forth paryſe doute nat ſhall rewe god well wore olde nat newe fader called euforbyus diſcrete wyſe right vertuous knowynge afore euery thynge preſcyence byfore wyttynge tell playnly thorugh phyloſophye heuenly ſawe hertes eye • e thynge ſo ſecree hyd knowynge pryuetee knewe wyt ſo ſage laſte whan age hondred yere wt lokkes gray hore remembre complayned ſore wepte alſo pyte tenderly fully affermynge parys vtterly wente grece rauyſſhe hym wyfe ſhulde folowe ſuche mortall ſtryfe vpon v ſothly cyte shulde aſſhes ſcyndres tourned ſhulde nothynge v ſocoure grekes ſwerde ſhall cruelly deuoure hye lowe playnly ſpare none wherfore praye amonge euerychone tell haue deſpyte wronge venge put reſpyte rancour olde rede ye lete tranquylle quyete haſtyneſſe ye nat ſubmytte fortune ſo falſely flytte perturbe nat none olde enmyte newe ſterynge felycyte ye iourney aſſente ye euerychone full ſore ſhall repente ye wyll algates thether ſende parys ſtede let ſome wende lyſt vyage ſpede counſayſe full rede sayde vnder ſupporte oonly grace ſodaynly gan echone chace pentheus loude agayne hym crye repreuynge hym prophecye fader theyr confucion ¶but ala reuolucion ioye wo felycyte thynge ordeyned nedes muſt ordre thynges wt fate ſo englewed ſhall falle may nat eſchewed whiche cauſed aſſente one vndiſcretly parys ſhulde gone vnhappely wt hap enuolued ¶and thꝰ cōcludȳg theyr coūſayl diſſolued caſuelly befell right aduyſe vnto eres ran caſſandra ſhe great afray ſodayne wo gan crye welaway ¶alas quod ſhe ala wyll ye ſhall parys grece go worde ſhe braſte wepe full pytouſly inwarde ſyghes depe gan wayle ſwowne payne furyouſly noyſe complayne wofull rage many pytous ſowne made mortall lamentaciowne dede ſhe myght hir nat withholde heer torne fyſtes folde ſayde ala hondred ſythe ſtormy fortune lyſt thou kythe thy cruell force oure aduerſyte vpon v vpon cyte mortall yre gery vyolence ſwerde vengeaūce worſe thā peſtylence ¶o troye troye thy gylte ala haſt thou done thy treſpas euerſed tourned nought wylde fyre thy ſynne dere abought pryam kynge vncely thy chaunce haſt thou gylte outher greuaunce thy goddes wyrched thorugh vnryght prouoke ſhewe theyr cruell myght vpon thy blode ala haſt thou moder myn ecuba alſo maner cryme importable offence haſt thou wrought haue ſuche recompence day abyde noble worthy quene thy ſones ſuche vengeaunce ſene wofull deth cruell horryble ala ye credyble counſayle ſuche harmes eſchewe mortall purpoſe fully remewe go nat ordeyned thought whiche ſo conſtrayned vnneth may wo endure hir fader wofull creature helde ſtreyght hir way falleth plat groūde hir wepynge water wounde hir chekes ſo teres rayne ſhe myght conſtraynt hir payne vpon hym ſhe gan clyppe crye beſechynge hym ſhape remedye pytous voyce ſhe y• knewe full wele matere playnly euery dele ſhall befaile full mynde ſodayne harmes ſhall behynde hir clamour nat vayne ſhall falle ſome clerkes ſayne ne may nat well men eſchewed eke fortune great aduerſyte haſty ire furyous wode vnkynde troyan blode cauſeleſſe agaynſt agreued rancour ſodaynly ameued blynde awayte catche atraūce vyolence hir vnhappy chaunce hath wt ſweyght tourned hir whele vnſtable ſhe enuyous mutable haſte troyens theyr confuſion wylfulneſſe vndiſcrecion agaynſt grekes quarell make therupon haue theyr counſayle take acheued ye haue herde deuyſe without aſſent moſt wyſe diffynacion ector herde concluded reaſon matere helenus counſayle take pentheus aduerted wyſely ſentence without faynynge full credence caſſandra neuer coude lye prudently herde prophecye fro poynt poynt caſte aforne ſuche myſchefe nat lorne floured yet theyr felycyte without damage aduerſyte fortune wyll haue hir courſe alway whoſe purpoſe holdeth ſayth ye nay ſhe made vyage forhede playne falſe vyſage ſugre ſhadde venym roote bytter taſte ſhewynge ſoote wrynkled double lyke horned ſnayle faythe theyr face fraude aye ye tayle haſte troyans accorde one parys ſhulde grece gone ye haue herde ſayne vpon caſte ordayne ¶how kyng pryamus ſent parys grece wt dephebus men armes take vengeaūce ye grekes toke ye fayre helayne quene vnto menelaus brought hir vnto troye capitulo xiij tyme approcheth whā ye ſonne ſhene golden wayne whyrled vp wene clere ſterres yades ſo rede whiche haue theyr ſyght crabbes hede plyade • ſeuenth ſterre bryght whiche ſyxe appere ſyght ſeuenth draweth hir aſyde couertly doth hir bemes hyde whylom ſhe dyde great offence vnto v cauſeth hir abſence ſhe dare nat ſhewe hir ſtremes clere hir ſuſterne openly appere whylom ſhe god mortall dyde ſynne crymynall whiche noyſed kou • thorugh y• heuen ſhe alone amonge ſuſterne ſeuen shroudeth v ſhamefaſtly hir chere ¶and whan titan zoudyak ſpere atwene theſe ſterres take ſee bole ſyxtene degree vpon tyme ioly grene may whan flora hir hewes gay hath euery playne
