haſte ſone mar knyght māly man worthy yet worthyeſt euer hardyeſt phebus bemysclere amonge ſterres ſo dyde appere excellynge ſtele armed bryght heuenly ſyght bothe nye ferre worthyneſſe lode ſterre whiche whan entred felde lyke rede bare daye ſhelde ſhelde whiche pure golde thre lyon ſtorye tolde whoſe coloure made mencyon fynde deſcripcyon paſſant reporte ryght borne breſte troyan knyght grounde rote hye proweſſe floure accompted worthyneſſe whiche ſo manly without abode amonge knyghtes grekes rode lyke man comynge ſtoned gan thrynge amonges whiche kylleth downe ſlethe mette nat dethe afore ſwerde grekes go wrake theyr wardes knyghtly force brake maugre ſeuered ſonder bare downe rydynge yonder caſuelly meteth waye protheſylaus whiche longe daye hadde ſore fought agaynſt troye ſlewe tho come waye hardy knyght worthy fyers kynge whiche troyans euer purſuynge hadde ſo hertely great enuye whiche thynge whan ector gan eſpye knyghthode gan take hede towardes hym gan reyne ſtede lyne ryght haſty ire rode ſwerde diſteyned blode cloue hede thorugh baſenet ſuche myght y• ſtroke ne let force mayle thycke plate fynally full mortall fate ſwerde ector thrugh nerf bone vayne worthy kynge parted hath twayne vtterly gayneth none armure agayne ſtroke ector endure kynge ſo full worthyneſſe stronge myghty great hardyneſſe receyued hath laſte fatall wounde lyeth dede parted grounde ector forth amonge grekes ryde ſo euer ſtroke abyde refute none diffence deth many greke daye ſleth whiche waye ſtode ſharpe ſwerde batheth blode alſo ferre myght hym ſe deth ſwerde fle mortal vengeafice vpon wrought many greke felowe ſought gan enquere myght theyr lyfe coude neuer ſe none ſo knyghtly behaue hym batayle playnely dempte ſuppoſayle ector noble warryour knyghthode may bere away y• flour amonge euer yet borne greke yt hȳ may ſtāde aforne daye gan ſo enchace ſtronde euen afore face ne durſte mortall ſtroke abyde whan hadde vpon euery ſyde grekes chaced wawy ſee wounded mate great aduerſytee hȳ reſte troyan knyght anone lyke mar hymſelfe home troye gone whoſe partynge grekes e • preſume manly agayne theyr hertes reſume newe theyr foomen aſſayle iuparte wolde auayle lyfe deth ſette outraunce fortune ſhe wolde auaunce theyr parte agayne recure felde enforce myght ſpere ſhelde anone forthwith make delay wynne agayne troyans may viij tymes ſythen begonne felde haue day loſte wonne lyke fortune lyſte theyr cure vp downe turne hyr eure hyr whele went aboute rounde right ſo day wan loſt groūde ſpecyally moſte deſmayde whan ector came hath thē ſo outrayde thrugh knyghthod made theyr hert tyue reſorte dyde aryue thus contynued maugre theyr myght whyle felde troyan knyght tyll phebus chare gan weſtre downe repeyred towne whiche hadde grekes wrought afore full ylle nowe hardy cruell fyers achylle aryued knyghtes alle myrondones men wonte calle whiche ſee taken hath playne whoſe cōmynge grekes haue agayne felde recured put themſelfe prees thorugh helpe worthy achylles whiche ſo felly troyans falle vpon hath ſlayne full many oon thre thouſande ſtele armed bryght hym brought redy fyght knyghtes echone full worthy renowne whiche achylles grekes champyowne haue mercyles theyr cruelte slayne many troyan cyte ſo feruent theyr mortall ire enuyous hate deſyre newe newe ſhede theyrblode achylles thought dyde hym gode ſwerde troyans blode ſhede ſoyle ſe lye blede rowteles melancolye hath ſo hote enuye without theyr deth may nat quenche ſwerde full depe made drenche longe daye troyans blode batheth werein flode whiche forged whette ſo kene many ryuer hely grene ran hurtes ſore knyghtes alway purſued afore hym flee walles troye cytee made full pyteous crye whyle fynde ſtorye grekes hooſt hoolly aryued lyke guydo deſcryued men armes ſuche multytude knyghtes ſhortly conclude theyr ſhyppes newe landed troyans aſtoned ſe abaſſhed gan wexe alle ſodaynely gan falle euery halfe paſſyngly great prees euer one hardy achylles ſwerde made theyr ſydes rede lay bodyes dede wounded ſome entre gate knyghtly gan debate furyouſly felle cruell knyght child ſlewe theyr faders ſyght beholde full great pyte yet ſlaughter gretter without nombre towne perpetuelly theyr confuſyowne lykely euer haue ouercome ¶if troylus ne vnto reſcuſe come yonge freſſhe luſty inly deſyrous come eke parys dephebus many worthy partye ſocoure grekes tho ne myght endure agaynſt ſtande deffence theyr pryde make reſyſtence worthy troylus ſo well yt tyme hym quytte thus ſothe greke hytte outher maymeth made deye wherfore deth fled weye achylles companye nyght homewarde gan hym hye towarde grekes glorye great honoure receyue hym lyke conqueroure whiche hadde ſo well ymet troye haue theyr gate ſhet made thē ſtronge thorughout al y• towne tyme kynge agamenowne ycherched hath place couenable whiche hym thought moſte greable lyklyed moſte conuenyent euery lorde ſette tente felde full large ſpace moſte competent lodgynge place dewe ſyght ſette cyte eche lorde ſygned ſhulde gan anone ordayne manſyons pytched theyr tentes pauyllyons ſuche myght centoryes haue ſtorme rayne themſelfe ſaue deuyſed habytacles tugurryes ſmale receptacle ſhroude nyght alſo theyr ſhyppes moche myght haue theyr hors lande ordayne ſhulde ſtande alſo beſy carye thynges neceſſarye nedefully vnto ſege longe eke made tey ſhyppes ſtronge porte ankres caſte aſſent beſyed full faſte conferme one entenciowne ſette ſege troye towne therupon bounde aſſured faſte abyde whyle lyfe many laſte fynally without repentaunce prudently made ordynaunce beſte coude longe nyght bete fyres whiche bren wōder lyght ſpace deuyded fro fyres ſette vp maner bares roūde aboute lodgynge paled felde compas acheue fyne purpoſe felly wrought kept ſelfe aye cloſe ¶and kynge treaſon falle let make watche without tentes alle hadde reſted afore mynſtrellys made ouermore ſayth guydo longe nyght kepe tydes tofore fyres bryght meryly ſowne inſtrumentes made reſte tentes afore wery fyght ſee faynted theyr myght eke made theyr armure awayte wyſely agayne aduenture diſceyte founde ſyde thus kynge knyghtly prouyde aduyſe nothynge hym eſcape nyght fynde dyde wake tyll morowe rowes rede phebus chare gonne ſprede thus eche kynge deſpoſed ought wyll procede tell wrought ceryouſly without within ſupporte thyrde boke begyn begynneth thyrde boke telleth howe troy an yſſued morowe fought grekes valyauntly ector bare hymſelfe daye capitulo xxij whan aurora hyr pale lyght vnder y• mantel y• myrke nyght curtyne hyr hewes fade yſhroudyde ye derke ſhade abaſſhed rody deſyre oonly hyr femynyne aſhamed durſte nat ſeyne bycauſe ſhe hadde ſo longe bedde leyne freſſhe phebus owne choſen knyght whiche ſhe hydde hyr ſothely ſyght tyll ſtede called flegonte enhaſted hym aboue oure oryzonte appollo bemys clere hath recomforted hyr oppreſſed chere ſaye dawnynge whan tytan eeſt ryſynge hete atempre right ſofte hyr emyſperye glade lofte ſame houre troyan champyowne gouernour werres towne worthy ector whiche cyte next pryam hadde ſouereynte towne guyde knyghtly excellence manhode ſapyence troyan knyghtes lorde eke cheuetayne whiche hath cōmaunded large playne hye lowe exceptynge none kynges pryces lordes euerychone ſame morowe mete yfere theyr arraye muſtre apere lyke name eſtate beſyde temple whylom conſecrate goodes called dyane moſte honoured ryche faane array haſte lyke deuyſe knyghtly man playne paſſynge fayre ſe ſette amydde troye cyte smothe right fayre full freſſhe floures worthy noble werryoures troye towne togydre aſſembled many beholde ſe famous knyghtes arme y• place ſome gan full ſtreyte lace theyr doublettes made lynnen clothe certayne folde aboute hym gothe ſome alſo dempte moſte ſureſte 〈◊〉 batayle ar • ſte dyde firſte theyr deſyres sabatous greues cuſſues voydres payre breche alder firſte mayle ſome eke ne wolde fayle haue mayle payre bra therwithall cuſtome payreguſſettes pety cote garnyſſhed golde vp vnto throte paunce plate whiche ſelfe behynde ſhet cloſe theron fynde enuyron abordure ſmalle mayle ſome choſe newe entayle ſurmyd foos hole breſte plate arere doos behynde ſhet elles ſyde armes rynged nat wyde voyders frettyd mayle cordes rounde freſſhe entayle vambras wynges rerebras therto theron ſette beſaguys alſo vpon hede baſenet ſtele within locked full wele crafty ſyght wrought vyſer ſome wolde haue plate bauer breſte faſtened aforne canell pece eſy borne gloues plate ſtele forged bryght ¶and ſome wolde armed lyght thykkes iackes couered ſatyne ſome wolde haue mayle wrought ful fyne hawberion late wrought caſſade weyghte nat ouer lade hymſefe welde lyke lyfly man ſome wyll haue choce geſeran doublet hawberion ſome oonly ſure gepon ouer poleyns rechynge thekne •• euys eke ſo longe vambras may cured ner pryckynge palet plate cower ſome wyll haue alſo vyſer ſaue face oonly anaſer ſome wyll haue payre platy lyght welde hym well whan ſhall fyght ſome wyll haue target ſpere ſome pauys body ſome targe made ſtronge laſte ſome wyll haue dartes caſte pollax heded fyne ſtele pycked ſquare laſte wele ſome ſwerde enemy mete ſome wyll haue bowe ſhete arblaſt ſtande aſyde ¶and ſome foot ſome tyde array themſeſfe foomen ſayle many one beſy nayle felawes harneys make ſtronge dreſſe ſytte nat wronge poyntes treſſhes maner thynge ſuche caſe longeth armynge haue connynge euery thynge telle vnto longe dwelle fayle ye mot haue excuſed ſuche crafte lytell vſed ignoraunce doth penne lette theyr ordre termys ſette ofte chaungeth ſuche harneys deuyſe ye therin expert wyſe dyſdayne nat ſpeke place theyr armynge grace right lyſte correcte euery dell whan ector ſawe well euery armed arrayed worthy knyght lenger hath delayed aduyſely wardes make prudently badde ſhulde take theyr grounde haſte put certayne ſtande ordre endelonge playne man founde recheles gate called dardanydes without abode ector made vnſhette bad men ſhulde fette preſence done haſte cyncynabor brother borne baſte vnto hym firſte euerychon lorde named glaucon kynges ſone lycye heyre many baner diſplayed eyre two ector gaue guarde gouernaunce firſte warde hath thouſande knyghtes ſette ſperes rounde ſwerdes kene whette theyr breſte full many ryche ſhelde werechoſen felde amonge beſte endure myght agayne grekes manly fyght vnto ector bad anone goddes name ſhulde gone gate ſothely rede ie • te fylle myſchefe nede aſſygned ſelfe place manly chere kynge trace wyſely hym awaytynge thouſande knyghtes haue ledynge wenge knyghtly abyde wayte hym vpon euery ſyde hym ſone archylogus age man right vertuous fulfylle longeth knyght bothe herte alſo myght next ector gan deuyſe next warde kynge fryſe tyme called zantipus vnto hym yonge ſtronge deſyrous aſſygned wayte vanere thre thouſande knyghtꝭ armed bryght clere whiche warde kynge alchomus alſo ector cōmaunded go byddynge mekely dyde obeye full knyghtly haue take theyr weye gate paſſyngly arrayed towarde grekꝭ baners freſſhe diſplayed theyr penons vnrolled euerychone ector aſſygned hath anone noble yonge luſty free brother troylus ſo freſſhe vpon ſe whiche knyghthode ſuffyſaunce thirde warde haue gouernaunce iii thouſande knyghtes yonge age flourynge force hardy courage suche cuſtome wont lede ector bretherhede full goodly ſpake ſayde departynge brother quod herte ſo louynge towardes kyndeneſſe though haue partye great gladneſſe thy manhode ſo ferre kouthe knyghthode thy grene youthe yet douteles fantaſye full ofte daye ſtonde iupardye penſyfehede warde beſy drede whan remembre vpon thy manhede leſt thy courage vyolent thy lyfe neclygent thy ſelfe put ferre aduenture ſurquydrye ſo moche aſſure thy force kynghtly ſterte euery peryll thy manfull herte hauynge rewarde ſuche mortall ſtryfe wylfulneſſe nouther deth lyfe aduertence thy ſauacyowne fortune turneth vp downe hyr whele meuable hye lowe martys ire wynde doth blowe whiche cauſeth full ofte ſyghe thynke wake whan ſhulde wynke reuoluynge aye thy haſty wylfulneſſe gentyll brother hardyneſſe thus ylke day vpon euery ſyde praye ſo wyſely prouyde hate yre thy foos purſuynge nat excede ſyttynge let prudence kepe mene wyſdome eke holde agayne reyne thy herte thy fyers courage fyred haue thy grene tendre age deuoyde drede eche peryll endure enemyes thy myſauenture reioyſenat myn owne brother dere myghty mar praye herte entere thus euery day troyans grounde theyr handes kepe ſounde lyke wolde dyde anone humylyte manly wyſe yonge iuſty knyght worthy troylus herte freſſhe lyght anſwered agayne ſayd glad chere myn owne lorde brother dere god fore fully ſhall obeye fulfylle lyſte ſeye vnto gentylleſſe nat declyne thorugh none rekleſneſſe poynt cōmaundement hole herte beſt entent ſhall take hede playnely none ye haue ſayde myn owne lord brother lothe offende greue wyſe lowly toke leue forth herode ſo lyke manly knyght beholde noble ſyght amonge men behaueth hym ſo wele thre thouſande knyghtꝭ armed bryght ſtele enuyron rode troylus felde day bare ſhelde paſſant golde iij lyon rychely chaumpe aſure wrought full craftely gate yſſued anone hym ladde knyghtes euerychone grekes holdynge next waye ector haſteth euer maye prudently wardes ordayne noble worthy bretherne twayne kynge hupon ardelaus aſſygned ſtorye telleth thus fouthe warde guye wyſſe lande called laryſſe bretherne two hadde reygned longe kynge hupon paſſyngly ſtronge ſtature lyke chaumpyowne ſaue ector troye towne none hym egall myght delyuere better knyght foon paſſynge deſpytous whiche brother called ardelaus foure thouſande knyghtes hadde lede ſeuen thouſande ſothly rede lyke wrytte guydo worthy ector aſſygned hath alſo one bretherne called brymarchus noble knyght armes right famous hadde manhode paſſynge excellence ector taken haue lycence rode theyr waye amonge prces thorughe gate dardanydes fyfte warde haue ledynge ector cōmytted kynge ceſoyne lorde prynce brother called pollydamas cyſones hye ſtature myghty armes paſſyngly endure vpon full many man behelde theyr kynge bare thynge ſhelde felde gowlys fynde ſygne guydo maketh mynde forth rode full ſterne pa noble kynge pollydamas whan hadde ector leue take whiche euer one full beſy make ſixte warde dylygence kynge called pretemenſe full worthy bothe werre pee duke hyght sterepes whiche alſo full worthy honde toke folke pauonye londe gouerne felde daye whiche people hath cuſtome aye without plate hawberion mayle ſwyfte hors theyr foomen aſſayle myghty bowes arrowes ſharpe groūde thorugh harneys mortally wounde folke ector eke alſo deyphebus aſſygned go felde guyde lede theyr waye faſte gan ſpede paſſe dardanydes full diſcrtely ector chees pauyſeres cladde mayle plate cōmaundynge yſſynge gate archer felde gone many worthy well armed euerychone awayte nat lore folke ſpake tofore pauonye hadde none armure prudent ector make ſure agreſt myghty regyowne hath choſen full worthy renowne beſte knyghtes euerychon two kynges eſdras phyon aſſygned take hede fotemen whan haue nede whiche phyon made full rychely rode chare yuory whiche wheles wrought full curyous tree ycalled ebenus whiche tree groweth ferre ynde blacke hewe alſo fynde whan korue tree wyll wexe anone nature harde ſtone whan graue eyther rounde ſquare pure golde roued chare fret perle many ryche ſtonys ſuch nother trowe ther none worlde ſhall nat fayne ladde myghty knyghtꝭ twayne men armes within withoute armed ſtele rydynge rounde aboute worthy kynges eſoras phyon ector hath called hym anone one bretherne ſo falle guyde leder alle name pyktagoras great troyan eneas tofore made mencyon ector goode delyberacyon vij warde aſſygned hath kepe vpon ſtedys luſty lepe ſuche vſed moche ryde full manly knyghtes houe ſyde whiche emphranye vnto troye towne come ſo ferre theyr regyowne foſtre ectors ſake whan hadde hym leue take rode full proudely forthe eneas gate wonder knyghtly pa brode felde tyll haue atteyned whyle ector hath ordayned lyke myn auctour reherce eyght warde folke perce worthy knyghtes manly ryght wyſe whiche cōmytted paryſe hym day awayte beſyly ector full benyngnely spake ſayde departynge brother myn maner thynge whan thou art paſſed dardanydes daye ferre put nat prees amonge grekes iupardye leſte thy foon myſchefe eſpye haue olde newe date theyr hertes full freſſhe mortall hate fyre breſte hath ſo enbraced harde arraced wherfore brother loke thou wyſe nat ferre fro kepe nye myſauentoure falle vpon ſo may ſocoure day myn owne brother dere parys full humble chere anſwered ſayde euery thynge wolde obeye vnto byddynge rode waye anone meyne felde cyte ector aye dyde beſyneſſe nynthe warde ordre dreſſe whiche thought hymſelfe lede whiche put ſothly rede fyue thouſande knyghtꝭ borne troye towne worthyeſt gretteſt renowne paſſyngly famous knyghthode borne deſcent troyans blode ¶and bretherne toke hym ten suche knewe mooſt manly men forayne fro ſtocke regallye lyne borne baſtardye ector great chyerte knyghthode coude themſe whan hadde knyghtly purueaunce wardes ſet gouernaunce lyke mar hymſelfe faſte gan hym ſpede without abode take ſtede whiche bokes called gallathe hors hauynge ſoueraygnete ferre men ryde coſte dare maketh ſo great boſte ſhape hyghte alſo fayreneſſe ſtrengthe loke great ſwyfteneſſe lyke hors perfourmed oute wt wyer men myght hym turne aboute lyke dare maketh mencyowne ector rode thorugh troye towne armed came hym wonder well foot hede full rychely euerydell ſhone bryght ſonne ſomers day pryam helde right way whan come kynge reherſeth ordre euery thynge hath done ordynaunce lowly ſayde ſo pleaſaunce noble royall excellence haue choſen beſy dylygence thouſande knyghtes full ſuffyſaunce fyue houndred haue attendaunce perſone alway ye footman cyte ſhall awayte euer one wherfore lorde faſte gone lowly praye worthyneſſe ſewe v good aduyſeneſſe towne alwaye eke ye togydre kepe knyghtes meyne beſeche full myght within boundes ſhall fyght ye ſuffre none paſſe kepe ye hole ſelfe place wyxe v ſtronge cyte haue nede ye may aye ſe v releue kepynge aſyde ſpecyally abyde moſte lyckely partye ſuſtene euer amonge ſhall men go betwene expleyt trouthe reporte whiche parte mar lyſte felde ſorte power ylke day fatalle ye ſhalbe caſtell walle refuge ſaue v ſmerte ſpecyally one thynge ye aduerte diſceyte fraude treaſowne compaſſyd behynde towne foon thorugh rekleſneſſe whyles beſyneſſe agaynſte felde fyght wyſe therto hath ſyght thynge tourne vnto damage thoughe engyne worke ſage victorye may conclude grekes fraude v nat delude engyne vn ware vyolence hopynge alway none offence hyghnes haue ſayde worde pryamus abrayde benyngnely chere countenaunce ſayde ector ſothfaſt ſuffyſaunce fynall truſte ſupportacion thy wyſe diſpoſycion hoolly putte thou lyſte ordayne next god ſhall nat fayne fayth hope ſykerneſſe welfare ſothfaſtneſſe cōmytted behole thy hande gouernaunce playnely lande thou ordayneſt muſt nedes prayer make goddes aboue celeſtyall preſerue partye eche myſchefe aduerſyte thou mayſte home cyte repayre honour laude victorye prayſe renowne memorye thy name put remembraunce perpetuelly thyne honour auaunce fare well myn owne ſone dere ector tho full humble chere leue toke forthe rode anone amonge lordes knyghtes euerychone rote nobleſſe knyghthod groūde ſtrength hardyneſſe ſtocke therto inuyncyble aſmoche poſſyble nature myght hym graunte kynde touchynge manhode bokes fynde hadde hym ſoueraygne excellence gouernaunce medlyd prudence nought ſterte hȳ ſo wyſe ware ſhelde fynde bare vpon breſte troyan champyon chief golde gowlys alyon depeynt therm baner bete ſelfe ſame ſo amydde ſtrete toke waye dardanydes beholde huge prees noyſe trumpettes claryons baners vnrolled longe freſſhe penons rede whyte grene blewe blake wyſe ector hath take felde without wt herte hole entent mar hymſelfe hadde preſent guydo maketh mynde rode warde lafte behynde manhode wolde nat abyde ſmote ſtede ſherpely ſyde fell courage hath hors ſo payned firſte warde hath attayned vale hylle fore frounteres nat aſtoned fell cheres grekes platly nat aferde lyke knyght euen afore theyr berde gan preaſe theyr foo mortall whyle vpon troye wall ſondry place hye toures freſſhe beſene may floures ladyes aſcended towne fayre ſo yonge ſtondynge enuyrowne quene eleyne paſſynge fayre ſene kynges doughtres goodly polycene many whiche womanhede herte full beſy drede inly gaſte fere frayde whan behelde felde diſplayde brode baners ſome tenderneſſe loue ſome kyndeneſſe pale dredefull theyr lordes ſome theyr face hydde eke fere nat bolde lyfte vp theyr ſyght beholde armure clere bryght glyterynge agayne ſonne ſhene theyr hertes tendre myght nat ſuſtene theyr drede thus • ette dwelle grekes forth ſhall telle ſo ye lyſte abyoe whyle muſt fordulled ſtyle agayne direct agamenon well may make exclamacyon ignoraunce ſtandeth ſo lyght whiche cauſeth full clowdy ſyght makynge ſpeke werre lacke termes muſt nedes erre connyngely wardes ſette cruell allector beſy lette nyghtes doughter blynded derkeneſſe crafte armes trouthe expreſſe ordre dewe felde deſcryue chauncer ala nat alyue refourme rede lacke ſlower ſpede noble rethor dyde excelle makynge dranke welle vnder pernaſo muſes kepe whiche hylle myght neuer ſlepe vnneth ſlombre whiche ala playne ſayne thoughe wede nat polymyte coloures forth wyll endyte cometh euen thought playnely wryte y• kynghath wrought manly knyght great agamenon lyke latyn maketh mencyou ¶what troweye entent founde ſlowe outher neclygent grekes halfe wardes make nay nay nat ſo hym lyſte wake tyme ſothly ſlepe lyke kynge day felde kepe neclygence myght herte fade daye fynde made sixe twenty wardes well deuyſed ſo prudently man myght amende ordynaunce firſte gaue gouernaunce manfull noble patroclus wt hym ladde myn auctour telleth thus myrundones ſo myghty ſo ſtronge folke achylles longe beſyde thylke meyne whiche brought countre cōmynge ſege troye rode forth waye felde made delay fyll ſo ſame day achylles kepte hym tente ſykeneſſe daye ne wente lecheſſe made hym abſtene woundes freſſhe grene caught day tofore whiche hele theyr akynge ſore counſayle kepte hymſelfe cloſe bed day nat ne roſe hope oonly bettre endure whan reſtored vnto cure men toke patroclus whiche marmes paſſyngely famous deſcent come great kynrede alſo hym rede haboundaunt golde rycheſſe ferre cōmended gentylleſſe hadde name hye diſcreſyon aye ſuche affeccyon entyer loue trouthe faythfulneſſe great deſyre inwarde kyndeneſſe beſy thenkynge ſo great feruence moche frenſhyp thoughtfull aduertence huge brennynge paſſynge amerous betwyxe achylles patroclus theyr hertes locked chayne ſo euer ſhall nat fayne ton hath wrought broder vnto brother herte confermed tother wyll goodes bothe comune deth euer ſo contune without chaunge theyr loue ſo abode ¶and patroclus forth anone hym tode felde myrundones tente abyteth achylles ſeconde warde kynge meryon aſſygned agamenon worthy kynge ydumenee duke hyght meneſtee thre thouſande knyghtes ſtele armed clene folke came athene aſſygned go thyrde warde kynge aſtalapho ſone hyght phylymene knyghtes came cu • ene fourthe warde without lettynge archelaus noble worthy kynge prothenor securydan whiche dayes ſo ſtronge man aſſygned hoolly thre knyghtes boece great lande famous fyfte warde kynge menelaus folke regyowne called spertence full hye renowne iles adiacent thyſe baner went menelay freſſhe couragyous vi warde kynge epyſtrophus aſſygned kynge elyde many worthy rydynge ſyde prouynce famous yle called guydo fordeſyle vii warde thelamonyus called ayax great kynge famous aſſygned ſ • • ely termyne • kes fro salamyne hym brought many another mo foure erles hym went alſo theſeus eke amphymacus thyrde called daryus fourthe named polyſarye viij warde ſhall nat tarye good aduyſe daye aſſygned vnto kynge called thoas ayar cyleus ix warde ladde x kynge phylyk hadde kynge xi dyde aſſygne ſothely bothe berthe lyne renowmed ſo great encreaſe myghty kynge called pallamydes kynge nawlus ſone hyeſt borne blode duke neſtor full famous knyghthode xij warde ladde grekes ſyde melancolyke ſurquedous pryde kynge honux ſone one mabente felde playnely whan wente ordre hadde wardes thyrtene proudely muſtrynge endelonge grene agayne troyans redy fyght eke kynge vlyxes hyght ladde hym fourtene • ede humerus kynge eke dyde lede fy •• eneth myne auctour wryteth thus duke called curybulus ſyxteneth ladde vpon daye whiche kynght kyng protheſylaye aſſygned great ordynaunce enforce vengaunce vpon deth theyr worthy kynge ector ſlayne grekes arryuynge kynge roydo ladde ſeuentene kynge occymene xviij warde hadde ledynge zantipus lyde kynge hadde kepe cōmytted garde grekes ſyde xix warde xx myn auctour lerneth v hadde kynge called amphymacus lyke knyght guyde wyſſe phylocetes kynge laryſſe one twenty ladde eke rede two twenty hadde dyomede heneus kynge cyparye whylom ſo noble ſo worthy thre twenty hadde gouernayle troyans proudely aſſayle xxiiij ſwerde ſpere ſhelde bynge prothaylus ladde felde carpenor carpedye kynge werre expert right wyſe workynge fyue twenty ryche well beſayne grekes ſyde brought playne ſixe twenty ſothely laſte coudeſe afore caſte euery thynge good inſpeccyon wyſe kynge great agamenon hadde hym prudent werryour ordayned emperour grekes hooſt wyſeſt echone wyſe forthe grekes gone felde pompe full royall enſygnes token marcyall haue take theyr grounde paſſyngely arrayed theyr ſtandardes rychely diſplayed brode banerys many freſſhe penowne agayne wynde yt made hydous ſowne right dredefull playnely theremen ſawe many creſtys clere many tufte golde ſyluer ſhene meynt fetheres redde whyte grene deuyſe wonder incruaylous folkes amerous token borne ſhewe openly loue brente inwardly hye empryſe day fulfylle herde loude noyſes ſhrylle ferre felde dredefull ſouns bothe trumpettes claryouns kalendes ſhedynge blode noyſe almoſte rage wode fomy brydelles mouthes blede furyous neyhyng many baſtarde ſtede praunſynge hors vpon eyther ſyde enſygnes myght pryde grekes partye troye alſo knyghtly wyſe haue euery warde ſtandynge place firſte ſonder lytell ſpace began reproche full entent ector tho full vnpacyent formeſt ſyde torye ire whome man myght accoye lyke lyon hungry rage yſſued furyous vyſage towarde grekes myghty ſtede ſpores made ſydes blede knyghtly herte ſo inly torne mortall ire rode toforne brennynge full hote melancolye whiche thynge whan grekes gan eſpye patroclus without abode ſurquedye afore wardes rode toforne bothe hooſtes ſyght encountre playnely myght worthy ector whan hym ſawe ferre right lyne dyameterre rode vnto hym hatefull tene ſpere ſherpe grounde kene thorughout ſhelde enuyous rage ſmote ector without damage excepte oonly hede ſtele afore forged whet full wele thorugh plate mayle myghtely gan glace ſkynne thyng myght trace albe came paſſynge vyolence yet ector dyde none offence ſadell one hym flytte though ſturdely hym hytte myght nat bakwarde bowe chyne partye make hym enclyne fatally confuſyon myghty man troyan champyon ire aye brennynge vpon hym hate frat ſo ſore left ſpere myne auctor wryteth thus ſwerde rode patroclus auyſed fully ſhalbe dede furyouſly gan ayme hede rofe hym downe theyr maner let breſte thorugh baſenet ſayth guydo ſo great payne ſtroke parted hym wayne mortall ſwerde whetted ſo kene patroclus myght nat ſuſtene vpon hors fyll downe grounde caught laſte fatall wounde beynge preſent knyghtes euerychone delyuerly vpon hym anone worthy ector ſtede downe deſcendyd lyke wode lyowne hatefull ire brennynge fyre hauynge herte inly great deſyre ſpoyle hym armure anone whiche full many ryche ſtone bothe rubyes saphyres ynde dayes playnely fynde kynges lordes knyghtes naye batayle went theyr beſte araye ſothly ector whan firſte gan ſe multytude ſtones pe • patro • lu ſo oryent ſheyne vpon arme hynge hors reyne meane whyle whyle hole entent catche praye ſo dylygent couetyſe theyr alder ſyghtes tyll meryon thre thouſāde knyghtes armed ſtele rounde aboute hym alle ſodaynely vpon ector falle dede corp patroclus ſaue purpoſe ector may nat haue lyberte ryche kynge ſpoyle whiche cauſed hym angre boyle kynge called meryon irous wode ſayde amonge echon gredy lyon wolfe moſte tauynous hatefull tygre paſſynge enuyous auaryce beſte ſaturable deſyre ſothly vnſtaunchable vpon praye thou ſhalt y• nat fede go elles ſewe thy mede truſte well concluſyon fyfty thouſande thy deſtruccyon one entent playnely wyll nat fayle thyne hatefull pry • e attones aſſayle ſodaynely ſperes ſharpe whette euery halfe gan hym beſette maugre force myght manhode enforcynge refte hym ſtede ſoth faſtely great vyolence conſtrayned ſtronge defence ſayth guydo falle vpon kne thorugh myght magnanymyte manhode hath horſe recured maugre grekes ſo moche aſſured ſtrengthe great myght recured lyke worthy knyght ſtede agayne amyddes foon right ſyne rode meryon full deſyrous hym auenged furye haſty cruelte therupon ſette delyte mortall • lody appety • e ſothe hym ſlayne anoon saue y• kynge whiche called glacon came reſcue hym kynge theſeus ſone hyght archylogus haue tolde meryon reſkewe th • e thouſande knyghtes gan hym ſewe full al ••• ted attones batayle lyfe • th ector aſſayle awayte vnware hym ſette al whyle y• euer mette ſwerde kylled bare downe fynally gayneth raunſowne greke durſte hym mete departynge felte full vnſwete made waye aboute hym euery fledde hym deth fere rode made patthe ful playne rede patroclus agayne repeyred ſpoyle hym myght amyd felde grekes ſyght wolde praye nat lyghtly lete tyll dumee myghty kynge crete two thouſande cladde plate mayle worthy kynghtes ector aſſayle whyles ſo deſyrous haue tolde ſpoyle patroclusi newe agayne confuſyon lyke fynde came kynge meryon ector myght take hede force refte hym ſtede ſothely none boote compelled fyght foote knyghode herte reſumeth wt ſwerde aboute hym conſumeth withſtande bothe hors man furyouſly troyan knyght began armes legges ſhuldres boon hewe amydde mortall foon grekes myght afore hym nat ſuſtene rede ſlewe fyftene beſy hym take ſuch ſlaughter gan amōge thē make ne durſte abyde afore face meryon ſelfe place meane whyle toke vp patroclus heuy chere face full pyruous • tede layde hym beforne tente anone hath borne alwaye grekes theyr cruell mode aboute ector furyous wode felly • ode fyghtynge vpon fote whiche ſome felte vnlote preſumed vpon hym preſſe manhode ne wolde ceſſe beſette hym euery ſyde hauynge truſte theyr great pryde fynally myſchefe hym take dempte myght nat eſcape theyr handes ſhortly none aduenture ſtede lyklyhede recure force caſte hym lette attones gan hym ſette ſpecyally amonge euerychone fynde ſothe howe one grekyſſhe knyght right worthy fame caryon playnely name hym aforced ector oppreſſe whan moſte myſchefe diſtreſſe beſette grekes hym enuyrownynge tyll fortune hym awaytynge longe daye felle fyght reſcuſe came atroyan knyght mydde grekes whan beſette toke ij dartes ſharpe kene whette furyouſly firſte ſhoke toon thorugh herte ſmote caryon darte felde gan glyde plate mayle thorughout outher ſyde fatally dedely wounde caryon glode anone grounde amonge hondred knyghtes ferys afore conſpyred theyr felle cherys ſlayne ector ſome maner waye eft agayne yonge knyght troye full delyuerly raughte nother ſpere caſte one ſawe afere auaunce hymſelfe ector felde thorugh platy playnely ſhelde lyne right ne ſhulde aſterte myght roofe hym thorughe herte haſte coude vpon troyans gan crye loude enhaſte knyghtly ſocoure whorthy ector ſtode aduentoure amonge grekes hauynge refute sool hymſelfe helpe deſtytute whiche crye grekes vnware firſte came worthy cyncybare brother ector baſte borne hymſelfe rydynge toforne knyghtes whiche guyde wonder proudely pryckynge ſyde sodaynely bothe one alle froſſhe grekes falle hadde ector rounde beſet aboute thorugh manhode great route enboſſhed backe threhondred knyghtes whiche yt ſpacke aſtoned gan withdrawe thurty firſte cruelly ſlawe maugre ector manhede amyd felde taken hath ſtede entred amonge prees daye knyghthode pereles whyle helde blody ſwerde honde tho agayne hym ſtonde helpe playnely rede brake karfe two threde knotte cruell antropos onely let purpoſe good leyſer ſpoyle patroclus therfore ire wode furyous full cruelly grekes quytte theyr mede whiche face faſte gan ſpede whoſe ſharpe ſwerde bathed theyr blode dyed rede dyde hym gode vpon auenged daye lyon played vpon grekes manhode haunte theyr pryde ſo mortally gan daunte hym fledde rode makynge hote ſtreyntes theyr blode endelonge renne vpon grene tyll tyme duke great athene called whylom meneſteus thre thouſande knyghtes full famous whiche bothe lorde guyde felde hath take vpon lefte ſyde deceyte full ſecrete wyſe ¶where troylus folke fryſe whiche hath daye ſo lyſte ſeke knyghthode kylled many greke lyke tygre gredy pray troylus bare hym longe day sleynge grekes many worthy knyght whyle beſyeſt fyght agayne foon kynge antipus kynge hyght alchanus vpon grekes ylyche freſſhe newe makynge theyr ſydes blody hewe one aſſent thre thorugh theyr māhede ſpecyally vpon bay ſtede ſo euer troylus rode euery greke ſwerde abode sodaynely made ſterue thorugh theyr plate ſo depe gan kerue contynued tyll duke meneſte troylus ſawe great cruelte ſlaughtre grekes made haſty ire face pale fade hent ſpere threwe reſt troylus ſmette euen amyd breſt ſternely maugre renowne erthe anone bare hym downe myddes mortall foon cruelly hym beſette anoon hym treyne layde oke laſe rounde aboute maner compaſe ſpere darte ſwerdes forged bryght hymſelfe diffendeth lyke knyght great manhode honour auaunce albe lyfe hanged balaunce ſtode felte full vnſwete poynt deth amonge horſe fete great awayte duke meneſte howe troylus myght haue take mortall hate caſtynge thought myſchefe take eſcape nought euery halfe ſo beſette ſwerdes rounde kene grounde whette alone ala mortally beſtadde ſeaſed hym forth haue hym ladde tyll myſeres worthy knyght troye gan crye ſtode waye sore abaſſhed right furyous wyſe ye noble worthy men fryſe manly knyghtes aye preuyd felde moſte renowmed bothe ſpere ſhelde conſyder nowe vnto hye fame aduerte glorye name daye thorugh neclygence power myghty vyolence grekes troylus ytake sool felde ye haue hym forſake ſhall rebounde alder ſhame ye ſothe greatly blame worthyneſſe floure take grekes lacke ſocoure ye take haſty wreche shamefull reporte honour ſhall apeche perpetuelly ſayde therof amys defaute troylus taken whiche named ſo worthy famous worde kynge alkamous melancolye felte herte ryue ire hente ſpere blyue pryckynge enhateth myght tyll playnely ſyght beſy troylus • ede full knyghtly ſyttynge ſtede ran one thorugh fell downe dede efte agayne pale thynge rede rancoure lenger wolde lette greke firſte mette thorugh body ſmet ſpere men myght ſe poynt fere breſte plate thorugh ſhulder bone grounde fell downe dede anone therwithall worthy fryſes alle came flokmele downe grekes falle myghtely maugre theyr diffence ſette vpon ſo great vyolence troylus daunger fre thorugh theyr knyghtly magnanymyte made hym recure ſtede ſpecyally helpynge nede zantipus ſtronge manly kynge whiche diſdayne cōmynge ou meneſte gan ſpere grate thorugh ſhelde mayle thycke plate ſore ſmote meneſte hadde dede ne hadde armour whiche ire gan tremble ſhake troylus hondes take eſcaped pryſoner deſpyte berde maugre power wherfore gan haſty hote enuye knyghtes furyouſly crye ſo myghty renowmed ſtronge payne venge wronge vpon troyans mete face haſt gan myghtely enbrace theyr ſharpe ſperes grounde byte felly foyne togydre ſmyte tho began great mortall werre fyre braſt ſhene ſterre baſenertes theyr plate bryght thorugh y• felde flaumeth ye fereful lyght lyfe deth toke tho hede downe playne lengthe brede wardes gan proudely auale lokes enuye pale aproche aſſemble yfere hate brennynge man may ſtere gan hurte ſpere ſwerde darte mortally vpon euery parte ſlaughter gan greatly rewe ylyche alwaye newe newe ector grekes thorugh worthyneſſe rode manly dyde oppreſſe mercyleſſe ſlowe bare downe without excepcyowne furyouſly routhe ſe newe duke meneſte repayred enuyous herte hondes troylus ſo ſterte ſlaughter eke meynee rode beſy ſ • ee troyan people whan myght mete auenge hym nothynge wolde lete tyll caſuelly amonges prees knyght mette hyght miſerees whiche deſpyte meneſte hadde reſkus worthy troylus maugre hym put hym pray ſo befelle ſelfe day mete agayne aduenture meneſte cote armure marked hym armes bare ſodaynely ware myght take hede furyouſly ſterne ſtede ſpere amyd renges alle bare hym ouer made hym falle maugre myght erthe downe fynde kynge hupowne deſcended ſtorye lyſte nat lye two thouſande knyghtes companye whiche grekes felly gan ſette y• berde kynge prothenor mette archelaus noble werryour boece lorde gouernour helpe oonly prothenor lyke tygre wood boor gan troyans aſſayle deth many one daye ſleeth kynge hupon thorugh chyualrye tyme melancolye full many greke gaue dethes wounde thus gan eche confounde suche mortall hate amonges tyll fortune knyght pollydamas troye ſyde ſone anthenor knyghtes hymſelfe tofor grekes enuyous pryde myd theyr wardes falle ſyde gan breke knyghtly diſſeuer agayne whoſe ſwerde myght nat ꝑſeuer ſo inly furyous hym helpe came kynge remus wynge parte brekynge many ſpere darte agayne grekes thre thouſande knyghtes beholde felly fyghtes ſothe vnto troye luſte heuenly ioye ſe grekes brake aſondre noyſe loude thondre felde ſtrokes gan aryſe whyle remus ye haue herde deuyſe vpon grekes ſo enuyous felde came menelaus worthy knyghtes spartenſe agayne remus make reſyſtence full proudely makynge delaye worthy remus kynge menelaye hors backe ſharpe ſperes whette myd felde enuye mette thorugh manly proweſſe renowne hors backe eche bare downe none ſtroke myght ſhone whyle anthenor ſone pollydamas luſty freſſhe lyght delyuer myght deſyrous honour atteyne mette felde neuewe eleyne myghty duke called mereus flourynge youthe right vertuous freſſhe armed newe luſty courage ſothe twenty yere age whiche ſo yonge noble knyght right renowmed bothe herte myght fortune befell ala troyan knyght daūz pollydamas ſpere thorugh ſhelde mayle plate hytte hym ſo cruell fate amonge grekes felle downe dede whiche thynge whan menelay toke hede ſawe hym lye ſlayne grene herte remembrynge quene quene eleyne whoſe neuewe dole whiche full delyuer pa remus rode cruelte alſo ferre myght hym ſe full knyghtly mette hym berde ſmette hym ſharpe ſwerde vpon hede hatefull tene ſtede myght nat ſuſtene wounde ſo paſſyngely mortall ſtroke pryllous fall knyghtes wende dede hadde hent hym vp began fle troye warde hym great paas befell pollydamas maner whan behelde made repayre knyghtly felde excepte ſome byddynge hadde worthy remus home troye ladde pale dede woundes wyde tho came grekes ſyde celydys luſty freſſhe kynge dare ſayth wrytynge ſothe boke lyſte telle celydys dyde excelle bothe beaute ſemelyhede ſhape porte goodlyhede surmountynge dare lyſte deſcryue fayreneſſe tho alyue lymmes compact ſo clene rede yonge freſſhe quene fumynye whiche beaute floure kynge celydys loued paramoure vpon hym hooly hir pleaſaunce ſo prynted hir remembraunce chefe reſorte ſothely hir herte vpon hym euery houre aduerte fynally departed nought day nyght houre hir thought fully hir owne knyght fortune luſty freſſhe lyght smote ſtede ſharply ſyde ſurquedye proudely gan ryde mortall hate full furyous paas right lyne pollydamas ſpere made hym flytte ſadell whiche dyde ſytte marked hym ſo great myght agaynewarde manly troyan knyght pollydamas deſpytous face celydys departed fro place aſwerde ſo ſmet hym hede ſtede fylle downe dede whiche grekes great confuſyon tyme fyerſer lyon ector grekes knyghtly gan enchace ofte made leſe theyr place euer rode neceſſyte afore ſwerde made fle suche vengeaunce hath take felde fayne forſake purſewe wolde neuer fyne tyll amonge people salomyne ector mette worthy kynge famous theyr lorde hyght theſalus many troyan day hadde ſlawe ector towarde hym gan drawe kynge tenter grece alſo manly knyght prudent bothe two raught ſpere haſte vnwarely vnto ector ran thorughe ſhelde plate mayle ſtele ſperehede forged ſo wele ſharpe ſquare ſo kene grounde gaue ector full peryllous wounde ector reyne gan ſtede proude tenter aquyte mede full wyſely haſte myght right ferre ſeuered ſyght wherof ector melancolyous herte wood furyous akynge wounde grene haſte auenge conſtreynte ten • greke ſhortly mette ſo bolde waye ſette without mercy deth anone rede encountred one whiche pryde wolde hym dyuerte ſwerde roſe herte thorugh harneys melancolye whiche ſtroke whan grekes gan eſpye aſtoned one entencyon peryllouſly beſette hym enuyron ſuche aſſaute gan aboute hym make thorugh theyr māhode myght hȳ take accorde great multytude cruelly gan hym include lyklyhede mortall ſtryfe myght nat eſcape lyfe hym ſo fell enuyous tyll kynge whiche hyght theſeus grekes ſyde oonly gentylleſſe suche routhe caughe vpon diſtreſſe ſe hym ſtande ſo nye vpon wrake thus vnto hym manly pyteſpake flour knyghthode rote hardynes welle manhode ſtok worthynes lyſt y• nat haue none aduertēce thy lyf ſaue knyghtly prouydēce wylfully moſte drede thy lyfe iupardeſt take lyſte hede mortall peryll thou arte beſette amonge ſo many cloſed yſhette alone ala deuoyde ſocoure thy ſelfe wylt fauoure fortune lyketh ordayne euery wyght ought complayne beholde ſo noble knyght whiche thorugh world caſt ſo clere lyght worthyneſſe wyll hym nat withdrawe rekleſly day ſlawe pyteouſly thy perſone leſe withdrawe thy hande yet ſyth yu mayſt cheſe thy hye proweſſe compelleth preye ſuche myſchefe thou nat ne deye whan ector hym gan take hede thanked hym goodlyhede maugre ſothly power myght grekes lyke worthy knyght ſcapyd myd foon went waye thorugh euerychon blody ſwerde alway honde waye pollydamas fonde full lyke man beſy payne diffende hymſelf agayne kynges twayne menelay thelamonyus whiche vpon hym full furyous wt ſpere greke thelamowne pollydamas ſmote erthe downe compellynge hym none vote agayne two fyghte fote aſſentyd fully hym wroke firſte haue wen broke myghty charnelle baſenet whan vyſer ſmet face naked bare felle hym mortall ſnare toke hym ſtorye deuyſe ſent hym forth full cruell wyſe towarde grekes many worthy knyght whan ector therof ſyght ſawethe myſchefe pollydamas caſte fully ſocoure caas prycked wooder lyon rode aboute hym enuyron ſwerde made large ſpace tyll came ſame place amonges greke furyous wode pollydamas ſelfe tyme ſtode socourles remedye tyll ector caſte eye grekes made haſtely withdrawe thurty firſte hath ſlawe ſeuered maugre theyr pryde tofore ſwerde durſte nat abyde agaynſt hym make none obſtacle knyghthode hye myracle pollydamas myſchefe firſte awhaped grekes honde frely eſcaped freſſhely tho kynge epyſtrophns menelay thelamonyus theyr knyghtes togydre hole cloos agayne troyans gette aloos newe entred batayle great ſtrengthe paſſynge apparayle myghtely troyans compelle theyr waye dare nat dwelle natwithſtandynge theyr great worthyneſſe ector knyghtly hye proweſſe fought ſo manly tyme rede cowardely haue ſlayne ſtede conſtrayned fyght fote many greke felte full vnſote none aboute hym ſtode ſwerde ne ſhadde blode though ſo thycke aboute layne voyded made aſpace playne compaſſe rounde behynde eke afore fete ſo well hath hym bore day greke none certayne harby hande hym layne ſo ſtronge ſturdy wall whan brother called naturall sawe hym fote amyd foon fruſſhe felle euerychon founde hym ſtorye maketh mynde diffende hymſelfe lyke tygre ynde hym helpe thorugh theyr hye renowne felle firſte kynge thelamowne ector ſo cruell founde gaue hym many blody wounde tyll one named dyndaron hath ſo ferre amonge rengys gon bore hym ſo oonly manhede hath wonne paſſynge myghty ſtede brought ector ſothly ſtode amonge grekes bathed theyr blode whiche haſte full knyghtly ſtrode amōge lyke mar hymſelf rode full many greke makynge ſterue ſwerde whetted kerue daunted hath theyr enuyous pryde tyll dephebus entrede ſyde felde knyghtly chere hym brought many good archere poeme whiche theyr arrowes kene fethers pecok freſſhe ſhene vpon grekes haue felde recured ſhotte ſo moche aſſured thorugh mayle thycke plate ſtele perced haue theyr harneys euerydele dephebus full lyke manly man kynge tentran hors backe tho ran furyouſly gan ſwerde enbrace wounded hym euen amyd face thorughe vyſer felle tene hors backe myght nat ſuſtene thus troyans grekes yronne agayne haue felde ywonne ſo yrous ſo wode theſeus full knyghtly withſtode knyghtes hym ladde rede ectora brother hadde ſtorye ſayth hyght quyntylene yonge freſſhe luſty armed bryght ſhene whiche kynge called modernus proudely falle vpon theſeus theſe twayne togydre aſſent falle hym great aduyſement fynally vnhappy chaunce wt theyr knyghthode brought hȳ outtraūce caſte ſhortly ſhalbe dede whoſe purpoſe ector gan take hede vnto gentery myght loude gan crye beſechynge thynge deye lowely byddynge dyde obeye withdrewe vengeaunce ector hadde fully remembraunce theſeus ſame daye tofore towarde hym ſo goodly hadde hym bore whan hym ſawe myſchefe diſtreſſe knyghtly thought quyte gentylneſſe lyke logeth euery gentylman theſeus full lowely tho began thanke ector eſcaped kynge thoas tho hath faſte raped felde knyghtes manye ſpecyally calydonye came phyloteas myghty kynge alſo agayne troyans haue ado firſte thoas ſpere ran furyouſly caſſybelan one ſones kynge pryamus gaue hym tho wounde ſo greuous without recure fell downe dede whiche ſtroke whan ector gan take hede herte gan deth complayne haſte dyde beſy payne brother auenge hym myght many one made lyght thorugh knyghthode hors bake ſothefaſtly went vnto wrake grekes ſyde came way worthely bare hym day tyll duke neſtor entrede fyght fyue thouſande ſtele armed bryght agayne troyans grekes ſocoure hym mette auenture kynge eſdras ſo myghty ſo bolde kynge phyon chare golde worthy noble chyualrye argeſta came ieconye kynges ſone ſame lande full renowmed worthy hande ſemble togydre ran ſame tyme many worthy man hath loſte lyfe vpon eyther ſyde ſlaughtre large woundes wyde ſoyle bodyes laye dede lyke ryuer ran ſtremys rede theyr cherys gryſely pale fade blode men myght go wade ancle ſlaughtre ſo huge kynge phyon ſocour refuge vnto troyans ſo bare hym ſtryfe many greke made leſe lyfe ſame day ſo well ſwerde whette vnwarely ſo ſore beſette multytude grekes rounde aboute lyfe playnely ſtode doute lykely myght nat eſcape grekes ſhulde anone take ne hadde holpe worthy ieconye eſdras loude gan crye ala quod routhe pyte ¶worthy phyon kynge ſhall take amonge grekes thorugh neclygence haſte ye dylygence reſkewe noble worthy kynge attones without tariynge maugre tho made reſyſtence grekes ſwerde myghty vyolence haue reſkewed noble kynge phyon large goon eſcape wonder gladde lyght ector many luſty knyght retourned dephebus alſo pollydamas many another troyan knyghtes deſyre newe grekes make ſore rewe aſſent fully purpoſe ſuche myſchefe grekes encloſe myght fewe ſhulde eſcape therupon knyghtly ſhape began freſſhely aſſayle felde grekes gan fayle theyr power leſe theyr lande fynally thorugh myghty hande force troianyſſhe knyghtes grekes hadde maugre theyr myghtes brought day confuſyowne menelay kynge thelamowne whan ſawe febly apeyre knyghthode made repeyre ſo lyke men haue themſelf diffendyd tyll eneas troye diſcendyd ewfremus duke manly man theyr knyghtes newe began efte agayne grekes oppreſſe ector aye thorugh worthyneſſe lyke lyon ſterne face euer one ſo gan enchace compellyd neceſſyte echone afore ſwerde fle conſtrayned ryght nede whiche thynge whan ayax gan take hede hadde herte great compaſſyon ſe ſlaughter confuſyon grekes ſyde guydo maketh mynde gan loke backe behynde ſawe many warde ſtode abrode many baner penowne abode amyd felde hole nat broke redy attones wroke nede troye towne whiche wardes without excepcyowne hole floure grekes chyualtye anone ayax gan hym hye ſore herte agreued crye hath ſo cōmeued haſte come reſkuſe amonges refuſe faſte gan aſſemble noyſe hors erthe gan tremble furyouſly togydre flynge myght men ſtrokys rynge ſperys ſharpe thorugh harneys borne thorugh ſheldes wrought ſtele horne breſte ſturdy ſquare brode fynde ayax rode eneas hym alſo great enuye atwyxe two nat deth myght theyr yre apeſe herte nouther myght haue eſe tyll ſperys ſharpe grounde whette hors backe haue togydre mette coupynge ſo ſore haue hytte eueryche erth ſmytte beholde knyghtly ſyght bothe fote fyght lyklyhede theyr wode rage outher falle full great damage amonge horſe becauſe ſtode vpon ſoyle louer ſparde blode phyloteas ayar come hath hym vp amonge horſe ynome knyghtly faught made memorye ſothely ellys troyans victorye hadde felde playnely ſayne tyll phyloteas wardes twayne euen face manly withſtode ſpere firſte ector rode vpon hym ſhafte fynde brake ſothly vpon horſe bake kept hym ſo well felle ſtroke remeuynge nat ſturdy oke sat ſadell vpryght chyne ſpere right lyne body depe thorugh ſhelde phyloteas ſmote felde lyfe knyghtes doute tho came ſo great route bynge humerus vlixes eke brought many worthy greke ten thouſande knyghtes manly men echone gan troyans aſſoyle anone cruelly euery halfe certayne multytude haue ſo layne diſpayred diſconſolate longe fyght awaped mate gan withdrawe faynted batayle eke theyr hors ſothly gan fayle theyr ſyde went vp ſo downe parys tho troye towne entrede full manly wyſe firſte mette kynge fryſe vlixes nye allye parys ſmote ſo great enuye hym ſlewe wherof grekes sore abaſſhed ſpere vlixes de auenge hym myght firſte whan parys hadde ſyght reſte gan ſpere throwe fynally bare lowe faylynge parys ſothly rede vnder hym ſlewe myghty ſtede maugre hym grounde gone hym wolde haue falle anone troylus tho mette hym berde furyouſly ſharpe ſwerde ſmote vlixes thorugh vyſer lyke condyte ſmall ryuer downe face blode ſtremys ran vlixes lyke manly man ſtroke aſtoned nat ſtede ſtyffe wall ſwerde ſo myghtely gan race thorughe vmbrer troylus face hym gaue large mortall wounde whiche ſtroke paſſyngly iocounde grekes ſuppoſyng theyr thought troyans fynally brought vnto traunce ſothely ſo hadde saue ector wt kynghtes whiche ladde hym eke parys dephebus brother knyghthod moſt famous troylus alſo laſte wounde alway ſo noble knyght y• founde attones ioyned one vpon grekes ſodaynely gone worthy ector alder firſte began grekes enchace afore hym ran lyke beſtes fledde fro deth euer one ſwerde ſleth mette durſte ſtroke abyde ſoon freſſhe woundes wyde ſlaughter made alway renewe thylke daye blody roſen hewe hath theyr platy theyr harneyſe ſteyned though hadde blode fro heuen reyned ſoyle redder myght nat ben aye ylyche ſwarme grekes flockmele fledde way guydo ſayth ylke day actor hadde formeſt playne frounter grekes layne behynde knyghtes garde lacke hym warde wherfore whan hadde ſought longe grekes ſawe newe wexe ſtronge knyghtes agayne repayred whiche themſelfe greatly diſpayred abſence tho whan hym ſe full inwardely recomforted glad herte haue lorde receyued theyr gladneſſe whan hath parceyued spake vnto full affectuouſly prayed full benyngnely remembre knyghtly theyr herte conſyder wyſely aduerte firſte wronges grekes haue yore agoo ouermore alſo grekes hadde day victorye farewell aye honour glorye troyan blode concluſiowne fynally eke towne shall mortally turne ruyne honour wont ſhyne thorugh worlde worthyneſſe eclypſe ſhall turne derkeneſſe ye day lyke men quyte wherfore praye man atwyte hye renowne cowardyſe ſette vpon full manly wyſe nat ſpare drede deth praye echone full lowely gan obaye deſyre without lenger tale entrynge certayne vale vpon grekes worthy knyghtes folowynge ector ſodaynely fall full mortally ware ector tho greke wolde ſpare euery theyr confuſyon kylled ſlewe aboute hym enuyron knyghtes rydynge ſyde made theyr • omen maugre theyr pryde leſe theyr londe flewe theyr ſyght tyll kynge whiche toas hyght grekes ſyde warde gan hym dreſſe newe full knyghtly gan oppreſſe troye kynge manly man hadde afore ſlayne caſſybelan one ſones kynge pryamus rode fortune felle thus bretherne fruſſhe mette whiche aſſent enuyron hym ſette ſadell many greke behelde amonge hors ſmethym felde rente firſte baſenet cruelly hadde hede ſmet vnarmed myſchefe ſtode saue duke furyous wode athenys rydynge great pace reſkued hym mortall cace knyghtes aboute hym rode hym helpe without abode aſpere ſharpe whette kene firſte felle quyntylene beſy thoas haue ſlawe bretherne made alſo withdrawe whan quyntylene hors throwe parys tho drewe vp myghty bowe duke lette arowe glyde thorugh plate hyt hym ſyde vpon ryb made hym ſore blede whiche ſtroke ne toke hede bycauſe oonly ſo feruent amyd foon helpe kynge thoas amonge hors bore grounde poynt deth many mortall wounde oonly naked hede duke fully deuoyde drede knyghode pecyllous caas amyd foon hath holpe kynge thoas lyfe made hym ſcape free ector aye cruell enmytee ilyche freſſhe thynge wolde leue vpon grekes manhode preue enforſynge hym theyr deſtruccy wone rode amonge vp downe kynge humerus hath bowe take ſhote gan hym redy make hatefully therin ſette arowe ector marked hath ſo narowe ſmote hym euen amyd face myght fertherpaſe ector ſmet hym ſo great payne wt ſwerde roſe hede wayne deth whan grekes knowe myn auctor ſayth haue horne yblowe vnwarly dredefull ſowne seuen thouſāde knyghtꝭ came attones downe aboute ector without abode force thorugh rode maugre theyr myght hym tho ſette ſlowe tho waye lette ſtynte nat playnely tyll cam fader worthy kynge pryam many worthy full famous renowne knyghtes faſte towne lay daye men hors foote knyghode croppe roote kept hym cloſe full hye prudence tyll ector came vnto preſence hym beſoughte great nede thre thouſande wolde hym ſpede vpon grekes theyr felle rage falle mooſt auauntage haſt worthy pryamus knyghtes freſſhe deſyrous towarde grekes hath waye take ſuche mordre gan vpon make many grekes lay dede playne pryamus ſo ſore hath layne euery halfe thorugh great myght full faſte fledde ſyght ſore newe vpon ſette fynde togydre mette actor ayax auenture theyr ſtedes ſtronge wonder ſure ſtorye ſayth haſte konne lyke wood lyon togydre ronne ſo great myght y• lefe lothe vpon playne vnhorſed bothe whyle menelay kynge sodaynely came rydynge ſlewe troye worthy amyrall thus ſlaughtre paſſyngly mortall benewed aye celydonas neue ſlewe kynge thoas madan met myn auctor wryteth thus grekyſſhe kynge called cedyus whiche wt ſwerde ſuche ſtroke hym ſette thorughe y• vmbrer eye ſmette sardellus troye eke ſame whyle ſlewe worthy greke lorde name hye proweſſe though guydo name nat expreſſe alſo came margaryton troye ſyde agayne thelamon bothe two inly ſette fyre hye diſdayne hatefull yre mette hors backe yfere kynge thelamon ſothly lere gaue vnto hym woundefull cruell tho came troyan phanuell prothenor ſmote downe ſtede thus ſones playnely rede pryamus thynge diſamayde grekes haue euery part outrayed ſo knyghtly daye borne many greke fatally hath lorne lyfe ſothe hate enmyte kynge duglas falle meneſte athenys duke gouernoure aſpere ire olde rancoure ran hym ſmet hym amyd ſhelde ſadell yet helde duke ſpere hadde none ſwerde duglas rode anone thorugh owmbrer rofe nye naſe aſtoned ſtode maſe whan ſawe condyte blode ſtreme rode aſyde fully deuoyde fere vnto tyme ſtaunched deamor owne brother dere whan behelde mortall blody chere hye diſdayne rode meneſte hym vnhorſeth vp anone ſterte myght fully vp aryſe another brother full cruell wyſe falle hym ſo thre attones vpon meneſte fully purpoſe ſhall leſe lyfe ſo knyghtly bare hym ſtryfe agaynſt wonder ſe vpon hym moſte cruell thre one thoras eldeſt echone whiche hym ſlayne beſy euer one broke haue baſenet whan tenter ſawe hym ſo beſet grekyſſhe kynge made mencyon hadde herte great compaſſyon thought playnly manhode hym releue myght foomen greue nought beſy payne ector e • le bothe twayne vpon tenter meneſte hadde ſlayne ne hadde ayaxbe whiche vnto ector faſte gan hym hye thouſande knyghtes companye withſtande hym meneſte ſaue handes myght hym haue parys tho kynge perce fyue thouſande reherce worthy knyghtes many troyan mo vnto ector attones go thryfty wyſe rydynge rowe parys made trumpet blowe whiche came knyghtly enbataylled many troyan full well apparaylled whiche felde ector conueyed one herte fully haue obeyed vnto byddynge troyan knyght freſſhe newe tobegynne fyght vpon grekes ferforth ſlayne many manly man aye ſlaughter pyteouſly reneweth many greke ſore herte reweth theyr great loſſe deſtruccyowne wrought vpon troye towne ſpecially ector fynde whiche day dare maketh mynde hande thouſande knyghtes ſlowe neuer dawed theyr ſowe greke dare none waye dwelle wt ſwerde coude ſo compelle leſe theyr grounde neceſſyte lyke ſhepe afore wolfe fle rede amyd victorye ector mette vnder tentorye amonge grekes meryon kynge ſpake without taryenge thou traytoure thy houre aprocheth faſte thou arte come ſothely thy laſte thy fatall day hath courſe yronne truſte well weſtrynge ſonne caſte platly quyte thy mede wt ſwerde haſte thy blode ſhede thou ſo bolde day lette ryche pray ſpoylynge kynge patroclus cauſe thou preſumptuous diſturbe thou ſhalt anone dede downe ſterte ſmote firſt hede hym ſpoyle alſo gan hym haſte meneſte came hym faſte whan behelde trauerſe backe aſpere whiche lacke smote hym great vyolence without ſyght aduertence worthy ector takynge hede wounde ſore gan blede went made faſte bynde meneſte ſtale away behynde nat purpoſe ſothly may mete ector ylke day whan ybounde ſore wombe ſtaunche blede furyous euer tofore repayred anger tore aye yre herte fret bare downe euer met sleeth kylleth ſo mercyles tho put themſelfe prees hardy hym mete boke lyke wryte darete ſothe ſtorye ſayth ſo men may gyue fayth credence poſſybylyte guydo clerely ye mayſe caughte latter wounde fynally grekes confounde affermyd certayne thouſande knyghtꝭ wt hande ſlayne without tho ſpake rathe newe alway gan ſwerde bathe grekes blode ſodaynely ouerlayne thorugh cruelte greke none hye lowe eſtate ne awhaped amate knyghthode manly excellence none make reſyſtence vtterly durſte take honde daye ector withſtonde made alſo menſyon thylke daye kynge agamenon ſayth guydo came nat felde cauſes great preſence helde grekes ſyde goth vp ſo downe ector ſo playeth lyowne theyr tentes fledde ſocours troye proudely victours sewed trace theyr blode wan treaſoure great gode ſpoyled full great diſtreſſe theyr armure theyr rycheſſe felle ware home troye good bare fynally day myſchaunce grekes hadde brought vnto traunce without recure ſothe euermore euery part layde ſo ſore thorugh manhode ector myght helpe many worthy knyght ſo felly agayne grekes wrought ſuch myſchefe playnly thē brought ne hadde theyr owne pyteous ſlouthe pryde oonly folye routhe hadde theyr volunte day euer hadde ſoueraygnete recured thorugh theyr hye renowne lordſhyppe domynacy owne whiche ſhulde haue laſte contynuell victoryouſly perpetuell haue endured ſaue cruell fate redy aye fortune debate agayne thynges gynne wylfulneſſe make fyne aye wretchedneſſe thorughe theyr enuyous diſpoſicyon ſodayne chaunge reuolucyon vnware tournynge hir falſe whele wyll nat byde whan thynge wele ala frele deuoyde ſykerneſſe cauſe dymmed derkeneſſe hath troyans thorugh falſe oppynyon yblynded ſo theyr diſcrecyon ſpecyally dyrked ſo ſyght worthy ector prudent manly knyght ſe afore ſhulde ſewe good aduyſe myſchefe eſchewe folowed backe behynde ala wylfully made blynde ſame day whan ſete ſofte victorye hylle lofte nat coude neclygence ſe falle theyr felycyte put backe theyr aduertence lacke reaſon hye prudence theyr hap haue voyded theyr grace preſently ſette afore theyr face man nat cōmendable fortune hym fauourable blaundyſſhynge forhede clere ſmyle hym ſpleſaunte chere oonly famour helpe hym oute whan myſchefe beſet aboute refuſe hap wylfulneſſe fortune auoydynge thorugh vnkyndeneſſe whan ſhe mynyſtreth hym hir grace another tyme ſhall hir nat enbrace whan hath nede hir helpe ſocoure hym catche fall rather ingratytude frowardly mowes hym delude whan beſte weneth ſtonde ſykerneſſe fortune aye ſo full brotylneſſe remouable redy flytte hyr welfull houre lyſte nat amytte hir fauour allyed another tyme ſhalbe denyed whan leueſt fynde hir ſauourable ſome houre ſothly nofable vnto ſome man ſhe graunteth deſyres wyll nat thouſande yeres parauenture one condeſcende vnto wyll luſte hym ſende hath falle daye vnhappely worthy ector ſo wyllfully wrought hede grekes ſpare fatally whan ſnare lyke conquerour victorye tryumphe honour myght haue brought thurgh hye renowne palme conqueſt troye towne whiche hath day refuſed folylye rode ector cruellye amonge grekes ſlowe bare downe ca • uelly mette thelamowne mene ayax nye allye hate cruell hote enuye ector rode lyke woode albe hym full nye bloode yet yonge luſty knyght dyde power full myght without faynynge haue borne hym downe whoſe fader hyght alſo thelamowne hym begat ſtorye telleth thus exyon̄ ſuſter pryamus ayax flourynge yonge age freſſhe delyuer great courage sette ector knyghtly hye proweſſe mette bothe theyr woodneſſe theyr ſtedes theſe manly champyownes eueryche lyke tygres lyownes began falle proudely aſſayle furyouſly ſeuere plate mayle firſte ſperes longe large rounde afterwarde ſwerdes kene grounde fyghtynge thus longe contune tyll befylle caſe fortune token ſygne ſome apparence nature kyndely influence whiche hertes doth full depe myne namely borne one lyne whiche cauſe paraunter theſe twanye naturally theyr rancoure reſtrayne theyr yre modefye onely ſo nye allye vnwyſt outher therof vnſure tyll taught oonly nature naturally blode wyll aye kynde drawe vnto blode may fynde whiche made ector kyndely aduerte meuyd ſteryd herte bothe knyghthode gentylleſſe whan ayax ſawe worthyneſſe ¶spake vnto hym full benyngnely ſayde coſyn ſaye trewely thou lyſte grekes forſake come troye dare vndertake thyne allyes thy kynrede thou ſhalte without drede full well receyued partye blode royall sothely deſcended hyeſt degre right ſhall ſuffyſe vnto kyndelye pleaſaunce repayre thyne allyaunce gentyll herte ſythe thynge ſo gode confedryd owne blode conceyue worthyneſſe whiche nature dothe impreſſe troyan blode thou arte deſcended whiche grekes longe hath offended wherfore rede leue vtterly anſwered agayne full humbly ſythen berthe greke youthe amonge foſtryde eke tyme natyuyte taken hadde ordre degre knyghthode eke amonges aforne ouer bounde ſworne trewe theyr nacyon makynge blode none excepcyon ſwore wolde conſerue beheſte ector made requeſte manfull gentylleſſe wolde knyghthode worthyneſſe shewe vnto hym ſo great affeccyowne make troye towne oonly withdrawe grekes purſewe theyr tentes make remewe reſorte agayne vnto towne knyghthode routhe compaſſy owne without aſſayllynge affraye made grekes ylke daye sythe vnto ought inoughe ſuffyſe felde ſo knyghtly wyſe manhode fully poſſeſſours theyr foomen fynally victours lyke tofore fully diffyned whoſe requeſte ector enclyned ala whyle haſty wylfulneſſe made anone without auyſeneſſe mydde felde trumpet blowe wherby troyans fully myght knowe wyll ſhulde withdrawe cuſtome playnely lawe vſaunce bothe nye ferre amonges expert werre whan moſte feruent fyght vpon grekes preue theyr myght hadde chacyd lowe ſtronde weyk power withſtonde troye one deſyre gan ſette ſhotte wylde fyre brenne theyr ſhyppes hye myſchaunce fynally put outtraunce ſo hadde trouthe • e hadde ector vpon routhe makynge troyans repayre towne vngracyouſly theyr confuſyowne ſtorye ſhall ſpecyfye tho putte ala iupardye lyfe deth whiche myght haue ſure whiche agayne neuer ſhall recure ¶how grekes ſent kynge pryamus haue trewes eyght wekes theyr bataylles trewes faylled ca xxiij haue mater complayne ſore fro daye farewell euermore victory laude fro towne denyed diſpoſicyowne mortall fate whiche contrarye mater lyſte lenger tarye troye entred theyr cyte ſhet theyr gate ſurete daye lyke made mynde thus ende euydo fynde wende haue done paraunter beſte whan ſonne ygo reſte toke theyr eaſe ylke nyght tyll morowe tytan clere bryght shadde bemys theyr emyſperye makynge day ſhewe merye whiche tyme troyans anone ryght hole luſty fyght gan arme purpoſe full day theyr foon mete platly may hole theyr wyll playne entent eke hadde cōmaundement tofore ector redy make theyr ſlepe morowe whan wake whiche thynge nat neclygent pryam grekes haue yſent meſſangeres ſame day pryme take trewes oonly tyme eyghte wekes whiche pryamus aſſent ector ſtory telleth thus hath graunted auctoryte wyſeſt cyte whiche tyme whyle leyſer haue grekes gan burye graue bodyes afore ſlawe lyke rytys theyr paynem lawe theyr myght theyr beſy cure ſome brent ſepulture encloſed lyke theyr eſtate thus helde feſte funerall fro day day durynge aye pee whiche ſpace fynde achylles patroclus deth hath ſore playned terys rayned inwardely loued hym herte anguyſſhe cruell ſmerte longe abode lamentacyon dyde make great affeccyon large toumbe remembraunce myd felde tho vſaunce amonge grekes great reuerence lyke honour excellence royall buryenge ſo patroclus ygraue protheſelaus theyr toumbes korue marbyll graye nye togydre playne laye werke aboute rychely ywrought erthe togydre brought solempnely lyke obſeruaunces theyr rytys circumſtaunces grekes vſed ſothely tho dayes fro poynt poynt longeth theyr layes ſuche eſtate royall holden feſte funerall theſe two whyle trewes doth laſte troye beſyed full faſte theyr myght theyr beſy eure theyr grene hurtes woundes cure aduyſe surgerye full well expert ſhape remedye sheyr ſwolle ſores ſofte theyr payne ſpace thyſe monthes twayne reſtored helthe euery thynge whiche tyme pryamus kynge suche ſorowe made caſſybellan herte wyght ne hym recomforte heuyneſſe day day inwarde tenderneſſe full pyteouſly gan ſobbe wepe bodye made kepe aboue erthe certayne ſpace tyll hadde choſen place buryeng ſepulture guydo v fully doth aſſure venus temple ryche ſhryne made workemen toumbe myne marbyll graye metall rychely whiche putte full ſolempnely dede corp caſſybellan beynge preſent full many manly man phane cytherea whiche thynge whan caſſandra within hir ſelfe conſydered behelde ſawe vp offred helme ſhelde ſwerde alſo vnto mar ſtede inwarde woo ſhe felte hir hette blede herynge noyſe pyteous crye tendre wepynge ſorowynge vtterly troye lamentacy owne whiche theyr frendꝭ thrugh al y• towne gan make ſlawe afore ſodayne rage hir herte tore inwardely ſhe myght hir nat reſtrayne furyouſly crye complayne ſayde ala full ofte wellawaye wofull wretch ye daye vnhappy eke graceles alſo infortunat inly woo bego howe ye may ſuffre great harmes kene whiche ye lykely hereafter ſuſtene durynge ſege towne beloke seynge foon redy wroke aboute beſet euery ſyde venged great pryde wote ryght well ye maye nat eſchewe ne ſhall vnto deth purſewe euerychone beſegyd place without mercy pyte grace ala ala ne wyll ye beſy ye wofull wretch ſhet cyte grekes ſeke pee ſwerde vengeaunce mercylees hye lowe execucy owne noble worthy royall towne euerſyd ybrought nought lyſte ye nat conſydre thought modres theyr childreſmale ſtretes ſhall face dede pale lye mordred thorugh grekes cruelte yonge maydens captyuyte wepe ſhall myſerye theyr ſeruytute towne alſo famous ryche ala pyte grekes fyre ſhall deſtroyed ſhorte tyme ſothly • leyne v ala bought dere syth hyr ſake ſhall euerychone pore ryche excepte none ende make wofull pyteous yre ſhalbe ſo furyous vpon v none mene saue oonly deth v go bytwene noyſe pyteous cry caſſandra ſo dredefully gan make aboute euery ſtrete thorugh y• towne euer ſhe myght mete lyke ſhe hadde hir mynde tyll pryamus faſte made hir bynde ſhytte vp routhe nat herde albe ſhe ſayde trouthe neyther wyſedome diſcrecyon counſayle wyt prudence reſon trouthe rede without lye ſpirite trewe prophecye auayleth nat ſuche ſapyence place audyence man inly neuer ſo wyſe counſaylynge hye deuyſe werkynge outher eloquence eche thynge ſe aduertence falle afore reſon amyd eye diſcrecyon yet dole without fauour holden fole vnfauoured wyſedome vayleth nought neyther trouthe dere bought lyke caſſandra hir wyſe rede deſpyſed taken hede troye theyr confuſyon cruelly ythrowen inpryſon whyle wyll leue hir dwelle grekes forth wyll telle firſte pallamydes gan grutche agaynſt y• ches beynge abſent kynge agamenon haue lordſhyp domynacyon namely ſyth nat worthy ſuche dignyte gouerne ſo great myghty ooſt thorugh worlde come euery coſt kynges prynces ſo worthy renowne therof hadde indignacy owne ſayde hymſelfe pouſtee amonge grekes gretter degree concludynge maner weye power ne wolde obeye pea werre ſubieccyon syth ne eleccyon platly affermynge thre whan choſe kynges degre thurty tyme abſent whiche ſwore nat entent accordynge oppynyon wyſe agamenon grekes ſhulde haue ſuche gouernaunce lo myſchefe lyeth varyaunce amonge lordes whan nat accorde drawe fully one corde enuye cauſe ſuche dyuyſyon couetyſe domynacyon eueryche wolde ſurmounte felawe curſed vyſe often hath withdrawe hap grace many regyon whan diſcorde falſe diſcencyon allyed ben hertes ſtryue amonge lordes kyndh •• may nat thryue tyll reformed agayne pee amonge themſelfe playnely lee whiche thynge grekes toke hede thought nat ferther procede matere pallamydes ymeued hadde amonges prees thorugh theyr wyt ſet quyete made hym rancour lete accorde fully herte nowe muſte ſtyle agayne dyuerte vnto werre telle manere trewes mette yfere lyke ſtorye maketh mencyon worthy kynge great agamenon whan trewes paſſyd ygone haſte gan ordayne anone myght waker dylygence deuoyde ſlouthe neclygence ſette wardes full auyſely achylle full prudently firſte warde cōmytteth lede ſeconde vnto dyomede thyrde alſo kynge menelay fourthe ſame day • e hadde meneſtee duke athene ledynge ſtele armed clene wardes folowynge agamanon kynge full manfully ordayned hath ſhall procede werke dede full circumſpect bothe werre pee worthy ector nat reckles ſette wardes towne knyghtly wyſe diſcrecy owne troylus ſo yonge ſo freſſhe lyght firſte warde many luſty knyght hath aſſigned wardes ſet prudently myght bet forth haſte hym lyſte lenger byde many worthy rydynge ſyde gate went towne towarde grekes troyan champyowne firſte whan ſawe fyerſe achylle ne coude lenger kepe hym ſtylle ſinot hors felly ſyde towarde hym cruelly gan ryde whiche thynge deſpytous eye whan achylles ſothly gan eſpye agayne ector manfull hardyneſſe herte enuyous gan ſtede dreſſe felde togydre mette rounde ſperes poyntes kene whette encountrynge knyghtly excellence eueryche thorugh great vyolence force bare vnto grounde full ofte happeth founde whan ſtronge dothe mete perygall eueryche fall ector firſte ſtrengthe moſte aſſured ſtede agayne hath anone recured lefte achylle tho gentylleſſe great haſte forth gan hym dreſſe amonge grekes ſo rode kylled ſlewe hym withſtode wt ſwerde made theyr woūdes wyde thorugh breſt ſome thorugh ſyde percy • hath waged foreuer brake ſheltroūs made diſſeuer herte hym thought dydehȳ gode bathe ſwerde grekes blode contynued tyll achylles caughte ſtede agayne amonge prees entrede amonges troye ſwerde made large weye sleeth bare downe y• euer mette none hardy hym lette tyll befell melancoly • ctor mette rydynge ſodaynely whan ſawe eche come fere without abode eueryche caught ſpere ran togydre areſte ector firſte ſmette hym breſte ſpere playnely tale ſhyuered peces ſmale achylles neceſſyte grounde goth wolde none vnhorſed erthe lay ector haſte may enforced hym catche ſtede many greke great nede came reſkues achylles loue put themſelfe prees thrugh help hors doth atta • e enhaſtynge hym myght payne auenged great miurye ſodaynely woode furye ſwerde ful ſharpe grounde whette ſmote ector vpon baſenet ſadell made hym remewe whiche ſtroke myght nat eſchewe noble worthy knyght force thorugh great myght maugre foon ſadell hath recured manhode moſte aſſured ſodaynely herte wexed ſo wrothe arage achylles gothe ſwerde ſo ſmet hym hede thorugh baſenet blode rede face gan ronne downe lyke ryuer chekes enuyrowne hymſelfe diffendeth knyght tho newe began cruell fyght wene two ſe wonder euery ſtroke great dent thonder range eyre none wolde ſpare ſothe theyr fyght fare lyke woode tygres bore theyr rage ſterne bulles whan ſauage ſempte ſothfaſtneſſe theſe two ſo full worthyneſſe contune longe fyghtynge endure tone bothe cruell aduenture muſte haue dede neceſſyte whiche thynge hadde pyte bycauſe worthy knyghtes bothe whyle fyghtyng fell wrothe moſte beſy grekes begynne theyr wardes entre inne troye ſtorye maketh mynde theyr party lefte nat behynde felde enhaſte euerychone knyghtly wyſe mete theyr fone preaſe alſo yonder knyghtes two ſeueryd ſonder tho came ſterne dyomede knyghtes whiche dyde lede full luſtely ſelue place hath mette proudely face whorthy troylus hors backe neuer hadde yet manhode lacke countre ſtorye dothe v lere eueryche vnhorſed knyghtly hath fere firſte hors recureth dyomede haſte gan hym ſpede aſſayle troylus ſtondynge vpon foote whan ſawe none bote knyghtly yet euer dyde man agaynſt hym diffende hym tho began dyomede hote fyre wonder enuyous hatefull deſyre ſwerde rancour none ryche cercle full ynde ſtones tyme troylus baſenet full cruelly hath racyd ſmet troylus ne wolde yt hym wtdrawe hym diffendynge hath ſtede ſlawe whiche ſat tyme dyomede maugre hym muſte alyght nede whan fote bothe twayne dyd theyr myght theyr cruell payne eueryche aſſayle ſwerdes ſharpe ſo plate mayle gan ſeuere ſonder race woode lyon mortall chere face tyll grekes ſtronge ſtoute felle myn auctour boke telle haue thorugh theyr myght made dyomede sodaynely recure ſtede troyan knyghtes tother ſyde haue troylus brought ſtede ryde whan horſed bothe two without agayne togydre go ſtronge foynes yfere ran eche felly tyll laſte cruell dyomede lyke ye may myn auctour rede caſe hap aduenture whiche man fully may aſſure fortune hir falſe vyſage hadde tyme troylus vauntage hym falle myſcheſe whiche thynge hym reprefe though hym toke amonge ſo great aroute euery halfe grekes ſet aboute syth doutous euer fyne fyght vp downe derk bryght wyght may aye victoryous pea werre ylyche eurous let euery man ſyth hap ſette doute take tourne cōmeth aboute though troylus take dyomede another tyme ſhall hym quyte mede ſtorye telleth place dyomede lytell ſpace troylus ladde forth pryſonere reſkewes ſtele armed clere many troyan came pryckynge nede maugre myght dyomede troylus haue handes take tho began ſlaughter ſake euery halfe wonder telle troyans grekes felle felde entrede menelay whiche troyans ylke day full beſy auenged hadde ſo cruell enmyte whan parys ſawe hym felde towardes hym right waye helde purpoſe theyr wardes ſette eche tyll togydre mette tho ſkarmyſſhe ſlaughter gan outher parte many manly man whyle ector ne wolde ceaſe amonge grekes cruelly preaſe new new hym rede lyke freſſhe blode ſhede ſwerde trace yſene grekes myght nat ſuſtene reſyſte ſtande afore face rode aye gaue hym place ¶tyll aknyght whiche boetes hyght yonge age whan hadde ſyght ector ſlewe grekes mortally euery ſyde hauynge mercy preſyd encreaſe name perpetuelly purchace hym fame furyouſly herte nat afferde caſte hym platly mete hym berde whiche thynge whan ector gan aduerte hye raucour enbracyd hath herte ſwerde indignacyowne rofe hym euen nauell downe fro crowne ſo great payne felde partyd lay twayne ector tho aſſygned hath ſtede ſquyer bad ſhulde lede troye towne without abode whyle furyouſly rode amonge grekes euer mercylees ſlewe put ſelfe prees ſhadde theyr blode herte deſpytous whiche thynge whan kynge archylogus rydynge beſyde ſawe gan eſpye boetes coſyn allye cruelly ector ſlawe towardes hym haſte gan hym drawe vpon deth auenged tode hym great cruelte fully purpoſe ector quyte ſodaynely gan hym ſmyte ector vnwarely hyt hym hede myghtely felle downe dede partyd two cruell aduenture natwithſtādyng myghty ſtronge armure agayne ſtroke diffence gyuen ſuche vyolence holpe hym maner thynge anone prochenor kynge hatefull yre foole hardyneſſe ſurquedye haſtyneſſe melancolye indignacyon caught herte preſumpcyon aſſayle ector inwarde foly pryde goth hym trauerſe ſyde furyouſly deſpytous herte cōmynge myght nat aduerte oonly came backe behynde vnwarely guydo fynde ector ſmote hors grounde ſo moch manhode foūde anone knyghtly herte without abode ſadell ſterte right fyerſly prothen purſeweth fynally honde nat eſcheweth ſwerde marked hym ſo wele thorugh baſenet breſte ſtele twayne withoute fayle roofe hym downe paunce mayle felle downe full pyteous wyſe whiche ſtroke grekes ſore agryſe ſpecyally hardy fyerſe achylle whan behelde lyked full ylle phothenor nye coſyne deſcendyd ſame lyne deth hath ſuche heuyneſſe inwarde thought ſo great diſtreſſe worlde ne wyſte hym ſo moche payne wo deth archylogus auenge full deſyrous herte many waye caſte wardes gan ſeke faſte many greke ector haue falle conſpyred fully ſoth amonge alle one entent ector aſſayle nought wolde nat auayle day ſo cruell rage myght hym haue none auauntage troyan knyghtes fauour fortune vpon grekes ſo myghtely contune thorugh conueyinge ector myght anone haue put flyght theyr tentes maugre ſtryue purſuyte woūded dryue laye aſwowe many greke mercyles ſlowe longe day tyll drewe nyght ſothly lacke lyght theſe troyan knyghtꝭ full worthy renowne aboute ector repayre towne entre honour glorye day grekes hauynge victorye thus leue theyr towne within forth grekes telle wyll begyn whan eſperus fayre bryght ſterre agaynſt eue caſte ſtremys ferre weſt ratheſt gan appere whan twylyght pale chere maner morneth abſence ſonne nyght approcheth copy donne ſame tyme whan tytan toke leue clerkes calle crepuſculum eue whiche nat ellys meane lyght phebus abſence derke nyght twylyght hatte mene daye nyght departynge betwene fully nouther bothe meynt heuen cluſtred depeynt bryght ſterrys euenynge whiche tyme agamenon kynge lordes ſodaynely hath ſent come echone anone tent whan aſſembled yfere tryſt heuy ſorefull chere gan y• ſlaughter ector complayne affermyng playnly myght neuer attayne vnto victorye whyle lyue wherfore gan conſpyre blyue deth hym many ſondry weye echone concludynge whyle troye nat lykely grekes wynne alone withinne chefe diffence proteccy owne ſoueraynely vpholder towne theyr myghty caſtell theyr ſtronge wall vnto grekes dedely foo mortall ne myght great force endure neuer right agayne theyr foos ſure ſtandynge hole ſayde degre whyle floureth felycyte wherfore echone one entencyon condeſcende concluſyon ſome ſleyghte awayte lymge whan moſte beſy fyghtynge amonge myſchefe diſtreſſe achylles beſyneſſe myght vnwarely hym aſſayle hym ſlee thynge fayle grekes gan theyr prayer make achylles vndertake empreſſe fynally ſute thorugh manhode execute haſty deth theyr mortall foo achylles without wordes moo theyr requeſt aſſenteth parfourme theyr luſte gan hooly hym confourme tyme let hym beware rede haſty iourne ſpede vpon ector power kythe lyſte fortune wronge hir face wrythe loke hym frowarde chere hym brynge vnto handes nere thorugh ſorte hap ector folylye put lyfe deth ieopartye lyſte vnto hym happe euen lyche falle hymſefe ſame dyche ector compaſſed hath ſhape wonder eſcape syth ector hadde without drede brennynge yre great hatrede achylles deth puruey hym founde place ſey conuenyent execucyon trowe ſhulde hym gayne raunſon mede herte quyete onely deth whan ſo mete ende fyne matere boke ye ſhall thus grekes made haue ende theyr counſayle one wende eueryche home theyr lodgynge toke theyr reſte tyll morenynge ¶howe troyans toke kynge thoas pryſoner ledde hym troye ca xxiiij whan aurora wt ſyluer droppes ſhene hitterys ſhadde vpon y• freſſhe grene cōplaynȳge ay wepyng ſorowe hir childrens deth euery ſomer morowe ſaye whan dewe ſo ſoote enbawmed hath floure eke roote luſty lycoure apryll may whan larke meſſager day cuſtome aye aurora doth ſalue ſondry note hir ſorowe tranſmue phebus ryſe ioye gladneſſe thorugh armonye leue hir heuyneſſe takynge hir leue ſeynt iohn̄ borowe ſame tyme grekes morowe luſty herte erely dyde aryſe armed theyr beſte wyſe caſte daye goon felde mete theyr foon ector hath ſame morowe alſo caſte hym fully grekes haue ado yſſued knyghtly troye herte hath ſo great deſyre ioye ſame day grekes fyght hym ladde many luſty knyght ſuche cyte borne forth rode hymſelfe aforne eneas many worthy folowed wonder faſte parys next hym dephebus ſythe troylus couragyous wardes made troye towne wiche dare maketh mencyowne within boke troye ſyde fyghtynge men went dyde ryde hondred thouſande armed go felde fyfty thouſande mo whiche haue caſte day eue one entent grekes greue ſo mette ſtrongly outher ſyde gan aſſemble togydre ryde full cruelly great hatrede tho parys dyde lede entrede full myghty ſtronge archeres perce londe many arbalaſteres wt theyr arrowes fyled ſharpe rounde quarelles ſquare whette
