grounde full many greke hath reuyd lyfe amyddes mortall ſtryfe agamenon felde come towardes ector hath ynome right way threwe hym ſtede amonge knyghtes dyde lede ſpared nought great prees therwithall anone came achylles awayte ector hadde layne ſodaynely myght payne ¶ector ſmote hede ſo ſore wt ye ſtroke myn auctour ſayth baſenet bowed ycraſed whiche ſtroke ector nat amaſed achylles ſhulde anone yfalle ne hadde eneas knynghtes alle worthy troylous come go betwene whiche twayne ſwerdes kene gan achylles felly aſſayle hewe plate perce mayle tho began ſlaughter euery ſyde men foote ryde lyke condyte woundes gan blede whyle cruell dyomede hap aduenture caas rode hath mette eneas right anone hadde hym founde ſmet hym gaue hym ſuch wounde lykely ſhulde nat recure therto better cure therupon full deſpyteouſly dyomede melancoly repreuyd hath troyan knyght enee ſayd hym heyle thou art whylom gaue pryamus kynge felle counſayle haſty bytynge ſlayne ſodayne vyolence whan laſte troye preſence truſte well haue wel mynde amyd felde efte fynde thou ſhalt thy counſayle mortally repente fortune wyll aſſente brynge right vnto hande good leyſer thyne owne lande full ſette thy labour quyte trouth ſwerde ſhal kerue byte kenely thy troyan blode ſhede fynally deth ſhalbe thy mede bere atwene handes twayne wt worde myght hȳ nat reſtrayne dyomede rode ſodaynely vpon enee ſo furyouſly ſmote hym hardy cruell knyght ſuche payne ſo great myght hors made hym falle maugre myght knyghtes alle whiche ſtroke lyked full ylle whyle ector hath achylle aſſayled ſo thorugh baſenet perced hath ſwerde hym ſmet ſo narowe brought hym poynt hye myſchefe ſuch diſioynt conſtrayned hym neceſſyte hadde hym take ne oonly sodayne reſkues chyualrous called ſone tydeus meane felle fyerſe dyomede whiche achylles hath holpen nede thorugh force armes twayne smote ector tho ſo great payne hym gaue wounde full greuous thȳge myn auctour wryteth thus aſtoned knyght manly man ſwerd haſte smote dyomede ſo furyous wrothe hors erth gothe pryde ſurquedrye whiche anone troylous dyde eſpye without abode downe ſtede lyght dyomede fote fyghte eche ſothfaſtneſſe aquyte hymſelfe lyke manly man nouther moche lyte degree manhode wyte whyle faught ector achylles togydre mette agayne amonge prees ran yfere fyerſly theyr rage woode lyon whan ramage right ſo ſothe fared theyr fyghtyng tyme menelay kyng full proudely ſhope hym troyans mete vlixes eke alſo polymete hym came neptolonyus pallamydes eke scelemus duke meneſtee neſtor thoas currynulus phylotheas aud theſeus made mynde knyghtes proudely came behynde partye towne came kynges without excepcyowne aſſembled theyr diffence agayne grekes make reſyſtence except knyghtes whiche ector ladde wardes made hadde ſame daye ſayth latyn boke knyghtly wyſe felde whan yt toke tho began felle mortall fyght whiche day ful many worthy knyght fatyshondes fynally falle fortune amonge wardes alle agamenon noble myghty kynge ſodaynely came rydynge pantyſylaus waye mette agaynſt anone hors ſette hym full knyghtly rode agayne mette ſayne horsbacke whyles wrothe vyolence vnhorſed bothe menelay parys mette newe whiche two well togydre knewe full deſyrous eche dere menelay caught firſte ſpere hytte parys inwarde cure ſureneſſe ſtronge armure myghty platꝭ wounde ſmall whiche effect greued nat ſtroke vnto grounde gothe whiche fall parys wexed right wrothe wonder confuſe alſo rede ſhame leſt reporte hyndrynge name came erys quene eleyne daye myght nat atteyne menely holde chaumpartye lykely ſowne vylonye whiche herte greued hym full ſore adraſtus kynge without rode kynge vlixes fonde knyghtly foughte honde honde faughte downe erthe lowe hors vlixes hath hym throwe full proudely ſigne victorye ſent hors home tentorye tyme amonges prees full ſodaynely kynge pallamydes falle hupon locke hore ire wounded hym ſo ſore felle dede grouelyng ye groūde mortall ſwerde ſo kene grounde beſyde neptolonyus aſſayled hath kynge archylogus whiche hymſelfe manly gan diffende faught many ſtrokes ſpende diffence wolde none eueryche hath vnhorſed tho came rydynge ſtede pollydamas gan take hede amonge renges lytell hym beſyde kynge pallamydes doth ryde cruelly ſo lyke manly man ſmote ſtede hym ran maugre myght worthyneſſe ſtorye playnely bereth wytneſſe oonly venge deth kynge hupowne ſtede proudely bare hym downe rancoure cruell hete deſpyte gan hym rehete tho beſyde kynge scelenus dedely hate herte full irous kynge carras aduenture hath met furyouſly ſtede ſmet alſo kynge phylymene duke falle athene maugre manhod myght hath hors berafte hym fyght ladde hym proudely ſyde hym lyſte ſhulde abyde phyloteas worthy kynge alſo ſelue tyme remus ado euery ſothly rede felawe hath made voyde ſtede theſeus kynge yt ſo ſtronge amyd felde ſo rode amonge great preſe hath met curyalus worthy kȳg knyghthod right famous bothe two armes wonder ſtronge themſelfe faught leyſer longe tyll eche woundes freſſhe grene fro horſbak felawe threwe endlōg ye grene afterwarde fynde two vpon foote knyghtly hadde ado armes ſomly deſyrous manhode paſſyngly famous whyle ſones naturell pryamus bare wonder well amonge grekes vp downe rydynge prudently togydre abydynge made ſlaughter grekes full pytous kynges duke lordes right famous rede worthy thelamowne tyme met kynge sapedowne theyr ſperes ſquared full ſharpely eueryche hath wounded mortally thorugh ſhelde plate haberion mayle ſtorye maketh reherſayle theyr harneys wexed blode rede fylle almoſte bothe dede great myſchefe amonge hors foot whoſe bledynge ſoyle gan wexe weet thorugh theyr harneys diſtylle whyles kynge thoas fyerſe achylle kynne allyed amyd felde ector haue eſpyed faught beſet amyd foon vpon hym one accorde goon mortally wolde auayle euery halfe gan hym newe aſſayle hate herte borne yore haue beſet troyan knyght ſo ſore ala hede hath ſmet vyolence ryche baſenet wounded hym felly hede ne toke hede worthy man floure chyualrye hym diffendynge tho ſo myghtely kynge thoas ſmet hym face ſo ſtroke rafte noſe two ſhorted halfe dele whiche ſtroke brother naturele manly ector faſte gan hye ſocoure hym whan firſte eſpye great myſchefe theyr cōmynge ſo manly bare fyghtynge agayne grekes thoas haue take • amon ſo made awake newe aſſaute ſharpe woundes kene take lefte vpon grene men borne home tent kynge thoas home troye went maugre grekes whiche helpe hȳ may dephebus alſo anthenore haue ſente hym forth troye cyte menelay tho began ſe rode parys ſtonde ſyde ſhope hym ſhortly hate cruell pryde wolde falle chaunce sodaynely ymen hym myſchaunce ware kept hymſelfe ſo narowe menelay marked arowe hede whiche wt venym enoynt intoxycate ſquare poynt kynge dredefull wounde diſpayred men founde whiche great haſte bare hym tent anone surgyens hath ſent whiche firſte hede toke wounde albe yperced full profounde thorugh harneys full depe bone cunnyngely dyde theyr crafte echone drawe theyr inſtrumentes ſubtylly certayne oyntementes ſerched haue wounde enuyron make clene corrupcyon prudently firſte toke hede venym nat procede rounde compaſſe clenſyd aboute bounde ſure withoute defenſyues made euery ſyde menelay lenger wolde abyde bad haſte brynge forth ſtede purpoſe full parys quyte mede hym fynde ſelfe ſame daye hym lyſte lenger put delaye euer falle grene wounde forth rode tyll hath hym founde aduenture vnarmed felde without ſwerde pollex ſpere ſhelde bowe honde rekleſneſſe refreſſhe hym weryneſſe menelay anone ſpere hath take yre • elly gan ſhake towarde parys great auyſeneſſe ſhulde haue ſlayne hym lyklyneſſe ne eneas whiche thynge behelde bore ſtocke ſtronge ſhelde diffende hym auenture deſtytute naked armure parys tyme ſuche peryll wherfore haſte hath eneas ordayned knyghtes armed bryght ſtele aboute parys kepe hym wele myſchefe confuſyowne hym conuey vnto troye towne right deſpyte kynge menelay whiche awayte ſo parys lay ¶whom ector hadde ytaken ſodaynely vnto troye ladde hym vtterly ne hadde grekes come diffence agaynſt hym make reſyſtence whiche ector came weye full many greke made deye remenaunt put vnto flyghte thorugh māhod y• day myghte troyans made grekes flee vnto theyr tentes neceſſytee ſewe ne wolde neuer leue ſlee kyll tyll drewe eue phebus gan faſte weſte drawe home thought ye beſte tytan goynge downe whan gan entre troye towne theyr gatꝭ ſhet theyr lodgynge wende day thus made ende tyll morowe rowes rede phebus carte gonne ſprede afore vpryſte oryent whiche tyme kynge pryamus hath ſent ſuche hym moſte pryue counſayle inwardely ſecre ſpecially ſent name worthy ector gretteſt fame parys eke dephebus troylus freſſhe deſyrous anthenor pollydamas troyan called eneas daye caſte hym nat goon felde mete foon whan paleys come theſe lordes haue right waye nome vnto kynge within cloſet whan huſſher hath dore ſhet eueryche hadde lyke degree place take dewe ſee worthy kynge made mencyon gan declare hertes mocyon menynge afore ſpecifye ſayde ſyres moſte affye knowen kynge thoas cyte taken pryſonere yet belocked pryſowne whiche euer hath vnto troye towne enemy great vnto power v offendyd bothe ferre ner many wyſe lytell retche ferre force myght ſtretche grekꝭ came ſege towne wyll deſtruccyowne therupon hath beſyneſſe wherfore dome rightwyſneſſe reaſon equyte ſaye playnely ſemeth vnto acceptable ye thynke coūſayle cōmendable lyke hath caſte deth ſhape holde rightfull nat eſcape deth receyue guerdon right requereth alſo good reaſon deth deth ſkylfull guerdonnynge vnto wytte right well ſyttynge saye aduyſe playnely caas firſte tho ſpake eneas ſayde lorde ſo none offence hyghneſſe gyue audyence thorugh ſupporte yt full wyſe ſhall reherce playnely deuyſe werke matere ſemeth firſte lyege lorde ſo dere noble royall excellence conſydre ſhulde full hye prudence euery werke operaſyon caſte afore concluſyon caſte afore concluſyon fynall ende may ſewe wyſe man oonly nat dewe ſe gynnynge ende nought bothe attones peyſe thought weye • iuſtly balaunce fyne folowe repentaunce ſay platly mene ye ought ſene kynge thoas one pryncypall amonge grekes blode royall ye conſydre deſcended lyne wherfore haue foule fyne ſlayne whyle pryſon myght happen concluſyon ye youres therto aſſente afterwarde ſore repente preue thus aduenture fortune man may aſſure lordes nother day grekes take happe may ſones ſo worthy renowne kynges towne truſte well ſuche gentylleſſe ye ſhewe theyr diſtreſſe wyl quyte whan caſe ſemblable fortune fynde fauourable whiche man cōſtrayne may bynde wherfore lorde haue thyng mynde thoas ſhorte auyſement shall deed thorugh haſty iugement another day grekes wyll v quyte rygour make theyr malys byte ſome youres euer nouther ſpare hye lowe degre though paraunter blode whiche thynge worldes gode myght falle ye ne wolde ſe wherfore rede let kynge thoas honeſtely kepe pryſowne lyke eſtate ſtylle towne lyſte ſayde another day lorde youres happe may caſuelly take auenture eſchaunge hym ye myght beſte recure without ſtryfe youre owne man agayne mater ſayne fynally full rede whiche counſayle ector toke good hede accordynge reaſon cōmendeth oppynyon pryam euer one entencyon stode alway fyx concluſyon playnely affermynge grekes may eſpye kynge ſpare gentrye wyll arrecte cowardyſe anone dare nat venge v foone drede hauynge hardyneſſe herte nouther rightwyſeneſſe yet neuertheleſſe aſſent ſhall lyue wyll myn entent deſyre fully condeſcende counſayle ſo made ende without ſaue eneas go trylous eke anthenor alſo halle excellynge beaute quene eleyne purpoſe ſe eke eccuba quene ladyes goodly ſene many mayde yonge luſty worthy troylus eneas dyde theyr laboure theyr beſy payne comforte fayre quene eleyne ſhe ſtode werre drede womanhede thylke tyme hir herte entere ſhe well coude make good chere hauynge connynge inly ſuffyſaunce bothe chere dalyaunce eccuba beynge halle example vnto woman alle bounte hauynge ſoueraygne excellencce wyſedome eke eloquence beſought tho wonder womanly counſayled eke full prudently haſte bothe nye ferre auyſely kepe werre nat iuparte theyr bodyes folylye aduerte caſte prudently diffence knyghtly towne gouerne diſcrecyowne ſpake fayth coude thynge feyne hir eleyne toke leue lenger dwelle went theyr way forth wyll telle grekes ſame morowe amonge ſelfe complayne make ſorowe theyr harmes great murmur rage loſſe coſtes great damage haue enduryd folylye laſtynge werre wyſte neuer whye deth ſlaughtre many worthy man syth tyme werre began hunger thurſte watche colde alſo full great vnreſte ſorowe thought wo togydre thynge nought ſothfaſtneſſe grounde ſought noyſe rumour eke ran thorugh hooſt yt day fro man man moſte amonge pore ſouldy oures whiche bare bronte euer ſuche ſhoures myſchefe werre comenlye though playne haue remedy thynges whiche ſytte full vnſofte thus grekes complayned haue full ofte many myſchefe hath falle whiche myght haue eſchewed alle ne hadde foly gonne werre grece nat come halfe ſo ferre theyr myſchefe confuſyon daye lamentacyon ¶whiche encreaſe ſame next nyght derked without ſterre lyght cloudy blacke ſo thycke ayre dymmyd ſkyes foule thynge fayre wyndy eke tempeſt layne almoſte fordrenchyd ſmoky rayne felde aſtoned yonder ſodayne ſtroke dredefull thonder openynge hydous leuene ſempte hye heuene cataractys hadde vndo cloudes ſkyes bothe two sodaynely wexen ſo blake lyke goddes wolde haue taken wrake hadde newe aſſentyd oon lande drenche deucalyon worlde without refuge ouerflowe freſſhe deluge wynde alſo ſo ſternely gan blowe theyr tentes ſtondynge rowe poſſyd ybete downe furyouſly theyr confuſyowne floodꝭ raughte thē fro theyr ſtādyng place bare forth full large ſpace wherof myſchefe great diſtreſſe great laboure hertely heuyneſſe grekes bydde ſame nyght tempeſt lacke lyght tyll floode gan agayne withdrawe wynde appeſe day gan dawe heuen gan agayne clere without cloudes freſſhely appere phebus eke feruent hete hadde ſoyle dryed vp wete moyſture enuyrowne playne grekes hadde theyr tentes ſet agayne adawed theyr nyghtes ſorowe thorugh aperynge galde morowe arrayed nothynge pee felde firſte went achylles ye ſhall entencyowne day fyght wt troye towne whan dryed luſty large playne wt phebꝰ bemys ye haue herd ſaȳe troyan knyghtes full worthy renowne deſcendyd ycome downe felde toke theyr fyghtynge place achylles mete face tofore went lyke tolde lordes knyghtes bolde firſte fynde without abode vnto hupon furyouſly rode mene hupon ſtature lyke geaunt bokes v aſſure achylles ſharpe ſpere thorugh body percyd hym ſo fere fylle dede wounde ſo kene kynge octamene fyerſly ector wolde haue gone without abode ector hym ſiewe anone cruelly quytte hym fatall mede ſodaynely agaynſt dyomede zantipus worthy kynge gan drawe full pyteouſly hym ſlawe right anone kynge epyſcrophus eke kynge hyght cedyus one aſſent proudely batayle begonne ector mortally aſſayle ſpere firſte epyſcrophus ran hym herte deſpytous guydo alſo doth deuyſe rebukyd hym vngoodly wyſe hym ſo ſore herte meued wherof ector furyouſly agreued hath mortally wounde made ſo large hym ne geyneth plate ſhelde targe fyll dede amonge men echone ector bad ſhulde gone furyes depe downe helle suche wordes amonges telle quod men take hede thus whan waged mede anone brother called cedyus suche ſorowe made epyſcrophus hertely dole ſo wofull chere pyte ſe inwardly deth thought thouſande knyghtꝭ yt brought auenged manhode alle deſpyteouſly ertor falle hym founde fyghtynge wt foon thorugh force euerychoon ſore enuyrowne haue hym beſet ſtede downe haue hȳ ſmet ¶whom cedyus aye cruell rage whan ſawe auauntage ector vnhorſed ſtede ſwerde lefte inwardely hatrede markynge hym ſo great payne force armes twayne fully purpoſe without delay ſlee ector playnely may ſtroke deſcende myght downe ector hate indignacyowne ſwerde full ſharpe whet ſhuldre hath arme ſmet reuyd hym lyfe eneas amyddes ſtryfe came rydynge woode furyous mette kynge amphymacus fell hym ſlewe hym rage grekes holdynge theyr paſſage came downe firſte menelaus hym kynge thelamonyus great duke alſo athene ſo moche manhode ſene vlixes eke cruell dyomede eke alſo helpe theyr nede came kynge machaon alderlaſte great agamenon theyr wardes fyll ſodaynly vpon troyans full manfully diffende ſelfe agayne grekes proude put full knyghtly coude eche ſothly mette ſpere ſwerde enuyouſly ſette mortall hate betwene whan ſonne merydyen myd day angell paſſynge hote ſhene grekes gan felly theyr tene myghtely falle troye made gyue weye force neceſſyte achylles ſo full cruelte amonge renges gan hym drawe kynge phylem enuyouſly hath ſlawe amyd grekes ſame tyme ector maugre ſlewe kynge alphenor eke kynge called dorous ſo cruell yrous thorugh vertue knyghtly honde troyans haue wonne agayne theyr londe vpon grekes made flee thylke houre torye cytee epyſcrophus full manlyneſſe felde hath take thorugh worthyneſſe grekes proudely none knyghtes falleth attones ſeuered made twynne gan felde faſte vpon wynne hauynge tyme companye amonges dyde guye acertayne archer whiche fynde monſtruous wonderfull kynde myddell vp vnto crowne man remenaunt downe bare horſe lykneſſe fygure horſes heer monſtre nature hadde ſkyn growynge enuyrowne full rough thycke voyce ye ſowne lyke neyhynge horſe rede though face lengthe brede ſhape mannyſſhe yet ſuthfaſtneſſe coloure ſemblable lykneſſe vnto fery hoote breynnynge glede whoſe eyen eke flawmynge alſo rede blaſe ouen mouthe ſyghte ſo vnkouthe ſo euer met berde bothe man hors ſore ferde face ſo hatefull ſo odyble loke ſo hydous horryble aye hadde cuſtome vſaunce bokes made remembraunce go vnarmed felde without ſwerde ſpere axe ſhelde thynge coude myſter fynde good archer bare bowe ſtyffe wonder ſtronge alſo tyller longe arrowes lyke tyller buſſhement truſſed wonder ner ſyde aye redy hande ſo outher ſee lande fynde none armure agayne ſhot playnely myght endure hors ſtede courſer durſte abyde nouther fer ner fledde anone theyr full myght faſte hym hadde ſyght ſo paſſynge odyous lyke deuyll ſo monſtruous foūde none ſo hardy knyght hors backe hadde force myght holde hors whan myght hym ſe anone backe wolde fle archer fynde wryten eke day ſlewe full many greke wounded arrowes kene thorugh ye plate forged bryght ſhene none afore hym abode theyr tentes faſte awaye rode myght nat hydous loke endure tyll befell wonder aduerture whyle troye helpe archer sewe chaſe theyr lodgynge ner ſlewe myſchefe drede beſyde tent mette dyomede archer neceſſyte ſtode ſo ne myght hym fle maner way backe remewe lyfe deth myght hym nat eſchewe many troyan tho backe flyinge hadde go wracke ¶wherfore anone worthy dyomede cruell herte faſte gan hym ſpede towarde hym proudely dreſſe archer great aduyſeneſſe firſte arrowe ſmette dyomede thorugh harneys made hym blede whiche ſtroke wexed ſo wood wrothe monſtre ſo hydous ſo lothe went paſe hym vnarmed fonde ye ſwerde helde honde gaue hym laſte fatall wounde fylle dede grouelynge vnto ye grounde deth grekes reioyſynge haſte theyr hertes reſumynge began ſelfe recomforte felde proudely reſorte conueyinge polixenare worthy duke ſo well hym bare vpon troyans day felde whan ector ſlaughtre hym behelde vpon duke anone gan ſette theyr ſtedes fyerſly mette ector hym ſlewe full great hatrede gallathe ſtede rode forth amonge prees ware mette achylles theyr ſperes longe large rounde purpoſe fully eche confounde ran yfere irous right wrothe ye ſtroke vnhorſed bothe achylles wth deſpytous herte firſte rede ſadell ſterte beſy inwarde peyne gallathe take reyne therof euer ector depryue bad men lede home blyue ector none bote full lyke man faught ſtondynge fote amonge grekes fomen alle knyghtes loude gan calle ſtede ſhulde ſewe haſte hors reſkewe ben attones fallen achylle maugre hym force agayne wylle haue hym berafte playne ector reſtored agayne knyghthode ſomoche hȳ ſelf aſſureth deſpyte ſadell recureth whiche afterwarde full dere aboughte lyke lyon day wroughte amonges rydynge deth fled ſwerde fere thorugh whoſe manhode troyans eft begyn vpon grekes felde agayne wyn befell amyd theyr great fyght anthenor certayne troyan knyght amonge preſe ſo fer gone grekes take anone theyr tentes ſent haſte albe ſone called pollydamas reſkue hym dyde dylygence manfully neclygence founde hym ſo lyſte ſeke full dere boughte many greke ſame day thorugh worthyneſſe cauſe oonly derkeneſſe gan drawe towarde nyght made ende oonly lacke lyght grekes went home theyr lodgynge eke troyans tyll mornynge phebus gan bryght bemys ſhewe aurora newe gan dewe erbys ſote grene leuys hayes freſſhe greuys syluer bryght rounde perlys fyne ſo clerely agayne ſonne ſhyne ſhewe ſelfe ſo oryent ſhene hylle vale euery grene rody morowe tyll hote bemys bryght phebus fyrye ſtemys vapoureth vp theyr moyſture ayre weder clere agreable fayre attempre alſo heete whan troyans caſte mete theyr fomen platly may went theyr beſte array theyr wardes felde rowe agaynſt grekes nat ſlowe ſhope forth without lenger lette tyll togydre manfully haue mette theyr ſperes theyr ſwerdes clere ran togydre deſpytous chere tyll ſhyuered ſondre many ſpere ſheldes ſtronge ſelfe ryuen pecys many targe hexys rounde brode large baſenettes ſmyte ſhrede full many knyght mortally gan blede ſothfaſtneſſe tell ſame day ſlayne many man outher parte moſt troye towne albe guydo maketh mencyowne perſone ſpecyall nouther ſyde generall saue concludeth playnely fyght laſte fro morowe tyll nyght whiche troyans haue full dere bought day fortune holpe nought tourned hole theyr confuſyowne ſo repeyred towne theyr tentes grekes faſte ſpede tyll morowe ſent dyomede ¶whith vlixes troye cyte trewes oonly monthes thre kynge pryam therto wolde aſſente two meſſage wente certayne knyght borne troye towne hyght dolon great diſcrecyowne alſo ryght famous rycheſſe curtely gentylleſſe deuer dyde dylygence conueye vnto preſence pryamus paleys royall ſee moſt chefe pryncypall ſat lordes enuyrowne many knyght full worthy renowne gan hym firſte ſpecefye hoolly ſubſtaunce theyr embaſſatrye trewes theyr entent tolde ſo aſſente wolde kynge benyngnely herde auyſe prudently anſwerde therupon honour ſaue good leyſer wolde counſayle haue lordes fully hym gouerne mater lyke diſcerne conclude ſhortly euerychone aſſentyd except ector alone vnto trewes ne wolde nat denye ector ſayde trecherye oonly ſlaughter falſe treſon theyr axynge vnder occaſon firſte berye grekes dede vnder coloure therof drede afterwarde ſelfe vytayle well knewe theyr ſtuf gan fayle enfamyned leſte ſhulde dye ſoughte ſpace ſelfe purueye outwarde ſygnes dyde eſpye wherfore quod lyketh nat lye apparence dare preſume whyles waſte conſume oure ſtuf within drede wyll prouyde yt haue nede auauntage myght v hyndrynge damage whyles encreaſe amende ſhall ſtore diſcreaſe diſpende yet neuertheles euer touchynge trewes monthes thre sythen ye aſſente accorde fro ſentence wyll nat diſcorde wyſe varyaunt thus trewes confermyd graūt outher ſyde thought beſte bycauſe ſhulde quyete reſte mene whyle eaſe releue felte theyr woundes ſore greue myght haue leyſer ſelfe recure whyle trewes dyde thus endure fylle tretee comunynge athenor thoas kynge anthenor delyuered ſhulde kynge thoas troye cyte ſo thoas ſhuld grekes home agayne oonly eſchaunge ye haue herde ſayne one nother accorded whyle ye byſſhop hight calchas remembred hym vpon doughter dere called cryſeyde hir eyen clere troye lefte behynde whan wente boke maketh mynde felte paſſyngly great ſmerte tenderly ſhe ſet herte enprented eue morowe chefe cauſe grounde ſorowe ſhe lefte behynde hym towne without comforte conſolacyowne caſte ſothly abſence ſpecyally great offence hath wrought agaynſt troye hym thought ſhuld neuer haue ioye tyll doughter recured hath agayne ¶wherfore calchas ſtorye ſayth certayne wyttes many wayes caſte myght whyle trewes doth laſte recure doughter ſome maner way fynde vpon certayne day porte wonder humbly wepynge eye wente pyteouſly complaynynge terys albe reyned whoſe inwarde wo ſothly nat feyned knee anone falleth downe tofore great kynge agamenowne beſechynge hym humylyte mercy hye pyte kynges ſyttynge place haue routhe hym grace woo haue compaſſyon may haue reſtytucyon doughter loued ſo prayinge theyr deuer thorugh theyr prudent medyacyon anthenor theyr pryſon ¶with kyng thoas ſhe myght eſchaūged lyſt theyr benygnyte requeſte goodly aſſente hym graūt forth anone ſente kynge pryamus haue cryſeyde calchas ſake therwith leyde charge hir wonder ſpecyally went embaſſatry troye towne kynge pryamus calchas ſo odyus hatefull eke thorugh towne reporte hym vp downe traytour alſo falſe worthy enhonged halfe treſon doubylneſſe ouer ſayde eke expreſſe diſſerued hath right lawe shamefully firſte drawe afterwarde moſt horryble deth may haue yelde vp breth lyke traytour deſpytous wyſe herte thynke deuyſe eueryche affermynge iugement deth none fully equypollent deſerte falſneſſe yonge olde playnely bare wytneſſe concludynge eke iniquyte wolde aſſent degre vnto thynge myght herte pleaſe cryſeyde hym eaſe caſte nat make delyueraunce leuer hadde gyue hym myſchaunce hym myght haue good large fynally effect charge ſo ferforth dryuen ende pryamus hath graūted ſhe ſhall wende kynge thoas ſhortly vnto hir fader daūz anthenore euer grutche kynge parlement hath therupon gyuen iugement vtterly may nat repelyd worde ſentence aſſelyd ſhe muſt parte hir eyen glade ſorowe playnely ſhe made hir partynge hereafter ye ſhall whan agayne cometh matere ¶howe durynge trewes thre monthes ector walked grekes hooſte ye cōmunycacyon achylles hym ca xxv ⸫ ⸫ ⸫ trewes affermyd ye haue herd deuyſe outher ſyde yt full wyſe full aſſentyd euerychone tyll thre monthes come gone lyke rede certayne daye whan agreable morowe graye blandyſſhynge pleaſaunt delyte ector herte caught appetyte lyke guydo lyketh wryte ſame day grekes vyſyte full well beſene wonder rychely many worthy company ſuche none ches tent firſte achylles fynde ſothe troyan knyght vpon ſtede toke waye ryght full lyke man made mencyon nowe hadde achylles great affeccyon herte bothe day nyght worthy ector haue ſyght neuer lyfe none occaſyon myght hym haue none inſpeccyon hym beholde good lyberte vnarmed myght hym neuer ſe wonder knyghtly well porte chere mette fere right manly theyr countenaunce laſte felle dalyaunce achylles firſte began abreyde vnto hym euen thus ſeyde ector quod full pleaſynge leyſer naked may theſe syth neuer myght haue ſyght whan thou armed knyght ſhalbe full greuous whiche ſo inly enuyous thou ſayne ſlayne anone handes twayne ſothe hoolly pleaſaunce cruell deth take vengeaunce full ofte werre eke fyght haue felte vertue great myght thy force thorugh many woundes kene vpon full freſſhe grene many place byſhedynge blode thou wre ſo furyous wode aye com • aſſynge deſtruccyowne many • mayle myn haber • owne thy ſhar • e ſwerde racyd hath ſonder cruell • ſeuered yonder mortally ſygnes ſhewe plate ſtronge percyd yhewe ha • eys forged bryght ſtele myght neu • r aſſured ſo wele thyne yr • whan thou lyſte ſmyte thy ſw • rde wolde kerue byte fleſſhe full depe full profounde ſheweth ye • many mortall wounde body large longe wyde yet appere vpon euery ſyde day day full ſore ake ſmerte whiche thynge ſemeth herte enbolleth newe nowe whan theſe hye deſpyte auenged fret enuyous rage may neuer breſte aſwage tyll vengeaunce fatall ſute cruell deth execute one thynge mooſt greuaunce whan haue fully remembraunce mynde conſyderyd vp downe howe thou madeſt dyuyſyowne ala patroclus yonge ſo manly ſo vertuous loued ſkylle ryght ryght ſelfe full myght hole herte inly kyndeneſſe tunge may telle expreſſe haſte thou made departyſyon v hole affeccyon yknet one hertely allyaunce without partynge diſſeueraunce entyerly faythfull hertes twayne ylaced locked chayne whiche myght nat none aduerſyte lyfe deth ſonder twynned tyll cruelly thou madeſt v departe thurgh herte ſo īwardly doth darte wyll neuer ſoth thoughte truſte well full dere ſhalbe boughte deth hym thynge parauenture endyd yere vpon oonly ſake cruell deth vengeaunce ſhalbe take enſure without bonde may lyue myn owne honde ſhall deth execucyon without abode longe delacyon right requyreth without drede deth deth fynall mede ſelfe theron ſhalbe wroke thorugh ye worlde hereafter ſhalbe ſpoke achylles venged foo patroclus loued ſoo though enuyous thy deth inly deſyrous ne wyte nat put blame well wotte thou arte ſame haſt dethe many day deſyred therupon inwardely conſpyred thus ſhortely atwene v two deth without wordes mo whan fortune hath tyme ſhape hope fully thou ſhalt nat eſcape truſte none ſay vtterly ector nat haſtely anſwerde agayne ſobre countenaunce auyſed well dalyaunce nothynge rekles euen thus ſpake achylles syr achylles without fayle thou oughteſt nat herte meruayle though power full myght herte wyll dewe ryght day day thy deth conſpyre euer one compaſſe deſyre laboure erely eke late purſue full cruell hate thou oughteſt nat wonder wyſe fully knowe ſentence wyſe maner ſo taketh hede rightwyſneſſe may nat procede outher wyght shulde hym loue myght deth purſueth deſtruccyon ouer confuſyon hath layde ſege aboute cyte kynred alſo vpon therupon felly doth preſume mortall hate werre conſume v euerychone wyſſe nat fynde herte lawe kynde suche one loue right equyte haue hym chere ſothly degre werre may frendlyhede debate loue right procede ſothly loue moſte ſpecyall faythfulneſſe hath orygenall hertes ioyned conuenyence one accorde difference doubylneſſe may degre nouther ioye aduerſyte lyfe deth ſondre diſſeuer loue contynueth euer hate contrarye whiche ſothly hertes whan varye procedeth rancour eye men may ſe debate enuye ſtryfe enmyte mortall ſlaunghtre bothe nye ferre moder whiche ſothfaſtneſſe werre fyn wherof longe seuereth hertes frendeſhyp kut two cauſeth loue layde full lowe wyll well thou knowe thy proude wordes herte thought ſothe agaſte right nought ſhall ferther breke without auaunt trouthe ſpeke ſay playnely henſe two yere may lyue werres ſwerde knyghthode forth acheue hope ſothe ſo mortally grene grekes whan mete thou ſhall fele full vnſwete ye contynue werres haunte ſhall pryde ſurquedye adaunte ſuche wyſe handes two werre fully full many greke ſore ſhall rewe well wote olde nat newe grekes gaderyd one ſurquedye founde euerychone oonly lacke diſcrecyon vndertake preſumpcyon hye thynge ſege layne ſelfe ouer charge vayne empryſes withoute fable weyght importable peys ſo great heuyneſſe fynally wyll oppreſſe pryde auale enclyne berthone eke enbowe backe chyne vnwarely cauſe falle ye haue done ſay one alle ouer full ſuerte thou achylles ſpeke vnto fatall deth firſte ſhall aſſay • tofore thy ſwerde thynge auiyle agaynſt thy worthyneſſe ſo ſo great hardyneſe courage wyll vygour force • ght meue thy herte manhode kiyght take derrynge darreyne betwene v two thylke quarell ſo befalle whiche ſtryue wyll aſſente playnely iupa • te tyll deth one v departe theſe lordes kynges prynces wyll accorde yfere fully one aſſent holde ſtable herte entent whiche felde oonly tweyne haue ſayde quarell may darreyne fynyſſhe condycyowne happe thorugh thy hye renowne venquyſſhe put outtraunce wyll make fully aſſuraunce firſte lorde pryamus kynge shall vnto grekes maner thynge ſceptre crowne hoolly hym ſubmytte poynt varye nouther flytte fully yelde ſubieccyowne lordſhyp within troye towne lyges captyuyte shall go theyr way cyte leue quyte gouernaunce without ſtryfe varyaunce therupon make ſuerte deuoyde ambygnyte tofore goddes othe ſacrament ſhall ſwore full good entent ouer fayth alſo ſaue aſſure pledge ye ſhall haue mene whyle kepe ſyde choyſe hoſtages abyde troye towne worthyeſte ye lyſte cheſe alſo beſte ye ſhall thynge euer ſaye achylles without wordes mo thou lyſte accorde full therto haue ſayde thy honour encreaſe make werre ſodaynely ceaſe lykly laſte longe betwene troyans grekes ſtronge thou ſhalt nat oonly wt honour fame thorugh worlde gette name therwith nat lyte thorugh thy knyghthod many man ꝓfyte fro deth ſhall eſcape lyue countre hole ſounde aryue lykly cruell aduenture dede werre endure come therfore let nat prolongued let day wene v two ioyned haue ſayde condycyowne diffence oonly towne haue victorye fortune axe nat anone ye breke vp ſege werre lete ſuffre v lyue quyete grece home whan ye gone whiche thynge achylles anone hote ire furyous alſo brennynge full hote anger wo aſſentydis deſpytous chere gan anone ector dreſſe hym nere ſayde wolde delyuer hym vtterly fro poynt poynt axynge made none excepcyon hole herte entencyon requeſte accepted euerydell ſemed lyked right well parte caſte gloue downe ſygne token confirmacyowne lyfe deth wyll holde day agayne ector happe happe may vnto whiche ector lyfly ſterte toke vp glad herte euer yet dyde man knyght quarell toke foo fyght man ſothe ryght deuyſe gald hye empryſe whiche noyſe great ſowne ran erys agamenowne anone came downe theyr tent lordes parlyament ¶where achylles ector yfere wytte theyr wyll matere wolde aſſente fynally put quarell full iupardy outher part atwene theſe knyghtes tweyne ye haue herde fully dareyne one voyce grekes denye ſayde ne wolde ſuche companye kynges duke lordes eke alſo lyfe deth iuparte atwene two courſe fortune ſubmytte hir face day chaunge flytte ſome troye concluſyowne iuparte ne wold theyr lyues theyr towne handes oonly knyght put auenture fyght pryam except whiche ſothly caas within hym ſelfe fully aſſentyd playnely put ſet iupardye hoolly honour regallye suppoſynge aye made memorye ector ſhulde haue hadde victorye empryſe toke honde pryam myght natwithſtonde agayne ſo many one entencyon contrarye oppynyon bothe grekes troye ſyde helde pea let ouer ſlyde ſo grekes parted echone ector achylles gone home troye hym leue whyle whyles directe ſhall ſtyle telle troylus lamentable wo whiche made parte lady fro ala fortune gery vnſtable redy aye chaungeable whā folk moſt truſt ī thy ſtormy face lyke theyr deſyre ye fully embrace thy ioye away tourne wrythe vpon wretch thy power kythe recorde troylus yt fro whele ſo lowe falſe enuye thou haſt ouer throwe ioye whiche inne lady make hym twynne whan beſt wende haue ſuryd woo hath enduryd muſt nowe helpe hym complayne whiche herte felte ſo great payne inwarde wo ſo great diſtreſſe haue cunnynge expreſſe whan knewe partynge cryſeyde almoſt woo payne deyde fully wyſte ſhe departe ſhall ſentence iugement fynall fader gyuen parlyament whiche wo tourment rent poynt haue fallen rage man myght peaſe ſwage hyd paynes whiche breſte gan dare lyke man furye gan fare ſuche ſorowe day nyght make complaynynge oonly hir ſake whan ſawe ſhe ſhulde aweye leuer hadde playnely deye lyue behynde hir abſence hym thought without hir preſence dede ſayne intoterys began rayne whiche eyen gan bolie breſte ſyghes vp ſwolle ſobbynge ſorowes depe ne rore wepe ſore loue herte gan conſtrayne ſhe ne felte nat lytell payne wepte alſo pyteouſly gan crye deſyrynge aye ſhe myght dye rather parte fro hym troye hir owne knyght hir luſt hir lyues ioye hir chekes terys downe diſtylle fro hir eyen rounde droppes trylle dewed haue hir blacke wede eke vntruſſed hir heer brodegan ſprede lyke golde wyre rent torne yplucked nat ſherys ſhorne ouer hir freſſhe roſen hewe whylom ymeynt whyte lylyes newe wofull wepynge pyteouſly diſteyned lyke erbys apryll reyned floures freſſhe dewes ſwete right ſo hir chekes moyſte wete cryſtall water vp aſcendynge hye hir breſte hir heuenly eye aye amonge hir lamentaeyowne ofte ſythe ſhe fyll ſwowne downe dedely pale dymmed hir ſyght ofte ſayde ala myn owne knyght myn owne troylous ala ſhall ꝑte rather let deth ſpere darte thorugh herte vaynes kerue rage ſtryue rather ala fro knyght twynne wo deth inne ne wylt thou come helpe make ende ſhulde troye wende abyde grekes goon dwelle amonge cruell foon ala ala wofull creature ſhulde werre endure wretched woman ſelfe alone amonge men armes euerychone thus gan ſhe crye longe day hir complaynte wt full great afray hir pyteous noyſe tyll drewe nyght vnto hir hir owne trewe knyght full tryſte heuy came agaynes eue myght hir comforte leue ſothe hath cryſeyde founde ſwowne lyinge grounde pyteouſly vnto hir went wofull chere hir armes hent toke hir vp atwene two began newe ſuche dedely wo routhe pyte ſene ſhe chere pale grene coloure lyke aſſhes dede fro hir face gone rede chekes deuoyded blode wofully atwene two ſtode ſhe ne myght nat worde yſpeke redy deth wreke vpon hym ſelfe naked ſwerde beſyde ſhe full ofte gan grounde glyde armes ſhe fylle ſwowne hym ſelfe gan terys drowne ſtylle dumbe ſtone mouthe wordes none wery ſpyryte flyckered hir breſte deth ſtode vnder reſte withoute menprys ſothely lyfe thus ſemed ſtryfe whiche two ſhulde firſte ypaſſe deth portrayed herte outher face ſuche coloure men go theyr graue thus wo gan togydre raue diſconſolate longe nyght good fayth ſhulde ryght proceſſe hole theyr bothe ſorowe made tyll next morowe fro poynt poynt ſpecefye wolde full longe occupye euery thynge make mencyon tarye tranſlacyon ſhulde hir wo procede ſemeth nede syth mayſter chaucer afore mater hath ſo well hym bore boke troylus cryſeyde whiche made longe deyde reherſynge firſt troylus contrayre aſcende vp loues ſtayre ſurquedye became one companye loues folke olde game whan cupyde made hym full tame brought hym lowe ſubieccyowne temple walked vp downe whan gynne hooke leyde amyd eyen cerclyd cryſeyde whiche day myght nat aſterte thorugh breſte percyd herte wente hym home pale ſyke wan wyſe troylus firſte began ſeruaunt mayſter telleth thus tyll holpe pandarus thorugh whoſe comforte medyacyon boke made mencyon great laboure firſte came grace ſo contynueth certayne yeres ſpace tyll fortune gan vpon hym frowne ſhe fro hym muſt go towne ſodaynely neuer hym ſe lo ende falſe felycyte lo ende wordely brotylneſſe fleſſhely luſte lo vnſtableneſſe lo double varyacyon worldly blyſſe tranſmutacyon daye myrthe wo morowe aye fyne ala ioye ſorowe cryſeyde kynge thoas anthenor ſhall go forth ala vnto grekes euer dwelle hole ſtorye chaūcer telle ye lyſte man better lyue proceſſe halfe ſo well deſcryue englyſſhe gylte ſayes rude boyſtous firſte olde dayes full fer parfeccyon lytell reputacyon tyll came thorugh poetrye gan tunge firſte magnefye adourne eloquence honoure laude reuerence thorugh lande gyuen ſonge laurer englyſſhe tonge hym gyuen excellence right whylom full hye ſentence perpetuelly memoryall columpna cardynall petrark fraunceyſe gyuen ytayle reporte neuer fayle honour dyrked name regyſtred hous fame amonge hyeſt ſete mayſter galfryde chefe poete euer yet langage name ſhall pallen none age euer ylyche without eclypſynge ſhyne parte wyll neuer fyne hym magnefye wrytynge playnely tyll dye god praye ſoule brynge ioye lefte wyll agayne troye ſtorye telle firſte guydo within boke ſpeketh troylus rebukynge hym full vncurteyſly ſo ſette herte folyly vpon cryſeyde full doubylneſſe boke guydolyſte expreſſe hir terys hir complaynynge hir wordes whyte ſofte blandyſſhynge meynt faynynge flaterye outwarde farſed many falſe lye vnderhyd varyaunce curyd aboue fayned countenaunce woman falſely terys borowe theyr herte though ſorowe lyke wolde trouthe deye thynke nother ſeye ſerpent vnder floures fayre venym hydeth doth repayre ſugre afore galle hydde behynde appropryd vnto theyr kynde dyuerſe double nature ratheſt deceyuynge whan men moſte aſſure vnder coloure euery thynge werke fayre aboue foule derke hydde ſo man may eſpye though ſo wofull eye outwarde wepe pyteouſly tother eye laffe couertly whoſe ſorowes tempryd allyes theyr coloure euer meynt rayes vpon chaunge mutabylyte stande hole theyr truſte theyr ſuerte ſure doubylneſſe alway double theyr ſykerneſſe semynge one whan beſte varye lykeſt corde whan contrarye thus varyaunt accorde holeſt ſeme whan diſcorde guydo ſayth fewe none hir herte apayed one yet one twayne thre foure theyr ſpeche fayne lyke one mo hole theyr loue well eke wo eueryche ſhall hym ſelfe deme next lyke doth ſeme thus hope ſtandeth eche alle treweſt aye redyeſt falle ſerueth beſte next apayred thus chaunge theyr loue fayred let man truſte catche whan may farewell morowe though ſure day fayre chaunge laſteth ouer yere folye bye dere thylke treaſoure whiche harde poſſede flyeth away whan men therof moſtenede happe chapman ſayth guydo yet day men may ſe ſheweth large feneſtralles chaumbres hye lowe downe halle wyndowes eke euery ſtrete alſo eke men may mete pylgrymages oblacyownes ſpectacles cytes townes ſayth guydo ſelle hym ferther telle eke ſayth ſentement fraude fully equypolent fraude ſleyghty compaſſynge woman lyke workynge ſet faythfulneſſe wenynge fynde ſtabylneſſe ſhall fynde ſtedfaſt mone poynt chaunge ſoone yonge caſte hym rage olde falleth dotage wherfore counſayle bothe two caſte brydell lyghtly let go techeth guydo god wot nat hath delyte ſpeke curſedly alway woman thorugh boke men may ſe ſo lyſte loke hadde enuye ſpecyall good fayth right wroth wt lyſte ſo debate yre whiche latyn tranſlate inwardely herte felte blede hye deſpyte clauſes rede reſowned concluſyon oonly malys accuſacyowne theſe woman full euyll mote thryue generally ſecte deſcryue whiche made nat thorugh diſcrecyon good badde none excepcyon blame foule mote falle cauſe one hynder alle dare well afferme rode agayne one badde hondred gode though ſome one bouble newe hyndreth nat trewe example alſo though ſhewe ſome one whylom ſhrewe good take ſhall hede hyndrynge womanhede though twayne thre double fayne agayne lothely colayne virgyns inly full grace leuen thouſande holy place man may fynde kalender full many mayde parfyte enter whiche deth ſtable trewe ſome roſen hewe marterdome blyſſe heuen wonne ſome alſo bokes tell konne lylye virgynyte vyolettes parfyte chaſtyte aſcended aboue ſterrys clere ſercle nynthe ſpere wherfore ioye euer gladneſſe eterne wherfore ſothe diſcerne though ſome clerkꝭ ſhrewes haue myſſayde let good woman therof myſpayde lacke one nat blame eke men may ſayde ſame trewe reprefe though ſo nother thefe worſe degree though tother hanged tree vnto woman hyndrynge none amonge hondred though one gouernaunce vycyous agayne thouſande vertuous ye lyſte lyghtely ye may fynde though guydo wryte haue kȳde double men ſhulde goodly take agayne maner grutchyng make nature werkynge hath full great powere harde courſe hir holde reſtreyne ſhe wyll nat gyded reyne coarted hir dewe ryght therfore eche man full myght shulde thanke god take pacyently woman double naturelly ſhulde men ley blame though myn auctor hyndre ſo name wrytynge oonly cryſeyde vpon hir ſuche blame leyde counſayle lyghtly ouer paſſe myſſayth hir place hyndre woman outher eue morowe take hede let ſorowe ſkyppe ouer ye lyſte nat rede tyll ye come dyomede hir ſent troye towne ceryouſly made mencyowne firſte ſhe hym delyuered anthenor kynge thoas troylus gan hir conueye many brynge hir weye dyomede waye gan hir brydell lede tyll hir broughte hir faders tent calchas fall good entent receyued hir lodgyd lay hir ſpeche durynge day maner hole euerydele reherſed ceryouſly wele troylus boke ye haue herde ſayne wryte ofte holde vayne guydo ſayth longe nyght cryſeyde forſoke hir owne knyght gaue hir herte vnto dyomede tenderneſſe womanhede troylus wexe hir herte colde without fyre ben theſe aſſhys olde none excuſacyon oonly kyndes tranſmutacyon appropryd vnto hir nature selde neuer ſtable endure experyence men may ofte lere nowe agayne matere muſt reſorte though ferre began wryte werre ¶how whan ye trewes endyd wente batayle agayne many man ſlayne partyes ye diſcrypcyon ye palays ylyon alſo dyed ſo many grekes peſtylence demaunded trewes xxx dayes whiche obteyned capitulo xxvi tyme paſſed trewes ytake next morowe whā tytā hath forſake vnder partye emyſperye nyght full merye aurora lyinge ſyde bed hym lyſte lenger byde ſhope hym vp caſte ſtremes ſhene troye walle whan ector armed clene felde faſte gan hym hye fyftene thouſande companye worthy knyghtes manly men fynde troylus hadde ten knyghtes eke baner ſewe haſt parys gan remewe towne perce longe eche bowe honde arrowes ſharpe truſſed theyr ſyde knyghtes aboute hym ryde hadde alſo thre thouſande fynde dephebus next hym came behynde thre thouſande knyghtes armed clene whoſe plate ſonne ſhone full ſhene next hym came troyan eneas rede ſothly theſame day troye towne hondred thouſande knyghtes renowne lyke recordeth dare frygius boke guydo wryteth thus grekes tofore day ſeuen thouſande went menelay knyghtes echone whiche dyde lede many went dyomede next foloweth hardy achylles mayne called myrundynes zanptipu • worthy kynge eke hadde thre thouſande knyghtꝭ whiche ladde felde agayne towne alderlaſte came agamenowne ſuche nombre grekes felle wonder telle whan wardes felde abrode hadde theyr place without abode agrekyſſhe kynge whiche yt phyllys hyghte anone ector hadde ſyghte towardes hym ſyttynge ſtede ſpere gan hym faſte ſpede whan ector cōmynge ſayne hente ſpere rode hym agayne thorugh ſhelde plate rounde gaue hym laſte fat wounde vpon whoſe deth auenged full many greke gan ector flee firſte worthy kynge famous grekes called zantipus hye diſdayne oonly phyllys ſake towarde ector hath courſe ytake ſpere ran hym full ryght ector firſte hyt hym ſuche myght thorugh harneys ſperes hede zantipus fylle grounde dede deth greke ſore playne dyde theyr myght theyr beſy payne euery halfe furyous wode auenge troyans blode thorugh paſſynge cruell hardyneſſe began troyans ſo oppreſſe many one day ne myght aſterte thoruh breſte yperced herte dede ſlayne amonge prees amonges whiche cruell achylles slewe lychaon eufrobyus noble knyghtes right worthy famous ycome theyr countre agayne grekes helpe cyte whyle troyans cōſtrayned ſo narowe ſpere quarell darte arowe ector wounded thorugh vyſer face lyke ryuer reed blode downe began rayle harneys thorugh auentayle wherof aſtoned whan hadde ſyght full many troyan toke hym flyght cyte faſte gan drawe chaſe full many one ſlawe myght felde remewe euer one grekes ſewe vnto walles almoſt towne tyll ector troyan champyowne knyght hode gan take hede albe wounde ſore gan blede yet manhode gan recomforte maugre felde reſorte namely whan hadde inſpeccyowne walles toures towne eleyne eccuba quene ſuſter fayre polycene many lady gan beholde hym thought anone herte gan colde ſhame knyghtes ſhulde fle lyke lyon cruelte made tourne manly euerychone waye mette meryon agrekyſſhe kynge nye allye achylles bokes ſpecefye ſwerde ector ſmote hym ſo hym rofe pecys two whan achylles ſawe hym dede parted two euen fro hede hent ſpere thought ne wolde fayle tohyt ector thorugh ſhelde plate mayle rode hym full enuyouſly amyd ſhelde ſmet hym cruelly ſtroke ector neuer adell remeueth nat ſat ſo faſte well ſwerde anone taryeth nought ran achylles enuyous thought knyghtly ran vpon courſere creſte ſhone ſo bryght clere ſuche myght ector hath hym ſmet percyd thorughe baſenet racede eke auentayle ſtroke many pece mayle achylles conſtrayned nede maugre myght ſtagre ſtede enclyne bowe backe whiche tyme ector hym ſpake ſayde achylles well aduerte great enuye thy cruell herte ſpecyally thou haſte yet beware counſayle thy ſelfe put ſo aduenture one thynge playnely enſure deſyre laſte ſome day felde mete may truſte right well gayneth ſocour ſhall ſo acquyte thy labour mortally vnderſtande ſwerde holde honde thy lyfe thou ſhalt nat eſcape cruelly vengeaunce ſhalbe take efte whan met euen vpon thy hede whiche thynge whan achylles toke hede aduertynge herde hym ſayne right wolde haue anſwere agayne ¶worthy troylus knyghtly entrede inne made ſondre twynne thorugh manhode companye worthy knyghtes dyde guye hye proweſſe owne myght hath grekes put agayne flyght ſlayne day drede sixe hondred knyghtes ſothely rede loſſe whiche grekes faſte fle theyr tentes neceſſyte tyll menelay dyde beſy cure make felde agayne recure thorugh whoſe manhode yt day doute worthy knyghtes hym aboute felde grekes recured anone tho fro troye came kynge odemon haſte poſſyble may came enbuſſhed vpon menelay hym vnhorſeth ſelfe place ſuche wounde gaue hym face fro deth wende nat eſcape doutles anone hadde hym take helpe troylus lad vnto ye towne grekes ſuche preſe came downe reſkewe hym great nede odemon ferther myght lede kynge menelay towarde cyte whan dyomede came meyne many worthy rydynge hym aboute troylus mette amonges route ſodaynely hap aduenture hym vnhorſeth eure anone hent ſtede bad ſquyer ſhulde lede vnto cryſeyde oonly ſake beſechynge hir ſhe wolde take gyfte hir owne man syth day hir loue wan amyd felde thorugh great myght hym whylom hir owne knyght haſte waye went therof made vnto hir preſent prayinge hir full humble wyſe lytell gyfte ſhe nat deſpyſe receyue remembraunce pleaſaunce pyte womanhede hir ſeruaunt called dyomede remembre come hir knyght ſhe anone herte glad lyght full womanly bad hym repayre agayne vnto lorde playnely hym ſayne ſhene myght kyndeneſſe womanhede gentylleſſe refuſe hym platly hir grace hir ſtraunge place kynde founde ſo comfortable euery thynge ſo ſeruyable may nat lyghtly mynde thynke hym ſo trewe kynde ¶with whiche anſwere meſſager gone vnto lorde tolde hym anone worde worde lyke ſhe hath ſayde therof full well apayde hym thought playnely herte recured paynes ſmerte forth hym armes knyght day durynge ſtronge fyght troye ſo manly haue borne grekes myght nat ſtonde aforne theyr tentꝭ haue thē chaſed downe ne hadde kynge agamenowne grekes hadde dryuen felde whiche thynge anone behelde came vpon many worthy man tho newe ſlaughtre agayne began euery halfe vpon large playne grekes haue troyans ſo layne efte agayne haue felde ywonne troyans conſtrayned tho begonne leſe theyr londe tyll pollydamas whiche knyghtes beſyde gan falle vpon endelonge grene troye full manly ſuſtene grekes gan ſo enchace whan came loſte theyr place ſtronde euen vpon ſee thurgh knyghthod made thē fle theyr lyfe drede whiche myſchefe whan dyomede behelde ſawe pollydamas mortally purſued chas hors backe felde fere cruell herte hent anone ſpere ſpryngynge rode hym full ryght agayne acquyte hym lyke knyght lyſte partye feyne ſtede helde agayne reyne raughte ſpere threwe reſte dyomede ſmote ſo breſte mortally lyke founde vnhorſed hym greuous wounde ryght anone knyghtly herte pollydamas attones ſterte vnto hors dyomede reyne proudely gan lede vnto troylus foot ſtode bathed grekes blode euery halfe whiche ſhadde amonges ſo knyghtly hym hadde ne myght endure ſuſtene ſharpe ſwerde grounde ſo kene delyuerly maugre foon ſadell vp ſterte anoon force armed vnwarely aduenture ca ſharpe ſwerdes none whette achylles togydre mette worthy troylus rancour pryde achylles ſmote felle aſyde downe hors lowe grounde natwtſtandynge grene mortal woūde roſe agayne faſte gan hym ſpede myght recure ſtede nought wolde nat auayle ſodaynely freſſhe batayle troye made mencyon compaſſe wyſe beſet hym enuyron eueryche armed bryght clene ector tho furyous tene dare telleth maner howe ſame day thouſande knyghtes ſlowe whiche withſtode oonly diffence achylles make reſyſtence tyme deth ſtondynge iupardye certaynely bokes lye lyklyhede myght nat eſcape myſchefe dede take ector hym ſo furyous rede thelamonyus reſkued hym great nede cauſed hym recure ſtede natwithſtandynge great prees duke lorde athene caſe herte hole entent helpe achylles wonder dylygent hym ladde many noble knyght bycauſe drewe nyght ſtorye maketh reherſayle made ende batayle troye entred towne made mencyowne hauynge delayes mortally foughte thurty dayes withoute interrupcyon outher parte great deſtruccyon aldermoſt theyr great pryde loſt moſte grekes ſyde saue pryamus loſte ſpecyall sixe ſones called naturall hadde full great heuyneſſe ſtorye lyketh expreſſe mene whyle ector certayne face wounded agayne thus haue cruell rage euery parte receyued great damage tyll kynge pryam troye ſent downe trewes vnto agamenowne ſixe monthes aſſente wolde therupon hath counſayle holde lordes beſte echone accorded therto graunte axynge concluſyon whyle within ylyon durynge pea outher parte aſſured woundes fully cured lay worthy ector protector towne ryche royall chefe doungeowne ylyon troye bare name whiche byldynge hadde ſuche fame ſhulde cōmende vp ſo downe dare doth deſcripcyowne wante cunnynge termys aplye boke doth ſpecefye wrolde none ſo ryche hye deuyſe byldynge lyche whiche ſtode delyte recordeth twelue ſtones whyte alabaſtre ſhortly conclude twenty paſe latytude grounde ypaued thorugh wt cryſtall vp hyghte parformed euery wall ſtones man fynde dyamountes ſaphyres ynde royall rubye ſo oryent lyght derkeneſſe dymme nyght enchaced bemes ſhene euer amonge emeraudes grene ſtones maner man worlde deuyſe reken pryſe value rycheſſe ther wrought large gret roūdeneſſe ſayth dare yuory pyllers therupon ſet corner pured golde aboue hyghte ymages wonder huge weyghte many perle many ryche ſtone euery pyller halle hadde one maſſyfe golde borned clere bryght wonderfull mannes ſyght werke meruaylous faſyon lyke eſtymacyon thynge ymade founded fayrye werke wrought fantaſye thorugh wytte man lyklyneſſe boke dare bereth wytneſſe lyke reken ſyght apparaunce thynge celeſtyall syth boke ye get wrytynge myght neuer ſe albe dyde excelle therof thynke nowe telle retourne agayne pryamus whiche whyle inly coryous myght beſy cure ordayne ſepulture ſones afore dede tyme ſyke lay dyomede loues darte wounded herte felte inwardly ſmerte wofull ſyghes whiche breſte abreyde full ofte daye loue cryſeyde ſhake feuer newe cauſed hym full pale hewe wexe bothe megre lene pyteouſly gan hym abſtene fro mete drynke ſolace ſene dedely face ofte day hir wolde playne diſſeaſe mortall payne prayinge grace ſhe wolde ſe vpon woo haue pyte mercy take hede hir ſeruaunt oonly womanhede planely ellys ſeye hir ſake ſayde wolde deye cunnyngly full ſleyghty wyſe kepe hym lowe vnder hir ſeruyſe delayes ſhe helde hym forth honde made hym weer ſtonde full vnſure betwene hope diſpayre whan grace ſhulde haue repayre put hym heuyneſſe daunger newe brought hym diſtreſſe diſdayne encreaſe payne double weer ſhe brought hȳ trayne woman holde man full narowe whan hurte cupydes arowe ſette hym many felle aſſayes day day put hym delayes ſtonde vnſure betwyxe hope drede right cryſeyde left dyomede entent ſette hym fyre woman kyndely deſyre whan man haue brought traunce vneuenly hange hym balaunce hope drede lynke hym chayne fyne vnſure twayne dryue hym forth yeres ſerue force lyue ſterue fyne loues fyry rage ſhe wolde haue hym inſeruage locked hym vnder ſuche keye wote nat lyue deye doute thus lette hym dwelle forth wyll ſtorye telle matere eke reſorte agayne myn auctour recordeth certayne trewes wered gone twelue dayes ſuynge one grekes faught wt towne great damage confuſyowne outher partye aduerſyte whyle great mortalyte bothe ſwerde peſtylence amonge grekes fatall influence noyous hete corrupt eyre engendryd great diſpeyre theyr lyfe felde leye day day ſodaynely deye theyr nombre faſte gan diſcrece whan ſawe ne wolde ſece theyr aduyſe kynge agamenowne trewes ſent towne thurty dayes pryamus kynge without graunted axynge ¶howe andronomecha ectors wyfe hadde vyſyon hir ſlepe hir houſbonde fought morowe ſhuld ſlayne whiche wold byleue hir nouther fader moder achylles ſlewe hym ca xxvij whan moreyne wofull rage peſtylence began aſwage trewes wered goon grekes caſte mete theyr foon vpon day plate armed clene whan phebus roſe bemys ſhene full pleſauntly gan ſhede lyght fynde tofore ſelfe nyght andronomecha faythfull trewe wyfe worthy ector hym louynge hir lyfe hadde gete child two wonder ſemely inly fayre alſo lamedoute called tone yonge tother ne myght gone aſtronanta rede hyghte fetured well paſſynge fayre ſyghte guydo lyſteth endyte moder pappes whyte yonge tyme ſoukynge arme hir breſtys embraſynge ſhe nyght made mencyon hadde hir ſlepe wonder vyſyon note ſothe may neuene outher dreme veryly ſweuene fro aboue reuelacyon whylom hadde kynge scipyon ſhewynge outher oracle goddes warnynge myracle ſotheneſſe ſlepynge ſhe lay hir thoughte playnely next day ector went fomen aſſayle wonte armed batayle hene ſhulde eſcape vtterly fatys hondes falle fynally ouer antropos ſhall fyne euermore lyues threde twyne ſhewe force hir fell myght whan parodye worthy knyght proche ſhall without wordes mo felde playnely go whiche aſtonyd ſtreyght ſhort breth ſhe lay abrayde vp deth ſyghe ſtynte ſlepe pyteouſly braſte wepe conſtraynte hir hertely ſorowe ſpecyally wofull morowe whan ſhe ſawe ſtocke worthyneſſe wonte manfully hym dreſſe arme hym ſtele borned bryght troyan wall ector worthy knyght fete felle downe lowly declarynge hir vyſyowne quakynge herte womanhede wherof god wote toke lytell hede therof hadde indygnacyon platly affermynge diſcrecyon truſte ſuche fantaſyes dremes ſhewed gladly meynt lye full iapes illuſyons whiche playnely concluſyons benat ellys folkes delude albe ſo theſe people rude therin ſome whyle haue affeccyon iuge deme theyr oppynyon dyuerſly may pretende ofte falle happen wende foloweth lyke concluſyon drede whiche lamentacyon encreaſe gan andronomecha hir ſwowne firſte ſhe cryed sayeng ala myn owne lorde ſo dere trewe wyfe ala ne wyll ye whiche ſo faythfull hoole affeccyon deſyreth aye ſauacyon vp ſhe roſe dedely vyſage lyke woman caught ſodayne rage kynge pryam eccuba quene haſte ſhe wente hir ſelfe mene hir wyfely herte trewe ſtele ceryouſly declared euery dele hir pyteous dreme whiche thorugh myracle hir oonly deuyne oracle ſhewed thorugh goddes purueaunce tolde eke fynall ordynaunce fortune falſe diſpoſycyon fully purueyed deſtruccyon hir lorde without delay felde go day ¶wherfore ſhe prayeth dedely hewe vnto kynge meccy rewe vpon hir wo haue compaſſyon ordayne diſcrecyon lordſhyp ſoueraynte hir lorde nat deſtroyed reckeleſhede wylfulneſſe worde kyndeneſſe aye ſomoche loue founde tofore quene ſwowne fell grounde ſayde ala full pale chere helpe caſe myn owne moder dere womanhede routhe grace lorde felde ne pace deuer moderly pyte benyngnely goodly ſe knyghthode hye proweſſe reſtrayne renowmed nobleſſe thylke day handle ſpere ſhelde go armed felde bothe twayne aſſent beſte condeſcende vnto hir requeſte fynally accordynge one whan wardes redy euerychone yſſuynge troylus firſte alle parys next grekes falle hym troyan eneas kynge sarpedon pollydamas kynge eroys kynge epyſtrophus eke kynge ycalled forcyus plate mayle eueryche armed clene alderlaſte came kyng phylymene kynges lordes renowne diffence come towne grekes knyghtly debate pryamus ſothly gate conueyed goynge ſet wardes noble worthy kynge full prudently thoruhe ſapyence gaue congee lycence vpon greke proue myght agaynſt full redy fyght fomen royall apparayle amyd felde abydynge batayle pryamus mene whyle lyke guydo remembreth ſtyle thylke fyne ye haue herde ſayne worthy ector repayred agayne hym contermaūdynge ne ſhuld gone thylke day fyght agayne theyr foon whiche thynge hye deſpyte brent whan ſawe lordes went gate alone abode whiche wexed furyous wode hoolly cauſe arettynge wyfe cherte ſo tender lyfe puttynge fully occaſyowne abydynge day towne preiudyce hir worthyneſſe diſencreaſe hye proweſſe lyfte thorugh tunges hye eſtate thorugh falſe reporte derogate caſte anone full knyghtly herte lyfe deth ſhulde hym nat aſterte within felde day founde though ſo wt many mortall wounde ſhulde pecys wen ſondre vpon playne diſmembryd yondre hole manhode herte ſette anone without lenger lette agayne arme hym full dylygent agayne precept cōmaundement fader rode forth weye fere whiche ſhe wolde deye wyfe newe crye gan ſhoute hir pappes alſo hangynge oute hir lytell childe hir armes twayne afore hir lorde gan wepe playne beſechynge hym routhe pyte wolde vnto hir ſoroweſe leſte hir wyfely trouthe manhode haue herte routhe vpon hir childe hir alſo whiche ſhe bare hir armes two nat myght hym cryinge kepe whan ſawe wofull moder wepe knelynge downe vnto hym ſhe ſayde hir ſobbynge ſhe myght abrayde myne owne lorde haue mercy nowe lytell childe whiche ye ſe pyteouſly afore wepe crye haue mercy lorde v dye haue mercy eke vpon cyte myn owne lorde haue mercy cruell deth paſſe ſhall echone lacke helpe ala whan ye gone crye andromecha eke hir ſuſter caſſandra eccuba fayre polycene eleyne luſty freſſhe quene whiche attones felle hym beforne heer vntreſſyd wepynge torne loude gan crye place beſechynge hym mercy grace thylke day abyde towne herte haue compaſſyowne hir complaynte hir wofull mone syth truſte twone alone hym abode reſyſtence agayne deth chefe diffence hym hoolly theyr affyaunce theyr ſuerte theyr ſuffyſaunce eche thynge myght greue yet ne myght herte meue abyde yet goodlyhede hym beſought theyr womanhede wolde enclyne herded herte ſtele myght lytell droppe fele oonly pyte theyr woto rewe lykly morne renewe fynally theyr diſtruccyowne cyte ſothly towne vnhap endeleſſe ruyne yet myght hym nat enclyne ne wolde concluſyon indurate herted lyon alway contynuynge rage whoſe herte myght ſofte ſwage nouther prayer waymentacyon hym reſtrayne oppynyon euery perell layde ſo ſyde way gan anone ryde thorugh wyfe none bote hir rage kynge ſhe ran maſed hir mortall wo ſhe vnneth myght ſpeke hym diffacyd rewefull hir ſyght hir hewe knoweth hir wyght loſte ſhe hadde bothe myght ſtrengthe plat ſhe fyll grounde lengthe tofore kynge routhe ſene beſechynge hym entent full clene grace conſydre hir wo helpe ector go ſeynge hir faythfull womanhede hir requeſt raughte anone ſtede prycked oonly hir ſake ſo great haſte hath ouer take worthy ector within cyte hent reyne great diffyculte maugre hym made hym tourne agayne ſuche wyſe durſte nat ſayne albe full lothe therto force prayer alſo ſtede made hym lyghte reſte eſchewe ne myghte ne wolde agayne fader ſtryue albe felte herte ryue melancolye hertely ire diſdayne newe ſet fyre inwardely ſteryd blode lyke tygre lyon wode depryued newly hir pray right ſo fared ylke day lyke bore tuſkes whette whyle grekes troye mette furyouſly walkynge vp downe diffence ſothly towne troylus firſte bay ſtede aduenture mette dyomede eche ſurquedous pryde ſharpe ſperes gan togydre ryde guydo ſayth without drede one bothe hadde anone dede ne menelay knyghtly go bytwene furyous tene ſmette hors full k • yghtly wyſe meryem myghty kynge fryſe menelaus marked hath full wele ſwerde full ſharpe groūde ſtele vnhorſed hym threwe hym grene ſtroke myght nat ſuſtene menelay hym ſo wode lykly euen ſtode lyfe ſhuld nat eſcape grekes full haſtely ſhape meryem ye haue herde ſayne ſette rounde vpon playne ſeſſe hym auentayle euery part cruelly aſſayle deſtytute dredefull caas hym helpe came pollydamas knyghtes gan nyghe nere whan hym ſawe taken pryſonere maugre vpon hym ſette theyr handes pollydamas hym fette whoſe reſkues ſo great ſtryfe many one therfore loſte lyfe grekes rather ſhulde eſcape theyr handes haſty rape caſte playnely ſhalbe dede fully purpoſe haue hadde hede ſtode myſchefe ſo great diſioynt hym helpe euen vpon poynt came troylus moſte knyghtly array manhode made ſuche affray amonges reſkues kynge maugre cōmynge delyuered myghty lorde fryſe cruell deth ye haue herde deuyſe therupon came thelamonyus proude armes euer ſurquedous thre thouſande full worthy euerychone vnhorſeth pollydamas anone amonge knyghtꝭ proudly bare hȳ downe troylus hath thorugh hye renowne myd foon gete hym hors agayne troye ſo ſore layne euery halfe thorughe grekes pryde myght afore nat abyde newe newe hardy achylles aſſayled myrundones compelled neceſſyte myſchefe made flee home walles gate towne great damage confuſyowne theyr partye backe ſo gon whiche thynge whan margaryton behelde ſawe game goth herte gan wexe wroth paſſyngly haue diſdayne ſtorye recordeth certayne bothe hardy famous ſone alſo kynge pryamus noble knyght great worthyneſſe whan ſawe myſchefe diſtreſſe troye gan fle caſte anone auenged vpon achylles great myght ran hym full lyke manly knyght hors backe townes ſake hym enforſeth achylles take amyd felde amonge knyghtes alle achylles ala ſhulde falle day hym ſlewe cruell aduenture thorugh troyans myght nat endure felde holde homewarde gan thē hye mortally make noyſe crye firſte deth margaryton purſuyte kynge thelamon made chaſe thorugh cruelte home gate troye cyte ſlewe kylled alway rode albe parys manly hym withſtode brethre baſte borne theyr grounde haue lorne lefte forſake vtterly felde home went broughte ſhelde dede corp margaryron theyr gate ſhette anone whiche myſchefe ector gan beholde ire herte gan colde ſayde platly without delay wolde auenge deth ſame day made haſte ſtede fet vp ſterte baſenet vn wyſte kynge lefe lothe gayne forth anone goth tyll paſſyd gate towne furyous tygre lyowne whoſe cōmynge thycke ſwarme tofore ſwerde grekes gan fleen thought tyme withdrawe firſte fynde hath ſlawe two worthy duke mette beſy waye lette tone ycalled eurypalus tother hyghte haſcydyus ſo troyans felde agayne haue wonne newe manfully begonne grekes ſewe folowe tras yet myſchefe daūz pollydamas ſame tyme grekes take ector hath ſo borne hym ſake ſoreſt layne thorugh knyghthod reſkued hȳ agaȳe put grekes ſo great diſtreſſe thorugh manhode worthyneſſe ſo euer thylke day rode ſharpe ſwerde bathed theyr blode ſo cruell ſo mercyles knyght callyd leothydes shope hym anone ector mete whyle moſte irous hete ſette hym full preſumptuouſly ector tho deuoyde mercy anone hym ſlewe threwe hym felde whiche thynge whan achylles behelde great ſlaughtre woundes wyde ector made vpon euery ſyde gan anone compaſſe herte vp downe caſte aduerte grekes neuer may ſure agayne theyr foon fyght endure kepe felde ſtryue whyle ector lyue wherfore caſte ſhope many weye engyne ector myght deye auauntage myght hym fynde therto eke polycenes ynde worthy duke alſo aſſent oonly herte hole entent hope ſtode ſuſter wyue loue felte herte ryue hir grace better ſtonde caſte fully take honde hye empryſe haue tolde whyle hym moſte bolde ector hym ſlewe none geyne whiche anone achylles hath ſeyne ire wexed herte wode bore tygre theyr cruell mode vpon ector auenged furyouſly hym gan fle ector caughte quarell ſharpe ygroūde threwe hym gaue hȳ ſuche wounde thorugh thyghe vpon outher ſyde felde myght nat abyde hym withdrewe anone wente men home vnto tente made anone surgyen bynde mortall wounde fynde whan ſtaunche ceaſeth blede haſte agayne toke ſtede leſt wounde dede afterwarde great drede thought firſte auenged vpon ector myght hym ſe hap ſorte wolde falle hym thought paynes alle hym beſte remedye honde myght dye lyfe roughte nat amyte ſo ector myghte quyte deth deth concluſyon hoolly entencyon deſyre fully ſuffyſaunce deth vnwarely gyue hym myſchaunce tyme ector vp downe wont playeth lyowne amonge grekes many ſondry place ſwerde gan ſo enchace deth myght hym ſeen fledde afore hym lyke ſwarme none ſo hardy hym ſette whyle grekyſſhe kynge mette hap aduenture whiche ſothe cote armure enbrouded hadde full many ryche ſtone gaue lyght whan ſonne ſhone full bryght clere ioye ſene perlys whyte emerawdys grene full many one ſette cercle baſenette rounde enuyrowne auentayle veluet fret aboue mayle saffres ynde ſtones rede arraye whan ector taketh hede towardes hym faſte gan hym drawe firſte fynde howe hath hym ſlawe force manhede hent hym vp afore hym ſtede faſte gan hym ryde wardes lytell ſyde good leyſer playnely may ſpoyle hym ryche array full glad lyght newe empryſe ala falſe couetyſe whoſe gredy fret whiche great pyte hertes may nat lyghtly ſtaunched etyk gnaweth ſo great diſtreſſe defaceth hye worthyneſſe full ofte ſythe theſe conqueroures theyr fame rent away floures deſyre hauynge gredy thought hye nobleſſe ſothely longeth nought ſuche pylfre ſpoylynge roborye apparteyne wrothy chyualrye couetyſe knyghthode lere one chayne may nat knet yfere kouthe ofte ſuche rauyne hath cauſe rote ruyne many worthy ſo lyſte take hede lyke ye may ector rede ſodaynely brought endynge oonly ſpoylynge ryche kynge deſyre hym hadde hors backe whan hym ladde rekleſly ſtorye maketh mynde caſte ſhelde backe behynde welde hym ſelfe lyberte haue opportunyte ſpoyle hym wyght ſpare breſte diſarmed bare except plate diffence aagayne ſtroke make reſyſtence ala tho ſo rekles floure knyghthode māhode pereles whan foo ylke day hym alone awayte ſo lay myſchefe hate enuye felde myght hym ought eſpye achylles cruell venymous hertely hate moſte melancolyous whiche couertely houynge hym beſyde whan ſawe ector diſarmed ryde hente ſpere ſharpe grounde kene ire hatefull tene vnwarely ector myght aduerte ala whyle ſmote hym herte thorugh ye breſte dede fylle downe vnto erthe troyan champyowne thorugh neclygence oonly ſhelde deth whan odemon behelde worthy kynge myght hym nat refrayne achylles rode payne hyt hym ſo amyd prees maugre myght myrundones dede guydo ſayth certayne wounde fyll gro felyng ye playne knyghtes ſhelde lofte layde hym caryed hym full ſofte vnto tent haſte leue dedely wounded man full ſore ſyke tyll may releue whan drewe eue troye great reuerence dyde theyr laboure theyr dylygence dede corp carye towne worthy ector whan tytan went downe temple dolefully wende day wofull ende thus longe nyght heuyneſſe ſkylle ryght wyll leue agayne retourne mater helpe mourne ¶of complaynt lydgate maketh deth worthy ector cap̄ xxviij ala ſhall procede ſtorye wo drede fele hande tremble quake worthy ector oonly thy ſake thy deth ſo lothe wryte ſhall helpe endyte vnto ſhall clepe calle certys none muſys alle accorde ſynge euer oon vpon pernaſo beſyde elycon aungelyke theyr armonye tunge none may ſpecefye great ſwetneſſe theyr goodly ſonge diſcorde founde amonge theyr muſyke entunyd ſo ſytte noughte helpe wo mater wt mournyng ſhent tragedyes tore rent complaynynge pyteouſly rage theatre dede vyſage ala clepe dare crye troublyd penne grace guye nouther clyo callyope allecto theſyphone megera euer doth complayne lyue euer wo payne eternally tourment dwelle cerberus depe downe helle muſt praye gracyous mater whiche ſo furyous wyghte complaynynge drery fere right well ſyttynge matere meynt heuyneſſe acordeth well chere dreryneſſe allyed vnyte ¶wherfore helpe thou wofull nyobe drery tere thy peteous payne penne dolefully rayne helpe alſo thou cruelly yxione belydes doth boget gone thy ſtone helpe thou zepherus thy ryuer helpe eke tantalus hungre haſte ſo huge pyne wofull playnte helpe fyne beſyneſſe ſtocke roote worthyneſſe knyghthod groūde māhod ſhours well tofore bare awaye bell derrynge floure hye proweſſe example alſo gentylleſſe neuer coude amys ſeye ala ector ala ſhuldeſt thou deye cruell parchas toke ye hede cruelly twyne fatall threde ye haſty ala ye ſo namely threde breke two thou antropos thorugh thy great enuye troye ala well mayſt thou wepe crye make wofull lamentacyon whiche haſte newe thy confuſyon loſte thy diffence thy ſtronge wall thy beret vp thy ſuerte royall thy honour chefely begonne ala ala thy bryght ſonne eclypſed thou ſtandeſt deſolate comforte diſconſolate thy lyght loſte thou derkeneſſe plounged arte ſoth faſtneſſe worthy thou haſte worthyeſt day yloſte knyghtlyeſt ſhall enſure euer borne whyle worlde may dure wonder though thou wepe ſore day day complayne hym euermore thy ſhelde ioye wo thou wont loue ſo tenderly thy hole herte may nat lyghtly ſterte haue hym euer thy remembraunce whiche ſoth thy full ſuffyſaunce guydo maketh mencyon man dwellynge towne ne hadde kyndeneſſe loue hym wryte expreſſe childe lefe dyed caas outher eyer ſo well belouyd goddes fate deſtyne diſpoſyd hadde myght haue woman alſo euery maner age deth falle ſuche rage thorugh cyte aboute euery ſtrete ſobbynge ſalte terys wete heer rent dedely wo furyouſly ronne fro mortall theyr aduerſyte beholde ala pyte yonge maydens matrones olde sobbe ſyghe theyr fyſtes folde loude crye ſayde fynally ala nowe ſhall faders cruelly ſyght ſlayne day day ala whyle man ſhall ſaye nay farewell helpe ector gone ſurneſſe v euerychone wont reſte nowe dede ala body whan caryed preſence pryamus kynge anone loſte offyce ſpekynge gan hym ſelfe ſalte terys drowne pyteouſly therwith fylle ſwowne vpon corp colde ſtone inly deſyrous deye anone without tariynge hym lay force rent away bretherne eke whan toke hede tryſte pale ſorowe nye dede haue ſelfe rage torne neuer trowe ſeen aforne bretherne yet ſuche another care eche hym ſelfe gan fare wolde haue dyed cors theyr lyfe platly gaue fors grounde many ſorowes ſore lyke wylde bulles gan crye rore routhe theyr dedely wo ſene herte ſtele myght nat ſuſtene ¶what ſhall ſaye eccuba quene ſuſter yonge polycene caſſandra prudent wyſe wyfe ſorowe deuyſe whiche rent ſelf tourment wo fynally wolde ſelfe cruell deth ſo wepe wayle ſhulde make reherſayle wryte theyr ſorowes theyr complaynges theyr pyteous ſobbynge throwes wepȳges wofull cryes pyteous ſowns theyr drery playntes lamentacyowns theyr woo ſpecefye large boke wolde occupye eche thynge ſhulde ordre telle trowe longe dwelle man tedyous many day lere woman wepte afore corp lyinge ſelfe defacynge theyr complaynynge wonder myght endure haue ſothely nature kynde wepe playne ſyghe ſore terys rayne tyll tempeſt theyr wofull rage may proceſſe lytell lytell aſwage thus leue ſyghe ſorowe make cely woman theyr clothes blake shroude theyr face wympled ī vayne whyle tourne mater agayne telle playnely kynge pryamus herte inly deſyrous caſte awaye entencyon corp kepe corrupcyon whiche naturelly men take hede corrupte muſt right nede kyndely diſpoſycyon may made none oppoſycyon aboue grounde body lye reaſon muſt putrefye crafte aboue nature vncorrupt myght nat endure ¶wherfore kynge ſhope hym ordayne preſerue hole fro thynges twayne odoure abhomynacyon therwith eke crafty operacyon ſlyght nat founde horryble lyfly vyſyble eye apparence lyke quycke exiſtence coſte kynge wyll ſpare nought made anone afore hym brought craftyeſt mayſters towne suche hadde moſte diſcrecyowne parfourme axynge curyouſly obeye byddynge faythfully theyr wyll entyer dylygence temple moſte reuerence cowne whylom dedycate full yore alſo conſecrate appollo olde foundacyowne beſyde gate ſtandynge towne callyd tymbr • theyr troyan tonge ſtorye botheradde ſonge phane ſpeke made firſte hye autere great deuyſe lytell oratorye perpetuelly memorye ſette ryche receptacle made maner tabernacle egall ſyght large ymage reyſed ryche ſtage borne vp eche corner puryd golde vpon foure pyllers eueryche full craftely ydyght aungell ſtode golde borned bryght ceryouſly werke ſuſtene crafty archys reyſed wonder clene enbowed ouer werke cure meruaylous celature rofe cloſure enuyrowne fyne golde platyd vp downe knottes graue wonder curyous fret full ſtones ryche precyous euery kynde man deuyſe ryally ſo thryfty wyſe derkeneſſe blacke nyght bemys theyr clere lyght enchacyd dyde ſhyne fro grounde vpright lyne degree men aſcende made ſo well man coude amende workemanſhyp euerychone parformed vp criſtall ſtone atteynynge vp fro table ba ſtandynge reſtynge ryche crafty tabernacle hauynge aboue vpon eche pynacle ryche rubye reyſed hye hyghte stode ymage huge large weyghte maſſyfe golde hauynge lykeneſſe worthy ector gan face dreſſe towarde grekes dyde ſtonde aye thretynge ſwerde honde amyddes great rycheſſe haue yſet good aduyſeneſſe dede corp worthy knyght ſyght man ſtandynge vp ryght ſotyll crafte lyuynge face chere quycke lokynge colour ſothly hewe beynge freſſhe roſe newe lyke ſuppoſayle lyued apparayle ſtede lyke tolde thrugh ſmale pypes wrought made gold meſure enbowed downe entre made crowne great aduyſe ſubtylyte eche partye extremyte body lyuealy porrect thorugh nerfe ſynewe dryuen direct ſecrete porys craftely extende wherby lycour myght downe deſcende kepe hym hole fro corrupcyon without tranſmutaſyon hyde hewe part tourne hede golde ourne fylde bawme naturall ran thorugh pypes artyfycyall thorugh necke hede many place penetrable vaynes face thorugh vertue force lycoure conſerued lyfely coloure freſſhe hewe quycke thynge pale myghtely bawme dyde auale comparyſownyd ſemblable ſoule vegetable whiche without ſenſybylyte mynyſtreth lyfe herbe floure tree ſemblably euery vayne corp vertue dyde attayne breſte arme ſpredynge enuyron moyſture diſcencyon hande fote ſothly rede thorugh bone ioynte gan vertue ſhede diſtyllynge myghtely flete fete full gommys ſwete vyoll ſtode tempred bawme ymeynt proceſſe may nat wexe feynt day day encreaſe amende whiche vapoure vpwarde gan aſcende cauſynge eyer enuyron delyſe reſemble paradyſe flauour holſome ſoote odour ſpyce gōme roote pure golde foure laumpes lyght tofore corp brennynge day nyght oyle ſothe credyble crafte made extynguyble ne myght myn auctor ſayth certayne nouther queynt wt tēpeſt wynde rayne proceſſe waſten yeres whiche eyre bryght borned wyres full craftely reyſed lofte whoſe ſwetneſſe men reioyſed ofte theyr courage lyked ſo well whan werke complete euerydell rounde enuyrowne full ryche freſſhe ſe made parcloſe eban tree ſo longe laſte may dure whiche tree oonly nature whan cut ſmelleth wonder ſwete may nat waſte brenne hete though layde amonge colys rede mydde flawme many fyrye glede nat conſumeth though men aſſaye ofte water houeth eke lofte kyndely grounde goth toſwymme heyght ſothe ſo loth lyke alſo techeth pluuyus tree whylom paſſyngly famous ſo hye pryſe reputacyon large myghty regyon worthy londe ethyopye ynde yore agon folkes fynde hadde tree ſo great honour gaue trybute emperour remembred antiquyte golde yuor ryche tree theſe gyftes famous royall quyte theyr dette hym ſpecyall whan pryam full thryfty wyſe parformed hath ye haue herde deuyſe ryche werke noble excellent hertely loue beſte entent ordayned eke guydo telle certayne noumbre preſtes dwelle temple theyr deuocyons contynuelly deuoute oryſons ſoule ector preye goddes ſpyryte lyſte conueye eternally dwelle yfere ioye blyſſe aboue ſterres clere whiche preſtes y• kyng gaue manſyons abyde poſſeſſyons whiche hath mortyſed perpetuelly ye haue herde deuyſed whyles knele praye wake caſte fully ende make fynally thyrde boke rude maner vnder toke whyles troye wepe morne vnto grekes wyll agayne retourne dulle ſtyle ſtorye trace oonly borne vp ſupporte grace ¶explicit liber tercius incipit liber quartus hereafter foloweth fourth boke whiche ſpeketh grekes made kynge pallamydes chefe captayne theyr hooſt depoſed kynge agamenon capitulo xxix ector thus dede ye haue herde ſayde achylles tente ylayde wt woundes mortall freſſhe grene vpon morenyng whan y• ſonne ſhene enchaſed hadde away derke nyght agamenon wyſe worthy knyght werkes paſſyngly prudent hath haſte lordes ſent whan aſſembled euerychone within tente ſayde anone syrs quod lordes kynges prynces duke eke yfere ye aduerte clere inſpeccyon ye ought echone hye deuocyon hoolly herte goddes herye wardely right merye ye conſydre wyſely take hede ennemye ector dede whylom berer vp troye theyr full truſte theyr honour theyr ioye theyr hole diffence proteccyon vnto v deth confuſyon vnlykly euer v haue hadde victorye whyles floured glorye agayne whoſe ſwerde myght nat auayle ſlewe nat aryuayle ye remembre firſte day noble kynge callyd protheſelay next ſhall nat fayne patroclus parted euen twayne felde amonge v euerychon slewe nat eke worthy kynge menon archylogus alſo prothenor eke kynge hyght alphynor phyllys alſo epiſtrophus ende brought zantipus meryon myghty ſtronge kynge waye came rydynge ſlayne hath kynges two cedyus drodyus alſo polycenes ſtronge polybete letabonia kynge phylete manly knyght kynge iſydyus eke kynge hyght humerus ire cruell tene worthy kynges ſlayne hath eyghtene whiche hyder came grekes londe power myghty honde laude honour goddes alle whiche cauſed haue falle dede encreaſe ioye diſcreſe foon troye ſhall fynde experyence laude alſo pryſe reuerence fortune v hath holpe wele tournynge hir double whele hye comforte conſolacyowne v echone ſyttynge enuyrowne ſtoude nowe parfyte ſykerneſſe thorugh deth hym y• dyde v ſo oppreſſe may wayte y• towne deth deſtruccyowne haſtely ende woo theyr truſte ector goo without may nat longe endure wherfore may fully v aſſure purpoſe hole ſhall acheue fynally daunte ſo greue vnto ſhalbe importable one aſſent ſtande ſtable theyr party tourneth wrake theyr hope fully put bake diſpeyred nonſuerte vtterly theyr cyte shall weer deth depende ſoth ſhall day day amende helpe god bothe ſee londe victorye redy honde voyde platly ambygnyte excluded eye ye may ſe bothe wantruſt foreyne drede counſayle procede ferther vpon foon ryde prudently whyle abyde kepe v cloſe paſſe boundes tyll achylles helyd woundes echone myghty vyolence oppreſſe whan haue diffence haue ſayde thorugh helpe achylles let v nowe ſende pee two monethes kynge pryamus ſo lyſte graunt v lykely
