playnely ſhall whyle flawme funerall conſume may dede bodyes pale lye abrode euery hyll vale whiche reporte haue repeyre fro day day infecte ſo eyre thorugh felde engendrynge peſtylence ſtynke ſo great vyolence whyle may eaſe reſte woundes cure ſemeth beſte aſſente therto euerychone vnto troye meſſageres gone haue trewes graunted kynge repeyred without tariynge therof made full relacyon grekes afore agamenon whan ende home tent euery lorde doth wende whyle trewes endureth pee amonge grekes kynge pallamydes complayneth ſore agamenon ſo hadde domynacyon aboue hauynge enuye day melancolye hye deſpyte indygnacyon full inly fret yrous paſſyon gan breke rancour ſhewe certayne ſygnes though ſpake fewe tyll day wyſe agamenon conceyued hath hye diſcrecyon hoolly thynge though ne wold ſpare fro poynt poynt hym ſelfe declare whan lordes togydre preſent tofore owne tent noble worthy kynge full circumſpect euery maner thynge nought rakell melancolyous attempraunce inly vertuous well auyſed wonder prudent whan knewe menyng entent conceyte pallamydes nat haſty rekles longe abydyng thorugh prudence reſon within boundes diſcrecyon whoſe tunge oonly sapyence reſtreyned neclygence haſty ſpeche ſothly rape myght make worde lyppes eſcape vnauyſed thynge hym aſterte firſte examyned herte aye ſpeche ſo thryfty wyſe conueyed doctryne wyſe vnder reyne wyt hye prudence fourme eloquence alway ſo ſayde reaſon went aforne worde tale lorne wyſe ſhewynge ſentence tofore open audyence sayde euen thus whan pee vnto kynge called pallamydes sothly quod ye take hede ſemeth playnely nede auyſely lyſte aduerte muſe ſo grutchynge herte hooſt haue gouenaunce wyſely conſydered euery circumſtaunce eſtate whiche man may denye wolde maner neuer occupye tytle fre eleccyon nat interrupt medyacyon brocage roted vpon mede aye vnder meynt fauour falſhede depycte coloure trewe entencyon ſupporte ſuche falſe ambycyon whiche thynge wyll quyte tofore nat wyte wyſe ſo hye offence ſtonde clere conſcyence without ſpot ſuche vayne glorye touchynge eſtate whiche tranſytorye ¶yet neuercheleſſe haue cure wyt helpe procure euery thynge touchynge comonte perſeuer myght proſperyte hauynge eye inwarde ſyghte vnto eſtate euery maner wyghte cōmytted gouernaunce great laboure beſy attendaunce indifferent vnto hye lowe helpe foſtre coude knowe ſtode myſchefe nede day nyght take hede beſte coude aduyſeneſſe aye dylygent nat felle diſtreſſe ſothfaſtely ſo loke ryght dayes thynkynge watche nyght herte inly aduertence without fraude ſlouthe neclygence faythfully full myght aquyte euery maner wyghte lyke eſtate without excepcyon man iuſtly reſon greke nowe lyue vnto gylte may duely aſcryue falſehede engyne trecherye loue hate fauour flaterye cauſe named ſpecyall haue lyke egall one beſy payne man hath mater complayne party hye lowe eſtate deuoyde rancoure debate amonges haue deuer generall thynge partyculer hyder towarde thȳg hath myſcheued god wote well ſhulde nat agreued herte ſet pryſe choſe diſcrete aduyſe domynacyon haue ſubieccyon eaſe herte tranquyllyte lyke lordes degre wyll fully haue obeyed lyke one vtterly haue deyed quarell haue vndertake deſtyne hadde ſo ſhape ſaye ſothe full loth fayne ouer alſo ye playne choſen without aſſent meruayle nat ſyth ye ne preſent longe ye remembre ryght towarde troye waye nat dyght ye conſydre nere ye came paſſyd full two yere ſo longe abyde cōmynge hadde grekes great hyndrynge paſſynge harme full great damage huge lettynge vnto vyage hadde without wene cōmynge taryed athene lykely ye nat well ſay nay haue yet vnto day ye thought nat credyble afferme eke impoſſyble grekes ſhulde maner wyſe dare take great empryſe abſence manly acheue wynde thynge leue ſo none offence grekes haue without preſence thorugh force water londe full many thynge parformed wt theyr honde acheued thorugh theyr worthyneſſe one thynge ye geſſe ſay degree ſhulde herte ſo reioyſe lordſhyp great eſtate pompos elate porte occupye aquyte trewely nat lye deuoyde ſuſpeccyon wyll make reſygnacyon tofore excuſe auyſed diſcretly ſe ye lyſte haue agayne morowe pryme without ſettynge lenger tyme prolongynge forth delay thus made ende day went theyr way oonly nyght tyll morowe y• tytan ſhad lyght whiche tyme counſayle generall grekes helde moſt ſpecyall lordes congregacyon haue tolde eleccyon whan mette yfere agamenon anone ye ſhall sayde euen thus ſadde countenaunce lo ſyres quod touchynge gouernaunce haue hadde domynacyon haue hereto hole affeccyon clene entent beſyneſſe euery thynge myght wylfulneſſe encreaſe parſeuer contune recorde take god fortune whiche haue conſerued cauſe floure felycyte honour hye nobleſſe stande hole ſounde yet ſyketneſſe whyle fame moſte flourynge ſemeth ryght well ſyttynge myn eſtate fully reſygne specyally whyle fortune benygne ſo many preſent alone ſuffycyent without helpe bere charge men moche may ouer lade barge namely tempeſt rage ſyth ye ſo diſcrete ſage burthen let releued man therwith agreued let v one entencyon without ſtryfe diſcencyon choſe ſuche one moſte acceptable echone moſte couenable gouerne diſcrecyon echone hole affeccyon aſſentyd ſpeke generall men may ſe naturall men delyte thyngꝭ newe truſte people faynt vntrewe aye vndiſcrete full doubleneſſe varyable theyr ſykerneſſe aye awaytynge theyr oppynyon chaunge tranſmutacyon selde neuer ſtandynge hole one day loue morowe gone full ſelde ſykerneſſe oonly nowe newfangelneſſe hath embracyd theyr affeccyon haue ſtede agamenon newe choſe oonly fauour pallamydes theyr gouernour grece lyke deſyre haue sceptre hole empyre called aboute euery coſte emperour grekes hooſte right tofore agamenon fyne concluſyon daye theyr parlement euery man went lodgynge home right way tent wounded lay hardy knyght hardy achylles whan herde pallamydes fro poynt poynt leccyon diſpleaſed oppynyon playnely thought aduyſe agamenon paſſyngly wyſe diſcrete vnto gouernaunce tother pleſaunce ſayde none eleccyon maner ſubrogacyon bycauſe hym ſelfe parlement cheſynge nat preſent arettynge paſſynge great offence choyſe made abſence wherwith herte inly wrothe ſo lefe lothe concluſyon ſtrengthe ſtode eleccyon ¶how kynge pryamus went vnto batayle auenge deth ector dyde meruaylous dedes armes ca xxx trewes paſſyd yweryd oute wounded eke recured aboute next morowe pryamus herte inly deſyrous grekes manly fyght ectors deth auenge myght olde pryam knyghtly felde whan troyans ſelfe behelde great wyll hye courage hym ſo ferre ronne age gan reioyſe plucke vp theyr herte ſpecyally whan gan aduerte great manhode worthyneſſe lyflyed hye proweſſe ſake euery maner man gan arme hym • haſte pryamus day lyue deye felde proudely hym conueye hondred thouſande fyfty towne lyke dare maketh mencyowne worthy knyghtes euerychone without pryam gone afore wente dephebus parys nexte pryamus menon kynge worthy eneas alderlaſte came pollydamas fynde ſterne full pryde pallamydes came totherſyde felde many ſtronge batayle firſte whan eche gan aſſayle kynge pryamus knyghtly wayches thorugh wardes pallamydes hym vnhorſeth thurgh hye renowne lyke knyght kylleth bereth downe proude grekes ſo rode none ſo hardy ſwerde abode ſo narowe gan coharte theyr wardes made ſonder parte ſo felle furyous day dedes meruaylous armes wrought wonder ſene meruayle may ſuſtene ſo great age felde endure credyble enſure ſe thorugh great myghte grekes put proudely flyghte dephebus alſo nat behynde agayne foon knyghtly fynde acquyte hym ſelf make go backe sarpedowne eke lacke yfallen neptolonyus proudeſt greke moſte ſurquedous moſt famous ſtrengthe myght whiche agaynwarde rode full lyne ryght sarped owne ſpere rounde delyuerly ſmote hym grounde sarpedowne full yrous herte without abode foot vpſterte neptolonye ire hote ye thyghe wt ſwerde ſmote anone kynge perce londe ſo worthy famous honde sarpedowne whan toke hede knyghtly hym reſtored hath ſtede natwithſtandynge menelaus vpon hym paſſynge deſpytous hym eke duke athene encloſyd haue amonge great prees kynge perce ala ſhulde falle ſlewe hym amonge alle full knyghtly faught lyke champyowne multytude encloſyd enuyrowne hym ſelfe alone ala deſtytute mortall ca thorugh whoſe myſchefe troye towne gan withdrawe tyll sarpedowne hath holpen recure theyr londe full many greke kyllynge honde kynge pryam ſo manly founde ſones called naturall whiche vpon hym ſo rode longe day manfully abode partynge nat playnely fro ſyde kynge togydre ryde full mortally grekes confounde pryamus many cruell wounde hath ſlayne many worthy man horſe backe amonge ran none day yonge olde troye towne ſo hardy ſo bolde none eſtate hath ſo well hym quyt amonge grekes ſo ryt fro poynt poynt reken euery thynge hath pryam noble worthy kynge alone confuſyon grekes deſtruccyon theyr outter myſchefe diſcomfyture afore whoſe face myght nat endure thynges two mortall yre inwardly ſette hym fyre hertely hate bare olde vnto grekes doubled many folde deth hadde remembraunce worthy ector countenaunce whiche platly thorugh worthyneſſe ſwerde ſhope hym redreſſe fret hate conſtreynt payne veryly thylke thynges twayne whiche day ſo loke ryght force doubled myght thorugh toke cruelly vengeaunce grekes brought outtraunce thurgh knyghthod put thē ye flyght grekes attones dyde theyr myght aſſent aſſemble one ſleyghte ſyde gone playne large fayre ſe betwene pryam troye cyte fyne oonly theyr entencyowne hym debarre entre towne euery way grekes haue ſet troye hadde tho belet theyr repeyre ſtorye telleth thus manhode pryamus whiche anone lyon ſtronge ſwerde gan ryde amonge ſeuered large woundes wyde ſlewe tho wolde ſwerde abyde euery endelonge playne parys eke hath ſo belayne myghty ſhote ſtronge archery purſuyte arbalaſterys ne myght ſhote ſo kene mortall harme abyde ſuſtene gan anone fle place kyng pryam ſo narowe gan chace nede neceſſyte thorugh ſlaughtre cruelte ſwerde ſharpe whette grounde greke felde yfounde fled away eueryche tent troye theyr cyte went bycauſe drewe faſte towarde nyght phebus hadde reued lyght ſo honour hye victorye worſhyp eke laude memorye perpetuelly palme alſo pryam kynge hath wonne mo day releaſe ſorowe rede next morowe hath yſent troye towne atrewes agamenowne whiche graunted ſelfe day pryme albe therof reherſyd tyme longe laſte boke expreſſe durynge whiche dyd beſyneſſe hertely laboure inwarde dylygence ordayne great reuerence corp worthy kynge perce londe without tariynge kyngly honour troye towne shall caryed regyowne buryed predeceſſours outher kynges progenytours whiche thynge complete ye aduys alyſaunder called parys firſte corp enbawmed rychely conueyed full ſolempnely wryte guydo huge route knyghtes rydynge hym aboute tryſte heuy cladde blacke echone chare right way gone towardes perce ledynge kynge dede corp towarde buriynge whiche halowed lyke eſtate royall whyle feſte funerall holde alſo great deuocyowne worthy ector within troye towne lyke cuſtome vſed tho dayes rytes theyr paynem layes whichefeſte made mencyon fro yere yere reuolucyon yhalowed ſpace fourtenyght many flawme many hydous lyght brent enuyrowne ſeyntuarye called anyuerſarye came aboute yere yere certayne day theyr kalendere whiche cuſtome remembraunce people ſhulde contynuaunce playne wepe alſo praye rede theyr frendes afore dede full pyteouſly theyr heer torne mornynge blacke knelynge aye aforne dede corp worthy knyght whiche tyme paſſynge myght done whyle trewes dure grekes truſtely myght aſſure whan lyſte good lyberte without daunger entre cyte day day troyans myght alſo vnto grekes frely come go whiche tyme full great delyte hath achylles caught apetyte entre ſe maner towne without wyſdome diſcrecyowne beholde playnely ſe hooly maner ſolempnyte forth went certayne day towarde troye haſte may vnarmed ſothly myn auctour ſayth without aſſuraunce fayth except trewes ſo lefe loth firſte temple goth appollo halowed feſte thorugh towne downe vnto leſte cleped anyuerſarye ye haue herde ſhulde lenger tarye many worthy preſent amyd temple hye lowe eſtat lordes ladyes affeccyowne euery parte gaderyd towne corp worthy knyght freſſhe coloure kept vnto ſyght lyfely eke quycke hewe beholde roſenewe thorugh vertue oonly gommys ſwete bawme gan aboute flete euery ioynt eche extremyte feſte ſolempnyte eccuba yonge polycene womanly goodly ſene many hye eſtate lowe tofore corp ſyttynge rowe heer vntruſſyd cladde wedes blake euer one ſuche ſorowe make routh pyte ſene playne deth mene worthy ector knyghthod groūd welle trowe ye guydo lyſte telle polycene hir wofull rage ychaunged hath vpon hir vyſage hyr natyfe colour freſſhe ſyght roſe lylyes whyte outher freſſheneſſe hir lyppes rede terys ſhe gan ſhede hir chekes cryſtall clere hyr heer alſo reſemblynge golde wyere whiche lay abrode lyke vnto ſyght phebus bemys ſpere bryght whan v doth lyght auale aye ſhe rent hir fyngers ſmale hyr golden heer hir blacke wede whiche thynge achylles toke good hede gan meruayle greatly thought god kynde euer myght haue wrought theyr werkes ſo fayre creature hym thought myght nat endure beholde bryghtneſſe hir face felte thorugh herte pace perſynge ſtremys hir eyen two cupydes bronde hath hym marked ſo loue hyr deſyre brente hote fyre ſoone ſodayne colde quoke alway fyxe hir loke arrowe god cupyde perced hym euen thorugh ſyde herte gaue hym ſuche wounde neuer lykely ſownde aye one loke hir caſte durſte gan preſe faſte towarde hir namely eye hym thought muſt nedes deye founde hir ſome grace geyne playnely y• place newe caughte loues ſnare helth welfare diſpeyred herte ſo ne knewe beſte eche thynge well aſſure ſet nought toke cure thought hole hir mo longe day thus went fro tyll phebus chare lowe gan declyne golden axtre ſo clere doth ſhyne ſaye ſonne went downe ¶whan eccuba quene troye towne hir doughter polycene alſo temple paleys go aye achylles hir ſyght whyle myght tyll lacke lyght maye haue leyſer opportune loke hir curſed fortune whiche haſte maked hath went knyghtes home tent anone withoute taryinge bedde goth full tryſte complaynynge aye hym ſelfe caſtynge vp downe mynde eke reaſowne hede fote hir beaute euerydell herte felte knewe full well fynall cauſe languyſſhynge polycene beaute moſte paſſynge loue ſo moche payne felte hete thought herte melte aye bedde walowynge fro conſtreynt hydde wo whiche almoſte hym thought yt deyde hym ſelfe euen thus heſeyde allas quod wo begone ſorowe knowe ende none ſuppoſe ſyth worlde began ne neuer wofuller man whylom ſo great myght renowmed euery maner wyght thorugh worlde bothe hye lowe none ſothe coude knowe man armes famous y•holde victoryous tofore tyme remembred ſtyle vnto day ala harde whyle nouther ector playnely none polycene worthy brother power hadde whan mette theyr myght ouer ſette felde force daunte pryuely dare auaunte ala mayde tendre age hath ſodaynely brought ſuche arge ſtremys hir eyen twayne perced hath clouen euery vayne herte may nat ſterte dede thorugh conſtreynt ſmerte ſhall wyſſhe teche ala ſhall leche ſhall helpe men ſaue deth graue hope playnely none saue hir mercy ala gone nouther prayer treſour rycheſſe force myght nouther hye proweſſe hyghneſſe blode byrthe kynrede may auayle helpe nede meue hir ſadde trouthe vpon wo euer haue routhe ¶what newe furye inportune rage hath brought herte ſuche outrage agaynſt whiche nat debate loue hir beſte dedely doth hate good fayth wyſely lyſte adueret lytell wonder though ſhe hate herte syth come hyder fro ſo ferre hir kynred make werre whiche confuſyowne hir knyghtly brother moſt worthy renowne haue fatally myn hondes ſlowe whiche worlde hadde felowe worthyneſſe manlyhede ala ala nowe may quake drede lyfe falle diſpeyre ſhulde bolde haue repeyre dare ala come theyr ſyghte wofull wretche vnhappy wyghte ſhall hardy appere preſence hir eyen clere certys ſe none mene weye fynally muſte deye diſpeyred ſtonde euery ſyde helpe nat prouyde right anone profounde ſyghes depe achylles braſte wepe dedely chere pale funerall face tourned wall routhe pyte ſene hertely furye paynes kene ſo oppreſſyd thought lyfe deth rought nought contynued tyll drewe nyght tytan hath withdrawe clere lyght euer one lyke wofull man ilyche ſyke coloure pale wan without ſlepe ſo fretynge ſorowe tyll lucyfer next morowe tofore ſonne bemys clere full luſtely gan appere oryent whan achylles vnpacyent without reſte pee quakynge aye feuer newe ſene playnely hewe tyll abrayde anguyſſhe ſodaynely called one hym preuy counſayle truſteth well vnto hym telleth euerydell fro poynt poynt hym ſtode ſent hym forth bycauſe coude gode meſſage ſtreyght troye towne full aduyſe informacyowne mater eccuba quene thorughe wyſedome amene myght diſcrecyon fynde way ſauacyon vnto lorde louyd ſo quene anone go mater wyſely gan conueye tofore grace wolde preye ſhe enioyeth gyue hym audyence tale none offence foole newe lere wherfore quene goodly gan hym euer hym lyketh ſayne worde yloſt ſpoke vayne tale man coude amende craftely gan diſcende ſubſtaunce tolde clerely oute premyſſes full well brought aboute fynally concluſyon chefe ſayde entencyon effectuelly wolde make pea vnyte atwene grekes folke troye whiche thynge knewe better weye werre theyr alder eaſe wytte prudently appeaſe mortall ſtryfe bytter rage allyaunce oonly maryage hir lyſte wyſe worthy quene hir doughter fayre polycene may wedded vnto achylles thorugh theyr myght fynall pee eccuba hir diſcrecyon thorugh hir wytte medyacyon hir prudence myght aboute brynge pryamus fully aſſentynge achylles myght doughter wyue myght parformed blyue lyke haue made mencyon couenaunt oonly condycyon grekes ſhall theyr werre lete ſuffre hym lyue quyete maryage theſe ylke twayne parformed knyt vp chayne whan ye quene hath knowen entent full ſoberly good auyſement tofore worde aſterte full pyteouſly ſhe ſyghed hir herte laſte ſobre chere ſayde thus meſſagere frende quod ſhe touchynge thy requeſte make beheſte leſte wyll condeſcende lyeth brynge ende thy lordes wyll herte entere vpon muſte firſte requere kynges wyll wyll gyue aſſent purpoſe whiche thou arte ſent ouer muſte wytte alſo ¶if parys wyllynge eke therto whiche thynge euery circumſtaunce wyll ſelfe make enqueraunce full faythfully pryam parys mene whyle theyr aduyſe without within dayes thre whiche tyme come agayne achylles wyll ſende fynally thou ſhalte knowe ende matere anſwere playne home goth achylles agayne ¶with full glad chere lord ye pleſe ſette herte better eſe auyſely hye diſcrecyon hath ſo made relacyon tolde tale ſo thryfty wyſe coude wordes ſo deuyſe brynge hope lordes herte full releſſe paynes ſmerte ¶wherby made ſorowe withdrawe thus whyle hope gan adawe amyd breſte eccuba quene pryam ſpake polycene touchynge ſonde achylles profre make pee tolde hym forgate thynge wherof aſtoned pryamus kynge spake nat worde halfe houres ſpace hym ſelfe gan compace full prudently myght mene achylles wolde haue polycene vnto wyfe aye wondrynge laſte ſyghynge wonder ſore diſcloſeth conceyt herte ſayde ala howe ſore doth ſmerte remembre may haue pee great offence achylles towardes playnely whan slewe worthy ector thorugh cruelte hoolly vpon euery ſyde aſſuraunce gouernour guyde myne platly ſayne therwithall myn eyen twayne alone ſothfaſt lyght shelde protectour thorugh great myght manhode agayne mortall rage grekes werre croked age ala confuſyowne ſlayne ſo worthy renowne achylles whiche may nat mynde herte neuer fynde allyed mortall foo rote grounde ſorowe woo full harde herte appeſe loue hym cauſeth myn vneſe euery halfe thorugh cruell foon proude grekes herted echon agaynſt fortune contrayre tourned newe quarell apayre cauſeth grekes wode furyous ala preſumptuous ector berafte way ſythen none choyſe may agaynſt herte though anger ryue mater aſſaye ſhall ſtryue though loth ſytteth full ſore yet eſchewe harmes whiche lykely hereafter falle ſaue myn ſones alle wyll conſente achylles make trewe fynall pee atwene grekes alſo cyte without playnely haue vnto wyfe doughter polycene leſte treſon mene wyll firſte ſo wende beheſte make ende without fraude myn aduyſe whiche counſayle aſſenteth eke parys rather concluſyon made none excepcyon trete quene eleyne menelay neuer ſhulde atteyne hir recure agayne vnto wyfe whiche parys without noyſe ſtryfe grutchynge outher vnto entent within hym ſelfe fully aſſent therby hopynge without fere drede perpetuelly eleyne poſſede right luſte man ſhall ſay nay vpon thyrde day achylles hath wytte matere eccuba ſent meſſagere ſhe tolde hym anſwere kynge ceryouſly gynnynge endynge aſſenteth well therto parys eke ſhe hir ſelfe alſo ſo playnely ſhe hym tolde touchynge pea purpoſe holde firſte heſte brynge aboute ſure therof hym nede nat doute ſhall haue purpoſe euerydele werke prudently wele hereupon informacyowne meſſager troye towne without abode haſte may achylles helde right way tolde hym hole effecte matere alway feruent entere herte brent hote glede ſawe way ſpede oonly pea ye haue herde telle aye breſte ſyghes gan ſwelle loue polycene caſte alway amonge paynes kene purpoſe awaye fynde whyles beſy mynde ſhulde purpoſe brynge aboute hym ſelfe caſte many doute anone diſpeyre rage vp ſterte cruelly caught hym herte whiche hath hym throwe ſuche weer hym thoughe power behe •• e fulfylle dede except hadde well leſſe drede euery thynge putte certayne wenynge greke wolde luſte ſayne deſyre varyable hym ſelfe thus fauourable parforme thynge denye luſty fantaſye maner louers euerychone ſuppoſe cheue anone thynge take honde diſioynt mater ſtonde though impoſſyble theyr foly aye ſo credyble ſo achylles truſteth fynally fulfylle heſtys vtterly suppoſynge aye worthyneſſe mainhode hye proweſſe whiche dyde hym ſelfe gloryfye pryde ſurquedye grekes ſhulde diſpeyred theyr truſt myght appeyred vpon troyans wynne londe ſo withdrewe honde helpe therwithall alſo home grece wolde go ſege oonly ſake theyr quarell vtterly forſake ſo day fyerſe achylle abode cyte ſpylle whiche thynge lordes aſſent aſſembled entent amonge achylles byddynge pallamydes whan gaderyd yfere tofore lyke ye ſhall achylles hath tale ygonne ſayd ſyres ſomoche konne wyſdome hye prudence renowmed eke ſapyence thorugh worlde diſcrecyowne ſo worthy alſo renowne kynges duke royall name eeſt weſt floureth yet fame bothe knyghthode manlyhede ſay praye take hede ſaye ye conſydre playne entent cōmynge hydre good auyſe deſtruccyon hadde grounde founded reſon cauſe roted tytle ryght ſo ye lyfte vp ſyght aduerte clerely mynde full ferre backe wytte ſette behynde prudent lokynge auyſeneſſe firſte whan foly haſtyneſſe toke vpon v come fro ſo ferre agayne troyans gynne werre iuparte lyues euerychone loue one man alone ye wote trowe mene kynge menelay defaurded quene telle trouth lyſte nat feyne ye well wote oonly eleyne groūde gynnynge debate ſo many worthy eſtate recurleſſe remedye lyfe good haue put iupardye londes lefte regyownes cytes eke ryche townes whiche abſence ſtonde deſolate wyues child eke diſconſolate woo abyde mournynge diſtreſſe whyles ſothe expreſſe fro day day beſet euery ſyde lye flede deth abyde ſorowe care laboure woo wot ye wyte well alſo sythe tyme werre began grekes many worthy man hath loſt lyfe thorugh dethes fatal woūde myght hytherto haue lyued ſounde home grece aſſured well ioye ne hadde come vnto troye remembre full great pyte ouer ſaye alſo amonge troyans theyr cruell mode haue loſte ſo moche blode hath full ofte made pale hewe day alſo grene newe hadde ector ſuche mortall wounde quarell ſharpe whet grounde aboue theygh ſo kene hede ſame daye afore dede happe ſhape fro deth vnneth myght eſcape whiche yet freſſhe vpon ſene large wyde yet grene ſmerte whiche ſore yet pleyne good fayth ſemeth eleyne ye aduerte wyſely thought ſuche pryſe ſhulde nat bought thorugh lyfe good yfere honour yput dredfully hange ballaunce ye remembraunce conceyue right caſte vp downe ſodayne chaunge reuolucyowne fallen hath ſythe werre began ſlaughter deth many worthy man hir ſake hath loſte lyfe yet worſte mortall ſtryfe doth moſte rebounde damage diſencreaſe eke diſauauntage lykely encreaſe ordenaunce nat made therfore remedye ſhape outher ſyde fyne oonly eleyne abyde troye ſtyll towne lette v caſte good inſpeccyowne eaſe ſome meane way kynge called menelay theſe hym wyfe ſome londe lyke eſtate ſuraunce bonde vnder wedlocke confermed vp newe vnto hym wyll founde trewe sythe without gylte ſynne may lawe eleyne twynne dyuerſe cauſes ynowe thorugh ye world euery wyght yknowe auoutry foule vyce lawe preiudyce though menelay iuſtly hir forſake whan ſo hym lyſte another take ſhall hym better queme pleaſe ſo v ſhalbe full great eaſe whan werre brought ende whiche lykely many man ſhende ſo forth contune great laboure ſo importune ne ſhall whyle mowe ſuſtene ſothe without wene troyans yet floutynge theyr myght wt haue full many worthy knyght helpe hye lowe degre therwithall ſo ſtronge theyr cyte euery part without withinne nat lykely wynne purpoſe though euer abyde wherfore wyſdome let v voyde pryde wylfulneſſe oonly prudence haue eye aduertence profyte vayne glorye whyle honour ſhyneth victorye wyſdome withdrawe honde syth may nat conſtrayne bonde fortune whele abyde ſtable wherfore rede ſhe mutable gery goddeſſe hir double chere let v gyue vp ſuche thynge lyeth whyles may worſhyp ſaue werre laude yet haue conſyder well manhede moſte foo ector dede whyle honour floure counſayle fortune loure ſaydeere chaunge hir bryght face whyle beſte ſtonde hir grace one aſſent one oppynyon without contradiccyon herte wyll bothe one alle honoure party palle grece home retourne lenger ſoiourne quarell haue longe ſewed douteles may bee ſchewed full great damage without fayle haue done ſhall folowe tayle wherfore beſte folye vp reſygne whyle hap welfull benygne moſt blandyſſhynge face fayre tyme beſte make repayre whyle ſtande party enmyes honour perygall fer aboue playnely coude haue eye felycyte whyle aſcencyon leſt ſome man wyll make obieccyon may nat ſo honour ſaue repayre playnely haue eleyne agayne cauſe whiche thynge anone anſwere ſhall man fantaſye diſhonour vyllanye arrette wolde maner kynde go home leue hir behynde shortely ſaye holde ſhame sythe haue one great name eleyne berthe gode amonges v ycome kynges blode suſter pryam lorde troye towne exyona thelamowne kepynge hath ſhall nat feyne troye towne parys hath eleyne ſythe nowe may none let tone ſet agayne tother ſurplus olde enmyte bet wixe v troye cyte counſayle bothe eaſe one aſſent wyſely apeaſe ſome hen wende tale ende anone kynge menelaus yre wode furyous kynge thoas duke eke athene myght lenger hym ſuſtene ſuffre hym ſo reckeles spake attones vnto achylles nat oonly thorugh inpacyence court perturbyd without prouydence tumulte gonne repreue achylles proudely cōmeue agaynſt hym oppynyon ſayde ſhortly concluſyon vnto reed ne wolde neuer aſſente condeſcende thynge mente gouernyd hym caas whiche thynge anone achylles full yre rancoure herte ſodaynely ſee ſterte went way rage tryſte pale wode vyſage ſhortly ſayde hym lyſt nat fayne ne wolde lenger payne helpe ſo ſpede agayne troynas maner nede bad anone hardy achilles knyghtes callyd myrundones ſpere ſhelde helpe grekes entre felde kepe cloſe home within theyr tent thus ȳre gaue cōmaundement men ye haue herde deuyſe withdrawe euery hye empryſe whan ſo euer go batayle whyle ſcarſeneſſe vytayle fyll hooſt fleſſhe brede wynne many greke brought vnto fyne ne myght endure diſtreſſe conſtreynt hunger dyde ſo oppreſſe tyll laſte kynge pallamydes thynge reckeles hath therupon made purueaunce remedye redy ordynaunce aſſent counſayle echon hath ſent wyſe agamenon worthy kynge meſſa beſyde • • ell ile oonly prouyde grekes myght ſpede releue great nede telephus kynge londe gentylleſſe hath put honde large wonder free renowmed humanyte ſocoure cōmaundynge anone purueours haſte gone euery party aboute enuyron thorugh landes regyon faythfully ſerche euery cooſt take vp vytayle grekes hooſt full haſtely made ſtuffe theyr ſhyppes playnely lade euery thynge neceſſarye grekes water carye requeſte agamenon without tariynge delacyon ſo kynge plente vytayle fraute ȳlade gan anone ſayle towarde ſege meynee aye coſtynge grekyſſhe ſee wynde good kynge blyue nauye troye dyde aryue fewe dayes grekes anone ryght repeyre full glad lyght expleyt good ſpede ſo well hath borne hym nede pallamydes anone ſayth guydo ſhyppes gone conſydre loke aboute nede within withoute amende repare lyſt coſte ſpare euery thynge without neclygence touchynge charge dylygence tyll trewes fully ronne werres newe agayne begonne whiche many man ſothly dere aboughte ceryouſly wryte howe wroughte purpoſe playnely ſentence vnder ſupporte pacyence dvrynge one dedely cruell hate ſtynte maye ceſſe date atwyxe grekes towne great damage deſtruccyowne outher parte felynge full vnſwete tyll daye caſte mete wonte proudely wt ſpere ſhelde theyr wardes entrynge felde armyd full bryght vpon outher ſyde enbatayled ſtoute full pryde full knyghtly haue choſe theyr groūde take theyr large baners wynde yſhake tyll togydre ſodaynely haue mette alderfirſte dephebus hath ſette freſſhe luſty herte yrous vpon kynge called creſeous enuye ſtorye telleth hors backe togydre ran dephebus firſte ſpere blyue thorughout breſte euen dyde hym ryue vnto herte ſpake deth grekes playne ſore loue ſuche woo make aſtoned haue felde forſake gan anone vnto theyr tentes flee whiche ſothe whan troye ſe vpon chaſe faſte gan ſpede vnto tyme worthy dyomede hym eke kynge pallamydes hye deſpyte cruell mercyles twenty thouſande worthy knyghtes alle vpon troyans ſodaynely falle mortally made leſe theyr weye reſorte home agayne troye eke grekes felle furyous ſame tyme came thelamonyus hyght ayax ſtronge knyghtly man lyke lyon amonge ran vpon troyans ouer ſette caſuelly waye mette cecylyen luſty freſſhe lyght tyme wonder manly knyght ſone pryam rede thelamon pryckynge ſtede slowe cruelly ſwerde anone raſynge arme ſhuldre bone heallas fyll dede felde deth whan dephebus behelde wodder anone tygre lyon ſpere ran thelamon ſmette hym ſo thorugh plate bryght force made hym lyght leſe ſadell ſete amonge prees whiche ſtroke whan pallamydes behelde ſawe clerely gan aduerte irous wood furyous herte caſte hym anone auenge thelamowne dephebus full worthy renowne mortally guerdon hym quyte ſpere grounde byte sharpe kene large rounde ſquare full cruelly ware thorugh harneys without areſte dephebus ſmote ſo breſte ſtroke brake ſhafte two tronchone hede alſo lefte breſte weye fynally muſte deye none helpe remedye wounde ſo cruell mortall lyfe myght nat abyde whyle parys came beſyde auenture whyle dephebus wounde ſo inly anguyſſhous gan haſte aproche nere face pale right heuy chere diſtreſſe wepte pyteouſly knyghtes cōmaunded haſtely wounded brother aſyde fere haſte ſhulde bere wardes fro great prees vnto payne relees brethe hym leyſer auente open eyre vnto hym wente maugre grekes wounded bare hym full eaſy pa towarde walle faſte towne great dole lamentacyowne full ſoftely grounde hym layde tyll laſte dedely man abrayde mortall loke face funerall chere pyteous ſo eche ball gan tourne vp deedly eye euen thus parys gan ſeye brother myn loued ſo haue pyte rewe vpon wo kyndeneſſe brotherhede wordes routhe take hede syth deth muſte ſondre twynne antropoſe ſhall lenger ſpynne lyues threde knotte breke wherfore brother praye wreke vpon deth henſe pace thou lyſte ſuche grace kyndeneſſe yet dede breſte ſperys hede rent away thou auengyd vpon foo truſte may wyt deed ſpirite paſſe fynally firſte deſcende depe downe helle eternally pluto dwelle myd boundes dyrke ben lowe fynally ſo may knowe deed ſeye gyue forſe ſoone deye whoſe requeſte parys toke good hede felde faſte gan hym ſpede thought woo pyteouſly wepynge whyle brother lay languyſſhynge nat awaytynge oonly deth vpon poynt yelde vp breth knyghtes parys vp downe wardes ſoughte aboute enuyrowne tyll laſte pallamydes fonde sarpedon fyghtynge honde honde kyng worthy ſarpedowne come diffence troye towne whiche hande noble knyght whyle full myght moſte beſy pallamydes preſſe lyke lyon whettyd woodneſſe pallamydes herte nat ferde let flye hym ſharpe ſwerde myghtely wonder theygh parted hath ſonder ſmote harde bone sarpedon fyll downe dede anone troyans whan ſlawe compellyd force withdrawe thorugh purſuyt kynge pallamydes whiche vpon ſo mercyles cruell wood lyon deth sarpedon whiche ala whan parys dyde eſpye marked hym cruell eye hente bowe paſſyngly ſtronge arowe tyller longe entoxycat venym hede ſmote therwith dede hytte hym ſo auentayle thorugh ſtuffe thykke mayle throte gan thorugh pace fell dede ſelfe place pallamydes manfull worthy knyght thorugh grekꝭ toke flyght made noyſe wofull crye deth complaynynge wonder pyteouſlye theyr lorde myghty gouernour late choſe emperour theyr chefe ſocour ſouerayne refu • ala ſtonde deſtytut gouernaunce broke diſarayed without guyde right ſhepe diſmayed diſconſolat comfortles yſhent eche flyeth vnto tent troye ſued chace hors backe wonder huge pace mercyles ſlewe fle euery ſyde routhe ſe without pyte grace lyke lyon gan enchace tyll compellyd neceſſyte conſtrayned thorugh theyr cruelte tourne agayne ſelfe diffende troye downe anone diſcende hors backe euen vpon playne attones none gayne gan grekes proudely outtraye cruelly ſo diſamaye fynally gayneth diffence mortall myghty vyolence troyans grekes ſo diffoyle alderfirſte leyſer diſpoyle grekes tentes golde rycheſſe whiche tyme troylus gan hym dreſſe parys eke downe theyr nauye thurty thouſande theyr companye kyllynge tho playnely mette theyr ſhyppes wylde fyre ſette walle troye cyte men myght well hydous flawmeſe gone deſtruccyon ne ayax ycalled thelamon thorugh manhode knyghtly excellence come anone made reſiſtence grekes many worthy knyght tho new began mortall fyght atwene troyans grekes ſtoute rede blode rayllynge aboute vpon playne ſo hydouſly blede bothe lengthe brede deed maymed full pale ſyght vpon ſoyle full many noble knyght atwexe ſo cruell hate theyr fyght togydre debate wylde borys euen ſo fare none lyſte ſpare felde worthy thelamowne thorugh knyghthode hye renowne manly bare hym grekes diffende man myght manhode hȳ amende thorugh ye world though men ſought daye ꝑſone hath wrought meruayle army thorugh great myght ſotheneſſe grekes anone ryght withoute hym hadde fynally ſhent theyr ſhyppes attones loſte brent thorugh purſuyt parys daye worthy troylus made ſuch affraye amonges thorugh hye proweſſe fyfty ſhyppes guydo doth expreſſe loſte brent thelamowne reſkus came knyghtes downe vnto ſee remenaunt ſaue troyans daye haue hyer hande mortall fyght thorugh force great myght troylus oonly whiche hath ſo many ſlayne grekes ſothe fayne withdrawe felde lete abydynge fonde full vnſwete wherfore gan leſe theyr place amonge whiche kynges ſone trace heber hyght wounded deth myght vnneth drawe breth aſpere breſte ſtyckynge achylles came complaynynge vnto tent euen laye whiche felde nat daye ſake oonly polycene loue ſo ſharpe kene aye herte ylyke grene newe heber mortall hewe complayneth ſore arrettynge cowardyſe manhode trewandyſe daye myght ſo ſhame withdrawe hym hyndrynge name felde hym full great reprefe grekes ſeynge myſchefe confuſyon vpon brynke theyr deſtruccyon abrode felde ſe ſo lye dede lyſte nat one take hede knyghthode grekes releue whyle heber gan hym thus repreue ſpere whiche body ſodaynely drawen ala eye vp caſte rancour yre full pyteouſly heber dyde expyre preſence achylles therwith came ſodayne re tent certayne knyght achylles axeth amonge grekes clerely ſtode anſweryd full yrous mode certys quod full vnhappely troye haue ſo cruelly grekes daye theyr fyght full ſhamefully put vnto flyght many ſlayne ala wela waye vnneth none ne went awaye vnhurte maymed withouten wounde felle v troyans yfounde eke ſuche multytude ſuppoſe ſhortly conclude daye oppynyowne nat lefte man within troye towne able ſtonde batayle ſpere ſwerde enmye aſſayle wene ſothe come oute v fyght ſo huge route ne myght force take honde felde agaynſt ſtonde nowe lorde draweth vnto nyght faynte fyght pleaſynge worthyneſſe manhode hye nobleſſe take encraſe fame euermore gete name owne glorye perpetuelly memorye ryſe vp arme anone ſodaynely vpon gone feble weke make reſyſtence agaynſt manly famous excellence victours euer conquerours durynge worlde remembraunce euer brought vnto outtraunce ſoth faſtneſſe haue drede achylles toke hym hede heber lay afore hym dede full colde ſtrake coloure lyke lede one lyſte yeue hym audyence vnto hym haue aduertence may worde herte myne ſayde make hym enclyne vtterly euen lyke ferde though maner worde ne herde thorugh eres paſſyd ſowne lo maner condycyowne cuſtome playne vſaunce theſe louers hangynge traunce honour worſhyp manhode proweſſe strengthe myght fame hardyneſſe encreaſe name vertue victorye knyghthode nobleſſe armes glorye theſe loue ley aſyde suche myght god cupyde whiche hertes hye hoke ſeaſe lothe playnely diſpleaſe outher chere countenaunce wyll dede diſobeyſaunce hir theyr ſouereyne lady dere loke hir eyen clere full well daunte theyr pryde venus ſoone ſo felly prouyde arowes kene perce nerfe vayne enlace firy chayne oonly thorugh importable charge reſtrayned go large whiche cauſe day douteles noble hardy achylles wolde nat withouten wene come felde drede polycene lyſte ſhe offended hir herte thynge eſcaped aſterte achylles thorugh myſgouernaunce whyles hynge thus balaunce grekes faught towne tyll bryght phebus goynge downe troyans neceſſyte lacke lyght entre cyte whyle homewarde repreyred lay dephebus lyfe diſpeyred complaynynge aye dedely wounde whan parys troylus haue hym foūde myſchefe gan wepe crye wolde routhe dye wofull noyſe pytous ſowne • alte terys gan renne downe theyr chekes vpon outher ſyde whyles vpon hym abyde wounded man gan drawe ende whoſe ſpyryte redy wende breſt wery goſte full haſtely another coſte dedely eyen tournyd vp ſo downe whan knewe relacyowne parys hath pallamydes yſlawe anone bad ſhulde drawe large tronchone ſtelen hede anone fyll downe dede corp gan faſte ſpede towarde towne nede dole wryte lamenciowne made sarpedowne thorugh cyte namely kynge quene euer one wepynge brother ſuſters dere vayne reherſe pryam hath great dylygence two towmbes made royall excellence dephebus kynge sarpedowne many ȳmage grauen enuyron many knotte koruen yonder buryed lytell ſonder lyke cuſtome theyr rytes olde whyles feſte halowe holde called feſte funerall grekes haue made ſpecyall ryche toumbe worthy kynge pallamydes buriynge soſempnely made ordynaunce amonges vſaunce great dole pyteous heuyneſſe haue kynge great worthyneſſe royally brought ſepulture myght longe nat endure without hede gouernour choſen haue theyr emperour one aſſent affeccyon worthy kynge wyſe agamenon made lettynge troye next day ſuynge theyr wardes felde goon fully purpoſyd fyght theyr foon grekes manly face mette worthy troylus ſo ouerſette greke none ſhortly telle thylke day afore hym myght dwelle cruelly gan chace came rode place fledde ſwerde theyr lyfe doute yonge kynghtes rydynge hym aboute suche vſaunt lede euer one grekes blode ſhede whiche lyke ſtreme diſteyned playne whyle ſo huge rayne ſame day ſo huge myſte euery man hath felowe myſte specyally vpon grekes ſyde ſtorme theyr woundes wyde manhode troyan knyght ¶worthy troylus ſo freſſhe ſo yonge lyght coact thorugh cruelte maugre theyr myght drede deth fle theyr tentys ſocoure fynde troyans aye purſuynge behynde full mortally ſterne paas ſtorme ceaſe caas home repeyre theyr cyte ſtronge tyll morowe larke ſonge troylus eft moſt manly batayle grekes newe caſte hym aſſayle guydo wryt yonge champywne thylke daye rode vp downe amonge foon thorugh hye renowne therne kȳge duke erlenor barowne ſwerde ſo wende theyr lyfe made mortall ende whyle phebus gaue lyght tyll laſte drewe nyght troye repayreth manfully ſeuen dayes ſuynge lyfe ladde knyghtes felle vpon grekes guydo telle aye newe newe gan ſo confounde cruell ſwerde ſo kene grounde ne myght mortall tene afore ſyght abyde ſuſtene vengeaunce toke rode waye forſoke traſe renges ſo rede ſothe felde lay dede whiche ſlaughter confuſyowne grekes newe ſent towne trewes pryamus kynge anone graunted theyr axynge two monethes fully aſſent lordes parlement wherof made full relacyon enbaſſatours agamenon theyr lodgynge forth wente vnto achylles ſente meane whyle meſſagers wyſe ſhall anone deuyſe agamenon guydo lyſte endyte lordes ſent achylles vyſyte certaȳe cauſes lyk ye ſhal whiche ſtorye reherſed vlixes worthy dyomede duke neſtor went playnely rede fyne oonly theyr counſayllynge herte myght brynge induce hym haue fantaſye wyllynge thorugh chyualrye ſtonde hath toforne haue ſo many theyr men ylorne lacke oonly hye preſence achylles dygne reuerence receyued right knyghtly chere whan ſet yfere lyke theyr degre anone audyence ¶whyle vlixes full eloquence gan tale prudently deuyſe achylles ſayeng wyſe syr achylles moſte renowmed glorye thorugh worlde memorye knyghthode ſhoures welle diſplaeſe nat ſhall telle youre noble famous excellence erys let none offence ſhall ſay goodlyhede pacyently ye wyll take hede wordes ſayde herte thought enſure fayne nought ſaye ye remembre well firſte cauſe purpoſe euerydell grekes ye haue mencyon fully ſette one entencyon well v parde whan come firſte cyte kynges prynces except none whiche ſothe reken euerychone ſelfe ſpeke ſpecyall one firſte moſt pryncypall aſſentyd full troye cyte thorugh manhode deſtroyed ſhulde perpetuelly brought vnto ruyne newe note doth enclyne worthyneſſe ſodaynely varye purpoſe contrarye conſyder firſte ſo ſage wronges done great damage grekes londe towne conſpyrynge aye deſtruccyowne ye aduerte wyſely thought ſlayne haue ende brought full many worthy ſythe gone full yore treaſoure man may reſtore deſpoyled v brought great diſtreſſe goodes raughte golde rycheſſe ſhyppes brent thorugh theyr cruelte ala ye lyſte nat ſe whiche may nat delayed thorugh manhode fynally outrayed syth ye haue ſlaȳe theyr hope ſuffyſaūce actor theyr affyaunce fully theyr truſte diffence alſo dephebus alſo go lykely apeyred fro day day fynally diſpeyred frowardly fortune loureth honour fame floureth worſhyp hye renowne atteyned hath exaltacyowne hyeſt prycke fortune whele great wronge ye loke wele wylfulneſſe vnkynde hir ye ſo frendely fynde frowarde whyle ſhe benygne influence gracyouſly aſſygne hir ſpokys meue vnto pleſaunce hap tourne wt plente chaunce whoſe helpe nedeth nat calle ¶wherfore ala wyll ye ſuffre palle noble fame wylfulneſſe whyle hyeſt worthyneſſe knyghtly prudence ſhulde nat • ſ •• rte whiche thynge euery gentyll herte shulde haue routhe compaſſyon wherfore praye diſcrecyon ye ſhape purpoſe amende ye wolde herte condiſcende v ſtonde knyghtly werre manhode ſpoke ſo ferre renowne worldes ende reported ſo men wende perpetuelly freſſheneſſe hewe day day encreaſe newe tryumphe hye victorye put ſtorye eke memorye ſo enprentyd foryetylneſſe power haue malys oppreſſe fame knyghthode dyrke difface ſhyneth yet ſo clere many place without eclypſynge ſothly leſſe whiche conſerne ye reckeleſſe wylfulneſſe cloude ſo lyght renowne yt whylom ſhone ſo bryght myghty hande manhode wt drawe conſyder firſte grekes yſlawe tofore tent wt mortall woundes wyde thorugh felde vpon euery ſyde haue diſdayne oonly lacke routhe ala whyle lytell ſlouthe ley hande theyr myſchefe whylom theyr ſtrōge myghty wall theyr chefe diffence theyr champyowne soueuerayne helpe proteccyowne ye haue ſo ofte ſhadde blode agayne theyr foon whan ſtode full myghtely theyr enmyes aſſayle without lytell may auayle ſothe ne none v echone ye knyghthode lyſte v gone agayne troyans ye wont truſte fynall hope alſo ye ſhall helpe ſocour vpon praye ye saye auyſe full wylle anone hardy fyerſe achylle whan vlixes concludyd hadde tale face anger dede pale sayde euen thus openly playne syr vlixes ſo right ye ſayne haue declaryd concluſyon purpoſe entencyon fynally brenne deſtroye royall cyte called troye holde ſothe lyketh nat lye entent grounded folye put v thorugh diſcrecyon reckeleſhede haſty mocyon lyfe deth ſuche iupardye ſpecyally chyualrye grekes londe ſo ſmale thynge many prynce many worthy kynge haue iuparted theyr body theyr gode yloſte theyr lyfe yſpent theyr blode myght haue full well home ī pee nat nowe kynge pallamydes yſlawe alſo ſayth newe ſo wyſe ſo manly ſo trewe lyfe pryſe alone cauſe whiche echone gaderyd ſo loke ryght grekes many noble knyght haue ſlayne bothe worthyeſt worlde ſeke manlyeſt euery lande regyowne grekes party towne chyualry knyghthod ye ſourayne floure wynne armes worſhyp honoure aſſembled come fro ſo ferre whiche ſothe dureſſe werre full many one felde dede veryly without drede ſhall well mo werre laſte euery day nombre laſſeth faſte worthy knyghtes dede without routhe dare ſaye conclude trouthe rage furyous wode full lykely gentyll blode thorugh worlde ſhall deſtroyed rurall folke great pyte shall haue lordſhyp hooly gouernaunce churles eke ſorowe myſchaunce euery londe ſhall lordes alone whan gentyll men ſlayne echone nat ector ſo noble knyght worldes ſonne lyght manhode floure ſlayne pyteouſly werre ſoth ſo myghte parauenture whiche may nat attayne nobleſſe ſhall nat fayne waye ſhall deth eſchewe myght purſewe fro day day whyle lye therfore ſhortely requere touchynge werre outher praye vayne herken ſaye nat purpoſe werre ſtryfe iuparte lyfe leuer haue pallyd name ſlayne haue ydell fame worthyneſſe deth yblowe wynde laſteth throwe though renowne pryſe blowe wyde foryetylneſſe leyth ofte aſyde lengthe yeres oblyuyon thorugh enuye falſe concluſyon laude knyghthode worthyneſſe wyſedome eke gentylleſſe fredam bounte vertue ſuche grace foryetylneſſe derke difface therwithall malys enuye yſeryd hath palme chyualrye falſe reporte wherfore ſaye wyll wyſedome ſuche folye let quyete forth lyfe nowelede ouer thre rede ſeke pea troyans ye may haſty wyſe without delay counſayle platly alle myſchefe deth vpon falle well done ye toke hede bothe vlixes thou dyomede neſtor eke ſythen ye wyſe werke playnely lyke deuyſe ſūme fyne myn entent ſo reporteth hym hath ſent anone ſhorte concluſyon bepeyred agamenon ſuche anſwere ye haue herde ſayne nedeth nat wryte newe agayne vpon kynge agamenon let make anone conuocacyon lordes theyr preſence fro poynt poynt ſothly ſentence hath reherſyd achylles deſyrous haue pee troye platly prayer wyll degre agayne troyans ſpere ſhelde helpe grekes armed felde wherfore kynge full wyſe vpon axed theyr aduyſe thought beſte mater ſythe ſtode ſo firſte ſpeketh menelay angry chere ſayde platly nay haue pea nat entent ne wolde therto aſſent sythen cytee concluſyon stode prycke deſtruccyon ector dephebus dede yt whylom truſt euery nede theyr diffence ago farewell truſte hope alſo without hole pryde may nat deth abyde truſte well without le though ſo achylles ne helpe v nat towarde empryſe therof nat drede maner wyſe withoute hym haue victorye manhode owne glorye full ſure therof certayne vlixes gan replye agayne qeſtor alſo ſodayne mocyon contrayre oppynyon affermynge playnely wonder though menelay ſothly ca vnto pea wolde nat aſſente openly wyſte mente grounde roote werre cauſe alſo come ſo ferre theyr londe quene eleyne ſake oonly tweyne grekes whiche man may denye theyr lyues put ſuche iupardye hym hir grounde ſought well wyſte rought nought menelay wo endure wyfe myght agayne recure ſayth ector dede hath heyre ſpeke manlyhede knyghthode wyll founde called ector ſecounde ¶worthy troylus whiche yt brother worlde nat ſuche nother worthyneſſe reken alle troye myghty walle diffence ector agone ye knowe well ſelfe euerychone ſo ye lyſte take hede whoſe ſharpe ſwerde ſore doth v blede euery day furyous hete amyd felde whan hym mete ſtede worthy dephebus whiche tyme wonderly famous brother parys nowe founde worthyneſſe knyghthode perygall haue none auauntage vnto houre rather great damage reken ſythe gonne ſothe haue lytell wonne lykely alway leſe contynue ſythe may cheſe holſome lyue quyete haue pea werre lete one aſſent ſythe ye wyſe ye worde calchas gan ryſe troyan traytour wt pale chere ire ſayde ye ſhall worthy prynces thynke ye done chaunge ſo lyke doth moone olde purpoſe firſte entent agayne wyll cōmaundement goddes euery thynge gouerne purueaunce ſo diſcerne ala ala ne wyll ye leſte credence fayth gyue theyr heſte whiche wyſe may nat fallyble ſothe impoſſyble vtterly troye cyte ordynaunce neceſſyte myght deſtroyed hen alyte ſlouthe nat wyte victorye worſhyp honour fynall palme eke labour reported water londe reſerued hoolly honde purpoſe ye forth contune hyndre nat folye fortune ſothe dare well conclude peryllous goddes yllude neclygence ſlouthe wylfully wherfore rede manfully herte thought full vnyte platly deuoydynge ambygnyte ſette vpon knyghtly reſume force agayne fully conſume cruell foon let ſhet withoute wan hope drede diſpeyre euery doute caſtynge parryll ſlouthe cowardyſe let manhode vtterly deſpyſe drede deth cauſeth hertes feynt cowardyſe atteynt fynally goddes haue hyght thorugh preſcyence theyr eternall myght victorye ye ſhall attayne lyke deſyre ſayne whan calchas concluſyowne falſe traytour vnto troye towne grekes hadde thorugh wordes fayre touchynge werre put diſpayre herte one caſte fulfylle hoolly counſayle though ſo achylle frowarde aye helpe theyr nede gaue force toke hede euerychone redy make ye ſhall felde haſte take trewes paſſed ye monthes wayne ye felde grekes ordayne troye agayne yſſue oute worthy troylus huge route grekes gan alderfirſte aſſayle ſwerde made firſte rayle rede blode thorugh theyr harneyſe bryght deth theyr fledde fro ſyght daye thorugh cruelte caſte hym fully auenged vpon deth ector vtterly dare reherſeth ſpecyally knyghtes troyan champyowne day hath ſlayne rydynge vp downe myn auctour guydo lyſt endyte saue hym ferther wryte boke yeueth hym ſuche name manhode knyghtly fame grekes put vnto flyght day tyll drewe nyght morowe dawenynge grekes haue phebus vpryſynge yarmed great dylygence agayne troyans ſtande diffence amonges day rede well hym bare worthy dyomede many troyan thorugh cruelte hath loſte lyfe tyll troylus gan ſe dyomede felde rydynge anone without lettynge ſpere threwe reſte troylus rode ſmote hym ye breſte myghtely nede downe horſe ſmote dyomede albe wounde hadde damage furyouſly troylus rage ofenuye gan hym abreyde whan downe loue creſeyde deceyte trecherye grekes faſte gan hye amonge hors myſchefe lay drawe hym haſte may ſhelde broſyd affrayde bare hym home ſo diſmayde ſtroke home vnto tent menelay ſame whyle hath hent myghty ſpere auenge dyomede troylus faſte gan hym ſpede fully auyſed vnhorſe hym anone troylus firſte made ſtede gone ſwyfte courſe towarde menelay anone erthe lay myghtely hyt hym ſpere ſhelde plate myght hym nat ſaue hym mortall wounde kynghtes anone hym founde preſe whan hym rent bare hym home owne tent grekes aye ſtondynge diſtreſſe thorugh knyghthode ye hye proweſſe troylus whiche hath ſo belayne euery part rode playne tyll vnto tyme agamenowne felde valyd downe many worthy aboute banere ſhone full ſhene agayne ſonne clere wt knyghtꝭ hym rydynge enuyrowne ſore enchaſed troye towne woundeth ſleeth put flyght hym ſelfe acquytynge lyke manly knyght without abode amonge troyans fyerſly rode worthy kynge great agamenowne ſpere troylus ſmette hym downe maugre grekes gayneth ſocour whan ſawe theyr lorde gouernour ſuche myſchefe grounde lyende hente hym vp made hym aſcende thorugh theyr manhode ſtronge ſtede wyt gan take hede conſyderyd wyſely thought diſioynt troylus thē brought grekes theyr great pryde tofore ſwerde myght nat abyde prudently hye diſcrecyon noble knyght kynge agamenon hadde aye aduertence gouernaunce thorugh prouydence whan ſawe grekes gan fayle wexe feble ſtande batayle lacke ſtuffe ſhulde recomforte full prudently made reſorte eueryche owne tent hath pryam ſent atrewes troye cyte ſixe monethes myght counſayle pryamus kynge without abode graunted axynge albe ſome guydo lyſte endyte euyll apayde ſo longe reſpyte theyr mortall foon maner wyſe yet graunt ye haue herde deuyſe stode ſtrengthe fully rede whiche tyme womanhede creſeyde lyſt lenger tarye though hir fader therto contrarye vyſyte haue ſyght dyomede come hir kynght ¶which troylus late caught woūde tent whan ſhe hath hym founde benygnely vpon beddes ſyde ſet hir downe ſelfe tyde platly caſte hir owne thought touchynge troylus yt nought lyue hope recure thought ſhe wold thynge vnſure purueaunce without ſtore gaue anone without hooly hir herte vpon dyomede lo pyte womanhede mercy eke benygne routhe newly hir olde trouthe nauture lette ſlyppe aſyde rather ſhulde ſe abyde man myſchefe theyr ſake chaunge nat ſo redy make lombarde ſtrete crowne doket poyſe good ſo prent ſet theyr lettre chaunge doth man abyde wynde redy tyde paſſage aye ſo lyſte pace man loſte lyſte ſeke grace daunger none counterfete diſdayne ſee calme rockes playne mercyles neuer man ne deyde ſoughte grace recorde creſeyde whiche fynally hath gyuen hir herte dyomede releſe ſmerte prayed hym right glad lyght calleth hym hir owne man hir knyght hym behyghte rather deye euery thynge howe ſhe wolde obeye honeſt hym pleaſaunce leuer ſhe chaunge varyaunce founde hir lacke pyte ſyctynge femynynyte nature nat vengeable fayth othe rather mercyable mannes lyfe ſtandynge diſtreſſe wyll dreſſe tell forth tranſlacyon ceryouſly agamenon durynge trewes tyme pee hym ſelfe wente vnto achylles beſechynge hym ſome rewarde haue knyghthode grekes ſaue preſence nomore withdrawe ſuffre ſo mortally ſlawe theyr enmyes pompous elate achylles alway indurate ilyche newe bothe herte thought purpoſe platly chaungeth nought fully enclyned haue pee aſmoche achylles entyerneſſe affeccyon louynge agamenon vnto hym graunted leſte great parcell touchynge requeſte ſaye achylles graunteth hym myrundones full knyghtly men oonly abſence grekes make reſyſtence felde agayne towne whiche graunte kynge agamenowne duke neſtor thanked hym herte alwaye contynuynge ſmerte loue fayre polycene ne knewe gayne woundes grene diſpeyred languyſſheth euer one whan trewes paſſyd gone vpon adaye morowe full benygne achylles knyghtes dyde aſſygne felde take agamenon ſtorye maketh mencyon gaue bendes freſſhe rede men may knowe theyr manlyhede withholde ſpecyall lyke man deedly mortall tent achylles abode felde hym whan rode oonly dole ſhulde hym twynne abſence werre begynne maugre wyll agayne towne forthe went agamenowne vpon troyans ſterne full pryde mette ſyde manly knyghtes troyanyſſhe blode whiche ſo furyous wode cruelly grekes oppreſſe backe fere gan dreſſe ſo inly felle kene tyll duke athene entrede grekes diffende vpon hym vnwarely wende came myghty troylus lyke wood lyowne ſtede anone bare hym downe put hym ſo prees tyll mette myrundones ſlewe daye full many one ſo fet troylus ygone grekes put vtterly flyght thorugh knyghthod tyl drewe nyght fro ſwerde raunſoū myght thē borowe guydo wryte next morowe full mortall ſlaughter outher ſyde amyd felde togydre ryde manly knyghtes wonder ſene faughte kynge phylymene helpe oonly pollydamas taken hath worthy kynge thoas gan hym lede towarde troye towne myrundones hym come downe wonder proudely gan ſewe thurgh myght thoas reſkewe hym delyuer ſo ſtronge troylus hurtled amonge furyouſly lyke champyowne caſte threwe thē downe ſlewe ſome made blede tyll cruelly ſlewe myghty ſtede whiche ſat yet neuertherles faught fote agayne myrundones hadde caſte troylus haue take parys tho gan ſo wake brother aboute hym rode place troylus ſtode vpon fete hym ſelfe alone myrundones ſlewe many one knighthod thorugh theyr manlyhede vnto hym brought another ſtede amyd foon made hym aſcende full knyghtly gan hym ſelfe diffende ſet grekes ſelfe ſtounde neuer yet better knyght founde felte well foon brother callyd emargaron faught puttynge hym ſelfe prees ſlayne ala amonge myrundones deth cruell yre troylus angre newe ſette fyre playnely purpoſeth auenge may ſwerde began make way parys aye faſte rydynge brother vpon hym awaytynge whiche yfere ſo mercyles fynde vpon myrundones force neceſſyte compelled playnely fle troylus ſo furyous vengeable eke ſo deſpytous gaue many mortall wounde yet ſothe day founde noble knyghtes quyt wonder wele crafte knewe euerydele longynge army rede made theyr ſydes blede thorughe mayle theyr plate ſhene ne myght playnely nat ſuſtene ſwerde troylus chaſyng ouerall albe kepte cloſe wall hole togydre wente nat ſonder troylus aye chaſeth yonder ſeuered maugre theyr myght tyll felde many worthy knyght came menelay kynge agamenon vlixes eke cruell thelamon dyomede whiche woundes grene recuryd ſayth myn auctor clene troyans ſodaynely fall theyr wardes theyr knyghtes tho began fyght renewe euery halfe blody hewe plate bryght newe ſteyned troye ſo manly haue peyned agayne theyr foon myghty ſtryfe many greke berafte lyfe moſte myghty batayle troylus came gan aſſayle euery parte many blody wounde knyghthode gan comfoūde aye fledde ſo aferde mortall ſtrokes ſharpe ſwerde theyr deedly foo deſtruccyon contynueth tyll kynge thelamon manhode whan behelde grekes made recure agayne felde gan troyans aſſayle wonder ſore tho began ſlaughter eche ſyde tyll troylus newe agayne grekes hathe ſo fyerſly ouerlayne myrundones euerychone afore ſwerde made gone theyr tentes felde ſake honde day hath take hondred knyghtes came weye thorugh proweſſe ſent troye euer one gan ſo enchace myrundones loſte theyr place achylles lyenge tent repeyre forwounde rent theyr harneys broke bothe plate mayle nombre fynde fayle hondred knyghtes ſlayne deed ala founde taas amyd felde thorugh gyrt wt many woūde troylus ſwerde ector ſecounde wherof achylles whan hadde ſyght heuy nexte nyght bedde walo wynge fro deuoyde ſlepe conſtreynt wo herte wounde ſo kene men fayre polycene wyttynge well dyde payne venged ſhulde nat attayne wyſe vnto deſyre thus brent double fyre loue ire made hym ſhyghe ſore cauſe loue aferde agayne towne ꝑſone offencyowne lyſte pryamus eccubathe quene offended namely polycene thus ſtode double weer herte ſatte hym wonder neer many wonder dyuers fantaſye haue louers poynt dye ryght euen ſo fareth wofull man woo rede ne entryked wende deye recure knewe better weye whyle lay throwes whyte lyke guydo playnely lyſte endyte ſtorye maketh mencyowne dayes ſeuen troye towne encreaſe augment theyr ſorowe grekes mette euery morowe thorugh force bothe theyr myght outher parte ſlayne many knyght whyle lay achylles grekes deth ylyke reckeles loue oonly toke maner hede ſo hole mortally dothe blede playneth woundꝭ large hym thought parcell charge moche hath thynge thynke ofte waketh whan ſhulde wynke thoughtfull aye ymagynatyfe wery owne lyfe tyll daye kynge agamenon seynge deth deſtruccyon grekes halfe without remedye troye ſent enbaſſatrye trewes certayne dayes ſpace myght therof haue grace lenger tyme platly endure leyſer sepulture worthy knyghtes deed aforne felde outher party lorne whiche taas full beſely ſoughte playnely wroughte durynge ſege great vyolence ſhall deſcryue pacyence ¶how achylles ſlewe worthy troylus ectors brother vnknyghtly trayled hym aboute felde hors tayle ca xxxi cruell force mortall yre martys myght alway ſet fyre wt newe enuye gonne olde hatrede brēnynge hertꝭ hote glede atwyxe grekes troye cyte whiche lykely nat ſtaunched tyll deth conſume mortall darte full many worthy vpon outher parte execute ala fynall fate eche enuyous deedly hate whiche ne myght deſtyne remewe parchas lyberte eſchewe antropos wyll ſuffre none mayſtreſſe guyder therother dethes ſhyp tyll goth vnto wrake fortune gan tourne hir face bake hye diſdayne fro troye cyte ſtorye right ſoone ye ſhall ſe whan trewes hadde take wered gan redy make proude grekes felde gone vpon morowe whan phebus bryght ſhone armed full ſhene eueryche deuyſe menelay firſte mette parys daye ſtorye rede eche ſmet ſtede • whiche tyme daūz pollydamas vlixes rode ſterne paas eche cruell enmyte ſtyffe ſwerdes gan togydre flee nouther manhode wyte aſpere ſquared byte myghty duke called meneſte rode lyne ryght myght ſe anthenor troyan full pryde ſadell caſte hym downe aſyde furye hatefull tene tho haſte came kyng phylemene oonly helpe towne gan aſſayle kynge agamenowne thorugh knyghthode hardyneſſe hym hadde brought great diſtreſſe outter myſchefe confuſyon ne hadde oonly kynge thelamon full proudely came hym reſkewe ſore gan purſewe ſpere vpon phylemene hors layde hym grene maugre force ſtorye telleth thus hym mortally irous yonge archylogus mortall couts ran vnto brumus one ſones pryamus kynge yonge delyuer beſte lykynge hym ſmette ſo great myght fell deed freſſhe luſty knyght deth whan troye eſpye made ſhoute pyteouſly gan crye wofull routhe deth complayne tyll noyſe gan vtterly attayne troylus erys platly rode lenger abode place felly gan approche ſwerde ſette broche without routhe grekes hatefull blode mercyles hym withſtode ſlewe daye cruell auenture greke none y• whiche myght endure tofore ſwerde gan ſo oppreſſe knyghthode hye proweſſe hadde put vtterly flyght ne hadde ben manhode myght myrundones whiche day one aſſent vpon troylus lay wherof full melancolyus courage manhode moſt famous ne lyſte lenger lette attones vpon ſette furyouſly gan amonge ryde ſome ſmote euen thorugh ſyde thorugh body ſome thorugh y• herte ſwerde thorugh doublet ſherte thorugh ſhelde plate thorugh haberion percyd hath lyke wood lyon ſlewe day many one maugre fledde euerychone grekes eueryche tent troye went swyftly hors tyll haue take ſuche murdre grekes make fynally better reſkuſe oonly deth ſo paſſyngly confuſe grekes myſchefe deſolate troylus ſo narowe brought thē chekmate coude better remedye hydouſly wayle crye deth forwounded gryſely chere achylles whan gan firſte dredefull noyſe wofull ſowne cauſed refleccyowne eyre agayne ſo coude knowe rochys harde kauernys lowe lyke one worde ſpoke two men wont called ecco confuſe lamentacyowne grekes ſyde whiche deedly ſowne pyteouſly achylles ronne lay agayne hote ſonne mortall woundes yeldynge vp breth roumble ſwowhe reſownyng deth suche noyſe grekes made ment achylles dyde enquere cauſe theyr clamour tolde hym lacke ſocour grekes eche centorye troylus ſlayne ſo victorye goth fynally troye towne euermore concluſyowne many greke lay ſlayne tent gapynge vpwarde blode yſpent thorugh conſtreynt woūdes ſmerte whyle achylles gan aduerte full ſodaynely came hym man whiche tale euen thus began ala quod may ye ſuſtene ſe men hereupon grene afore youre face ſlayne lye dede lyſte nat one take hede ſtonde ſtylle penſyfe tent vpon poynt ſelfe ſhent haſty houre ye abyde fyfty thouſande knyghtes beſyde redy armed plate mayle caſte playnely attones ſayle doute vnarmed ye ſtonde ye knyghthode manly take honde reſyſte ſelfe place lyke man mete face whiche anone cruell mode achylles lyke wode armed hym fomynge bore farewell loue ſette ſtore haſty hete yre ſo kene forgat fayre polycene hir beaute yt whylom made hym ſmert rage vp anone ſterte toke ſtede lyon wroth agayne troyans felde goth lyke wolfe hunger gnawe right ſo gan agayne foon drawe rode without excepcyowne woundeth ſleeth kylleth bereth downe lytell throwe troye gan ſwerde knowe whiche infecte newe theyr blode none yet yt hym withſtode mortally gan aboute hym layne deed bodyes enlonge playne tyll caſuelly troylus gan eſpye achylles caſte eye gan hors ſpores conſtrayne rode hym myght payne achylles hym ware alſo smette ſtede made hym go towarde troylus ſelfe tyde full courſe togydre ryde full lyne ryght theyr ſperes ſharpe whette ſuche myght haue togydre mette hye diſdayne ſayne grounde felle bothe twayne achylles caught ſuche wounde body ſo depe profounde longe lay myn auctor ſayth certayne helthe reſtored agayne troylus eke thorugh plate mayle wryte guydo hadde wounde ſmall whiche vnto hym dyde greuaunce thus daye contynuaunce dayes ſixe ſuynge proude grekes mette cruelly amyd felde troye towne great damage confuſyowne outher party playnely nay many worthy ſlayne day day theyr rancour hertely hoote enuye albe guydo doth nat ſpecefye none theyr name playnely boke ye ſhall fynde ye lyſte loke al whyle ſodeyn thȳge penſyfe tryſte pryamꝰ ye kynge achylles tourned hath ſo clene herte away fro yonge polycene chaunge ſo ſodayne ſo newe thought beheſtes nat trewe deceyte doubylneſſe fraude falſly newe fangylneſſe ſleyghty treaſon vncouert gyle rage loue laſteth whyle vtterly founde beheſte lyke wynde man may areſte fareth worde diſcordaunt fro dede whiche wyſe man take ſhall hede lette paſſe reckeles albe achylles whylom caught within loues ſnare hym lyſte nat nowe one toſpare hye rancour lady offende nat lyke troye wende eccuba nouther polycene ¶wherfore pryam ſpake vnto quene angre gan hir abreyde ſhe hir truſte ſo entyerly leyde achylles ſo falſly mene wherfore full tryſte polycene enclyned hir eyen clere counſayle hir moder dere haue weddyd achylles fyne oonly ſhulde haue pee wene grekes troye towne falſe concluſyowne fyne trouthe yſene whan achylles woundes grene fully curyd certayne day gan compaſſe euer may ymagyne enuyous herte vengyd woundes ſmerte vpon troylus ſtacke aye mynde auauntage myght hym fynde hym bare ſo paſſyngly hatrede herte brennynge glede whiche day nyght may degre fully queynt tyll auengyd hoote rancour gan ſo hym gnawe auyſed platly ſhalbe ſlawe hondes whan ſo falle day hym gan calle myrundones knyghtes euerychone vpon morowe whan grekes gone tofore towne ſtele armed bryght agayne troyans purpoſe fyght come proudely felde oppoſyt many ryche ſhelde newely depeynt coloures freſſhe fyne vpon whiche full bryght gan ſhyne firy tytan golde treſſyd ſpere vpryſte bemysclere whan felle enuyous achylles knyghtes called myrundones vpon troylus gan hym complayne beſechynge theyr payne agayne troylus felde day catche hym myſchefe may beſely theyr dyllygence hym haue theyr full aduertence one aſſent ſo ryde thynge ſette aſyde nought ellys take hede saufe fynally agayne hym procede myght catche hym trappe within ſelfe troylous clappe encloſe ſette hym rounde aboute wyſe go nat oute whan beſet amonge alle nat ſlee hym ſo euer falle thorugh theyr myght māly hym cōſerue tyll hym ſelfe come make hym ſterue ſwerde none wyght loo manhode preyſe ryght vengeaunce deth rancoure pryde compaſſyd treaſon knyghthode layde aſyde worthyneſſe enuye ſlawe falſhede lofte trauthe backe ydrawe ala armes ſhulde falle trecherye bytter galle shulde worlde many knyght befoūde trauthe ordre bounde ala ala achylles conſpyred hath myrundones dethe one worthyeſt wyght euer beſte knyght ala wo herte fele dede ſake ſtorye whan rede whan fortune hath thynge ordeyned though euer wayled compleyned gayne remedye though men galen aye crye touchynge matere wryte forth lyke ye ſhall myrundones haue theyr lorde behyght theyr power theyr full myght fulfyll cōmaundement felde grekes went troylus firſte oppoſyte knyghthode hathe ſo great delyte without abode manly mete ybrent ſo feruent hete hardyneſſe hye courage worthyneſſe vaſſelage hym ne lyſte lenger abyde folke began ryde amonge grekes folke hye renowne wt ſwerde woūdeth bereth downe sleeth kylleth vpon euery halue mortally may ſalue theyr ſorys ſounde deth ſo rode yeldynge vp breth furyouſly gan enchace made leſe lytell ſpace theyr londe echone afore hym flee troylus ſwerde ſuche crueltee maugre felde hath wonne ſame tyme whan bryght ſonne hye ſouthe mydday marke ſhoone euen houre whan drewe noone whan myrundones gadred one compaſſe wyſe rounde aboute hym gone furyouſly one entencyowne made cercle aboute hym enuyrowne whan ſawe hym helpe deſolate herte nat diſconſolate vpon ſyde thorugh manlyhede lyke lyon toke hede thorugh famous knyghtly excellence tygre ſtondeth diffence manfully gan encoumbre gan leſſe diſcreaſe theyr noumbre ſome maymeth woundeth y• dethe ſome made yelde vp brethe ſome layde erth lowe ſome made ouerthrowe ſwerde theyr blode wete great myſchefe vnder hors fete vpon ſtede ſturdy wall worthy knyght man moſt marcyall playeth pley amonge myrundones hym ſelfe god wot alone helpeles tho ala myght force auayle whan thre thouſande knyghtes hym aſſayle euery parte bothe lengthe brede cowardly firſte ſlewe ſtede theyr ſperys ſharpe quare grounde whiche ala ſtante grounde without reſkus refute ſocoure day chyualrye floure welawaye haue hym ſo beſet hede ſmote baſenet brake harneys hym aſſayle ſeuere ſtele myghty ſtronge mayle diſarmed bothe necke hede ala whyle wyght toke none hede knyghtes longynge towne yet alway troyan champyowne knyghtly wyſe naked hym ſelfe diffendeth tyll achylles ala came rydynge furyous wode whan ſawe troylus ſtode longe fyghtynge awaped amate folke alone deſolate sole hym ſelfe myſchefe pyteouſly achylles wonder cruelly behynde vnwarely toke hede ſwerde ſmyteth hede caſte forthe cruell curſyd herte thought platly ſhulde hym nat aſterte ſhewe malys wolfe vnmercyable full vnknyghtly vengeable vpon body lay deed colde ala euer ſhulde knyght tolde wryte reherſyd ſo foule dede boke ala men ſhall rede knyght ſtorye ſo horryble vnto erys paſſyngly odyble achylles cruelte ala deed corp toke taas vengeably bonde fynde tayle hors behynde hatefully euery wyght behelde drewe hym ſelfe endelonge felde thorugh renges wardes alle ala euer ſhulde falle knyght herte ſo cruell hatrede ſo deſpytous fell drawe man dede thou omer ſhame rede aſtoned y• holdeſt thy ſelf ſo wyſe achylles ſette ſuche pryſe thy bokes chyualrye aboue echone doeſt hym magnefye ſo ſleyghty ſo full fraude gyueſt thou hym ſo hye pryſe laude certys omer thyne excellence rethoryke eloquence thy luſty ſonges thy dytees ſmerte thy hony mouthe doth ſugre flete yet one thynge thou greatly arte blame cauſeles gyue hym ſuche name tytle tryumphe glorye paſſyngly put hym memorye thy bokes ſaye wryte ſo thurgh knyghthod ſlewe ectorys two firſte hym lyke vnto none troylus yt owne brother thou arte meued affeccyon whiche thou haſte grekes nacyon preyſe hym ſo thou canſte endyte thou ſhuldeſt aye fauour wryte trouthe playnely indifferent ſaye ſothe clerely entent whan ſlewe ector felde afore diſarmed ſhelde beſy eke ſpoylynge kynge hadde beware cōmynge hadde hym quyt thorugh chyualrye falſe deſeyt trecherye ne hadde ſo lyghtly hym gone troylus alſo naked alone amyd thre thouſande cloſyd beſhet ¶whan achylles hath hede ſmet backe full hym lyghte pryde mortall traunce wounde felte ſuche greuaunce dethe lay huge whyle ſwowne ſpace halfe myle tyll myrundones aſſembled one great labour hente hym vp anone full deedly pale ſo gan blede ſette hym ſtede laſte herte caught agayne ſmet hors hate hye diſdayne towarde menon faſt gan hym hye whan comynge gan eſpye full lyke knyght lyſte nat abyde hyt hors ſharpely ſyde mette achylles proudely playne theyr ſwerdes togydre layne gan hurtle horsbacke yfere herte enuyous deſpytous chere kynge menon auauntage achylles wode rage poynt abrought hym confuſyowne tyll wardes newe come downe outher parte bothe yonder whiche ſodaynely ſeuered ſonder ſtorye telleth playnely began ſlaughter many manly man nouther party felde ne wolde leue pryde tyll drewe eue phebus gan aſſwage hete gan bathe wawes wete bryght bemys occyan fro felde home goth euery man theyr lodgynge ſeuen dayes faughte yfere made delayes full mortall cruell aduenture whyle achylles beſy cure woundes grene ſores ſounde hath newe treſon founde vengyd vpon kynge menon wytte ſet therupon ſo cruell enuyous achylles charged hath myrundones worthy menon amonge enbrace hym founde opportune place theyr myght theyr beſy thought theyr hondes eſcape nought tyll hym ſelfe auengyd hym ſo befell menon ſe nexte morowe lyke manly knyght agayne grekes armed fyght troye ſyde wonte auenture day fylle ſo achylles menon mette eche gan ſette horſe backe full great enuye ſo longe theyr melancolye myn auctor wryt togydre fyght eche made force lyght whan menon ſtode vpon grounde myrundones wente abounte hym rounde charged fyerſe achylle whan allas without goddes wylle dyſſeuered knyghtes alle myſchefe vpon hym falle deſtytute alone helples ſuche poynt ſlewe hym achylles ſtorye lyke founde menon firſte gaue hym ſuche woūde tofore deth felle ſtryfe diſpeyred playnely lyfe achylles falſe treſon take hede omer deme thy reſon falſe fraude ſleyghty gyle treſon caſte afore many wyle achylles iuge ryght euer ſlewe worthy knyght prodycyon recorde take kynge menon tytyle laude ala entryked fraude falla thou omer mayſte coloure though thou paynte gold aſoure thy wrytynge venym nat encloſe thorne hyd vnder roſe whoſe malys aye dareth rote though floure aboue fayre ſote men fraude vnder may nat ſe treſon ye gette wyll tell grekes day meneſte kynge menelay dyomede thelamonyus troyans paſſynge deſpytous cruelly cryeng oft ala deth ſuche woo trowe man lyue whiche coude right halfdele deſcryue theyr pyteous wo lamentacyowne certeyſe nat boy ſuche renowne drery wordes wepe crye complaynynge phyloſophye thorugh boke accuſynge aye fortune ſelde nought one contune ſo full tranſmutacyowne ſtace thebe make boſte ſowne dreryneſſe wryte nouther deth feſtes funerall makynge ſorowe aduerſyte let thy wepynge thou nyobe ¶y • e ſuſter alſo mellenger cuſtome haue fle ſo fer fro yere yere brother complayne thou wepteſt thyn eyen twayne edippus kynge thebe cyte thou wofull myrre calixtone ſo well rage bemene dydo eke cartage quene lette dole contrycyon phyllys eke thy demophon ecto eke newe doſt begynne crye wayle alſo thou corynne whylom ſo great affray deth oonly thy popyngay boke telleth v duyde let woo layde aſyde make comparyſowne vnto woo troye towne deth oonly worthy knyght loue euery maner wyght hye lowe olde yonge age falle newe ſuche rage coude theyr wo none ende whoſe ſalte terys wyll theyr eyen ſhende pyteous lamentacyowne euery ſtrete thorugh towne ala coude theyr ſorowes telle trowe certeys pluto depe helle tourment paynes kene nouther ſhe proſerpyna quene nouther wery woode tycyus ixyon hungry tantalus ne coude nat theyr bytter payne furyouſly wepe complayne troyans troylus thy ſake ſuche ſorowe make wepe kynge pryamus wepeth nowe face full pyteous maketh ſorowe eccuba quene ¶who wepeth nowe fayre polycene wepeth nowe parys eleyne nowe wepe vnto terys reyne troyans dedely ſwolle chere neded wepers hadde ynough theyr owne ſtore ala nowe euermore helpe ſole comforte deſtytute ſhall nowe refute nowe ector alſo dephebus troylus eke ſo vertuous dede ala ſhall theyr ſocoure ſuſtene werre theyr cyte concluſyon deth fully deſtruccyon theyr toures theyr walles ſtronge day alyſaunder full ſecrete wyſe vnto hym ſhall deuyſe wepynge eyen full heuy chere sayde euen thus lyke ye ſhall parys quod ſhe ala ſaufe goddes wylle thou knoweſt well fyerſe achylle ſones hath ſlayne nye echone none lefte thy ſelfe alone hath made ala gayne full cowardly child barayne bothe ector troylus eke therto whiche euery trouble wo fully comforte pleſaunce ſolace wherfore caſte playnely compace ſome engyne deth ordayne lyke treaſon dyde payne trayterouſly ſwerde ſmyte right ſo thynke treaſon hym quyte ſytrynge right equyte ſythe thou woteſt platly hath ſette herte loue clene oonly doughter yonge polycene fyne oonly haue hir wyue whiche caſte hym ſende blyue come treate matere temple appollo temple moſte chefe cyte whiche tyme wyll thou thy ſelfe armed full pryuelye certayne knyghtes thy companye armed alſo agayne ſame daye wyſe ſcape nat away handes dede haue ſayde therfore take good hede vnto thynge herte preye fro poynt poynt byddynge obeye aſſenteth hole herte behotynge hir ſhulde nat aſterte hym toke twenty mo manly men well durſte temple full good aduys yhyd byddynge parys whyle eccuba couert hir entent hir meſſager achylles hath ſent ye haue herde concluſyowne come haſte vnto troye towne effect hir meſſage oonly treate maryage haſte cōmeth hir ſonde coude thynge vnderſ • onde hir treaſon hyd playnely aduerte ſo hote marked herte • oues bronde firy glede oflyfe deth toke hede ſette aſyde wytte reaſon caſte afore good diſcrecyon lokynge full prudent ſothe loue blent troye whan ſhulde gone lyke fareth louers euerychone whan haue caught herte fantaſye peryll though ſhulde dye haue myght power warre tyll vnwarely trapped ſnare theyr maladye ſo furyous thus achylles anthylogus neſtors ſone haue way nome towarde towne togydre come temple ye haue herde telle parys tho lyſte lenger dwelle vnwarely knyghtes alle achylles myſchefe falle eueryche ſwerde full bryght ſome bokes ſay nyght whan deth longe afore deſyred eccuba parys conſpyred achylles mortall caas amonge naked hent ſwerde ſelfe ſteuen lyke knyght ſlewe ſeuen force maugre theyr myght whan parys therof hadde ſyght thre dartes raughte kene ſquare ſodaynely ware full ſecretely hyd vnder ſhade markynge hym noyſe made caſte hym euen euer hede ſhafte thorugh body ran therwith knyghtes nat fewe ſharpe ſwerdes gan vpon hym hewe lefte hym nat tyll lay grounde full pale deed many mortall wounde rightfully reaſon ſyt thus fraude falſhed quyt achylles hye treaſon deth deth ſkylfully guerdon egall mede without fable mercyles vengeable thylke day guydo wryteth thus achylles anthylogus parys temple yſlawe afterwarde body drawe achylle fro holy boundes cruelly throwen vnto houndes deuoured brode ſtrete canell rennynge wawes wete without pyte maner routhe lo ende falſhede vntrouthe lo fyne ſuche trecherye falſe deceyt compaſſyd enuye lo knotte concluſyon god quyt aye ſlaughtre treaſon lo guerdon fynall mede ſo delyte falſhede euery thynge platly ſayne lyke guerdon doth attayne ye may ſe achylles whiche nyght temple le lyfe aye cuſtomable fraude treaſon vengeable befell requeſte eleyne bodyes theſe ylke tweyne conſerued hungry rage beſte foule gredy ramage yet lay amyddes cyte full openly men myght ſe great gladneſſe towne tyme agamenowne kynge pryam ſent maſſagerys haue lyſence fette home berys graunt haue corſys take grekes ſuche ſorowe make pyte routhe eueryche ſpake thus vnto fere farewell truſte achylles dede farewell hope hoolly ſpede farewell ioye chefe diffence hadde manhode ſo great excellence farewell ala ſoueraygne aſſuraunce farewell knyghthod ſuffiſaunce nowe ala vnlykely shall euer wynne gette cyte v ala ſo frowarde fortune myght nat contune alway wo payne endure made haue ryche sepulture achylles ſtones precyous another anthylogus ſhulde lenger dwelle ceryouſly rytes telle theyr buriynge wo make theyr wepynge theyr clothes blake ſome loure theyr hode ſome go mylke blode dolefull herte fyre ſhete caſte gōmys ſwete amyd great flaumbe funerall playes called palleſtrall • wraſtlynge wake vayne vndertake telle wherfore lette fully purpoſe lyke ye ſhall ſe reſorte concluſyon telle great agamenon lordes haſte hath ſent whan aſſembled tent full prudently kynge manly man great aduyſe thus tale began syres quod fortune varyaunce hir chere frowarde double coūtenaūce ſodayne tourne hir falſe vyſage hertes hath put ſuche arage murdre god man odyble achylles cruell deth horryble compaſſynge eccuba quene ſemeth ſhalbe ſene manhode hertes knyghtly force aduerſyte endure vertue ſuffraunce tyll deth ye take may vengaunce manly quyte outragyous offence whan tyme cōmeth make recompence ſyth ye manly prudent wolde firſte ſe playne entent mater ſo wyſe hereupon aduyſe one aſſente voyce comune ye wyll werre forth contune ſege ygonne vpon towne tyll brought deſtruccyowne grece reſorte agayne cauſe oonly achylles ſlayne whylom ſtronge chāpyowne diffence proteccyowne fynally dede hereupon lette ſe rede saye openly lenger tarye ſome anone gonne varye grutche caſtynge fro stondynge doute beſte ſome ſayde tother ſyde lyfe deth wolde ende abyde ſome wytte rude theyr partye gonne conclude wolde home agayne retourne ſayde wyll ſoiourne styll ſege happe happe may thus treate longe day euery man lyke oppynyon tyll laſte concluſyon accorded fully one fro ſege neuer gone vnto tyme haue towne thorugh theyr knyghthode full poſſeſſyon theyr fce wyll ſpylle ſaue achylles buryed ygraue truſte euery worthy knyght fynally goddes haue behyght haſte ſhall towne poſſede hope fully deuoyde drede vndiſpeyred theyr oppynyon anone ayax thelamon worthy knyght famous hande amonge tho grekes lande sayde euen thus playnely ſentence syres quod preſence counſayle platly rede ſtandeth ſo achylles dede ſone haſte ſende hyder come ſe ende ſege helpe v nede ¶whiche nowe abyt kynge lycomede byſayel named pirrus ſome hym call neptolonyus right luſty freſſhe lyklyneſſe able attayne great worthyneſſe reporte fame
