kouthe drawe hym armes youthe ſothfaſtly bokes lye haue redde herde prophecye fynally troye cyte without hym ſhall neuer wonne thus bokes ſaye olde memorye grekes ſhall haue victorye tyll come ſone achylles wherfore haſte nat reckeles sende hym done anone cōmende counſayle euerychone rede fully aſſente aduyſe full prudently ſente haſte embaſſyat wyſe kynge full famous eſtat mene prudent noble menelay forth goth ſelfe ſame day iourney gan hym faſte ſpede tyll came vnto lycomede olde kynge ye haue herde telle wherfore tyme wyll leue hym dwelle grekes mene whyle directe agayne ſtyle ¶howe parys thelamon ayax ſlewe eche felde capitulo xxxiij tyme yere whan ſhene ſonne crabbe courſe yronne hyeſt aſcencyon whiche called ſomer ſtacyon whan vertue euery roote drawen vp bawme ſoote crop freſſhe floure moſt luſty hewe coloure tyll phebus chare deſcencyon crabbe towarde lyon holdeth courſe firmament mene whan retrogradyent dryeth vp moyſture wete herbe floure feruent hete veer afore hym made grene whyte tourneth bemys ſhene bothe ſede grayne decoccyon naturelly digeſtyon firſte rawe fruytes floures watery eke plente humoures dryeth vp rypeth fulle feruence men may pulle eche kynde ſeaſon fro yere yere reuolucyon theyr braunches freſſhely ſprede whan cheryes powbly rede firſte iune ſeweth may whan hoote mery ſomers day dwery lyke geaunt longe ſame tyme grekes ſtoute ſtronge rancour brent theyr enuyous hete haue ſhapen theyr foon mete bryght armed felde go troye towne alſo theyr wardes ordeyned euerychone felde haue take mete theyr foon gan aſſemble vpon outher ſyde thelamon foly pryde ſame day hym rede hadde deth drede diſarmed batayle areſt mayle plate bare vpon breſt foly ſurquedous outrage bare hede bare eke vyſage bare alſo without baſenet naked eke vyſer palet herode day thynge aferde hauynge wepen naked ſwerde wylfully lefte home ſhelde ſpere whan toke felde full lyke knyght ſyttynge ſtede hym foloweth dyomede lyke mar hym ſelfe aboute hym meyne faſte came duke meneſte kynge vlyxes agamenon pryamus wt troye towne toke eke felde wt full heuy chere bothe ferefull great diſpeyre inly full drede yſſue ector dede ¶worthy troylus alſo dephebus hym ſelfe demyd playnely thus feblyd greatly myght theyr deth grekes fyght goth hap happe may parys eke full knyghtly array kynge phylymene pollydamas ¶worthy eſdre eneas one aſſent ſeye ſame day knyghtly lyue deye theyr diffence vtterly iuparte goddes lyſte felde departe proudely firſte grekꝭ gan perce parys tho perce fyll aſyde ſonne ſhene archery arrowes ſquare kene grekes gan • ondre diſſeuere felde myght nat perſeuer • oonly ſhot ſtronge archery perce londe arbalaſterys whiche made fle right nede tyme proude dyomede whan grekes ſawe ſodayne flyght releue lyke manly knyght come vpon felly tene firſte ſette phylyment worthy kynge came troye ſyde whiche agayne gan hym ryde dyomede hath lytell wonne ſwerdes ſtyffe togydre ronne beholde noble ſyght eche quyte hym lyke knyght togydre ran horſe backe man coude nouther ſe lacke euer one troyans ſo felle vpon grekes ne myght dwelle kepe theyr londe ſo made blede maugre force dyomede ſlaughter ſo hydous ſo ſtronge thorugh y• felde wofull noyſe ronge mortall crye wounded folke lay slayne ſoyel endelonge way tyll meneſte ſyttynge ſtede worthy duke gan take hede myſchefe grekes beſet hent anone ſpere ſharpe whet smytynge hors felly ſyde thorugh renges knyghtly gan ryde ſtynt nat ſo furyous tyll mette pollydamas troyan knyght manly man vnwarely hym ran hytte hym ſo many mannes ſyght erthe made hym lyght ſwerde grounde whan lay hadde hym ſlayne ſylfe ſame day rage cruell tene ne hadde oonly kynge phylymene hym reſkewed auenture whiche ſo frendely hym dyde cure maugre myght meneſtee handes went free bathyd ſpreynt blode whyle ayax proudely rode ſurquedy wylfulneſſe foly rage foule hardyneſſe nakyd body hede euerydele amyd foon armed bryght ſtele troyans ſuche ſlanghter made lay dede bothe ſonne ſhade thorugh felde thelamon amonge rode woodder lyon troyan none myght hym tho wtſtonde whyle helde blody ſwerde honde wonder nakyd rode without wounde ſo longe abode guydo maketh reherſayle wryteth eke great meruayle vnſlayne myght ſo contune whan thynge ſhapen fortune myght befalle euer thynge wele wo ioye aduerſyte whan one ſhall dye whan ſhall eſcape ſhe ala alder firſte iape brynge aman vnwarely myſchaunce whan beſte weneth haue aſſuraunce lady tranſmutacyon lyke fyll worthy thelamon ſame day whiche foly pryde amonge foon gan ſo fer ryde ylyche freſſhe right began ſlewe perce many manly man hym ſelfe toke maner hede knyghtly herte ſo voyde drede tyll parys ſawe great hardyneſſe howe knyghtes dyde oppreſſe enchaſynge ſo mortally narowe without abode anone toke arowe entoxycat ſharpe venymous ire fell deſpytous ſhot hym ſelfe tyde ſayth guydo ſmet hym thorugh y• ſyde hurte • eye felte well muſte deye whan ſawe none remedye forth rode ſuppryſed enuye thorugh y• prees ſwerde ay ī honde tyme parys fonde vnto hym pale chere ſayde thus anone ye ſhall parys quod mortall wounde thyne arrowe ſharpe ſquare ygrounde hath fynally lyfe put diſpeyre neuer grece haue repeyre right ſo ſhall ſhort concluſyowne awaye ſhape troye towne thy lyfe thou entre ſhalt herte venym byt ſo ſore gayne none deth ¶but yet tofore yelde vp breth truſte right well may ſocoure thou ſhalt firſte predeceſſoure go afore depe downe helle pluto eternally dwelle right neceſſarye tyme ſet whiche may nat tarye trouthe morgage depoſe haſte ſhall make deuoſe atwyxe quene eleyne twynne aſondre eke falſe theyne whiche lynked coloure wedlocke hath ſo longe ſhet vnder locke oonly fraude falſe engyne alſo ¶but nowe knotte ſhalbe broke two right hande trouthe darayne thorugh cauſe oonly twayne werre many worthy knyght lyfe hath loſte many another wyght outher ſyde bothe ſake ſhall ende make loue foule auoutrye fynally parys thou ſhalt dye handes thy chaunce yt worde ſwerde gan enhaūce aboue hede ſmote hym face fyll deed ſelfe place hede partyd hath twayne right forth ſayne ayax ala mortall wounde fyll deed alſo gruflynge vnto grounde full pyteouſly troye haue parys take vp weye bore hym home theyr cytee dyomede duke meneſtee many greke rydynge enuyrowne sewed chaſe euen towne cauſe tytan gan lowe downe arke dayes bowe weſt vnder rowes rede eſperus gan lyght ſhede ſay drewe nyght grekes repeyred anone ryght eueryche lodgynge place take theyr reſte nyghtes ſpace saue rede agamenowne grekes made faſte towne ſette theyr tentes papyllyons habytacles newe manſyons pryde faſte wall troye diſpeyred ouerall refute coude grekes lette aſſent faſte theyr gate ſhette nyght walles wake ouer ſuche wo make thorugh cyte parys ſo dede fynally rede wepe crye ſorowe euer one y• ſones pryamꝰ gone fortune ala hath ſo appeyred theyr lyfe diſpeyred hope good welfare perpetuelly lyue care vnto deth faſt bye maner remedye vpon ſyde refute none kepe cloſe within wall ſe pyteous thynge ſuche wo maketh kynge parys deth deedly ſmerte hym thought platly ſorowfull herte recurles wolde ryue tweyne terys gan ſtyll reyne wolde ſorowe deye quene ala ſhall ſeye eccuba owne moder dere cryeth wepeth wofull chere polycene ſo wo begon ſuſterne alſo euerychone haue theyr heer theyr clothes torne hadde theyr owne deth yſworne drery woo pyteous peyne forby fayre quene eleyne wayleth cryeth deedly hir eyen whiche whylom ſo clere dyrked dolefull terys ſmerte corp ſodaynely ſhe ſterte clyppyd hir armes twayne pyteouſly enbrace reſtrayne lyke ſhe wolde hym dye anone ſtyll ſhe lay dombe ſtone marbyll colde hir lymes craumpyſſhynge redy towarde hir buriynge tyll men force corp hir hent ſhe hir heer chekes rent ſhe fallen rage chaunged ala hir vyſage hir natyfe coloure hir rody hewe whylom freſſhe roſe newe ſhe lyke vnto aſſhes colde hir handes aye togydre folde hir ſelfe ſhe ſmote hir pale face euer amonge corp ſhe dyde embrace hir ſwownes ſhe fyll grounde twenty tymes wept full wounde wo ſhe ſo wapyd amate comforte ala diſconſolate herte beynge inly deſirous thorugh hir rage paſſynge furyous dye attones hir owne knyght towarde deth encloſyd hir ſyght ſhe lyſt lyue trowe neuer man woman ſawe falle ſuche diſtreſſe ſuche diſioynt deedly heuyneſſe wo ſo pyteouſly yraue nat cleopatre goynge hir graue wofull teſbe fro kaue ſterte whan ſhe hir ſelfe ſmote vnto herte faythfull trewe oreſtylle whan ſhe ſawe hir lorde agayne hir wylle marcus prolancus vnto ſhyppe gone loue fyll downe deed anone ſorowe trewe iulia feruence faythfull porcia whiche one fyll deed ſodaynely ſhe ſawe blode ſpeynt ſo cruelly hir lordes dredefull grauement porcia ſo trewe hir entent whan hir lorde brutus loſte lyfe bycauſe ſhe myght haue knyfe colys rede ſlewe hir ſelfe ala nat alſo ſelfe caas arthemyſya quene tarſe londe manſalus graue whan ſhe fonde hir owne knyght whoſe bone ſmale full wofully chere right pale poudre made dranke euery morowe wo furyous ſorowe theſe echone yet may nat atteyne vnto ſorowe quene eleyne fynally wyll hir ſelfe parys ſake ſhe loued ſo hym ſhe wyll nat lyue day wreke playnely ſhe may vpon hir lyfe rather diſſeuere thus wo aye ſhe doth perſeuere hir herte parys ſat ſo depe ala ſayth woman nat douteles haue nature though ſo wo endure yet feyne ſalte terys fynde plente ynough theyr owne kynde ſorowles morne compleyne ſaye nat quene eleyne wo wounded herte fro deth ſhe wende nat aſterte dethes darte hir herte made ryue yet ſhe roſe agayne fro deth lyue oonly grace hir felle rage euery wo proceſſe muſte aſwage ouer gone waſted myracle eche venym made tryacle euery wo hath remedye though eleyne fayne wolde dye hir kynde ne wolde aſſent yet therto ſodaynely ſlee hir ſelfe wo woman man ſhulde hir wyte lyſte hir wo endyte lyſte vnto tedyous hir paynes furyous hir cruell wo lamentacyon whiche wolde meue compaſſyon ſothe wryte euerydele herte though made ſtele kynge pryam quene alſo hadde ſuche couthe hir pyteous wo ſe hir ſo wepe complayne hir felte aſmoche payne dyde almoſt parys hereof pryam deuys rage mortall wo amyd temple ſacryd iuno ordayned hath full beſy cure corp ryche sepulture haſte therin made ſhette ſothneſſe ſhulde lette totelle rytes gyſe made theyr paynym wyſe coſtes buriynge ſhulde longe tariynge ceryouſly thereon abyde wherfore nowe lette ouerſlyde theyr paynym rytys ſuperſticyous ¶how pantaſyllya quene amazone came ſocoure kynge pryamus troye howe pirrus achylles ſone ſlewe hir⸫ capitulo xxxiiij tell wyll kynge pryamus cōmaūded hath myſchefe nede thorugh troye towne oonly drede ſhytte theyr gate ſtrongly may therupon bothe nyght day kepe watche ſhortly troye diſconſolate theyr olde ioye refute wepe ſorowe make ne durſte vndertake agayne grekes felde gon tyll day kynge agamenon meſſager good auyſement pryamus troye hath ſent requerynge hym manhode lyke knyght yſſue grekes fyght wonte chyual • ye kynge pryam axynge gan denye ſhortly ſayde hym ſent ne wolde aſſignemenet nat one paſſe gate towne owne fre eleccyowne whan euer hym lyſte without compellynge yet ſothe cauſe tariynge ¶was hardy quene femynye towarde torye faſte gan hir hye hir lande lytell regyon whiche bokes make mencyon ſyght firmament plage oryent called reygne amazonys whiche cuſtome vſe oonly woman therin ſhall abyde wonte armed ryde haue armes great experyence theyr laboure theyr dylygence fynally haue excercyſe fro day day martes hye ſeruyſe ouer theyr cuſtome vſaunce day made remembraunce man ſhall nyghe nere thre monethes yere ſay iune apryll may woman haue cuſtome aye vnto ile lytell beſyde men ſelfe abyde fro yere yere togydre euerychone vnto men theyr lande gone abyde regyon tyll tyme cōmeth concepcyon without tariynge lenger whyle anone home vnto theyr yle repeyre countre vnto tyme delyuered faſte childe borne lacke kepynge nat lorne foſtryd tyll thre yere agone amonge woman right anone ile beſyde adiacent vnto men childe haſte ſent kynde maſculyne falle femynyne woman abyde ſtylle ſhall tyll actes mercyall full well experte ſhe eke knowe handle ſpere drawe bowe lyke ſtatutes regyon whiche bokes make mencyon ſette bytwene ewrope aſya lande pantaſyllya whylom lady gouerneſſe full renowmed ſtrengthe hardyneſſe thorugh world length brede yet ſothe ſpeke womanhede hir myght ſhe hadde huge pryſe bothe ſhe vertuous wyſe wonder diſcrete hadde honeſt name nat withſtondynge excellence fame hir renowne armes glorye conqueſt hye victorye moſte ſurmuntynge drede woman rede ſothely yet bokes bere wytneſſe womanhede gentylleſſe kepte hir ſo nothynge hir aſterte whiche loued hir hole herte ¶worthy ector hir myght oonly ſo noble knyght hir ioye worldly pleſaunce hir hertely eaſe ſoueraygne ſuffyſaunce ſothe ſhe wake wynke euer one vpon hym thynke fayth without ſlouthe vnto hym ſhe bonde trouthe confederat olde affeccyowne whan ſhe herde troye towne beſegyd grekes felle hardy quene lyſte lenger dwelle haſteth hir faſte euer ſhe may towarde troye full good array wrothy woman hir lande full well experte preuyd theyr honde well horſyd eke armed rychely fynde hir company thouſande maydens rydynge hir ſyde worthy quene durſte well abyde hir brought ſtele armed bryght loue ector hir owne trewe knyght hir way faſte ſhe gan hir ſpede helpe hym ſhe ſe nede thynge ſhe coude hir delyte towarde hym faythfully hir quyte hir luſte hertes ioye whan ſhe come troye herde telle relacyowne dede moſt worthy renowne ſhe ſo louynge ſo trewe anone ſhe gan chaunge chere hewe pyteouſly wepe crye fared ſothe ſhe wolde dye wo hertely heuyneſſe thought ſhe wold thurgh hir worthyneſſe auenge deth platly ſhe may grekes ſo vpon day prayeth pryam wt great affeccyowne open gate towne go grekes fyght may knowe experte ryght woman great worthyneſſe quene famous hardyneſſe ſo kynge hopynge beſte without abode graunted hir requeſte next morowe whā phebꝰ ſhone ful ſhene tofore goth phylymene noble kynge paffagonye hym knyghtes manye folowed worthy eneas troyan eke daūz pollydamas quene pantaſyllya gate called dardanyca towarde grekes proudely yſſued oute hir woman rydynge hir aboute whiche anone whan grekes dyde eſpye felde gan faſte hye firſte worthy meneſte pantaſyllya whan dyde ſe ſpores made ſtede gone ſpere rode hir anone quene aſtoned neuer adele kaught ſpere ſquaryd wele rounde ſhafte hede well grounde coupe ſmet hȳ downe groūde maugre hym reuyd hym ſtede haſte came dyomede cruelly quene • ryde ſhe faſte tother ſyde rode eke hym plate bryght ſhene mette theyr ſperys kene hytte ſo felle dyomede myght manlyhede ſhe hym made • adell leſe myght tho nat cheſe deſpyte men echone hath ſhelde hym berafte anone delyuereth proudely ſhe rode mayde vpon hir abode lyke tygre gredyneſſe lyke ſoth lyoneſſe dayeſhe fared rydynge vp downe amonge grekes tyll thelamowne gan beholde ſlaughter ſhe made hye deſpyte rancourouer lade myght ire nat ſuſtene gan reyne hors fall vpon quene whan ſhe cōmynge dyd eſpye fyll hym hir melancolye mortally maugre knyghtes grounde ſhe made hym fall grekes put ſo great diſray euer ſhe rode ylke day myght afore hir nat ſuſtene thorugh helpe kyng phylymene myn auctor recordeth boke amyd felde thelamon ſhe toke ſent hym forth thorugh hir hye renowne pryſoner towarde troye towne tyll vnto reſkus came cruell dyomede cruelly gan hym lede fyll vn warely huge route knyghtes rydynge hym aboute theyr handꝭ maugre al theyr myght hym delyuereth lyke manly knyght whiche tyme hardy quene anone hir woman aboute hir euerychone grekes hath afore hir playne wryt guydo ſo mortally belayne ſhe made neceſſyte felde hir ſwerde fle veryly incredyble leue maner impoſſyble ſe woman grekes ſo enchace whiche myght nat abyde afore theyr face felde wyſe ſtonde dryue ſelfe ſtronde downe clyffe ſalte ſee ſlewe ſo huge great plente fynally hadde deſtroyed euer vtterly accloyed ne hadde dyomede ſtonde diffence knyghthode made reſyſtence day party grekes ſtode ſturdy wall alone theyr helpe chefe ſocoure worſhyp honoure pantaſyllya made memorye repeyred conqueſt victorye hir woman troye towne vpon houre phebus goynge downe ſyde hardy quene armed ſtele rode kynge phylymene pryam hath great reuerence knyghtly receyued dyde dylygence refreſſhe euery maner thynge myght vnto theyr lykynge theyr hertes coude beſt deuyſe full goodly wyſe thanked hath noble hardy quene hir goodneſſe hir lyſt ſene helpe hym great nede offrede hir guydo rede hath treaſour rycheſſe hopynge fully thorugh hir worthyneſſe vpon grekes auenged kepe hym cyte maugre grekes whiche ſay nay rede day day ſtynte nat proudely aſſayle agayne whoſe ſwerde myght nat auayle mortally ſhe made theyr ſydes blede tyll menelay frokynge lycomede repeyred neptolonyus whiche bokes called eke pirrus whylom ſone cruell achylles ſe full huge prees grekes goynge enuyron ſucceſſyon borne heyre achylles receyued myrundones great honour great ſolempnyte glad theyr yonge lorde ſe echone made affyaunce eke ſworne bonde aſſuraunce lyfe deth hym trewe lyeges chaunge newe obeye luſt maner thynge agamenon kynge made hym knyght thelamonyus ¶with ſwerde gyrte anone pirrus sayenge hym ſelfe place y• bawdryke whan hym dyd embrace take hede quod myn owne coſyn dere reſemble manhode chere knyghthode eke worthyneſſe thy fader whiche ſothfaſtneſſe tyme ſo noble knyght ouer thy full myght auenge deth thou thy payne grekes worthy duke twayne full humbly began downe toknele ſette ſpore vpon eyther hele maner golde bornyd bryght wyſe pirrus made knyght ye haue herde full hye preſence great honoure due reuerence lyke cuſtome grekes layes ryghtes vſed tho dayes anone hath agamenon full glad great affeccyon delyuered hym fully ſentence armes hole without difference whiche achylles lyfe bare worthy fader ſhuldres ſquare next heyre lyne diſcent treſour alſo tent armure delyueryd anone vnto pirrus grekes euerychone eyght dayes ſuynge thorugh hooſt full ſolempnely halowe honour yonge knyght tyl morowe whā phebꝰ ſhone ful bryght lyght ſhyneth fro ſo ferre diffaced hath ſtremys ſterre lucyfer dayes meſſagere whan grekes gan plate bryght clere enarmed day ſoure ſwete fully purpoſe theyr foon mete manfully theyr tentes wyde agaynſt troyans began ryde warde warde proudely felde pirrus bare day vpon ſhelde faders armes lyke ſayth guydo ſame hadde vpon alſo cote armure became hym wele forth rode armed bryght ſtele caſuelly formeſt mette firſte pollydamas knyght troye full manly man furyouſly pirrus hym ran hors backe myghty ſwerde gan hurtle hym berde myghtely hatefull ſtryfe pollydamas hadde loſte lyfe ne hadde reſkus ben without tariynge phylymene noble worthy kynge oonly knyghthode worthyneſſe pirrus gan hym dreſſe ſwerde ſmet hym ſyghte hors made hym lyghte ſtroke myght nat ſuſtene ſothfaſtly worthy phylymene pirrus hadde ytake anone saue knyghtes aſſembled one paffagonye came hym rekewe pirrus aye ſo fyerſly gan purſewe vpon kynge myrundones beſet myſchefe amonge great prees many knyght noble kynge yſlayne reſke wynge ſtode deth ſo ſtreyt caas tyll fortune came pollydamas reſkus dyde full myght hym delyuere quyte hym lyke knyght ſotheneſſe ſuche reſyſtence pirrus knyghtes ſtondynge diffence aye myſchefe ſtode kȳge phylymene tyll pantaſyllya femynye quene hir woman great companye gan thynge auenture eſpye whiche echone delyte theyr armure day clade whyte veryly lylye floure ſnowe flaketh fro iupyters toure whytneſſe freſſher ſene felde hardy quene whiche firſte amonge grekes chees proudely falle myrundones amonges rydynge vp downe horſeth thorugh hir hyerenowne ſlewe vp euery ſyde makynge theyr renges ſeu • r wyde tyll thelamon furyous hete ſpere vn warely dyde hir mete arage ſmote hir playne ſhe anone full lyfely roſe agayne wt hir ſwerde ſo marketh thelamowne hors ſhe made hȳ lyght dow ne plat grounde handes twayne hir woman dyde theyr beſy payne make theyr quene hir ſtede recure whyle ſtode auenture lyfe worthy phylymene pirrus knyghtes hym ſo kene maugre men haue hym take geyneth nat diffence make grekes haue ſo ſtrongly hym beſet forth lad hym myght bet towarde theyr tentꝭ thorugh felde whiche thynge whan quene behelde hir woman aboute hir rode purſued without abode fynally haue ſo ſewed thorugh theyr force reſkewed maugre manhode myrundones pantaſyllya ſo mercyles vpon grekes neceſſyte thorugh hir force hir cruelte afore hir ſwerde durſt nat abyde whan pirrus ſawe hir great pryde knyghtes loude gan crye ſayde ſhame vyllanye woman ſo leſe theyr londe ſlayne ſo felly hir honde wherfore echone hertes doth reſume aſſent let v nowe conſume • ryde none away eſcape ſome remedye ſhape ylke day theyr force confounde shamefull reporte v ſhall rebounde perpetuelly ſlepe wake pirrus gan ſwerde take furyouſly knyghtly hardy quene happed pirrus knyghtes ſpake hirlyſte nat one tourne bake thret take hede platly ſhe hadde hym drede right proudely gan drawe nere hym ſayde anone ye ſhall thou pirre ſone achylles ſlewe ector knyghthode pereles thorugh treynys trecherye malys oonly falſe enuye vnware whan thynge dyde aduerte whiche neuer may herte grene ſtycketh remembraunce vpon deth vengeaunce ſyt well ſemeth vnto deth venged vpon firſte thy faders blode loue hym ſo gentyll ſo gode deth ſhuld y• world cōplayne nat oonly men theyr beſy payne quyte deth woman eke alſo theyr myght helpe eke therto right requyreth without excepcyon full execucyon ſtonde ſame plyte thou haſte v woman deſpyte power ſhortly ſentence thou ſhalt haſte haue experyence knowe force ſothely euerydele right ſhorte tyme truſte right wele felde ſhedynge blode ¶wherfore pirrus wexed gan wode tygre bore wood lyon frat coloure complexyon ire fell deſpytous toke ſpere pale furyous ran hir myght payne agayne warde ſhe lyſte nat fayne encountrede hym deuoyde fere pirrus firſte bracke hir ſpere myght hir nat remeue hir ſadell lytell greue ſhe agayne ſo ſore gan hym hytte ſtede may nat ſytte deſcendeth endelonge playne vp roſe full great diſdayne toke ſwerde honde anone made ſtede lyne ryght gone vpon quene paſſynge wortyneſſe inwardely hate woodneſſe herte yfret ſmet hir many ſtroke euer ſhe ſat ſtyll oke force hir yre pale efte agayne ſhe made hym auale erthe maugre payne thus fyghte laſteth twayne large whyle tyll myrundones haue take theyr lorde force prees made hym hors recure agayne tyme ſelfe playne baner deſcendyd downe worthy kynge great agamenowne kynges duke endelonge grene theyr wardes wonder ſene prudently felde batayled haue troyans mortally aſſayled ¶but tho haſte kynge phylymene ye haue herde reſkewed quene whan hath thanked hir worthyneſſe knyghtes gan hym dreſſe pantaſyllya aſſembled bothe one vpon grekes gan gone men may ſe ſperes ſharpe grounde eueryche bere vnto grounde men may ſe proudely without lacke manly knyghtes renne horſe backe woman mortally oppreſſe fell grekes thorugh theyr hardyneſſe oonly thorugh force myghty quene deed lay couerynge grene ¶wherwith came daūz pollydamas fro deth reſkewed hym eneas kynge eſdras eke troye cyte tho wardes gan togydre fle eyther partye fell furyous ¶but moſte neptolonyus pirrus hyghte y• grekes champyowne irous wood troye towne made ſwerde theyr fleſſhe byte pantaſyllya proudely hir quyte ne ſpareth nat mortall woundes wyde grekes ſlee vpon euery ſyde theyr confuſyon pirrus falle glawcon halfe brother pollydamas anthenor eke fader pirrus ſo cruell yre melancolye newe ſette fyre smot glawcon ſo toke hede amonge prees fylle downe dede pantaſyllya hir woman ſame tyde pirrus falle hir whan hadde ſyght rode vnto hir lyke manly knyght hurtle hors backe yfere auenture ſwerdes ſtyffe clere eueryche made alyghte hatefully fote ſo ſyghte longe outher myght wynne tyll made force twynne wardes went atwene mene pirrus hardy quene tyme daūz pollydamas wood ire herte amyd grekes brother deth mette loue ſleth without mercy hatefull tene alone worthy quene suche ſlaughter grekes make felde vtterly forſake gan toflee theyr tentes downe tyll dyomede ayax thelamowne pirrus eke made tourne agayne ſothe ſo ouerlayne ne myght day releue thus faughte tyll drewe eue moſte damage grekes ſyde tyll phebus gan bryght chare hyde lowe weſt ſhroude lyght vnder courteyne blacke nyght eyther parte thought beſte departe drawe theyr reſte toke theyr eaſe nyght may moneth ſuynge day day without interrupcyon faught yfere albe mencyon made therof wryte ſpecyall perſone generall euer dyde euell well troye boke fynde neuer adele saue quene lyke wryt guydo hir woman hondred hath forgo ſlayne thylke moneth day deth playnely ſhe may shall well quyt ſo fortune fauourable frendely contune hir face chaunge nat contrarye ſhe euery day ſo varye ala whyle ſelde one ſoiourne gan fro quene hir loke away tourne enhaſte thorugh hir vngoodlyhede antropoſe breke hir lyues threde ſtorye playnely ſhall lere benyngnely ye lyſte fatall houre harde remewe cruel deth nomā may eſchewe lyfe fynally eſcape specyally whan parchas haue ſhape approche gan may none bene ala whyle hardy quene ¶whiche day furyous wroth felde troye goth gan grekes proudely ſette alder firſte pirrus hir mette mortall hate indignacyowne ſhe haſte renges downe rode vnto hym ſwyftly hir ſtede whoſe ſporys ſharpe made ſydes blede mette theyr ſperes reſte bare ſo euen markynge breſte theyr ſhaftes ſothly tale gan ſhyuer peces ſmale without bowynge outher backe chyne neyther made enclyne saue hede forged harde ſtele pantaſyllya grounde wele pirrus breſte percyd hath ſo depe plate ſoth mayle myght hym kepe ſharpneſſe ſperes hede blode party rede whiche ſtroke whan grekes gan eſpye aſtoned loude gan crye attones noyſe ſowne vpon quene felde came downe compaſſe wyſe goynge enuyrowne thorugh hir proweſſe hir hye renowne hir diffendeth meruayle ala ſo ſore hir gan aſſayle hewe haue hir baſenet amyd grekes ſo thycke ſhe beſet ax ſwerdes ſquare hir hede ſothe made bare hir ſhuldres naked eke ala mayle hewen rere bra pirrus lyke founde anguyſſhe oonly grene wounde doute playnely ſhulde eſcape towarde quene faſte gan hym rape auenged ſo euer falle amyd felde amonge grekes alle whan ſhe ſawe came ſo faſte force oonly mete hym yet ſhe caſte hir ſwerde firſte gan hym aſſayle hir ſtroke happed hir fayle amonge prees ſo narowe ſhe beſet pirrus ſwerde ſo ſharpe whet ſodaynely hir arme ſmette ala none armoure hym lette raceth thorugh ſhuldre bone quene fyll downe deed anone malys • venge hym herte yre fret ſo ſore chere anger pale hath hir hewen pecys ſmale whiche foule cruell dede euer one pirrus ſo gan blede nyghe deth mortall wounde lacke blode fyll grounde traunce full longe gruflynge lay tyll knyghtes haſte may haue take hym vp layde hym ſhelde dolefully home felde haue hym borne wounded woman quene ala ſorowe inwarde deedly wo whan ſawe theyr lady ago deed ſo deſyrous haſte wood furyous rage without gouernayle grekes gan newe aſſayle auēge theyr quene ſo hertly kȳde ſlewe ſothely fynde two thouſāde grekꝭ thē ſo wode ala great diſ • oynt ſtode oonly lacke haue gouernour ſhe gone theyr chefe ſocour whiche alſo ſpeke hardyneſſe woman lady mayſtreſſe hir honde rede oye troyans ye ſtande great drede amyd felde gouernaunce day come vnhappy chaunce haue ye leder none gyde farewell truſte euery ſyde grekes vpon ſo ſtronge ye felde may nat kepe longe caſte felly quyte ſame day dare lyſte endyte wryt homewarde drawe ten thouſande troyans grekꝭ yſlawe theyr wardes came attones downe mortally without excepcyowne kylle ſlee withſtode moſte vpon woman wode auenged playnely rede euery halfe theyr blode ſhede without mercy remyſſyowne chaſynge troyans home towne felde none abode pyteouſly tho ſtode ne none otherrecur caſte kepe theyr towne ſhytte theyr gatꝭ faſte theyr hope clene agone fyght theyr fone theyr truſt knyghthode away theyr worthy men ſlayne weylaway refute none theyr cyte kepe cloſe may none thought myght kepe longe theyr walles ſo myghty ſo ſtronge hadde plente vytayle though worlde attones aſſay may ſure whyle kepe euermore man ſhall wyn ¶yet neuertheles erely eke late grekes made tofore euery gate full myghty watche awayte full ſtronge preuy ſpyes goynge amonge theyr foon none eſcape away none engyne ferforth may whyle within troye towne make deſcripcyowne quene ſo great ſorowe euery wyght bothe eue morowe ſhe ala ſlayne hir mede whiche came ſo fer helpe nede aldermoſte ne myght haue deed corp burye graue reuerence honour dewe whiche gan grekes ſewe great prayer great beſyneſſe vayne ydelneſſe theyr requeſte grekes ſo wrothe fynally many ſondry othe oonly malys hote enuye deed corp denye ſhortly ſayde mortall enmyte houndes ſhall deuouryd gayne theyr rancour cōpeſſe pirrus gentylleſſe ne wolde aſſent ſo foule dede wood wroth cruell dyomede sayde openly ſyttynge ſhe fayle hir buriynge ſlayne hadde ſo many worthy man thus ſtryfe amonge grekes gan great rumoure altercacyowne tyll laſte vnder troye towne hir haue dede corp ytake cruelly profounde lake haue hir caſte lete hir lye vnto troye agayne wyll hye tell forth lyue pyne cruell mar haſt made fyne thorugh thyne yre y• worthy blode troye ala haſt thou ſo wode agaynſt ſlee theyr knyghtes haſt thou lette thy bytter venym fall ala thou ſterre infortunate worlde make debate hatefull ſterre hote combuſt drye firy irous grounde enuye haſty euer full diſcencyon coleryk thy complexyon murdre deth aye thy delyte takynge vengeaunce moſte thyne appetyte firſte meuer anger hate rote contek cauſynge debate ſtryfe murmur moſte thy deſyre feerfull loke wylde fyre gaſtfulleuer thy wode ſyght leuen ſo flamynge thy lyght lyke twynklynge ſpakes rede great fyres abrode ſo ſprede conſumynge aye melancolye hertes enbraced enuye thy wrathe aye ſo fretynge ſo kene cauſeſt men longe lene conſumpt ſklendre browne cytrenhewed vnmercyable right euell thewed wonder ſleyghty engenyous compaſſynge ſuſpecyous tryſte ſolen full heuyneſſe aſſentynge curſydneſſe awaytynge deth roberye murdre alſo trecherye without remors conſcyence venymous thyne influence helper arte vnto falſe treaſon houſe scorpyon crowned arte caprycorne bole thy kyngome lorne therin thy deieccyon thy power loſte domynacyon haſte alſo thy ſubieccyon exyle werre chaynes pryſon proſcripcyon captyuyte thy malys troye cyte wolde god coude chyde ryght haſte kydde thy felle myght thy rancour hoolly outtraunce firſte vengaunce ſperes ſharpe ſwerdes kene whette pryſon encloſe ſhette vengeably dare nat oute grekes felle aye lyinge aboute nat holde maner wyſe thy temple ſacryfyſe neyther bulles borys wylde beſtes euer vnmylde tygres berys wode lyon whiche thou art ſouerayne patron nat holde brymſtone ſmoke thyne auterys whiche art ſo felly wroke ala nowe worſte alle thou haſte ſhad chefe thy galle amonge ſelfe brynge treaſon fayned trouthe ſymulacyon make hertes amonge ſelfe deuyde lo ſerpent diſcordecan glyde full ſlyly tyll haue caughte place voyde away happe grace venym diſcencyon whan ſprad regyon comon borugh towne cyte amonges men hye lowe degre whan hertes loue nat one farewell fortune theyr grace clene agone diſcorde holdeth reſydence well worſe ſwerde peſtylence worſe outher fer nere foo famylyere may harme hym luſte enmye vpon men truſte deſcryue ſhortly clauſe rote trewe cauſe myſchefe confucyon euery lande diſcencyon peryllous pryue recorde take troye cyte founde fortune frendly aye nede tyll longe byd hate gan brode ſprede prudence ſothly hath prouyded regne ſelfe deuyded shall recules tourne wylde waſte dweller deſolate haſte mar enuye lorde amonge ſelfe ſowen hath diſcorde agayne whiche may ſocoure worſe werre ſothly ſemeth treaſon cured vnder fayned pee roote olde anchyſes ¶with ſone called eneas daūz anthenor pollydamas haue contryued amonge vtterly vnder veyl concelyd ſecretly falle grekes troye haue firſt may theyr owne lyues ſaue ſome engyne ſleyghtes treate ſo may nat caſte maner weye wolde rather traytours troye pryuely ſo nat eſpyed couertly grekes ben allyed ſtonde hole towne trouthe wylfully neclygence ſlouthe suraūce othe olde made towne refuſe playnely concluſyowne allyaunce lette ſlake ſlyde theyr lygaunce ſette alſo aſyde theyr auyſe thought beſte caſte lyue reſte meryer eke erneſt game ſaue theyr lyfe wandre forthe ſhame wylfully dye myſchefe trayſſhe towne helde reprefe myght eſcape ſelfe lyue lyſte thynge towne ſtryue ſought ſothe ſoure ſwete mene waye lyue quyete therupon haue theyr way nome vnto kynge whan come preſence full couert wyſe vndercoloure began deuyſe telle theyr tale ſo fynally teyr counſayle pryam vtterly maner nat reckeles purſewe grekes pee ſo gette may yelde agayne kynge menelay without ſtryfe freſſhe quene eleyne ouer nat diſdeyne harmes done parys gon full yore cytheron iuſtly reſtore bvt ala falſe iniquyte counſayle roſe vnder ſecrete venym ſugre vnder galle well wyſte grekes alle ne wolde accorde concluſyowne haue pea troye towne whyles ſuche myſchefe brought treate therof ſothe nought pryamus eccuba quene ſones polycene yet left hym towne myght haue reygned longe ſucceſſyowne grekes full nat repentyd vnto pea holly hadde aſſentyd counſayle gyuen late sythen grekes well elder date proferyd firſte tenedowne aduyſe kynge agamenowne fynall pea ſhortly ſeyne wolde reſtore agayne eleyne amendes requyred reaſon damage wrought cytheron meſſengers firſte whan ſente pryamus wolde nat aſſente requeſte iuſtly brought pea meanes ſought pryde denyed wylfulneſſe ala ſo guyed lacke oonly wyt prudence haue wt coſt great diſpence ſlaughter men many great damage ſharpe ſhoures cruell rage abyde fully mortall werre full ſure wyll nat differre tyme forth treate pee lyſte thynge ſo reckeles vnauyſed ought trowe ye wyll ſo lyghtly go home grece without recompenſe wolde ſeme neclygence speke nat therof wyll nat tpecyally troye cyte myſchefe ſtande vpon fynall fate remedy ſhape late grekes thought right truſte troye ſtode theyr luſte holdynge ſelfe veryly victours theyr foon fully conquerours without doute ambygnytee counſayle ylke enee anthenor anchyſes ye haue herde treate pee ne roos ſothe doubleneſſe oonly treaſon hye falſneſſe pryamus conceyueth theyr chere lyke boke ye ſhall day whan pryamus ſone called amphymacus counſayle helde towne thre haue made ſuggeſtyowne vnto kynge touchynge treate anone diſcrete auyſe prudently wolde aſſente gan vndergrope playnely mente oonly wytte diſcrecyon put execucyon makynge therof maner delay proudely ſtondynge bay anthenor without reuerence spake kynge open audyence ſhortly ſayde ſterne chere thou lyſte counſayle platly thou mayſt cheſe thou wylte thou wynne leſe fyne thou getteſt worke thy counſayle kynge wonder ſoberly anſwered agayne full benyngnely syre anthenor ye ought nat greue myne entent nat repreue wyſe counſayle prudent rede conclude comon ſpede people ſauacyon wyte right well iuſtly reaſon vnder ſugre curyd galle preiudyce lyeges cauſynge myſchefe fyne wyll vtterly declyne right requyreth alder eaſe ſemeth ſhulde nat diſpleaſe thy conceyte none offence euery man holden prudence worſt leue better take wyſedome ſewe folye forſake remedye ſeke ſore worde troyan anthenor ſodayne ire gan chaunge blode abreydynge foot ſtode full felly ſayde vnto kynge ſekerly wonder thynge wyſedome auyſeneſſe blynded ſo wylfulneſſe ye may nat noſyde ſe great myſchefe aduerſyte vpon euery ſyde may nat diſſymule hyde diſioynt playnely ſtande nat foon alſo hande haue ſette walle rounde aboute fere dare nat yſſue oute ſo bolde vndo gate fyghte v deedly hate ſo feble ſo ſtronge ſothly yet haue amonge fyfty kynges worthy renowne confederat deſtruccyowne therupon platly wyll abyde whiche vowed haue theyr great pryde neuer parte henſe fro towne tyll walles tourned vp ſo downe ¶your worthy ſones alſo dede wonte helpe nede manly knyghtes ſlayne euerychone v ſaue remedye none vayne treaty diffence wherfore rede reaſon prudence ſlayne cyte leſe two harmes leeſt cheſe ſaye entent ſyttynge expedyent treate p • lenger feyne reſtore agayne eleyne loue many worthy man hath loſte lyfe ſythen werre began parys vnderſtone ygraue beſte rede ſothe ye may haue ſende hir home agayne menelay profre ferforth ye may reſtore within lytell whyle harmes done parys ile whiche men wont cythera calle rede afore alle yt worde vp roſe amphymacus counſayle full contraryous ſhortly ſayde ſhall nat anthenor hath rade degre euer thus without reſpyte ſpake hym hye deſpyte ⸫ ⸫ ⸫ thou anthenor haue eſpyed wele may truſte neuer adele v ſtonde great nede trouthe fayth nowe dede falſhede hath ſlayne ſtabylneſſe ſtede thy ſykerneſſe fynde ſothly varyaunce come fayth thy lygeaunce thy heſtys made ſtande thy kynge thyne othes ſo double menynge hyd thyne olde aſſuraunce come thy fayned falſe conſtaunce ſtede whiche mutabylyte hath take place lyke may ſe newe chaunge thou art ſo remewable vpon groūde thou mayſt nat ſtande ſtable thy trouth gone olde affeccyowne y• ſhouldeſt haue ſtande wt towne fayth v lyue deye truſte hope exyled aweye thy perſone ſhortly wryte beſy arte kynge excyte diſencreaſe eſtat royall vnto grekes ſo thrall ſeke pea drede thou ſhuldeſt rather thy manlyhede haue proferyd hym cyte diffende thy lyfe outtraunce diſpende wherfore ſothe aſſure rather ſhulde endure twenty thouſande ſhall ſpere ſhelde vpon day ſlayne felde thy worde holde prophecye procedeth trecherye doubylneſſe falſe treaſon vndermynynge prodicyon though thou outwarde ſhewe fayre venym hyd thy tale doth repayre lyke ſerpent ſtyngynge vnder floures fele ſuche counſayllours wyſe wordes deſpytous full bytyngly hathe amphymacus openly anthenor repreued counſayle ſo agreued seynge treaſon wolde mene tyll eneas gan go betwene floryſſhed ſpeche full flaterye gan tale ſo modefye lyke mente trouthe entent therin double entendement ſpake one yet mentetwayne amphymacus oonly refrayne attempre hym melancolye oonly tyll myght tyme eſpye lyke purpoſe may procede execute fully vp dede whan founde hadde ſpace vnder pretens trewe face tale gan breke oute many troyan ſtandynge hym aboute ſhortly ſayde concluſyowne touchynge diffence playnely towne henge hoolly balaunce bothe hope truſte aſſuraunce cyte taken haue theyr flyght fynally manhode myght knyghthode togydre ago grekes haue ſtoutely fyght whiche hath loſt many worthy knyght redy vpon v ſet dare nat gatꝭ vnſhet ala ſuppryſed ſo drede ſemeth great nede good aduyſe ſeke mene myſchefe ſhall v demene parte ſothfaſtly ſay knowe none ſo redy way prudently pea trete pryam ſodayne hete without abode chere face pale rancour gan interrupte tale attempre myght nat herte fretyngly treaſon made hym ſmerte myght hym ſelfe nat reſtrayne thus ſayde vnto bothe twayne anthenor alſo enee wonder greatly ye hardy trouthe ſhame ſo varye ye ſo rebell contrarye oonly falſe colluſyon v brynge deſperacyon lyeges ſhall nat fayne falſe entent catche v trayne ala may ye herte fynde agayne nature vnkynde whylom counſayle chefe euery thynge brought prefe ye abſent coude thynge fyne ala ye caſte declyne away fro barayne left ſooll remembre great adooll wyght ala ſo chaunge ſhall truſte man whan ye founde double entent ye nat thynke aſſent counſayle auys whylom ſent forth parys grece full yore ago anthenor thou woteſt thy ſelfe alſo thou firſte made embaſſatour therupon chefe counſayllour touchynge ſonde made exyon cauſe mocyon though ſoth parys ſhulde go grece thou woteſt well ſo ine durſte preſumpcyon haue ſent parys vnto cytheron without aduyſe auctoryte eneas playnely vpon grekes werre haue gonne trowe ſothe neyther konne excuſe hym ſelfe ye auyſed euery thynge wrought deuyſed execute counſayle tweyne whan parys went eleyne grounde roote ſpeke ſpecyall thou enee cauſe pryncypall preſent alſo whan euery thyng wrought grece whan ſhe hyder brought ſothe regyowne neuer hadde come towne thou haddeſt therto contrayre albe thou woldeſt thy wordes fayre thyſelfe excuſe audyence thou knewe nought offence fully vnwyttynge dede ſonnes euerychone dede ye meſe alone deſtytute counſayle chefe refute purſewe grekes pee foryetell reckeles remembre infynyt outrage mortall werre ſlaughter damage cruelte deſtruccyowne haue wrought hereupon towne veryly whan recorde deed nat accorde treate lyke ye deuyſe eſpye many ſondry wyſe entent right peryllous ſnare couertly vnder falſehede dare wyll confuſyon ye acheue entencyon fynally ye haue ſhape impoſſyble eſcape shamefully myſchefe dye without recure remedye fyne knowe doute treate ye aboute right anone troyan eneas ire rancoure ſo ameued agayne kynge ſwellynge herte ſodaynely dore ſterte hadde wroke full many worde agayne kynge yſpoke went way anthenor alſo pryamus ire wo sodaynely braſte wepe myght hym ſelfe nat anguyſſhe kepe anger frat vpon hym ſo ſore within hym ſelfe conceyuynge euydence diſcrecyon couert gyle falſe treaſon hym cyte iſhapen haue auyſed dredynge aye theſe ylke twayne ſome engyne conſpyred trayne grekes wolde hym betraye wherfore kynge caſte wolde ſaye shape away theyr malys withſtonde treaſon toke hande oonly right dede founde vpon ſelfe myght agayne rebounde full execucyon theyr contryued conſpyracyon reſorte agayne full dewe wyſe oonly gan firſte deuyſe treaſon treaſon conuenyent falſehed guerdon pertynent ſhamefull deth fynall mede wherfore ſhape great nede remedye olde pryamus calleth ſone amphymacus pyteouſly alone twayne terys drowned gan hym complayne anthenor eneas ſayde ſone take hede ca thynke thy fader dere yfere • ſones lefte lyue thou alone therfore blyue touchynge treaſon conſpyred yſworne euer falle let v toforne oonly wyſedome away make may firſte trappe take puruey euen lyche iuſtly may falle oyche whiche haue made v ytreyned haſt lette ſo ordeyned mater cloſe kept mewe fyne oonly nat eſchewe ſlayne equyte ryght place euen towarde nyght purpoſe playnely theyr ſake agayne houre counſayle make vnder coloure make calle thou vnwarely ſhalt vpon falle knyghtes ſworne vnto mater ſecre right anone amphymacus aſſentyd vnto pryamus accomplyſſhe full ſecrete wyſe fro poynt poynt ye haue herde deuyſe bvt ſothe ſayde full yore agone olde wyſe yt counſayle none worlde ſo pryuely ycaſte wyll platly laſte people whiche rurall sayth yt ſecretes whiche nat knowen erthe wyll make mynde diſcure owne kynde nature vp caſte diſcloſe thynge men wont cloſe let euery man beware gode counſayle go ferre abrode ſpecyally lordes haue great nede men ſtonde moſte drede great awayte vpon layde whan happeth thynge ſayde one ſpoke lordes mouthe falleth ofte full kouthe reported yſprad full wyde many coſte ſtonde aſyde ware ſodayne auenture ſome hap dothe aſſure wyll firſt hym reporte amys therfore ſothe beſte beware kepe theyr tonge purpoſe caſte ſhulde nat ronge ſpoke abrode amonge folkes rude gladly aye worſte conclude euery thynge whyle newe reporte varyaunt vntrewe reaſon thynge expowne wyll folke towne lyke purpoſe whiche deſyre fare wyſpe fyre whan brenneth bryghteſt blaſe sodaynely waſteth maſe ſuche folke platly tryſte fyre water holde theyr fyſte beynge bothe ylke indifferent hote colde lyke theyr entent newe chaungeth ſo theyr courage calme foloweth ſodayne rage day loue tomorowe hate truſte comon laſteth date lette nat lorde make ſecree counſayle ronne enee pryam wende hadde full cloſe rumour wynde aroſe falſe reporte ſo ferre blowe eneas anthenor well knowe ende gynnynge euery maner thynge hole counſayle pryamus kynge bothe two full one entent eke theyr aſſent conſpyred togydre ſworne couertly caſte awaye aforne fynally troye cyte theyr engyne ſhall deſtroyed accorde caſte playnely thus happe kynge pryamus sende ſhortly conclude wolde come ſuche multytude armyd men ſe nede hym ſhulde thynge drede eneas cyte great power auctoryte bothe blode kynred allyed golde greatly magnefyed thorugh cyte moſte ſpecyall myght power perygall ſayth guydo vnto kynge anthenor almoſte euery thynge vnto hym egall powere bothe twayne one herte entere conſpyred haue ſothe agayne towne fynally concluſyowne grekes myght haue ſurete theyr treaſoure go lyberte theyr allyes borne troye towne whan brought deſtruccyowne lyfe good • aufe without whiche tyme daūz anthenor eneas pryamus hath ſent accomplyſſhe fyne entent haſte ſo great route came knyghtes ſtuffyd aboute therof aſtoned pryamus made ſende amphymacus cōmaundynge hym chaunge purpoſe well wyſte counſayle nat cloſe ſygnes gan well vnderſtonde mater whiche hadde honde diſcured confuſyon bothe murdre conſpyracyon apparceyuynge warde ſyght great power troyan knyght fauoure eneas comon foſtryd whiche proudely open audyence tofore kynge declareth ſentence fully concludynge maugre ſayth nay none mene way refute gayne remedye oonly pea ſo denye eſcapynge playnely none therupon comons euerychone one voyce gan gale crye counſayle greatly magnefye albe kynge therto contrarye eneas lyſte lenger tarye differre fyne purpoſe wonder irous ſee roſe full vngoodly ſpake vnto kynge ſhortly ſayde without tariynge ſo befalle thou lefe lothe purpoſe pleaſed outher wrothe thou mayſte well truſt ſhall none fynally herken maugre thy wyll alſo thy myght ſame day yet nyght pea grekes ſhall trete whan kynge ſawe feruent hete bothe comon eneas gan anone diſſymule caas prudence clerely gan ſe tyme may none wherfore ſythe myght nat amende wyſely gan condeſcende purpoſe platly enee ſayde wolde goodly take gree accept lyſt ordayne ſo kynge lernyd fayne agayne conceyte platly herte otherwyſe coude nat aſterte coacte force vyolence whan ſawe aduertence myght dyuerte ſyde fraude ſowen ſo wyde without grutchynge falſly gaue aſſent anthenor ſhulde forth ſent comon choyſe treate towne whiche tofore concluſyowne grekes accordyd fynally touchynge effect ambaſſatrye fro poynt poynt wolde ſtonde varyaunt fro toke honde hadde afore hym full conceyued better chere receyued whyle anthenor oute treate grekes ſtoute ye haue herde pea fynall towne aboute euery wall troye gan aſcende blyue braunches many freſſhe olyue token pea grekes eke agayne amyd felde endelonge playne shewed myght ſene eke olyue luſty bowes grene conferme fro proynt poynt thynge ſtode diſioynt worthy kynge great agamenon cōmytted hath hye diſcrecyon fully power auctoryte grekes playnely vnto thre firſte pea trete vnto wyſe worthy kynge crete vlixes dyomede theſe mo thought nede wyll holde ſtably fynally nat varyable ende platly make therupon aſſuraunce take eyther parte bonde ſacrament ſo anthenor ywent aſyde worthy lordes thre whan theyr lyberte tumulte alone pryuely anthenor full trechery replete falſhode doubylneſſe gan purpoſe vnto expreſſe behotynge traſſhe cyte wolde make hym ſuerte firſte hym ſelfe hym eneas shall fredam haue euery maner caas theyr allyes goodes euerychone lyſte large gone theyr choyſe dwellynge towne theyr rycheſſe poſſeſſyowne without harme damage lyke ſe auauntage theyr perſones voyde abyde ſworne grekes ſyde couenaunt holde party reherſed afore ſpecyall theyr othes bounde varyaunce founde neyther partye platly ſtryfe behyght vp peryll theyr lyfe whan aſſuraunce thre charged kepe ſecre ſayd thynge di • curyd vnto tyme aſſuryd ende groſyd vp dede good toke hede lyſt theyr purpoſe perturbyd ſhent cōmynge without auyſement tonges longe large wherfore gan con • oure charge wyſe pryue wyghte thre none eſtate neyther hye lowe fully fyne theyr entent ne knowe couertly purpoſe hyde quod anthen vpon euery ſyde voyde away ſuſpeccyowne myn aduyſe troye towne wyſe kynge called taltybyus shall go kynge pryamus hore yronne rage coy porte ſleyghty right ſage therwithall ſadde demure ſtylle troyans thynge ſhall myſylle come treate pee aſſuryd wryte douteles troyans agree wyll therto euery thynge fynally anthenor grekes hath behyght thus ſhall deuoyded anone ryght thorugh cōmynge ſuſpeccyon tyll haue concluſyon ye haue herde parfourmed euerydele whiche thynge grekes lyke wele apoynted vpon euery thynge wyll olde kynge anthenor ſhall troye go axed eke alſo pantaſylle body haue cyte men myght graue dewe honour longynge hir eſtate voyde away ſuſpeccyon debate anthenor drewe eue grekes taken hath leue kynge repeyreth towne wherof made anone relacyon kynge pryam without delay haſte vpon next day made aſſemble cyteſens secretely deuoydynge foreyns anthenor open audyence thorugh halle whan made ſylence tale gan ſugryd wordes ſwete makynge bawne outwarde flete rethoryk eloquence chere worde none offence ſhewynge ſo circumſpect man coude maner caas ſygne outwarde countenaunce perceyue hym varyaunce harde treaſon eſpye effect declarynge embaſſatrye clere reporte anſwere agayne meanynge though nat playne vnderneth fraude fraught ſleyghty wolf tyl pray hath caught cloſe couert ſpeche ſerpent tyll may wreche hydynge venym vnder floures longe bee ſtyngeth tonge whan hath ſhad hony ſote sugre crop venym rote right ſo ſoth tonge scorpyon anthenor roote treaſon tale tolde face pleyne lyke ſonne ſhyneth reyne fayre ſheweth though weder wonder dyuers troubly ſe tygre full doubylneſſe couertly treaſon dyde expreſſe nat mente trouthe towne fully affermynge concluſyowne grekes myghty ſtronge lykly eke abyde longe day day redy aſſayle alſo plente vytayle concludynge aye remedye agaynſt holde chaumpartye ſtryue ſayde hadde yet lyue theyr worthy knyghtes hardy lyon theyr manly men theyr champyons whiche theyr lyues platly iuparte cyte caſte nat departe tyll theyr purpoſe acheued fynally nouther toure wall gate yren though ye ſhette grekes ſhall ſyde lette wyll v wynne laſte wherfore nedeth mene way caſte sythen myght fauour fortune may nat longe agaynſt contune wherfore quod ſo ye condeſcende right well thynge amende remedye ſo ye nat varye ſaye contrarye mene ſhortly doute embaſſatoure whan oute grekes laſte whan ye ſent ſayd goodly wolde aſſent vnto pea condycyon ye wyll make reſtytucyon harmes vyolences wronges done alſo offence parys wrought grece cytheron right ſemeth reaſon theyr requeſt meynt equyte dryuen neceſſyte vnto theyr luſte iuſtly enclyne maugre wyll werre fyne theyr eleccyon may nat make rebellyon mater ſo fer ybrought ſtryue agayne ſoth helpeth nought may apeyre thynge auayle therfore beſte counſayle prouerbe hath ſayde yore man conſtrayned ſore may nat flee falle trayne let hym cheſe leſſe harme twayne gretter prudently eſchewe let golde ye kept mewe ſaue lyfe make redempcyon better demeth reaſon spoyled oonly rycheſſe wylfully dye diſtreſſe lyfe better glode gode set nought ſauynge blode foly man welfare thorugh couetyſe golde ſpare lyfe dependeth balaunce let golde farewell go myſchaunce may hereafter ſort auenture golde grace good ynough recure ſythen haue tolde may bye pea fynally golde treaſour ſtynt eke werre foly playnely differre grekes vtterly accorde ſo recorde ye aſſent without varyaunce may pea perturbaunce ſo lyght recured ſoone aſſured iuſte reporte entencyons wyll wryte oblygacyons couenauntes nat hynde ye ſhall faute fynde whan aſſuraunce outher parte hadde therupon endentures ſhalbe made fayth ye may nat repreue fully truſte leue without fraude relacyon wyll make dylacyon ſignefye certayne hoolly effect ye wyll ſayne people loude gan crye one voyſe magnefye euer anthenor hath ſayde vpon hym haue charge layde theyr anſwere entent fynall recorde reporte thynge forgetten caas haue aſſigned alſo eneas hym go ſame thynge preſence olde kynge taltybyus whiche alſo entent ¶with anthenor troye ſent whiche thre haue playnely vndertake ye haue herde fynall pea make albe couert treaſon mente theyr way forth anone wente playne power cōmytted towne kyng pryam hath ay ſuſpeccyowne anthenor alſo enee ſhall deſtroye cytee hym ſelfe tryſte hertely wo ſayd ala beſte myſchefe falle yet worſte alle nowe thorugh myn aduerſyte bounde compelled neceſſyte maugre hede maner raunſon lyfe make redempcyon vnto foon haue moſte herte ſe right well may nat aſterte muſt paye gayneth ſocoure good golde ryches treaſoure moſte foon dare nat denye yet ſtonde lyfe iupartye without refute hangynge balaunce ala conſtrayned thorugh wofull chaunce obeye theyr luſte mortally hate dryuen therto byrthe thorugh fate parchas haue deſteny yſhape engyne may nat eſcape whyle pryam gan thus cōpleyne anthenor came quene eleyne beſechynge hym embaſſatrye gentylleſſe ſpecefye thorugh prudent medyacyon fynde away conſeruacyon hir eſtate fynally ſhe menelay may reconſyled ſo falle treate holde hir lorde grace wolde reſtore hir vnto hir degre oonly mercy hye pyte anthenor vnto hir requeſte gaue audyence makynge beheſte wolde herte entere dylygent treate matere therwithall hym ſhe toke hir leue thus done ſame eue anthenor pray god gyue hȳ ſorowe grekes went next morowe oonly treate apeas fynall whyle feeſt funerall holde troye myn auctor wryteth thus lorde called glaucus manly knyght tofore lyuynge ſone pryamus kynge ouer lyke ſayth guydo kynge pryam beſyed hym alſo pantaſyllya body myght conſeruyd freſſhely ſyght loue worthy quene puryd golde ſtones ſhene lete make veſſell full ryall fylde full bawne naturall kepe corp fro corrupcyowne tyll werre grekes towne thorugh treate yſtynted clene kynge called phylymene deed quene myght affeccyon carye home hir regyon auncetres buryed lyke maner olde antiquyte cuſtome vſed tyme vayne therof ryme paſſe ouer vnto tretee atwene grekes troye cytee partye grekes rede firſte vlixes hym dyomede aſſigned kynge crete anthenor eneas mete yfere ſhortly ſentence conduyt firſte lycence noble wyſe agamenowne entred troye towne conueyinge eneas whoſe cōmynge ſuche ioye comunes whiche thynges newe reioyſe aye thoughe rewe wenynge full well theyr oppynyon good medyacyon vlixes kynge crete dyomede came eke trete theſe thre ſhuld make faſte fynall pea euer laſte full ende theyr alder ſorowe therupon erely next morowe pryam lette make conuocacyowne worthy within troye towne whan aſſembled one wyſe vlixes roſe vp anone tale gan ſuche wyſe prudently wordes deuyſe herken euery man hath ioye ſpecyally troye inwarde menynge fraudelent full lytell wyſte entent theyr pleaſaunce ſo coude fayne firſte axeth thynges twayne one cyte wolde haue golde huge quantyte recompenſe harmes another thynge axed alſo without abode amphymacus ſone kynge pryamus perpetuelly exyled neuer entre troye cyte golde prayer raunſon done ſuggeſtyon anthenor falſe malycious oonly contraryous ſhulde treaty pee nat reckeles ſay trouthe amphymacus therfore ſothe ſerpent enuyous hath founde tyme byte thought wolde cruelly hym quyte trouthe oonly entent ¶therfore full expedyent prudence euery man charge tonge nat ouer large trouthes nat ſayne wyſedome ſomtyme fayne diſſymule aduerſyte specyally whan men trouble ſe theyr ſpeche may nat auyle better theyr tonge fayle folyly theyr damage ſpeke men muſt amonge kure ouer reke trouthe thynges oonly prudence humbly ſuffre pacyence falſe reporte folkes enuyous ſo holde hym vertuous better whyle abyde ſay rancoure pryde sylence ſothe hath ofte haſty ſtryfe hadde victorye prserogatyfe palme debate wonne well ſo ſuffre konne ſpeche nat preſumptuous tolde amphymacus nat withſtandynge trouthe mente yet worde exyle wente albe god full iuſtely afterwarde hath anthenor quyte rewarde ſame hyt falſeneſſe duely ſyt ſay iniquyte exyle captyuyte iuged proſcripcy owne relegat troye towne perpetuelly procurynge eneas loo right full kynge may ſe prouydence full iuſtly make recompence doubylneſſe ſymulacyon ſuche contryued falſe treaſon auengeth falſehede parte ſhall hyt ſame darte ſcapeth nat haue wounde falſehede aye wyll agayne rebounde roſe firſte orygenall reſorte agayne right doth ball fraude euer doth hym caſte truſte right well wyll laſte ſupplanteth ſhall ſupplanted good exaumple ye ſhall ſe anthenor ſtorye ye rede whyles treaty procede touchynge exyle proſcripcyon captyuyte relegacyon caſte amphymacus herde noyſe meruayllous great tumulte wonder ſowne lyke lamentacyowne ſondry folke playnynge diſtreſſe hertely wo warde heuyneſſe treate euen whan gone confuſe crye gan anone ¶wherof vlixes eke dyomede sodaynely fylle drede suppoſynge theyr oppyowne ſome rumoure falle towne amonge people como • te haſty rancour auenged loue amphymacus cauſeles exyled thus volunte agayne trouthe ryght wherfore dradde whan drewe nyght murdred comons towne fraude conſpyracyowne falſly compalſyd olde enmytee anthenor falſe enee ſothly yet maner man coude wyt wherof began eſpye firſte aroſe paleys thorugh cloſe herde well lay nought wherof aſtoned theyr thought affrayde ſodayne drede vlixes moſt alſo dyomede lyſte comons ſet anthenor without lenger let make ſure tumulte cry grekes hath conueyed ſecretely whan aſſured theyr place vlixes firſte chaunged face gan pynche ſore ſelfe whyle anthenor treaſon gyle heſtys ſo fro day day ſleyghte put delay semynge fully ought coude eſpye deceyt fraude trecherye couenauntes hath behyght one falſe troyan knyght ſadde chere ſobre countenaunce well auyſed dalyaunce anſwerde agayne playnely dyde expreſſe wyſſe quod take vnto wytneſſe hye goddes euery thynge may ſe without faynynge haue beſy fro poynt poynt purpoſe acheue nat greue fynally ye lyſte one thynge parturbeth matere whiche ſhall ſo none offence playnely remembre preſence ſay olde antyquyte firſte byldynge troye cyte whylom ycalled yllyon cauſe oonly foundacyon kynge ylyus ſythe go full longe founder walle ſtronge made mencyon called named yllyon whiche great beſy charge pallas name made temple large paſſyngly reuerence whan phane moſte excellence perfourmed maſonry full wele ſaue rofe complete euerydele myghty ſtone byldynge well aſſured lede tymber cured agayne tempeſt obſtacle fyll wonder oonly myracle dare well afferme certeyne suche another neuer ſeyne ſo lyſte ſe conſydre meruayle ſo celeſtyall came downe y• hye heuen plyades ſterres ſeuen thorugh eyer holdynge paſſage lyke fayre meruaylous ymage worlde though men ſought ne none halfe ſo well ywrought trewely ſuppoſe pygmalyon remembred roſe tyme hadde cunnynge graue peynte ſo curyous thynge wrought dylygent laboure hande aungell heuenly toure thorugh goddes myght dyuyne ordyaūce hyder ſent thorugh puruyaunce relyke oonly grace prouyded ſame place abyde proteccyon diffence ſauacyon perpetuelly whyle worlde may dure agayne myſchefe myſauenture euery trouble trybulacyon ſuſteynynge releuacyon ſoueraygne helpe eke cyte whiche neuer may deſtroyed none engyne men may purchace goddes haue graunted ſuche grace ſuche vertue annexed eke therto troye ſothe may neuer fordo tyll relyke ſtole away yet ſothe man may place ſtere remewe preſte dewe oonly offyce touche honde myghtely conſerued bonde attempteth concluſyon remewe preſumpcyon fyne platly ſhall fayle force none may hym nat auayle ſothe wyll nat remeued except hym duete apperteyneth ye haue herde forne ouer man yet borne rede tell degree veryly ſtone tree deuyſed ywrought wyght ſo ſotyll thought ceryouſly tell manere mynerua ſo freſſhe clere ſterne goddeſſe thorugh hir great myght ſo dredefull bothe loke ſyght whiche hir breſt haueth criſtall hir ſhelde egys goddeſſe inmortall ygraunted hath bokes lerne thorugh hir power whiche eterne holy relyke memoryall hir temple byldynge moſte royall conſerue aſſaute brede ſocoure euery maner nede agayne theyr foon vnto troye towne whyle kept deuociowne alway ſucceſſyowne kynge kynge lyne downe iuſt tycle lynealy ſuccede annexyd take hede prudently auoydynge neclygence conſerue dewe reuerence bounde yholde ryght ſhall enmye power haue myght damage hyndrynge towne called palladyowne lyke clerkes wryte ſayne pallas make hir towne certayne relyke ſent fro heuen downe conclude ſhortly reaſowne cauſe purpoſe ſo let quod vlixes ſyth may beno bet labour ydell vayne without recure certayne thou haſte ſayde towne degre thorugh relyke may nat deſtroyed foly vndertake vnto grekes beheſte make without thou haddeſt well ſure quod anthenor yet recure haue hyght ye ſhall haue towne though dylacyowne maner anone ſhall telle ſo ye lyſte whyle dwelle without noyſe outher perturbaunce preſte whiche gouernaunce relyke ſhalbe ſpoke vnto good aduyſe ytretyd ſo ſhall full aſſent golde treaſour ſhalbe blent accorde ſhall purpoſe brynge relyke whiche kept ſo cloſe place ye lyſte aſſygne ſtyll porte goodly benygne werkes tyll haue brought aboute fully thynge nothynge doute dare ſelfe take well honde whan menynge vnderſtōde toke leue went towne firſte voyde ſuſpecyowne theyr goynge anthenor hath hyght wolde go ſame nyght pryamus make ordynaunce bondes aſſuraunce pea ſhulde ymaked knowe eke quantyte golde ye ſhall receyue thus ſhall beſte purpoſe apparceyne kynge knowe eueryde • e conſente lyke wonder wele euery thynge anthenor hath fayde ſo parte glad well apayde went theyr way made tariynge anthenor goth vnto kynge hym counſayllynge make delay calle lordes agayne next day lyeges aſſemble yfere fynally engroce matere ſyttynge expedyent whan kynge open ꝑlement crowned ſat regalye anthenor gan ſpecyfye audyence men myght knowe eche eſtate bothe hye lowe grekes wyll agree therto ſūme golde alſo whiche axe pea ſhall ſtande twenty thouſande marke haue hande puryd god whiche muſt anone payed ſyluer may nat delayed muſte eke haue ſame quantyte ouer accorded certayne meſours couenaunt alſo whete floure theyr lyues ſaue theyr repayre large ſee whan ſayle home theyr countree collect made anone good aduyſe euerychone redy acercayne day man durſte tho ſay nay contrarye anthern hath ſayde ſo well euyll payde full aſſent concluſyowne haſte thorugh towne collatours gadered vp golde lyke ſūme haue tolde pore ryche ſparyd none whiche tyme anthenor gone vnto preeſt called tonaunt ſhe myght wyſe hym daunt make herte fully enclyne full craftely layde hoke lyne luſty • eyte falſe coueytyſe excycynge hym full ſecrete wyſe wolde aſſent condeſcende vnto entent put hym poſſeſſyon relyke called palladyon without abode may delyueryd gaue hym golde huge quantyte hym blende moche behyght done full pryuely nyght shortly concludynge condeſcende wolde eſtate amende paſſyngly euer heyres ſhulde haue golde ſtore plente ynough none indygence shulde haue power hym offence vnto vowe make quod anthenor platly vndertake golde good thou ſhalt haue ſuffyſaunce treaſour paſſynge habundaunce thou ſhalt ſykerneſſe thy kyn excelle rycheſſe thou delyuer lyke myn axynge palladyon whiche thy kepynge behote thou mayſte truſte bonde ſhalbe ſecree lyſt hyndrynge thy name ſo thou drede ſhame eſclaundred ſo foule dede ſhape ſhall thou nede nat drede agaſte maner wyſe ſuche away ſothe ſhall deuyſe man ſhalbe ſuſpecyous thy perſone engenyous deme amyſſe mater goth well ware loth diffamed ſo falſe thynge knowe therof aſſentynge maner towne shulde haue ſuſpeccyowne lece let leuer hadde deye ſhall therfore caſte another weye honour ſaue ſo thou shall go quyte ſay vtterly neyther ſhall beholde ne parceyuere thefte ſtonde hole clere euer falle without ſhame vlixes ſhall bere blame dede thefe alſo men ſhall ſay whan ago engyne ſleyghty wyle thorugh treynes falſe gyle hath ſtole away palladyowne temple leſynge twone fynally durynge lyue men ſhall hym falſehede aſcryue gylte aretten offence thou oonly innocence thorugh worlde iniquyte shalbe excuſyd platly go free nedeth nat tarye matere come attones lo thy golde thou ne ſhalte lenger delayed ſyth thou ſeeſt diffyculte parte pereyll reprefe shame drede ſcalundre myſchefe delaye nat take thynge honde firſte preeſt gan hym withſtonde full myghtely ſayde nothynge nouther prayer manaſynge golde gode ne maner mede ne wolde aſſent ſo foule dede thus anſwerde pryme face ofte ſythe happeth men purchace gyfte good ſpeke wordes playne trouth pouerte myght neuer attayne mede falſhede may conquere tytle right men trouth lere gyftes great hertes enclyne golde maye ſtele marbyll myne preſtes herte hath ſo depe graue anthenor ſhall purpoſe haue poſſede palladyon thorugh falſe engyne conſpyracyon preeſt called tonaunte whiche falſhede myght hym beſt auaunte relyke fro temple rente vlixes anthenor ſente towne haſte myght ſeruaunt ſecretely nyght wherof troyans mortally diſmayde thorugh treaſon fynally trayed wrought preeſt coueytyſe blent falſe anthenor beynge aſſent ¶how grekꝭ made hors braſſe wherin men armes vnder coloure pea brought troye whiche vtterly dyſtroyed euer cap̄ xxxv troye ala well mayeſt yu morne wepe complaynynge wthertely ſyghes depe falſly defraudyd palladyon put euer poſſeſſyon myghty goddes worlde gouerne euery thyng thorugh myght cōſerne ryght deyte trouthe falſhede may togydreſe euery herte thorugh puruyaunce toke ye nat preeſt vengaunce traytourſly thorugh iniquyte golde good trayſſhed cyte troye ala without recure ſhall emforth ſure place ſtonde ſykerte syth holyneſſe ſo hye degre may infect corrupt mede euery herte ought quake drede ſe ala falſe ypocryſye preſtes ſhulde worlde exemplefye good doctryne perfeccyon make ſo ſoone tranſmutacyon double entent ſo daynely varye douteles seyntuarye pollut founde conuerſacyon naked bare deuocyon ſhynynge theyr parfyt lyght yturned dyrkeneſſe vnto nyght vnto place ſhall men ferther go take example ought certys roote grounde euerydele coueytyſe ſo loke wele whiche greyne ſo fer yſowe ſo lyſte auaryce knowe amonge preſtes ſhall ratheſt fynde therwithall made blynde theyr eſtate may nat ſe ſothneſſe degre gredyer rauynous worldely good coueytous preſtes catche may gone ſythe many day theyr breſt fyxhed rote coueytyſe whiche ſyt ſo ſote man may arrace hym remewe theyr tayle euer doth ſewe falſe worme moder noryce myſchefe euery vyce golde nowe ſo ſhynynge ſo bryght perſynge eke ſo clere lyght preſtes ſtemes blent ſothneſſe theyr entent coueytyſe receptacle poſſede eke tabernacle theyr herte aye ſo gredy enbrace auaryce hath lodgynge place myd theyr breſte vyce vyces cauſeth vertue rather falle abyt ſo ſupplaunte recorde take preeſt tonaunte treaſour anthenor hath ſolde ryche relyke hadde holde palladyon whyle troye towne haue gaderyd vp aboute euyrowne ryche pore thorugh cyte golde ſyluer huge quantyte floure whete paye theyr raunſon whiche ſūme entencyon made kepe wyſely conſerue temple longeth mynerue purpoſynge one affeccyowne cyteſens thorugh towne hopynge therby fare bet vpon day aſſygned yſet appollo theyr paynem wyſe solempnely make ſacryfyſe ſlaughter beſtes wt encenſe blode whiche day whan preſtes ſtode compaſſe rounde aboute autere gan kyndle cole bryght clere vpon autere playnely rede offre vp beſtes dede flawme great leuen appollo ſtellefyed heuen whan offre moſt laboryous befell two thynges meruaylous firſte ſacryde fyre ne wolde brenne lyke hir deſyre flawme vp aſcende alofte albe aſſayed full ofte ten tymes yet ne wolde aye queynt ne myght ſe nought ſmoky reſolucyons horryble blacke lyke exalacyons newe lyme whan meynt water colde hete queynt myght maner wyſe lacke fyre theyr ſacryfyce aye foūde wonderfull obſtacle next myracle theyr auter whan gan ſprede entrayles beſtes dede queme appollo wt flawmes bryght fayre came anone downe ayre royall egle full perſynge loke clawes offrynge vp toke entrayles lyenge enuyrowne deſcence makynge ſuche ſowne none ſo hardy herte manhode aſtoned ſtode ſuppryſed thorugh nerfe euery vayne meruayle caſe ſodayne egle abydynge ouer towne full hye gan ſore towarde grekes enhaſtynge myght theyr ſhypes ſodaynely lyght entrayles beſtes alle egle let fro clawes falle wherof troyans whan toke hede diſamayed mortall drede ſygnes haue clerely comprehendyd theyr goddes greatly offendyd agayne towne whan fyre went oute wolde put doute ſure meruayle mente caſſandra haſte wente fully haue declaracyon therupon playne expoſycyon ſhe tolde platly drede quenchynge theyr fyres rede vnto demonſtracyon yre indignacyon appollo hath troye bore blode ſhad achylles temple ſlawe vengeably murdred ydrawe without maner reuerence honour done excellence appollo beynge preſent phane plate adiacent defoulyd pollut blode wherfore ſhe ſayde ſhortly gode went proſeſſyon herte contryte deuocyon toumbe achylles nyght oonly fette theyr taprys lyght sacryd fyre brennynge wake fully purpoſe aſſent make murdre ſatiſſfaccyon whiche fyre none occacyon shall nat quenche flawmes holde thorugh none aſſaute ſtormy wyndes colde ſacryfyce vpon autere tofore appollo brenne ſhall ſo clere troye wrought hir rede egle ſhe badde take hede thynge token oftreaſon pronoſtycke declaracyon fynally troye ylyon shall tourne haſte deſtruccyon flyenge fowle royall ouer towne myghty wall fethers maylyd bryght ſhe entrayles clawes kene troye fynall demonſtraunce sothfaſte ſhewynge ſygnefyaunce grace ewer hap olde fortune lyklyhede myght nat contune perſeuer theyr firſte lyght attones haue take theyr flyght palladyon myght nat withholde ſtole lyke tolde man may fatall chaunce refuſe grekes eke faſte gan muſe inwardly theyrwyttes ſought entrayles egle brought therupon gan togydre rowne tyll yt calchas dyd euery thynge expowne vnto full gan aſſure fyne auenture conclude ſhulde vpon theyr welfare bad alſo coſte ſpare perſeuere herte ſtable fortune ſelfe enhable counſayllynge theyr beſy payne solempnely haſte ordayne certayne offrynge borne felde fayre pallas hir criſtall ſhelde hir make ryche ſacryfyſe ſtorye ordre ſhall deuyſe byſſhop calchas locke hore traytour forſworne ſyth go ful yore falſed hath trouth aliaūce clerkes haue put remembraunce theyr locke letter olde newe exemplefye man vntrewe though yeres paſſe faſte aweye ruſt ſclaundre lyghtly wyll nat deye fret therof ſo corroſyfe laſteth full many mannes lyfe full harde arrace awaye whoſe venym full ſelde made allaye reporte therof blowen ſo wyde perpetuelly wyll abyde remembred newe freſſhely mynde recorde hym coude away fynde olde calchas euyll mut ſterue vnder colour offrynge mynerue make grekes entre towne ſleyghty ſerpent fader patrowne fyndre vp treaſon gyle compaſſyd hath founde wyle grekes ſhall cyte wynne take pretendynge ſacryfyce make vnto pallas ſhall expreſſe traytoure meroure falſeneſſe grekes bad theyr payne mynerua offrynge fayne haſte ſhulde ſpede aſſent dyde make ſtede large wyde coper bra crafte ſynon contryued myght receyue large wele thouſande knyghtes armed bryght ſtele thorugh ſleyghte compaſſynge ſotyll wytte meruayllous workynge wyſe crafty greke synon whiche thorugh caſtynge diſcrecyon parformed hath ryche ſtede bra ye haue herde byddynge calchas aduyſe appyus wyſe holpe alſo ſtede deuyſe fyne oonly deuocyowne grekes myght requere towne whan made graunte lycence preſente reuerence myghty pallas ſtele armed bryght amyd hir temple large full lyght offrynge fynde occaſyowne haue entre frely towne pylgrymage theyr vowes fulfylle whiche ſtede daren ſhall full ſtylle thouſande knyghtes calchas deuyſe ordayned hath ſo ſlye wyſe crafte synon appyus large ſtede makynge meruayllous vnder pretenſe oblacyon complete full perfeccyon werkemanſhype tolde afore ſame yere troye forlore whan ſege ſothly gan fyne cyte brought ruyne thorugh grekes myght wall ſtronge bete downe large thycke longe whiche yere made mencyowne alytell afore takynge towne kynges echone came fro ſo ferre alyue lefte mortall werre ¶whan ſawe pryam couenaūt vnto grekes vtterly made graunt haſte poſſyble paye raunſowne toke leue went towne firſte fynde kynge phylymene hym ladde body quene pantaſyllia home hir countre full rychely buryed ij thouſande knyghtes yt kynge brought vnto troye firſte comynge mo fyfty home hym ladde woman quene eke hadde thouſande ſtorye ſayth certayne foure hondred home agayne thus whan fro troye gone morowe nexte pryamus anone lordes rode towne acorde confirmacyowne pea fynall vpon outher ſyde felde grekes hym abyde relykes openly yborne outher party ſworne forme afore recordyd anthenor grekes accordyd grekes firſte ſwore dyomede troye takynge lytell hede othe condycyon curyd aboue vnder falſe treaſon sythe grekes tho theyr ſwerynge ne bounde ſelfe maner thynge ſtonde ſpecyall holde kepe generall poyntes hole engroſſyd thylke treate daūz anthenore grekes helde traytour fraudulent whiche full double entent meynt treaſon ye haue herde toforne whiche obſerue oonly ſworne fraude othe nat wordes playne theyr aduer ſaryes take trayne excludynge theyr meanynge ferre pea face herte werre openly confermed theyr honde inly treaſon aſſuraunce bonde though venym cloſyd wt wall nat hyd fro hym knoweth certaynely ſo clerkes teche ſwereth falſly ſpeche flouryſſhynge outwarde fayre coloure deceyue trewe neyghboure forſworne ſo euer treaſon hyd though men may nat ſe ſo worde away yborne ſwereth crafte crafte forſworne may made none excuſacyon god knoweth entencyon demeth herte worde right nought wyll knoweth thought euery man nyghe eke fere therfore beware man hym forſwere grekes dyde troyans deceyue fraude coude nat conceyue suppoſynge grekes hadde faythfull trewe theyr ſurete thynge herte thought whiche ende full dere abought whan founde fully reuerſe theyr ſpeche dede ſo dyuerſe vayne wryte theyr fayned othes theyr wordes whyte cherys coude fayne conclude quene eleyne durynge treate vpon ſame day delyueryd kynge menelay payed raunſowne graunted tofore gaderyd towne golde ſyluer alſo floure theyr ſhyppes dylygent laboure full great haſte euery thynge brought thorugh cyte came nought grekes ſymulacyon makynge coloure deuocyon thorugh holyneſſe vnder ypocryſye falſly fayned fraude flatery kynge haue prayed haue lyberte freely entre cyte make aſſeth oblacyon thefte palladyon offre vp ryche ſtede bra goddes called pallas ¶what kynge pryam lyketh aſſygne ſhe wyllnge benygne theyr repeyre ſaylynge ſee home grece towarde theyr countree whan ſhe quemyd large ſtede whiche ala pryam toke hede treaſon hyd coude nat aduerte graunted hole herte whan lyſt brynge towne falſe entyſynge ſuggeſtyowne anthenor alſo enee hauynge drede ambygnytee entent ſuſpeccyon nouther fayngynge falſe treaſon right frendely lyke beheſte condeſcendeth vnto theyr requeſte theyr auowes myght obſerue offre vp hors vnto mynerue grekes tho great dylygence full great honour huge reuerence haue ſhapen proceſſyowne brynge ſtede troye towne men armes beynge aye thein calle troye wyn ſhorte tyme ſtode date whan hors brought gate ſo narowe ſpace ſtede towne pace albe aſſayed ouer whefore pryam bet downe wall make large right theyr deuyſe whiche thynge ala vnwyſe cauſe che • e confuſyowne hors came towne humbly forth gan procede temple large ſtede pallas mekely downe knelynge attones made offrynge fayned chere falſe deuocyowne wherof herte glad towne ſpecyall troye ſothe ſayde aye fyne ioye occupyeth men full ofte ſe vnwarely cometh aduerſyte gladneſſe myſauenture whan men beſt wene ſton de ſure worldly blyſſhe none affyaunce dyuers vnhappy chaunce full deceyte euer meynt trouble truſte varyaunt double ſelde one abydynge throwe worldly luſte though blowe pompe pryde boſt ſowne anone paſſeth recorde troye towne wende well ryche ſtede haue ſure deuoyde drede perpetuelly haue tolde tofore whan grekes haue hors ybore tofore pallas ye haue herde telle lyketh nat lenger dwelle boundes myghty towne purpoſe greke synowne haue cōmytted hole gouernayle ſtede whiche wyll nat fayle whan ſeeth beſt opportunyte engyne trayſſhe cyte grekes haue whyle founde newe ſleyghte fully confounde ſay haue made theyr ſonde kynge pryam wolde go fro londe vnto ſee towarde tenedowne thyder ſayle concluſyowne eleyne good • yſement ſecrete wyſe thyder ſhalbe ſent dradde vpon londe delyuered ſhortly theyr honde grekes wolde malys theyr payne party ſlee eleyne ſhe grounde gynnynge theyr wo roote cauſe alſo ſlaughter many worthy man sythen ryme ſege firſte began wherfore ſayde ſtynte ſtryfe ſure ſaue hir lyfe beſt lende hir ſyght secretely tenedowne nyght thus fayned full falſe treaſon pryam put ſuſpeccyon alkaunce wolde neuer theyr lyue reſorte agayne troye ſtryue thus made pryam wene honde deceyued clene theyr deceyte knowynge neuer adele herte thought nat wele grauntynge myght pleaſe whan hadde leyſer good eaſe fro troyeſayled vnto tenedowne ¶with theyrnauye falſe greke synowne troye wakergan take kepe houre whan men theyr firſte ſlepe haſte ſleyghty gynne many vyſe many ſotyll pynne ſtede made aboute gone crafty lokes vndoynge euerychone goth gan anone calle within hors worthy knyghtes alle ſecretely man myght eſpye traytourſly gan hym hye vpon walles ſelfe ſame nyght towarde grekes gan ſhewe lyght lay tofore tenedowne redy armed falle vpon towne whan ſodayne lyght eſpyed hors backe anone haue hyed towarde troye armed clene wente ſame walle whiche hors late broke mortally wroke knyghtes eke ſtede bra haue met full ſterne paas gan anone thorugh cyte euery halfe kylle ſlee blody ſwerde vpon euery ſyde made theyr woundes brode large wyde whyle ala thynge aduertynge mydnyght houre dedde lay ſlepynge full innocent thought nat gode bathed yrowne blode bothe man childe without excepcyon grekes ſparynge condcyon olde yonge woman wyfe mayde crye pryamus abrayde llepe ſodaynely woke whiche lay nyght hede ne toke daughter murdre towne tho wyſte treaſowne falſly compaſſyd vnto cytee anthenor alſo enee whoſe malys doute venym broken oute galle conſpyracyon vnder ſugre ſymulacyon hath ſo louge cloſyd hyd dede execute kyd nowe fraude fully treaſon caſte alſo falſe colluſyon taked abrode yblowe autours openly yknowe hath enuye contryued hate theyr engyne ſette abrode gate hath deceyte olde conſpyracye fayned othes one allye openly ſhewed theyr falſeneſſe diſcloſed theyr doubylneſſe ferre abrode geyne ala wylde fyre ſeyne toures hye wynde yblaſed wherof pryam aſtoned amaſed awapyd ſterte bed comforteles temple fled appollo ſaue hym myght aye flawme fyres bryght brent towne couſumeth ryche byldynge whylom ſo royall walles theyr rofes huge coueryd lede chefe refuge ala bare bareyne makyd grekes aye theyr ſwerdes nakyd murdre ſlee ſo go twenty thouſande nyght mo kylled haue longe day ſlaughter great affray spoyle robbe take fynde treaſour good lefte nat behynde myghty honde ſturdy vyolence temple without reuerence haue deſpoyled thorugh ye towne gredely rent racyd downe golde ſyluer ornamentes alle totore goddes foule mote falle kynge pryam aye deedly chere appolio makynge prayere furyouſly hertely wofull man ſoth rede ne wayte deth fatall eure caſſandra holy creature warde wo deſyrous ſterue complaynynge ran vnto mynerue makynge hir lamentacyowne gentyll woman towne ala wolde dye full pyteouſly ſobbe wepe crye theyr dooll lette dwelle theyr ſorowes ſhulde telle ſtorye theyr wo deſcryue penne ſhulde routhe ryue reherſynge eke euery ſtrete theyr clothes blacke redy moyſte wete ala bothe one alle theyr lordes downe aſwowne falle theyr blode bedewed yſprent men may ſe criſtall terys meynt theyr wepynge theyr woundes grene laye blede agayne ſonne ſhene deedly iyen caſtynge vp whyte vayne wryte maner theyr mortall ſorowe guydo wryt ſame morowe anthenor hym falſe enee conueyued haue thorugh cyte myghty grekes vnto ylyon royall toure ryche manſyon whylom moſt excellence whiche founde diffence hye lowe none eſtate lefte alone deſolate golde rycheſſe twone shet encloſed chefe dongeowne man withſtode brake locke raught away ye gode treaſour ſhet within eche partye myght wyn gaue force lefe lothe pyrrus temple goth appollo great cruelte fyll pryam knelynge kne ſwerde furyouſly wode tofore auter ſhadde blode hye raughte lengthe brede ſtremes woundes rede ſtatue golde borned bryght appollo great myght power ſterne face defouled pollut place oonly deth worthy kynge pyrrus ſlayne whyle lay knelynge olde hatrede enuyous pryde whyle anthenor enee ſtode beſyde routhe pyte beholde ſehym lye ſtones colde pyteouſly tofore auter blede wherof ala whan eccuba toke hede hir doughter fayre polycene heer rent golde wyer ſhene inly ſuppryſed ſorowe herte whan began conſydre aduerte noble kynge blody ſtremes rede drowned eyen dyrke dede pyrrus ſwerd gyrt thorugh outher ſyde mortall fere durſte nat abyde inwardly thorugh darted ſyght rage toke flyght yet ſothe thorugh cyte wyſte neuer whytherwarde flee reſcuſe none remedye kynne frende none allye grekes ſwerde towne ſo ſet hir flyght wofull quene hath met eneas cauſer wrake vnto rebukynge thus ſhe ſpake thou traytour moſte malycyous thou falſe ſerpent adder enuyous crope roote fynder falſeneſſe soures well vnkyndeneſſe myghteſt thou thy herte fynde vnto thy kynge ſo vnkynde gynner grounde exaumple treaſon fynall cauſe deſtruccyon myghteſt thou deuoyde pyte beholde ala thorugh thy cruelte kynge ſhedde ſo blode euer hath ben ſo gentyll ſo good gracyous lorde ſpecyally ouer thorugh hye bounte honoured ymagnefyed lyue may nat denyed lyeth deed temple ala thou nat oonly traytoure caas deth conſpyrynge vukynde pyrrus conueyinge ſhuld hȳ fynde tofore appollo mydes cyte thou ſhuldeſt duete rather haue ben proteccyon myghty ſhelde ſauacyon haſte cyte towne ylorne whiche
