thou foſtryd yborne gretteſt reputacyon lordes dwellynge towne thou haddeſt whylom moſt pleaſaūce remembraunce ¶yet thy herte drope gentylleſſe mercy pyte deedly rage full tene rewe doughter yonge polycene grekes ſwerde hir youthe ſaue thy herte may routhe haue manly pyte hir maydenhede diffende hir nowe kepe hir drede thou canſte fynde weye wyſe ſhe may nat deye hereafter whan men ſe rede falſe treaſon foule dede thou haſte done vnto troye towne may partye proteccyowne thy fame venym allye treaſon whan men wyll aſſaye iuſte reporte thy name accuſe dede may helpe excuſe agaynſt tonges ſpeke enee wyll ſay thou haddeſt yet pyte polycene oonly gentylleſſe therwith ſugre bytterneſſe thy decert blowe forth fame reherſayle foule blame ſhall thorugh worlde borne ſklaundre infect whan yu art torne thou ne ſhalt ſhame mowe ſuſtene ſhall doughter fayre polycene thy diffence agayne ſuche famous ſtryfe ſo thou ſaue hir lyfe forſe though thou make blyue ſwerde grekes thorugh herte ryue ſo prayer wofull quene eneas toke hym polycene whoſe traytour herte cruelte hir youthe meued pyte oonly routhe breſte aroſe ſecretely put hir vp cloſe lyſte grekes founde occaſyon agaynſt hym ayax thelamon toke warde andronomecha actor wyfe wyſe caſſandra temple longynge mynerue grekes ſwerde theyr lyues conſerue menelay toke quene eleyne garde ſo great payne bode herte many day toforne ala cyte lorne grekes aye beſy theyr yre ſlee kylle cruelly fyre euery ſyde bete downe paleys houſe walles towne ſpare nought goth fyre feruent hate brent theyr deſyre olde enuye auenged ne lefte within cyte thynge vnbrent alſo ylyowne rage tourned vp ſo downe made none excepcyons oonly take poſſeſſyons anthenor euyll mote fate eneas grekes ſpare vounde theyr othe thus grekes furyous wrouthe haue day robbed ybrent tyll kynge agamenon hath ſent lordes aſſemble yfere pallas temple oonly theyr wyſe aduyſe vpon thynges twayne firſte wolde holde nat fayne hoolly theyr hope without excepcyowne wonne firſt towne ouer axed alſo touchynge goddes wolde golde treaſour poſſeſſyowne haue thurgh hye renown̄ anſwerd without tariynge wolde theyr fayth kepe euery thynge ſworne heſtys holde ouer ſayde wolde golde treaſour good cyte right requyreth alſo equyte iuſtly partyd dyuyſyon euery wyght made diſtrybucyon lyke meryt hye lowe degre kynge eke reaſon ſe eche rewarde laboure longeth conqueroure man haue mater compleyne ſo fylle ſpekynge eleyne eueryche oppynyon tofore ayax thelamon shortly ſayde ſhe hath deſerued deth ſo many haue yelde vp breth playnely affermynge parlement rightwyſneſſe trewe iugement ſhulde nat eſcape lyfe gynnynge cauſe theyr ſtryfe rote grounde theyr ſorowe wo ſo ſayde eke many nother mo noyſe great affray agamenon kynge menelay ne durſte worde hir party meue ſaue ye quene lyſte grekes wold greue agaynſt ſo great rumour tyll vlixes chefely hir ſocour thorugh wyt eloquence deuer dyde dylygence ſaue hir lyfe fully purchace grekes gette hir grace guydo alſo doth v lere agamenon grekes gan requere graunte hym chefe guerdo • caſſandra haue poſſeſſyon hir lyfe hym abyde eke eneas anthenor beſyde elenus grekes tolde werre neuer aſſent wolde prudent vertuous counſayllynge contraryous tho hye lowe eſtate troye firſte began debate wixe grekes myghty towne eke helpe medyacyowne achylles buryed ygraue deed corp houndes ſaue whan ſlayne full cruell wyſe nyght tyme ye haue herde deuyſe ſothly caſſandra bothe murdre herte full wrothe ſory eke many another thynge wrought towne wtout theyr wyttynge malys innocent grekes haue fully aſſent graunted prerogatyfe parlement haue theyr lyfe elenus firſte teers drowned tofore kynge pyteouſly hath ſwowned abraydynge deedly face humble wyle beſought hym grace knyghtly pyte haue aduertence ſpare ſwerde fro blode innocence mercy nat diſdayne graunte lyfe ſones twayne worthy ector brother moſt entere eke rewe theyr moder dere oonly grace ſhe nat dede wydowe left alone rede wote nat whyther ſhe may dyuerte ſo kynge ameued herte wordes wofull chere benygnely graunted prayere gaue eke lyfe fredam go moder hir child two ladyes gentyll woman alle mercy grace calle graunted eke compaſſyon ſafe conduyt fre pardon lyſt towne abyde countre adiacent beſyde put hole theyr eleccyowne thankynge hȳ fyll knee downe many tere dewed face ſo kynge parteth fro place grekes right anone fully purpoſe ſhyp gone haſte ſayle towarde theyr countree ſuche tempeſt roſe vp ſee wawe wynde alſo cloudes blake moneth dare nat take water ſalte drede neptunus ire alſo golus vnto euery thynge contrarye londe made longe tarye ſee aye ſo fell bolyinge tyll grekes clachas enquerynge one aſſent myght euer one ſo dyuerſe ſee rage eue morowe anſwerd god gyue hym euyll ſorowe olde ſhrewe propheſye ſo well whan hym lyſt lye tempeſt cauſed goddes furyes infernall neuer wolde appeſe ſtylle tyll murdre platly achylle auenged ſhedynge blode whiche ſayde appollo eke wode temple hym conſecrate thorugh deth troye vyolate blode agayne made ſatyſfaccyon wherfore muſte thorugh redempcyon hir roote ſpecyall thorugh hir beaute orygynall cauſe deth yonge polycene gynnynge firſte mortall tene therfore appollo ſhe myght vp offred ſacryfyce pleaſe deyte deth agayne make recompence right deth firſte offence grekes muſte vtterly fulfyll deſyre haue wyll large ſee ſayle quyete pyrus tho furyous hete gan enquere aboute euery man polycene wyght tell hir worde ſhortly ſhe saufe ſome ſayde eneas anthornor hadde hyd hir pryuely wherof roſe amonge ſodaynely suche grutchynge grekes aboute theyr lyfe doute inwardly thynge toke grefe tyll anthenor god gyue hym euyll prefe may treaſon wardeyne bere ye keye ſhewe malys euery weye longe hath ſought tyll chaumbre olde hath hir founde grekes tolde brought hir forth vnto theyr preſence cruell force hatefull vyolence without pyte compaſſion hir delyueryd agamenon ala haſty iugement without reſpyte auyſement shortly hath dempte ſhe ſhalbe dede flourynge hir maydenhede excepcyon aſſygned agamenon vnto pyrrus tyrannye ladde hir forth faſt gan hym hye place ſhe ſhulde deye great preaſe weye gan croude ſhoue beholde ſene yonge mayde fayre polycene hir beaute hir ſemlyneſſe hir womanhede excellent fayreneſſe yfere whan toke hede hadde routhe ſhe ſhalbe dede without gylte treſpace men may ſe vpon many face ſalte terys faſte fall downe pyte compaſ • yowne man childe none ſo harde herte felte hir ſake ſmerte hir goodly face whan beholde ſe fayne wolde myght haue delyuered hir force anone pyrrus hōde wende echone without hir deth neuer haue repayre grece weder fayre calchas hadde made ſuggeſtyon brought oppynyon laſte whan polycene dede wyll mayde clene graue achylles brought kneleth downe wt humble thought caſte vp hir eye gan ſyghe ofte goddes humbly ſofte dredfull herte deuocyon made wyſe hir lamentacyon oye almyghty yt worlde gouerne euery thynge conſydre diſcerne worlde ſo huge large rounde bothe eyer ſee heuen eke grounde deuyſe worde wrought ſoth faſtly knowe euery thought right euery maner wyght without lettynge ſo perſynge ſyght thynge concelyd ywrye beholdynge eternall eye euery thynge may attones ſe vpon ſoule haue mercy pyte grace benygne cure vpon woo pyteous auenture haue ſome routhe ſhall deye wofull ſpirite lede conueye lyſte nowe ſhall pace vnto ſelfe place confeſſe humylyte hethertowarde haue chaſtyte lade lyfe kept maydenhede ſeruyſe bothe thought dede porte chere countenaunce feture dalyaunce one myſloke neuer yet abrayde ſothe dye ſhall mayde ye well knowe ſynne innocent though nowe dempt iugement deed without gylte wytneſſe inmortall clene entent accuſyd yet ala may nat excuſyd ſwerde vengeaunce muſtebyte routheles whiche thynge wyte ſtonde clere pure offence diſcharged conſcyence dare afferme fully gylteles touchynge murdre worthy achylles whiche ſlewe brother louyd nowe cauſe myne aduerſyte yet wyll dede worde thought vnto deth aſſentaunt right nought therof right ſory herte albe may nat aſterte deed oonly ſake alone vengeaunce ſhalbe take without mercy full cruell wyſe blode make ſacryfy • e goddes theyr wrathe queme people blynde ſothe amys ye deme agaynſt herte ſo cruell mercyles yrous fell without routhe mykell indurate ſlee mayde alone deſolate herte ala pyte gone harder trouthe outher ſtocke ſtone cruell oppynyon forlacke pyte tygre lyon certes ye greatly blame oughte therof haue great ſhame aſſent ſo foule dede ſlee mayde quakynge hir drede graunte hir none oportunyte wepe hir virgynyte cruell pyteous wreche blode gylte hereafter ſhall apeche accuſe alſo great enuye goddes ſhall iuſtefye euery vnright bothe hye lowe full egally make knowe trouthe playnely ſpare degree make open ſecree ſaye nat ſelfe complayne haue reders fatall payne deth welcome vnto lyfe take gree sythen brether moſt worthy renowne ſlayne buryed towne fader deed vn weldy age alone lefte rage haue abyde pyteouſly ſe fynall ruyne cyte whiche herte ſytteth ſo ſore leuer haue wepe dye attones reles woo sythe kynne paſſed agoo longer lyue deth better yelde vp breth lad cyte amonge ſtraungers lyue pouerte deth welcome longer lette thy dredefull darte fyle whette tendre herte therwith ryue agayne thy myght ſhall neuer ſtryue tyme kythe thy powere wyll herte entere clene mayde ſo began without touche maner man lyfe ſame day lytell auaunt make yet may myn ende goddes alle whoſe helpe clyppe calle theyr mercy mekely cōmende wofull ſpirite pray ſende euery mayde better happe grace haue nowe longer ſpace hertely ioye honour contune without aſſaute infortune lede theyr lyfe proſperyte maydens remembreth vpon take exaumple ye ſhall kepe ye wolde fewe terys wepe whan ye thynke vpon polycene age yeres grene whan ſhe ſlayne cruell auenture goddes haue cure dredfull goſte hoolly betake eternally thus ende make yt worde hir hede ſhe gan enclyne full humbly whan ſhe ſhulde fyne hir eyen helde lede downe pyrrus wodder lyon diſmembred hath ſharpe ſwerde mayde yonge dredefull ferde ouer cruelte ſhewe peces ſmale hath hir hewe endelonge faders ſepulture ala myght cruell herte endure mercyles ſo foule adede aſtoned ſothely whan rede hir deth dyde hym gode lyke tyraunt caſte abrode hir blode tygre routhe haue rounde enuyrowne aboute faders graue ſprent hate cruelte thou pyrrus thou mayſte full well ybe achylles ſone lyneall diſcent lyke hym herte entent thou ſothe deuoyde pyte werſe yet one degree thy fader lyuynge ne radde neuer yet ſo foule thynge though wolde hatrede hym abrayde rancoure euer ſlewe amayde fynde well hadde parte whylom loue cupydes darte made hym ſore lyue ſmerte whan wounded herte caſtynge oonly eye wenynge therby wyſtly deye myght nat ſodayne ſtroke eſcape afterwarde fate hathe ſhape murdred loue polycene thou haſte ſlayne thy cruell tene furyouſly without routhe ſhame whiche thynge foule hatefull fame thorugh al worlde hereafter ſhalbe ſprede whan ſtorye reherſyd rede ſhalbe ſayde pyrrus routheles slewe yre mayde gyltles woryed ſhall thy name moſt odyble dede paſſyngly horryble loue oonly fayre polycene deth whan eccuba quene hath ſeen ala ſhe beſyde ſtode wo gan wexe wode ſorowe hir wytte ſhe wente hir clothes hir heer ſhe rente rage wot nat ſhe doth gan anone hondes toth hir furye crache eke byte stone caſte fyſtes ſmyte ſhe mette tyll grekes made hir bynde ſente hir forth alſo fynde yle troye partynent ſhe ſlayne oonly iugement grekes ſtoned deth whan ſhe hadde yelde vp breth wofull quene cruell auenture grekes dyde make sepulture ceryouſly metall ſtone toke corp buryed anone great honour ſolempnyte longe men myght ſe ryche toumbe coſtfull royall ſet made memoryall eccuba whylom great fame gaue place name called longe mynde ¶locus feſtus guydo fynde thus quene oonly ſorowe wode whan hir doughter hadde ſhadde hir blode grekes ſtone dyde hir ende make ye haue herde playnely ſake polycene whylom calchas vnto appollo falſly offryde pyrrus ſwerde achylles auengynge make ſee calme blandyſſhynge goddes take vengeaunce vpon grekes euyll chaunce come falſe goddes euerychone theyr ſtatues ſtockes ſtone whiche ſerpent olde ſnake sathan hym ſelfe gan dwellynge make fraudently folkes illude full ſotyll hym ſelfe include ymages make holde forgyd ſyluer golde erroure falſe illuſyon hath ybrought confuſyon thorugh myſcreaūce ye worthy kynde man sythe tyme alder firſte began falſe honour ydolatrye worſhyp vnto maumetrye ſacryfyſe beſtes blode apeſe whan wode queme bothe eue morowe pray god gyue ſorowe ſo within withoute none excepte falſe route saturne mar pallas iuno iubyter mercurius pluto nouther flora doth floures ſprede nouther bachus grape whyte • ede cupydo eyen blynde nouther daphne cloſyd vnder rynde thorugh tellus myght laurer tree thou dyane thy chaſtytee myghty venus cytherea thy dartes proſerpyna lady arte depe downe helle belydes draweth welle ixyon thou zezyphus thyne appyll thou cruell tantalus furyes infernall ye ſpynne lyues threde fatall vpon rocke euery maner man muſes ſo ſynge wene coppys nyſus cyrra vpon hylle beſyde cyrrea cybele cere thy corne golus dredefull horne herde ſo ferre whan thou lyſt blowe ianus frons backe corbed lowe pryapys genyus preſte curſeth aye candellys feſte thoechone frowarde kynde ymeneus whoſe power bynde hertes knet maryage tyll goddeſſe diſcorde rage diſſeuerth dyuyſyon nouther maues haue theyr manſyon myd erthe dyrkeneſſe woo elues wont goo vndyrmeles whan phebus moſt ſhene nouther fawny tendre greues grene water nymphes naydes satirye nouther dryad goddes woode wylderneſſe goddes nouther leſſe morpheus god ſlepe holde hym woode taketh kepe obſeruaunce may nat fayle haue myſchaunce ende playnely mede ſuche feyned falſeneſſe drede roſe deuyll firſte engyne ſleyghty treynes ſerpentyne oonly mankynde whan made loute falſe ydoles whiche doute deuylles dauyd bereth wytneſſe ſautre wryt expreſſe confermeth endytes goddes paganyſme rytes one excepteth none made golde ſyluer ſtone forged braſſe metall tree eyen haue yet may nat ſe fendes ſo dauyd ſayth haueth fayth hope credence delyte drede wyll hym quyte ſuche guerdon ſoule ſleeth perpetuelly ſo fyne deth theyr ſeruyſe whan men henſe pace theyr lyfe vnhap euyll grace myſchefe woo confuſyowne men may ſe exaumple towne wende well aſſured haue haue ſtonde longe proſpyryte agayne theyr foon thorugh helpe appollo venus eke fauour iuno thorugh pallas myght dyane mynerue wont honour ſerue cerymonyes ſacryfyce ye tofore haue herde deuyſe haue brought vnto ruyne cruell deth bed fyne may ye ſe venym byte ende ſuche olde rytes euydence noble towne may auayle palladyowne may nowe helpe theyr frauded fantaſye theyr olde falſe ydolatrye ala ala bought ſore farewell troye farewell euermore farewell ala cruell thy fall wryte ſhall thy ſake forſothe whan take hede inwarde woo herte fele blede whan remembre thought ruyne thou arte brought nought whylom ſo noble ſo ryche worlde trowe none lyche perrygall ſpeke fayreneſſe ſpeke knyghthode worthyneſſe clerkes ſay thy byldynge knewe worlde ought rewe thy pyteous waſte walles wylde whylom ſo royall whan men gan bylde thy toures hye kynge pryamus firſte began moſte ryche gloryous ſette ſee noble ylyon wryte lamentacyon conuenyent troye thy ſake thy great myſchefe complayne crye certes trowe nat olde ieremye ſo wepte captyuyte thylke noble royall chefe cyte ieruſalem deſtruccyon hole tranſmygracyon iewes thou ezechyell tyme whan myſchefe fell vnto kynge ycalled sedeclye babylon thy propheſye ſtones cruelly yſlawe departyd ſawe ye bothe two coude ſo complayne danyell felte ſo great payne kynges tranſmutacyon beſte tyll thorugh oryſon danyell reſtored mynde agayne ete nomore gras ¶yet veryly though ye thre wepynge hadde lyue preſent eke deſtruccyowne noble worthy royall towne haue bewayled myſchefe wo ſlaughter ſege outher partye full cruell wyſe terys myght nat ſuffyſe haue bewept theyr ſorowes euerychone treaſon wrought aſwell theyr ſone hereof may nat auayle lyke gynneth ſayle agayne wynde whan maſte doth ryue right ſo vayne ſtryue agayne face bytterer galle vengeaunce vpon troye falle preſume theyr furyes ſharpe whette ceryouſly boke ſette great thynge dare nat vnder take euen pyteous ende make ſege ſympleſſe though ſtyle blotted rudeneſſe metre ruſty vnfyled fourthe boke haue complyed humble honde drede y• doth quake vnto grace hoolly betake mercy thynge diſpeyre makynge repeyre grekes lenger dwelle theyr auentures ſee telle theyr reſorte home theyr countre receyued oonly ſupporte ſo ye nat deſpyſe fyfthe boke ſhortly ſhall deuyſe ¶here begynneth fyfth boke troye whiche ſpeketh howe grekes retourned grece dyſtruccyon howe peryſſhed almoſte ſee eſcaped dyed myſcheuouſly capitulo xxxvi whan eolus doth ye wȳdes rore apeſed blewe ſtormys gouernor lorde alſo fully accorde whiche myghty iuno lady ayre tomake ſkye weder fayre clowde none heuen dyde appere neptunus blaundyſſhynge chere aſſent ſtorye ſayth ſothe make ſee fro tempeſt calme ſmothe without boyllynge trouble wawe myghty grekꝭ ſhypward gan thē drawe repeyre home theyr countre hadde wonne cyte put theyr fomen fully werſe fortune aye frowarde peruerſe hath theyr merthe meynt aduerſyte whan wende full aſſuryd haue ſtonde ſtedefaſte quyete vlynde lady falſly made flete yrſugre galle diſcordaunce amonge ſelfe brynge varyaunce theyr hertes rancour pryde contagyouſly ſeueryne deuyde whan ſat hyeſt theyr glorye palme conqueſt victorye fully reioyſynge thorugh theyr hye renowne crowne laurer poſſeſſyowne hadde alſo theyr luſt wonne whan bryghteſt ſhone luſty freſſhe ſonne eeſt weſt theyr worthyneſſe clowdy ſkye vnwarely derkeneſſe eclypſed hath party theyr lyght diffacyd holſome bemys bryght theyr welfare proſperyte enuyous falſe contagyouſte ſerpent pompouſe ellat amonge ſelfe tomake debate induſynge rancoure diſcorde entre within ſhyppes borde agayne vlixes worthy thelamon preſence kynge agamenon purpoſed hath playnely matere tofore grekes anone ye ſhall syres quod ſo nat greue ſemeth iuſtly reaſō may meue touchyng ye wȳnyng gettyng towne golde rycheſſe poſſeſſyowne fully delyuered taken honde treaſoure founde londe thynketh inwarde ſyght ne hath nat ben departed halfe ryght amonge v iuſte dyuyſyon egall diſtrybuſyon conſydred firſte tytle equyte euery wyght eſtate dignyte remembred eke ſharpe ſhoure worthyeſt meryte laboure decertys mortall ſtryfe grauntynge eueryche prerogatyfe lyke fortune hath deſeruyd ordre hath nat obſeruyd amonges v without excepcyon delyueraunce palladyon whiche vlixes ſay without drede tofore vniuſtly doth poſſede hym vſurpynge falſe oppynyon merytorye retrybucyon apparence tytle grounde vnder pretenſe coloure falſly founde relyke reioyſe ſhulde ryght ſleyghte wonne rather myght vſurpeth maner vaunt gyuen hym graunt echone chefe guerdon wyll make replycacyon relyke nat hym mete whiche ſhall nat reioyſe quyete may diſtourbe hym lette cleyme duely dette guerdon conuenyent ye lyſte indifferent reaſon oonly doth ſeme atwene v two egally deme iuſtly firſte euery circumſtaunce outher meryte weyed ballaunce firſte conſydered forth fro day day whyle ſege lay ye ſhulde plente vytayle ſyde fro myſchefe fayle ſhall wtout auaunt breke knyghthode armes ſpeke felde longe contynuaunce manly force ꝑſeueraunce vpon foon ſo fell kene day day armed clene nedeth nat make mencyon right honde ſlewe phylemon ye well knowe whiche kepynge yonge ſone pryamus kynge freſſhe luſty great fayreneſſe hym hadde infynyte rycheſſe treaſoure golde paſſyngly plente euerydele brought ye remembre lyſt take hede ye quyte indigence nede occaſyon great gode thorugh manhode ſhad nat y• blode mercyles full cruell wyſe ſake kynge fryſe treaſour cofres ſought yfere ſege ybrought knyghthode ſythe go full yore haue nat eke augmented made grekes londe poſſeſſyons conqueſt oonly two regyons thorugh prudence labour wonne sythen ye ſege firſte begonne prouynces troye adiacent encreaſe ſo dylygent achylles worthy warryoure ye experte full well laboure wrought auauntage ſythen ye ſo prudent ſage nat foryetyll fully remembrynge nedeth nat reherſe euery thynge diſpreue manly knyght tytle cleyme hath ryght dome cōmyttynge oppynyons reherſayle condycyons nouther hath manhode proweſſe force knyghode nouther hardyneſſe poynt haue rewarde dorynge preued cowarde experyence hath ſhewed dede whan cometh nede worde wynde ſleyghty cōpaſſynge falſhode euer ymagynynge euer yet daye preuyd thynge hym acheuyd whiche myght entytled laude ende medlyd fraude vnder coloure cure alle pretende fayre lyke paynted walle dyuerſe hewed nouther hye lowe may man playne menȳge knowe ſuche ſleyghte cōpaſſyd treaſon troye gat palladyon whiche great ſhame ſclaundre v alle conqueſt thus befalle treaſon haue cyte wonne knyghthode men reporte konne crop rote reherſe ſhall vlixes grounde cauſe gynnynge firſte vnhappy fame reboundeth alder ſhame ſyth trouthe platly knowen wyſte tale endyde deme ye lyſte vlixes aduertence conceyued hath great inpacyence thelamon great enuye feruent rancoure melancolye forbare hym firſte full great aduyſe full prudent right wyſe thought wolde make therof iape worde haſte ſhulde eſcape nouther none vnbrydled countenaunce outwarde conceyued regardaunce abraydynge ſtable face syres quod ſo may haue grace vnder ſupporte hye preſence tale may haue audyence nouther doute drede equyte ſhall poſſede palladyon durynge lyues day maugre myght ſay nay ye lyſte reaſon ſe ſege layde firſte cyte haue ſelfe double wyſe quyt well knyghthode ſothly wyt thorugh counſayle beſy cure ofte cauſe theyr diſcomfyture aye dylygent auauntage worught compaſſyd vnto theyr damage day ſothe ne hadde hadde floured theyr felycyte theyr force contuned welfare trouthe ſhall nat ſpare dempt lokyd reaſon moſte cauſe theyr confuſyon ſo euer agaynſt replye ofte wente embaſſatrye importable coſtes diſpenſe treate aye concludynge ſentence forthrynge entencyowne diſencreaſe hyndrynge towne whan ſawe mene none myne aduyſe wyttes euerychone force cyte wyn whyle hadde y• relyke within therupon ſo ſotelly ywrought vnto palladyon ybrought ¶whiche thelamon malys ſtryueth olde hatrede vnto gylt aſcryueth hoolly thynge y• haue worught ye ſo prudent thought aduerteth wyſely ende maketh honde quarell fully taketh palladyon iuſtly prouyde fauour let layde ſyde syth thynge ye platly vnderſtonde let v demynge ſtonde one aſſent ſo mater wende lo tale ende thelamon ire full feruent hate made inpacyent enuye inwardly ameued vlixes hath diſpyteouſly repreued oonly malys hye diſdayne vlixes rebukynge hym agayne full bytterly without abode anone ſo twayne made full mortall fone preſence agamenon furyouſly ayax thelamon melancolye pale nothynge rede thratte vlixes ſhalbe dede hondes ſhulde nat eſchewe grekes tho rancour remewe quarell put arbytracyon menelay agamenon cauſed full mortall ſtryfe ſentence anone diffynytyfe put vlixes poſſeſſyon perpetuelly palladyon hym confermynge abyde ſtable cauſe fauourable vlixes lyke guydo wryt ſo goodly hath hym quyt vnto eleyne gettynge towne beynge cauſe hir • auacyon diſpeyred hir lyfe drede grekes wyllynge haue hir dede thorugh prudent medyacyon maugre myght thelamon hath quene fro deth preſerued albe ſhe hadde well deſerued grekes ſayde theyr oppynyon thus defrauded palladyon ye haue herde worthy knyght manhode great myght thorugh gan herte brede paſſynge enuye full great hatrede thought wolde auenged ſome day vpon vlixes menelay eke alſo vpon agamenon brake lyke wood lyon knyghtes aboute hym y• ſtronge ſayde playnely great wronge deed wolde auenged ſpecyally ylke thre therwithall furyous wrothe tournynge backe anone goth herte fret full mortall tene many greke quarell ſuſtene herte ſore gan diſdayne agayne vlixes tother twayne full ware ſo euer falle theyr knyghtes made aboute calle great ſtuffe wake ſlepe awayte manly kepe full good watche enuyron cloſe full erely ſonne aroſe worthy ayax bed vpryght ymurdred ſelfe ſame nyght bledde morowe founde onpeces hewe many mortall wounde thynge cruell horryble god man lothſome odyble full many greke wofull morowe wepe ſe knyght ſo murdred ſlepe crye noyſe ran thorugh hooſt one fro man man conſtreynt foule dede eueryche felte herte blede full deſyrous make ordynaunce murdre vengeaunce hauynge therof great ſuſpecyon menelay agamenon vlixes moſte ſpecyall comon voyce hym arrettynge foule fame myght nat aſterte pyrrus moſte toke thynge herte makynge vowe furyous wode venged playnely blode thelamon vpon vlixes hede hym manaſynge ſhalbe dede ſore hym fretynge ſorowe vlixes erely morowe drede pyrrus taken hath ſee ſheppes faſte gan flee wente platly rede palladyon toke dyemede hauynge herte full great remors pyrrus taken hath cors thelamon loue ſpecyall dyde make flawme funerall large great colys hoot rede amyddes feruent firy glede full many greke ſtondynge beholde lette brenne aſſhes colde ſtorye tolde herloſed vrne golde full reuerently hath ſhette therupon hath prynt yſette armes curyouſly ygraue myſchefe aſſhes ſaue ſent home great affeccyon conſerued regyon kynge whyle alyue euery thynge perfourmed blyue rytes tho dayes vſed euer one pyrrus hath ymuſed vpon murdre traytourſly ywrought caſte ſhulde full dere abought pyteous deth thelamon hauynge aye herte agamenon hadde eke ſuſpect olde menelay wayte eche lay makynge ſelfe wt theyr knyghtꝭ ſtronge trye hath right wronge pyrrus ne wolde let lyghtly gone thus made mortall fone ylke thre platly deth thorugh falſe enuye whiche hertes ſleeth whyle amonge thē ſelf vntrewe stryfe vpon ſtryfe gan euery day renewe debate multeplye tyll anthenor gan thynge eſpye wyſdome ſtynte diſdayne reconcyled vnto pea agayne cauſed accorde made feſte full royall beſechynge full lowely thre graunt hym therat gentylleſſe grekes myght echone outwarde conceyue alone feſte manly made calle wryt guydo worthy grekes alle hye ne lowe none excepcyon ſhulde make deſcripcyon lordes eſtates ſete ſondry courſes gyftes grete anthenor gaue euery ſyde longe abyde plente ſo great ſuffyſaunce fynde fyll dalyaunce syttyng met ſpeke enee brought hate enmyte diſdayne ſhortely ſentence put hym many great offence ſpecyally theyr haſty tene whylom concyled polycene ſleyghte made hir withdrawe whiche cauſe achylles ſlawe shortly concludynge one oppynyon fynall exyle troye towne nat withſtandynge graunt lyberte gyuen hym abyde cyte alſo longe hym lyſte deuyſe grekes haue annullyd fraunchyſe fro loweſt vp vnto meſte preſent hye feſte douteles nat well eſpye brought conſpyracye troye boke fynde saue hym ſelfe wytte anthenore ilyche falſe bothe one degre ye haue herde betrayſſhynge cyte lyke hadde ſpronge one roote whā knewe none boote eneas dome modefye prayed theyr courteſye leeſt graunte hym grace foure monthes myght haue ſpace make ſtuffe apparayle hymſelfe puruey vytayle eke graunt hym wolde aſſent thylke ſhyppes parys went cytheron vnto temple olde nombre two twenty tolde full graunt petycyowne retourned home troye towne tryſte heuy ſe beholde waſte cyte walles olde ſorowe felte herte blede within hymſelfe whan taketh hede remembred aduertence falſe treaſon great offence hym compaſſyd towne aforne howe ſo ſodaynely hath lorne grace grekes ſtode diſconſolate whylom ſo great eſtate herte fully diſpayred vnwarely ſo euyll apayred vnto grekes behynde backe beyng vngylty without lacke coude nat well deme saue ſygnes dyde ſeme anthenor moſt wyte caſte playnely wold hym quyte thorugh towne made ſende blyue thylke fewe lefte lyue comynge anone cōmaundement whan euerychone preſent syres quod ye ſe fortune towardes gynneth diſcontune aye vnſtable hir eyen blynde ye experte ſelfe fynde whylom frowarde tourned werſe clerkes called aduerſe whan hir lyſte hir cruelte ſhewe ſtandeth ſo ye fewe muſt parte ye ſtylle abyde ſo ye wyll prouyde stondynge alone deuoyde ſocoure amonge ſelfe make gouernoure nat ſe ye ſhalbe acloyed euery parte fynally deſtroyed ſely ſhepe ne rede diſparpled whiche drede wherfore beſt dredfull thynge one aſſent cheſe kynge moſte able eſtate occupye aſſaute manly guye anthenor knyghthode renowne accorde oppynyowne wherfore haſte vnto entent without abode lete hym ſent comynge playnely towne vpon hede let ſet crowne grauntynge hym ſceptre regalye wyſedome may guye aſſaute parturbaunce knyghthode prudent gouernaunce aſſent makynge delay neuer one lyketh ſay nay right gladde maner thynge ye haue herde make hym kynge full lytell ſothly theyr ſonde eneas menynge vnderſtonde ne mente treaſon falſehede entrynge ſhalbe dede full traytourſly awayte liynge ſlee hym falſely cōmynge anthenor thynge ware dyſarmed came wepen bare eneas huge route ſwerdes drawe ſet hym rounde aboute tyll troye yonge olde ran atwene manly hym holde theyr knee fyll mekely downe beſechynge hym haue compaſſyowne worthyneſſe alſo manhede lyke knyght take hede left people bare beſechynge hym dredfull ſwerde ſpare rancoure yre leue leſt ſlaughtre wolde greue comon beſought hym rewe quod eneas nat vntrewe nat double traytoure eke falſe worthy enhanged halſe deſceyte fraude welle amonge comon worthy dwelle hath nat chefe occaſyon vndoynge deſtruccyon newe ſerpent whiche gothe vndiſſerued make grekes wrothe agayne falſe coll •• yowne myne exyle conſpyred fro towne whiche may nat repellyd withdrawe ſwerde firſte ſhalbe ſlawe falſhede may fynally daunted right hath traytourſly ſupplaunted grekes menynge fer yle engyne playnely exyle caſte myght haue bothe ioye aduerſyte haue parte ſo falle durynge lyfe amonge alle thurgh wronge kourbed deſyre hath fyne perturbed whiche herte abydeth alway grene nat cauſe eke polycene yſlawe achylles graue yet ye wolde hym ſaue vtterly ſhall mene gayne ſo euer agaynſt playne whoſe herte al treaſon hath compyled perpetuelly ſhall exyled towne ſhall man lette aſſent tyme ſette whiche ſhulde raunſon pace fyne gete none grace thus bothe falſe brother lyke brother eueryche hath exyled traytours bothe troye cytee anthenor hym eke enee anthenor gan hym redy make haſte hath ſee ytake many troyan great apparayle wynde good began ſayle many coſte many ſondry yles nedeth nat reherſe myles perrelles playnely whiche great myſchefe eſcaped ſee haue ioye therupon dwelle auentures telle ſhortly lytell whyle aryued vp noble yle whylom gorbodya ycalled bylt cyte ſtrongly walled wryt guydo large wyde longe vpon roche whiche paſſyngly ſtronge whiche enuyron myn auctour telles woddes ryuers many luſty welles hadde plente maner thynge tethydes called kynge helde pea ſceptre crowne fortune lyſt nat frowne fauourable fully wylle conſeruynge hym pea tranquylle without trouble many daye afore acceptyd anthenore right welcome ſtorye ſayth vnto hym confederate fayth fully aſſured came lege man whan tethydes euer worthy kynge dyde magnefye fro troye great nombre allye came ſoth vyſyte hym ſe enhabyte myghty ſtronge cyte full curyouſly bylte lyme ſtone dayes called menelone whiche dyde great rycheſſe croche beſyde ſee ſet vpon roche beſy plente aſtore traytoure ſhulde wryte name penne ſo cloyed whoſe falſhede troye deſtroyed ſtorye ye haue red ſeyne muſte playnely reſorte ageyne reherſe beſy cure caſſandra tolde euery auenture grekes ſhulde falle ſhe tolde amonge alle ſhe prudent vertuous traytourſly within owne hous agamen ſhulde murdred fatall ende thynge myght fle let hym beware prudently prouyde lyfe ſhall nat longe abyde agayne fate none rede eke guydo wryt whā thelamon dede falſe murdre ye haue herde toforne two ſones hadde ofſondry wyues borne cōmytted kepynge worthy tentre full manly kynge nouryſſhed ye ſtorye ſayth ſothe tyll worthy knyghtes bothe tone called anthenycus tother hyght antiſſacus ſhape full ſemely wonder fayre face ſhortly guydo doth forth pace lyſt lenger proceſſe make bryngeth menelay hath take leue grekes agamenon eueryche ſayle regyon many greke theyr companye though grekes firſte gan denye laſte inſtaunce payne hadde leue ſayle bothe twayne ſee faſte gan hye myd autumpne whiche colde drye melancolyke complexyon whan phebus paſſyd lyon heuenly beeſt beeſt moſt royall halfe yronne ſygne virgynall whiche ſomer naked bareyne whan cere hath full ryped euery grayne tyme yere ſtraunge full dyuers ſondry floures red whyte pers whiche may ſo luſty glade vpon theyr ſtalke gan droupe fade enclyne theyr freſſhe luſty cheres goynge canyculeres whan wycked humour inwardly habounde ſodayne feuer folkes confounde make ax ſhake cuſtome wyndes gynne wake bothe bough leef cauſynge falle tyme whan folke bachus calle fro ſtorme rayne grape conſerue hydous tempeſt make nat ſterue dureſſe fretynge froſte thorugh full ofte moche fruyte loſte moyſture cometh fro ſkyes euen alſo eke thondrynge leuen whiche vnwarely ſuche weders kene boyllynge vp many wawes grene rorynge rough frowarde manaſſe paſſyngly peryllous paſſe albe blandyſſhynge whyle dredful calme though ſmoth ſmyle truſt wyll longe abyde recorde grekes ſuche luſty tyde ſee haue take began ſayle theyr ſtuffe theyr apparayle home grece full many luſty man golde treaſour y• wan ſege infynyt rycheſſe dayes thre deuoyde diſtreſſe ſee obeyed fully theyr wyll deuoyde trouble wedres yll full luſty within ſhyppes borde foure wyndes beynge accorde conueye euery maner coſte gladly euer whan men truſte moſte vnto fortune ſtonde hir grace sheſodaynely chaunge hir face smyle afore mowe bake ſhe vnwarely tourned wrake chauntereſſe ſtormye quene whan grekes effectuouſly beſt wene theyr paſſage fully aſſured vpon ſee called egee falſe goddes anone forſooke boreas fell wynde awooke hydous dredfull noyſe ſowne tourned theyr quyete vp ſo downe made wawes gryſely aryſe ſtorye ſhortly doth deuyſe bryght daye tourned nyght heuen derke except dredfull lyght leuen whiche made ſore gaſte thondre ſeuered ſayle maſte theyr toppes ſmette peces ſmale water made lowe auale fyre lyghtnynge ſodaynely therwith wolcanus forgeth ſtyth hath borde fro borde flawme rent two twenty theyr ſhyppes brent without eſcape platly refuge thorughe rage fell deluge wrake wofull nauy goth whylom grekꝭ mynerua ſo wroth dyde hir reuerence ſpecyally great offence ſpytefully cylleus ayax wrought whiche tempeſt full dere abought whan ſhyppes almoſt ydrowned goddeſſe hath ſo hym frowned vengeaunce ſo felly hym awaked fayne ſwymme naked ſayth myn auctour myſchefe ye londe founde ſonde almoſte deth without remedye hym mynerua hath ſo great enuye ſo woodly hir temple wente caſſandra tofore hir auter hente cruell force hatefull vyolence lo perell offence hye deſpyte holy place doute nat ſhall fayle grace ſo euer vſeth dede laſte god wyll quyte mede rewarde hym lyke diſſerueth ſuch thyng many greke ſtreueth bycauſe oonly ſuche occaſyon exemplefye preſumpcyon folyly atame haue tolde agayne god ſo bolde shall repente ſooner weneth many man harmene meneth suffreth vengeaunce treſpaſſe one firſte auctour goth nat quyte alone many offence abayth ceryouſly guydo wryt ſayth suynge ordre wofull auenture euery greke homewarde dyde endure hye lowe ſparynge none eſtate ſome welfull ſome infortunate bothe theyr woo theyr welfare right fyll ſtorye ſhall declare grece whylom worthy kynge manly ryche prudent oflyuynge hadde ſothe lyke wryt guydo tyme worthy ſones two pallamydes eldeſt brother oetes called tother bothe twayne one moder borne ſtorye reherſeth hath toforne pallamydes noble knyght full famous eke power myght fer ſpoke many ſondry cooſt hadde alſo grekes hooſt wyſedome whylom gouernayle ala ſlayne batayle thorugh vnhap martys cruell tene whan ſonne ſhone moſt bryght ſhene knyghthode worthyneſſe lyke tofore ſtorye bereth wytneſſe deth doth playnely ſpecefye nowe malys hatrede enuye ſuche haue tunges infortunate make oonly kynge naulus debate grekes contryued haue newe hye treaſon falſe full vntrewe ſoth neuer wrought effect ymagyned thought falſe thynge yfeyned malyce kynge ſo manly ſo wyſe ſo prudent pallamydes shulde enuye god wot cauſeles ſege troye cyte vpon nyght falſely murdred ſlaughter lothſome dede • vlixes dyomede fully wrought ye haue herde deuyſe whiche euery herte ought agryſe falſe alſo tale haue fayned kyng naulus haue traytourſly cōplayned albe dede neuer mente grekes alſo aſſente murdre conſpyracyon menelay agamenon albe ſothe euery • ele falſe hanged hye halfe tale ſo forge contryue make frendes cauſeles ſtryue thorugh fraude falſe colluſyon kynge naulus put ſuſpecyon grekes hadde conſpyred douteles vpon murdre pallamydes makyng theyr groūde dyd fayne fro troye ſent lettres twayne pallamydes inmedyatly dyrect whiche concluded treaſon effect hye eſtat falſly allyed confederat troye ſūme golde haue fayned ytolde hadde cyte good receyued huge quantyte fyne oonly grekes betraye prolonge platly delaye ſege gettynge towne engyne medyacyowne conferme ſentence make naulus gyue full credence ſayd playnely concluſyowne lettres whiche y• ſent fro towne yfounde encloſed ſhelde vpon knyght yſlayne felde comprehendynge hole trecherye treaſon full confederacye atwene towne pallamydes veryly though gylteles gyue open euydence make prefe great offence ſayde vlixes affermynge certayne accorded chaumberlayne offyce pallamydes wonder ſecrete thynge reckeles aſſente conſpyracye wrongly compaſſyd brennynge hote enuye behotynge hym guerdon great mede lyke deuyſe execute dede take treaſour ſūme gode full ſecretely knyt hode hyd whan voyded prees vnder bedde pallamydes put grekes ſuerte treaſoure ſame quantyte ne myght denyed lyke lettres hadde ſpecyfyed whan founde knowe thorugh hooſt noyſed yblowe bothe lettres golde alſo fro poynt poynt accordynge bothe two whiche y• kynge aſſentynge treaſowne receyued hadde troye towne aſſented ye haue herde telle grekes tho lenger wolde dwelle ſhope forth one entent haſte came vnto tent kynge full innocent clene lytell knewe wolde mene vpon hym full knyghtly ſtode theyr ire furyouſly wode venged loude gan crye may man theyr malyce modefye hym ſo mercyles fynde moſte ſpecyall kynge menelay agamenon oonly meued indignacyon wolde haue proceded vnto iugement haſty rancoure withoute auyſement treaſon auenged bee nat withſtandynge hye degree ſotheneſſe whan worthy kynge conceyued hath malyce werkynge firſte aſtoned inwarde ſyght ſodaynely ſtert vp lyke knyght wyſe worthy pallamydes hardy lyon amyd prees thynge agaſte hym knyghtly gan expreſſe playnely ſayde wolde nat refuſe acquyte hym ſelfe horryble caas nat exceptynge ſo worthy byrthe blode hye kynrede deuoydynge knyghthode māhede gaue lyfe deth fors tofore iuparde cors within felde lyſte ordeyne lyke knyght quarell dareyne lyſt durſte vndertake excepcyon hym lyked none make hye lowe ſo bolde preue reaſon haue tolde beſechynge make delay prolonge hym ſame day manly requerynge may haſte y• falſly thynge compaſte anſwere ſtoned echone hooſt nat one hardy ſhall nat feyne chaump cloſe quarell dareyne nouther vlixes nouther dyomede chefe worker foule dede ¶but vlixes cuſtomable euery thynge deceyuable double werke full aye diſceyte lyke ſerpent lyeth awayte whiche vnder floures ſo glyde trace right ſo vlixes fayned face whan y• ſawe knyghtly hye proweſſe manly chere hardyneſſe hye renowne pallamydes anone falſhede put hym ſelfe prees lyke frende mente nat wele brotell glaſſe pretendynge outwarde ſtele one firſte gan hym excuſe counſayllynge longer muſe matere theyr alder eaſe crafte gan ſo appeaſe touchynge rumoure hye treaſon hath voyded ſuſpecyon theyr hertes concludynge tertayne accuſynge made vayne conſpyred oonly hatrede albe hym ſelfe roote dede ¶but whan ſawe myght nat acheue ye haue herde worthy kynge greue ſpot treaſon hym laye hehath anone founde another waye aſſent fully dyomede vnder pretenſe playnely frendelyhede comynge hym agayne certayne nyght vnderſuraunce trewe knyght counſayle kepe outher ſote ſoure enformynge hym great treaſoure golde good infynyte ryches hym diſcured vnder ſecretenes whiche ſothly man dyde knowe hyd encloſyd welle lowe within felde lytell ſyde whiche hym lyſte fro hym nat hyde truſte vnto hym diſcure wolde beſy cure ſame nyght hym go vnto welle thre mo fette away great ſūme gode ſothe thynge vnderſtode mente aſſentyd anone ſo thre togydre gone vnto well lyke haue tolde moſte manly bolde pallamydes lyke hym telle deſcended lowe welle suppoſynge haue treaſour founde ala hym falſly confounde haue murdred hym wt ſtones great huge botome hauynge refuge whā acomplyſſhed entent repeyred eueryche tent tale ſtorye telleth v feyned ye kynge naulus touchynge deth pallamydes deſclaundre gylteles vlixes dyomede innocent platly rede grekes bothenygh ferre ſlayne knyghtly werre durynge ſege parys arowe falſe fayne full narowe fynde tale neuer yet thought treaſon ſhuld haue wrought touchynge lettres ſent towne ſuche conſpyracyowne grekes wrought fable vnſoth falſly feyned make naulus wroth vlixes dyomede alſo agamenon grekes mo lette homewarde theyr waye hyndre alſo ſaye repeyre theyr regyons naulus occaſyons oetes ſone manly man accorded may one aſſent auenge mercyles cruell murdre pallamydes ordayne theyr home paſſage worke fully theyr damage grekes muſte neceſſyte homewarde ſayle foreby countre wherfore kynge ſhapen hath wyle hyl • e hye lytell yle wynter ſeaſon euery maner nyght make fyres ſette vp lyght cauſe ſee erre grekes ſawe fyre ferre vnware harme caſte lande coude perell vnderſtande ſhope theyr full myght aryue faſte lyght wherwith ij hondred theyr ſhyppes brake amonge rockes fully go wrake drowned many worthy man thus vengaunce alderfirſte began kynge naulus hath grekes take deedly hate ſones ſake great myſchefe confuſyon grekes nauye agamenon great perell deth eſcaped hadde almoſte amonge beiaped erles duke worthy kynges crowned thorugh trayne ſee drowned menelay alſo dyomede eſcaped myſchefe rede whan daunger gone oetes wood foryre one herte ſhope another wyle thought wolde agamenon begyle compaſſynge full mortall ſtryfe let ſende lettre anone wyfe myghty great agamenon whiche included falſe treaſon euen lyke ſhall nat lye thus effect dyde ſpecyfye firſte hir lorde agamenon kynge hadde ſege wrought wonder thynge preiudyce ſclaundre hir name albe hir maner blame lyke wrote platly treſpace knyghtly honoure foly difface ſay guydo telleth thus loued doughter kynge pryamus beaute hadde hir wyfe take hir herte fynally forſake worthy quene whylom great fame clemeſtra ſothly hir name wonder ſemely right fayre deſcent borne ſtocke royall hir celly nge eke hir excellence albe ſhe neuer dyde offence yet hir lorde newe fangylneſſe toke nother lettres dyde expreſſe fully purpoſe anone repayre though clemeſtra bothe good fayre ſodaynely hir exyle londe many thouſande myle warnynge hir ſhe prudent ſubſtaunce ſentement oetes wrote vnto quene albe kynge innocent clene hir fore lyuynge louynge trewe maner thynge hir pleaſe paſſynge ententyfe worde dede durynge lyfe fer oughte reaſon deſyred lettres falſly conſpyred haue hir put parcas innocence gyue haſty credence thankynge firſte oetes trouthe ſo goodly hym lyſt haue routhe vpon hir wronge hye compaſſyon yet ſtorye maketh mencyon afterwarde ſhall deſcryue ſhe falſeſt one alyue vnto hir lorde longe abſence haſte ſhe made ſtronge • ffence agayne thynge gan hir purueye ſuche fraude ſhe nat ne deye hir werke ſothe ſhe wyte whiche ala muſte anone endyte ſtorye platly doth lere whiche dolefull mortall ovnſure truſte worldly glorye wt ſodayne chaūge put memorye ioye vnſtable vayne ambycyon vnware tourne reuerſed vp ſo downe ydell fame blowe vp ſkye ouer whelmyd twynclynge eye pompe boſte tryumphe victorye lyke ſhadowe waſte tranſytorye fortune falſe vnaſſured man neuer fully lured hye lowe maner eſtate bonde fayth conferate agayne whoſe myght man may hȳdiffende tourne ſhall diſcende whan ſyt hyeſt thyne vnſtable whele thy brotyll fauour forged nat ſtele meynt allayed mutabylyte welfulneſſe falſe felycyte ſodayne ſweygh frowarde yu canſt auale freſſhe chere anger pale hye diſdayne thou ſpareſt degree prynces duke hyeſt theyr ſee myghty kynges worthy emperours rycheſt reygne theyr royall floures sceptre crowne yu canſt pull downe take wytneſſe agamenowne ſo noble myghty lyue ſondry auctours hye renown deſcryue ſothfaſtly excellence myght nat make diffence kynges baner ſewe conſpyred murdre voyde eſchewe reſcuſe none coude make whiche ala penne fele quake doth myn ynke blotte boke myghty god y• thyne inwarde loke seeſt euery thynge thurgh thy eternal myght wylt thou nat equyte ryght punyſſhe chaſtyſe ſo horryble thynge ſpecyally murdre kynge ala payne ixyon helle mane sathan dwelle nat egall equypolent venge murdre ſuffycyent excedeth comparyſon felonye falſhede treaſon wherfore lorde ſeeſt knoweſt thorugh thy power eternall suffre ſuche lyue vpon ye grounde worſe tygre cerberus hounde chayned lyeth bounde helle gate whiche malyce playnely though hate berketh firſte offence murdre gladly wrought ſylence men aduerte take kepe ala prynce ſle hym ſlepe pyllowe whan ſlepeth ſofte cryeth wreche hye god lofte axeth vengaunce take faſte though abyde wyll laſte ala kynge ſpoken ſo ferre ſo worthy outwarde werre cruell fate paſſynge odyous diſpoſed hath owne hous mortall ende execute agaynſt whiche refute right ſhyppe londe ſette quene clemeſtra ye ſtronde hȳ mette humble chere loke full benygne ſhewed full many faythfull ſygne wyfely trouthe hir countenauce albe herte varyaunce nat parceyued playnely hir face kynge goodly dyde enbrace ſoth trouthe mente paleyſe hye way went nat aduertynge treaſon ſhape whiche ala myght nat eſcape falſhede coude thynge fele ne may lenger concele agayne hir lorde clemeſtra wrought hir bonde wedlocke ſhe ne thought trewe loke ſothly ſpouſayle agayne hir malyce lytell myght auayle vnto hir lorde hir trouthe conſerue newfangelneſſe cauſed ſtreue hir olde fayth hir aſſuraunce hir loue abode fykyll chaunce longe abſence hadde hir herte appalled loued one egiſtus called whiche afore hir grace ſtode nouther byrthe blode lytell nought reputacyowne renowned manhode renowne knyghthode hye proweſſe labour beſyneſſe good awayte vpon hir nyght therfore beſt furthrede hir ſyght suche drede hadde ſhe lyue alone sorowles ſo well ſhe coude grone nat ſay lyfe ladde except ſhe hym doughter hadde exyona guydo ſayth ſhe hyght vnto hym clemeſtra behyght aſſurynge hym vpon payne hir hede ſhulde reygne whan hir lorde dede enhaſte concluſyon hir worthy lorde kynge agamenon nexte nyght murdred yſſayne falſe egiſtus quene full fayne lenger bode ſtorye lere haſte wedded yfere hir falſe ſleyghty compaſſynge meſſene ſhe made hym crowned kynge put hym full poſſeſſyon ala ſynne hath domynacyon furthre wronge abate ryght worlde falſhede hath myght full ofte ſythe hath rightwyſeneſſe eſtate ſette worthyneſſe loo ſynne auoutrye brought murdre conſpyracye synne vpon ſynne lynked twayne enbraced fendes chayne perpetuelly helle endure ala ſhall hymſelfe full aſſure fro cruell murdre body withdrawe whan kynges theyr bed ſlawe whiche bryngeth alyenacyon extort tytle falſe ſucceſſyon may coloure pretenſe ſeme full ſtraytely god ſhall deme iuſtly venge dewe recompence intruſyon brought vyolence felly quyte ſuche horryble thynges ſodayne ſlaughter ſpecyally kynges greatly drede euery regyon fynde agamenon clemeſtra falſe double quene hadde ſone paſſynge fayre ſene right gracyous euery mannes ſyght horeſtes boke ſayth hyght wonder ſemely yonge age great fere mortall rage lyſte ſlayne drede anulle tytle nat ſuccede hym preſerue nat ſhent kynge taltybus power hath hym ſent full ſecretely countre vnto kynge called ydume helde ſceptre royall ſete full myghtely lande crete carkaſys named quene hadde doughter called eke clymene borne heyre regyon made eke mencyon horeſtes reken thynge quene alſo kynge cheryſſhed well ſtorye lere clymen theyr owne doughter dere eke kept hadde cherte fro poynt poynt lyke degre attendaunce conuenyent dewe eſtate euer vpon hym ſewe ſuche moſte expert ſage gouerne hym tyll came age reioyſe god gaue hym myght herytage whiche hadde ryght clere diſcent happy chaunce thus leue hym vnder gouernaunce yonge lone agamenon muſte make dygreſſyon ¶fro mater telle dyomede auentures guydo rede wofull fate paynes ſmerte whiche ala myght nat aſterte remembred playnely wrytynge oeres ſone ryche kynge called naulus ye haue herde toforne suche heuyneſſe herte hath borne vnto grekes repeyrynge home fro troye luſte inwarde ioye hyndre bothe hye lowe cauſe nat vnknowe ſo paſſynge enuyous wyll thought ylyke deſyrous myght ſothly le deth venge pallamydes lyke tofore ſtroye deuyſe ſo prudent ſo wyſe oetes malyce wrought traytourſly newe menes ſought myght maner weye dyomedes vnwarely deſtroye thynge caſte nat fayle ceryouſly make reherſayle grece kyngdome wyde large conyumpt one calydonye arge full habundaunt rycheſſe rente whiche kynge called pollente worthy man noble fame ſone aſſandrus name doughter paſſynge fayre ſyght ſothly egra fynde ſhe hyght hir fader lyke wryt guydo hadde nomo thyſe childre two hath wyſedome ſo prouyded myghty reygne deuyded atwene two diſſees eche parte lyue pee exclude fro indigence nede ſhe wyfe vnto dyomede albe tofore ſtorye hym ſayde whylom loued well cryſayde nat ſay doubleneſſe well wot guydo bereth wytneſſe boke ſothely ſayth none aſſandrus owne wyues brother full luſty freſſhe full manlyhede troye wente dyomede ſee fordyuen vp ſo downe ryued vp regyon called boece diſconſolate tempeſt dryue wery full mate refreſſhe none thynge whiche lande thelephus kynge whoſe ryuayle whan herde ſayne herte hadde hye diſdayne bolde ſo great offence entre grounde hauynge lycence yet ſothe dyde damage hye lowe maner age nortoke nat myght diſauayle vnto lande vytayle whiche payde iuſtly fyne fleſſhe fyſſhe brede wyne yet indignacyowne kynge thelephus deſcended downe great array harme myght ſo gan bycker fyght aſſandrus full hye proweſſe lyke lyon fomen gan oppreſſe wonder knyghtly ye feld vpon wan ſlewe day many worthy man hye courage manly pryde whan kynge whiche ſtode aſyde sawe men ſlayne euery parte hye diſdayne hent anone darte caſte hym ala mortall fate ꝑcyd hath thurgh mayles thurgh plate aſſandrus felle downe dede ſoyle aboute blode rede deedly wounde ſo began blede wood tygre tho came dyomede hym auenge bare hym lyke knyght sleeth kylleth put vnto flyght ſuche ſorowe gan make knyghtly routhe brothres ſake ne wyſte beſt fynde myd wo beſte foule deed corp ſaue lyke eſtate lette make graue buryed hym rytes olde oetes ſuſter tolde ſlayne fraude dyomede fyne myght full poſſede reygne arge hole without ſtryfe purpartye annexed wyfe deth myght ſeaſon take tolde hir eke ſhe forſake fayre egra hir womenhede hir lorde called dyomede tolde helle chayned ouermore forged hath fayned enuye aſſandrus loſt lyfe howe hir lorde hath take nother wyfe hir diſhonour ſhame paſſyngly great ſclaundre hir name preiudyce ydone hir eſtate tolde make debate lyke wrote concluſyon clemeſtra agamenon whiche hir herte made ſore greue put hir fully byleue treaſon ye haue herde tolde yre ſhe pale wexe colde vnkyndeneſſe ſo hir herte ſleeth heuyneſſe hir brothre • deth neuer yet guydo doth aſſure woman loued better creature ſhe loued hym maner age firſte nought ſhe ſette hir herytage comparyſon hir brothres lyfe loo oetes made newe ſtryfe ye haue herde ſtorye rede gylteles worthy dyomede whan hath longe ſege layne kyngdome wold haue come agayne myghty honde worthy quene hir lyeges aſſentyd bene exyled regyon may made medyacyon thus hym ſelfe mate diſpeyred diſconſolate agayne repeyred salerne londe great rycheſſe tenter thorugh worthyneſſe crowne ſceptre hadde reygned longe lyeges knyghtes ſtronge brother apax thelamon murdred tofore made mencyon dyomede pore deſtytute may salerne fynde refute whan tenter firſte gan hym eſpye ſewed hym full great enuye hauynge hym aye ſuſpecyon touchynge deth kynge thelamon dyomede certayne nyght full ſecretly hath taken hym flyght fro salerne faſte gan hym hye hope fynde better remedye helpe ſocoure ſome place fortune wolde graunte hym grace hymſelfe aſhamed confuſe man forſake abiect refuſe right ſo fared wandrynge fro ne wyſt beſt bvt fynde troyan eneas al whyle ſtyll troye oonly routhe compaſſyowne ſupporte lefte towne beynge alway theyr lyfe doute theyr fomen rounde beſet aboute lyued lacke hede contynuelly myſchefe drede knowynge refute comforte caas tyll counſayle eneas ſupporte great nede ſent haſte dyomede knowynge full well deſolacyon proſcrip fro regyon beſechynge hym manhode routhe hym enhaſte without ſlouthe ſtuffe get ſouldeours alſo manly euery man without abode troye lede ſocoure great nede dyomede came taryed nought theyr requeſt beſought releue ſharpe ſhoure hym brought many ſouldeoure eneas way hym mette frendely wyſe towne hym fette hym made paſſyngly great chere gan comune yfere theyr auentures bothe lande ſee entermedlyd great aduerſyte man may deuoyde eſchewe take parte hym dewe ſorte hap doth brydell lede ſtorye ſhortly procede cely troyans almoſt ſhent theyr fomen yles adiacent beſette aboute enuyrowne thorugh manhode hye renowne dyomede ſouldeours knyghtes noble werry reſkued holpen vtterly foure dayes foughte knyghtly wyſe deffendynge cyree thorugh proweſſe alſo enee ſlewe toke withſtode diffence troyanyſſhe blode suche fonde cyte falſe henge vp hye halſe punyſſhed theyr great wronge dyomede thus gan wexe ſtronge longe proceſſe made mencyowne chefe protectoure nowe troye towne enmye none large ſpace durſte abyde hadde grace lygaunce ſo made loute thus name ſprede gan aboute fame great oppynyon dylated vnto regyon ſwyfte reporte calydonye arg • whiche quene greatly gan charge aſtoned whan ſhe taketh hede power gan myght drede lyſte wolde hir londe vpon hir wynne knyghthode werre newe begynne ſecretely gan muſe thynge hir lorde hir myghty kynge late exyled yput flyght hath grace founde fortune ſyght remounted ſo hye eſtate wherof ſhe hir ſelfe chekmate wayes caſte ſhe prudent hole aduyſe hir parlement without grutchynge rebellyon hym reuoke regyon ¶and therupon hym lowly ſent lettres meſſager forth went cauſe annullyng exyled fully reconcyled hole aſſente lyeges alle full lowly euerychone calle theyr offence theyr treſpace without rygoure grace anone lyke manly knyght mercy ſothly ryght whan hath theyr ſonde well conceyued theyr menynge fully apparceyued ſtynte ſtryfe thought beſte goodly wyſe grauute theyr requeſte reygne within certayne day repeyred full ryche array whoſe cōmynge full glad lyeges bene reconcyled bothe quene rancoure olde offence oonly wyſdome put ſuſpence one herte blyſfull lyfe lede troye boke hym rede lette hym lyue felycytee agayne reſortynge tell enee hath tyme ſpent whiche fro troye wt many troyan went ſhyppes ſtuffed meynee ſayled forth many ſtraunge ſee many daunger many ſtrayte paſſage tofore aryued cartage ledynge hym fader anchyſes way fynde le wyfe crewſa fatall auenture woo dyde endure ſo lyſte ceryouſly ſene falſehede quene mene dido womanhede floure gaue hym hir rycheſſe treaſoure iewellys golde y• myght hym pleaſe euery thynge myght hym eaſe vnkynde rede eneydos ye ſhall fynde falſely ſtale away nyght tyme whyle ſhe bedde lay conqueſte alſo itaylle hadde many ſtronge bataylle auentures workes fyne hym fall ye may ſe full ſouerayne ſtyle fro poynt poynt compyled virgyle wryte made ſythen go full yore troye boke ſpeketh hym procedeth ſhall endyte horeſtes caſte hym quyte fadres deth playnely nat ſpare ye lyſte guydo ſhall declare requered equyte ryght iuge moſte myght egally holdeth balaunce deth conſpyred vengaunce voyſe blode doth ſo aye contune crye wreche clamour importune ſothe iniuſtly ſhede murdre wrought wyll haue egal mede guerdon hath diſſeruyd may nat flee iugement reſeruyd hym ſytte hyeſt trone beholdeth hym ſelfe alone full rightfully noble myghty kynge though ſuffre foryet thynge conſydereth inſpeccyon murdre agamenon myghty lorde yt moſt ſouerayne gode made mynyſtre ſame blode ¶yonge horeſtes full hye proweſſe execute dome ryght wyſneſſe gaue hym grace power myght anone toke ordre knyght • lyke tolde whan foure twenty wynter olde freſſhe luſty wonderly prudent wardely deſyrous entent fortune wolde hym nat withſayne herytage recure agayne ¶whiche egiſtus falſly hym denyeth crowne iuſtly occupyeth falſe tytle hir wyfe horeſtes wyll iuparde lyfe auenture whyle hym laſteth breth firſte venged fadres deth vpon tho treaſon wrought alderfirſte full lowely beſought kynge y•dumee goodlyhede forther hym great nede kynge benygnely anone aſſigned hath hym gone thouſande knyghtes manly right ſtronge redreſſe great horryble wronge egiſtus wroughte vyolence wyſedome dylygence horeſtes gan hym ſo purueye within whyle ſeye hym gat ſtore wyll nat lye another thouſande companye worthy knyghtes one accorde go hym wt theyr ſouerayne lorde euery thynge byddynge obeye ye haue herde egiſtus werreye thus horeſtes full ryche array gan hooſtey made delay lodgynge alderfirſte gan cheſe cytee called troyeſe receyued great reuernece kynge named forence manly knyght bookes ſpecefye bare herte paſſynge great enuye egiſtus double occaſyon firſte deth agamenon eke hadde doughter dere hym wardly entere good fayre yonge age whylom gyuen maryage egiſtus doubylneſſe falſe treaſon new fangylneſſe kynges doughter hath vtterly forſake haſte dyd lybell make forge wryt repulſyon albe hadde trewe occaſyon egiſtus hir forſoke saue falſly wyue toke quene clemeſtra agayne ryght lawe whan aſſent murdred haue ſlawe gamenon tofore tolde whylom ſo myghty ſo bolde hatefull falſe conſpyracye well murdre auoutrye venge bothe dewe recompence worthy knyght y• myghty kyng forence offrede horeſtes make hym ſtronge go hym helpe venge wronge hym ladde armed bryght ſtele foure hondred knyghtes horſed wonder wele takynge felde manly chere ſo horeſtes kynge yfere ryden forthe many manly man ¶but horeſtes werre gan whan bryght phebus bole ſhone temple full lowely gone goddes beſt wyſe humble herte dyde ſacryfyſe fully hope better fare bode lyfe deth ſpare without mercy remyſſyon deth venge agamenon clemeſtra moſte wyte make firſte ſwerde byte moder hondes twayne ouer beſy payne without pyte mercye ſhewe ſmale peces tyll ſhe hewe diſmembred ſonder ioynt fro ioynt eke foryet nat poynt iuſtly punyſſhe rygoure ryght egiſtus eke falſe vntrewe knyght nat ſlowe neclygent execute cōmaundement goddes lyſt falle horeſtes knyghtes alle forenſis myghty kynge alſo one herte ſege go cyte called methene within whiche falſe quene clemeſtra god gyue hir harde grace whan horeſtes ſeged hath place knyghtes ſet rounde aboute falſe exiſtus yryden oute gadre men wreke falle vpon ſege breke myght maner ſyde great ſtuffe thus gan ryde takynge vp men euery cooſt tyll hym made full myghty hooſt horeſte whiche ſege lay gouernaunce eſpyeth day day ſent men full ſage ſtoppe wayes lette paſſage made knyghtes full huge route purſue hym euery coſte aboute ſege man fully begonne aſſaute hath towne wonne entrede nyght full late ſette wardes ſtronge euery gate doungeon moſte ſtrong pryncypall byldynge myghty royall horeſtes firſte moder fonde quene clemeſtra lady londe whiche drede ſore gan quake mercyles anone made hir take put chaynes tyll nexte morowe egiſtus god gyue hym euyll ſorowe ſtuffe myght accroche towarde towne faſt gan approche purpoſe full horeſtes greue within ſodaynely releue ſothe myght nat auayle cyte myght abayle horeſtes knyghtes vnwarely haue hym mette attones proudely hym ſette firſte ſlewe men put flyght taken hym maugre myght chaynes lyke hym fynde mercyles full faſte hym bynde ſhet hym vp fetryd pryſowne falſe founde towne aſſentyd wynynge helpynge murdre worthy kynge great werkers conſpyratours agayne theyr lorde ryſynge traytours take bounde rygoure ſame nyght ſhet vp toure tyll morowe lyke lot drawe eueryche vnder fonge lawe lyke decerte excepcyon none whan nyght paſſed gone phebus role eſſwarde ſpere tour ſhone full bryght clere ¶whan clemeſtra rote falſehede brought forthe quakynge hir drede horeſtes iugement yfet ſwerde ſharpe kene whet lyke goddes charged hym toforne peces ſmale hath hir ſhorne made hir bere townes boundes vouryd beſtes houndes pyte none breſte reſeruyd quyt hir fully ſhe hath diſſeruyd fro poynt poynt forgat right nought thā chayned egiſtus forth brought iuſtly dempt rygour lawe herdell naked drawe thorugh towne myght ſe hye hanged tree rot drye agayne ſonne loo howe murdre hath guerdon wonne loo falſehede maſter awake traytours towne ytake galowes enhonged euerychone tyll ſeueryd ſonder bone fro bone hye hylle agayne ſterres ſhene thus towne fro treaſon purgyd clene trouthe augmentyd ymoryd reygne horeſtes full reſtoryd ſtorye ſewynge ſhall expowne daye whan toke crowne whan y• myſte euery cloudy ſkye falſe treaſon conſpyracye tryed vpon euery ſyde falſehede hadde place abyde ſtorye ſayth ordre reherſynge ſame tyme menelay kynge ſee full wawes fro troyewarde aryued crete frely eſcapyd many drede peyne quene goodly freſſhe eleyne cauſe ſhe ſo famous fayre great prees meruayllous repayre fro euery parte hir beaute beholde troye walles nat full olde deſtroyed noble royall towne many man full worthy renowne hath loſte lyfe may man ſay nay eleyne wyfe menelay whan thynge done may none whā kyng knew fully brother gamenon murdre euerydele full tryſte lyked thynge wele inwardly felte full great ſmerte neuewe hadde alſo herte mene horeſtes ſo mercyles lyke tyraunt graceles modre ſlewe pyte morrall y•re cruelte fully caſte wolde blyue ſceptre crowne platly hym depryue full affermynge hatefull caas lawe vnworthy faders reygne heyre poſſede iuſtely conſydred horryble dede attones furyous wrothe without abode vnto ſhyp gothe melancolyke great tene crete ſaylnge athene toke londe ſhyppes borde ¶where duke neſtor gouernour lorde whiche receyueth lyke gentyll knyght power dylygence myght menelaye rancoure great hete gan duke ſecretely trete fynde mene inwarde ſyght depryue horeſtes ryght therupon haue iugement athene holde parlement lordes regyon gyue theron diffynycyon whiche ſhewed openly ynoughe horeſtes owne modre ſloughe maner great offence hym ſelfe tho beynge preſence whan thynge fully dyde eſpye partye gan agayne replye felte hym frely large hym allegynge hadde charge goddes ſhortly declare mortall ſwerde nat ne ſpare vpon clemeſtra roote falſe treaſon ſlewe hir lorde kynge agamenon murdre thorugh hir malys wrought wherfore horeſtes humbly beſought lordes manly herte equyte conſydre aduerte malyce rancoure rage hym depryue herytage syth ſone agamenon borne heyre regyon ye haue herde called methene albe moder clemeſtra quene compaſſyd hadde deſtruccyon duke neſtor ymeuyd reaſon ſuſteynynge horeſtes ryght roſe vp anone lyke manly knyght offrynge hym ſelfe proudely ſake hye quarell vndertake body deth darreyne lyſt tytle withſeyne none companye durſte worde agayne hym replye hoole ſtode oppynyon knyghtly medyacyon bare hym ſo feynynge thynge horeſtes ycrowned kynge meneſte beynge aſſent whan diſſolued parlement horeſtes lyeges trewe receyued crowne newe treate lordes many one kynge menelay made atone gan theyr ire theyr rancourelete y•dumee worthy kynge crete prudently gouerneth matere hermyone yonge doughter dere menelay quene eleyne yonge ſo freſſhe beaute ſouereyne yweddyd without tariynge horeſtes newe luſty kynge bycauſe allyaunce deuoyded rancour diſtaunce atwene kynges menelay olde horeſtes right tolde thus leue beſte eche reygne lyue pea reſte ſtryfe ceaſyd caas erygona doughter egiſtus ye haue herde telle ſorowe drede lyſte lenger dwelle toke rope lyſt thynge ſpare therwithall gan hir ſelfe gnare ſtorye ſayth hye vpon tree hir fyne ye gette wyll forth ceryouſly entreate ſtorye telle greate ovlixes ordre wrytynge thyne auentures come rynge full wonderfull londe ſee entermedlyd great aduerſytee guydo firſte deſcryuynge thy repayre sayth thou founde weder foule fayre agreable thonder ſowne ſtylle ſmothe wt clwdes frowne ſayth alſo thou dyddeſt ordayne thy paſſage myghty ſhyppes twayne apparaylled marchaundyſe thou myghteſt moſte ſecrete wyſe euery myſchefe ſee eſcape ¶but thou haddeſt felle iape auctour thy reſorte doth wryte ſayth vlixes wordes whyte yrobbed rycheſſe gode contraryous wynde ſo agayne hym ſtode dryue confuſyon myghty ſtronge regyon thelamon reygned lyue hent take blyue ¶by myghty honde ſeſyd breſt mercyles put vnder areſt hym hadde ſuſpect workynge touchynge murdre ſame kynge ſo wroughte ſleyghty wyle tale ſette ſuche ſtyle playnely hath iaped fro theyr honde freely eſcaped except queynt fare treaſour ymade full bare paſſage hym vnkouthe fyll agayne wolfe mouthe veryly ſpecyfyed kynge naulus men haue hym eft eſpyed take bounde chayned mercyles murdre kynge pallamydes ſtorye reherſeth certayne prudence ſcaped agayne bothe expert wyſe olde though maner nat fully tolde eſcape thorugh beſy payne daunger theſe kynges twayne tyll thurgh fortune came fro myſchefe fre preſence kynge ydume ſymple array torne apparayle wherof kynge greatly gan meruayle toſe pouert ſo lowe manere made hym good chere though tyme infortunate hym receyueth lyke eſtate whan bothe twayne alone complaynynge vlixes made mone vnto kynge full ſage ceryouſly ſorte paſſage face ſad ſobre chere fro poynt poynt anone ye ſhall lorde quod ſhortly expreſſe truſte haue gentylleſſe ſhall myn auentures alle reherſe right falle firſte whan troye londe forſoke water ſhyppes toke anone wynde peſyble blowe y•le whiche vnknowe called mirma great hab •• daunce thynge pleſaunce may ſyluer golde bought redy founde wanted right nought abode full longe whyle ioye treaſoure gat troye ſhyppes ſtuffed men hole ſounde cōmodyte ylke gounde lyked ſo countre enuyron diſporte recreacyon tariynge thought nat full longe man dyde vnto v wronge tyll daye eyer ſtyll wynde alſo fully wyll ſayled forth quyete pee vnto porte called clauſtafages wherwith meyne longe many day founde thynge accordynge pay weder luſly agreable fayre may truſte outher wynde ayre vpon fayth ſmothe ſkye agayne ſhyppe faſte gan hye taryed nought toke anone ſee smothe calme endurynge dayes three weder founde lacke ſodaynely heuen tourneth blacke hydous tempeſt wawes grene hope haue diſpeyred clene troubled ſpirite made ſo penſyfe without refute eſcape lyfe toſſyd dryuen many ſondry yle tyll laſte caſte vp cecyle recurynge londe great annoye payne tyme reygned kynges twayne remebre douteles tone called sorygenes whiche vnto full contraryous tother named coclopas bretherne byrthe concluſyon ylyke cruell condycyon though ſorte hadde ſhape none bothe twayne fylle attones oppreſſynge full great diſtreſſe spoyled ſhyppes treaſour rycheſſe pyte lyked nat ſpare tyll lefte deſtytute bare good ala mortall chaunce moſte greuaunce whan golde may nomore reſtrayne ſent downe myghty ſones twayne alypham full large longe polypheme myghty gyaūt ſtronge men auenge thē ſo fayne haue hondred ſlayne diſarayed ſtonde diffence malyce ſodayne vyolence toke myſchefe almoſt lorne alphenor myn owne brother ſworne hatefully haue v founde chaynes caſte ſtockes bounde ylocked pryſon make platly mencyon myghty man great polypheme ſuſter hadde ſhortly deme one fayreſt euer yet borne myght beaute ſo beſette aforne nature hir gaue ſuche prerogatyfe clene mayde ſothly wyfe flourynge bothe fayreneſſe bounte alphenor whan dyde ſe albe fetred pryſon loue loſte wyt eke reaſon wexe mad ſo narowe ſhe dyd hȳ bynde saue vpon hir alway mynde cloſed aye peryllous wounde ſyxe monthes thus lay bounde ſay platte trouthe tyll polypheme hadde vpon v • outhe thorugh grace medyacyon quyt v fre pryſon ſhewed v mercy pyte ſorowe great humanyte alphenor ylyke one entent bronde cupyde brent felte parte many mortall fyt tyll ſo wrought ſotyll wyt nyght leef loth ſtale mayde way goth thorugh helpe men wt hym tyme morowe houre pryme polyphemus gan v ſewe whoſe myghty honde myght nat eſchewe ſuche aſſaute v gan make force haue mayde take alphenor mauge rage polypheme vnto damage knyghtes ſo ſore vpon lay myght vnneth ſcape away ſaue ſelfe compaſſyd enuyron deth purſued champyon whan ſawe gayne fle deth ſhortly ſayne whyle geaunt moſt freeſly ſette ſwerde eye ſmette vnto ſhyp companye fledde haſte man myght eſpye ¶where came alphenor fere whan wawes gan clere gracyous wynde gan v wake countre haue anone forſake nat holſome v abyde ¶but man lyke wryt ouyde polyphemus geaunt drede hadde eye amyd forhede whiche vlixes ſmote ſtroke lyke browes braunched oke heer longe berde loke childre aferde whan hadde loſt ſyght amonge hylles ronneth day nyght rage fynde hym ſome refuge caſte rockes great ſtones huge euery parte enuyron countre vlixes auenged thus ſayth ouyde concluſyon boke tranſformacyon methamorphoſeos ye may ſe whan ſo euer leyſer ce • youſly ſtorye rede wrytynge forth wyll procede vlixes face deed pale ydumee tolde forth tale • erſynge thus ſuppryſed awaked fro polypheme whan eſcaped thorugh vnhappe infelycyte yle myddes ſee dryue whan gan nyght elodiū lytell kyngdome hyght ¶where circe great enchauntereſſe thylke tyme lady goddeſſe th •• coude hir crafte ſo wonderly ꝑforme ſodaynely man tranſforme haue lykeneſſe leſe reaſon horſe bere tygre lyon wolfe fox hir lyſte deuyſe hir dredefull craft ſhapen ſuche wyſe myghty hir ſtraunge pocyons hir letuaryes confeccyons ſhe alſo ſo fayre vpon ſe fro hir power man myght fle werke ſorcereſſe ſo founcyd vpon hir fayreneſſe fynally thus ſtode yere hir abode playnely hadde power none myght departe nouther day nyght luſty lyfe ladde whiche tyme childe ſhe hadde right inly fayre goodly ſyght thelagonyus ſotheneſſe hyght whiche afterwarde well reherſe proceſſe wexe manly man ſotyle ſecrete prouydence hir crafte hadde experyence maugre hir enchauntementes olde ſtale away ſhe myght nat holde fynally fate conclude connynge hir crafte gan delude men ſcaped fro hir honde went large fre hir londe thynge lytell dyd auayle way gan ſayle ſleyghte lytell whyle yblowe vp yle ¶where calypha ſuſter circe crowned quene helde hir ſceptre pee whoſe craftes ſo myghty ſo ſtronge maugre wyll ſhe helde full longe ſhe ſothe ſpeke womanhede bounte fredome goodlyhede surely hadde ſo ſouerayne excellence myne abode none offence ſo euer crye clappe laſte ſcaped fro hir trappe came yle right lyne whiche ſpecyally thorugh hye power dyuyne ordeyned yore myracle ſpirituall oracle man haue temple sodayne anſwere hym lyſt enquere queſtyons demaundes alle ſoules ſhall eke befalle whan men dede grauen vnderſtone gan axe temple anone myn auentures ſhulde ſewe man myght fate eſchewe lyke myn entent hadde anſwere full conuenyent saue befalleth whan ſoule gone diffynycyon vnto none thyng aſſoyle accordeth nat ryght reſeruyd vnto goddes myght excedeth reaſon wyt man fro thenſe forth ſayle gan dryuen wynde parte ſocoured lyke haue deuoured karybdes profounde welle syrenes meremaydenes dwelle fro breſt ſcales ſyluer ſhene theyr ſhape fyſſhes freſſhe clene ouer kynde doth compaſſe appere femynyne face lyke virgyns nature without ſpot vndefouled pure cuſtome wawes flete ſonge heuenly ſwete aungelyke full armonye veryly ſugred melodye rauyſſhe wolde man lyue inly ioye almoſte herte ryue make man ſodayne hye pleſaunce foryet hym ſelfe leſe remembraunce deuoyde hym clene owne thought tyll vnwarely myſchefe brought theyr ſonge take kepe ſhall brought mortall ſlepe anone may nat withdrawe wyll drenche ſhyp lowe vnder wawe thus ſwetneſſe theyr heuenly ſowne bryngeth man con fuſyowne ſo euer theyr boundes paſſe ¶but lyfe ſcaped grace myn eres waxe gummes clere ſtopped ſo ne myght touche werble theyr inſtrumentis wherby reaſon man blynded fynally thorugh ſotylte men eſcaped fre saylynge forth mate weryneſſe tyll came vp full great diſtreſſe phenyce toke anone londe caſte anker ſhyppes bonde ſothly fyll v full vnfayre people cruell contrayre oonly malyce fyll anone ſlewe men almoſte euerychone treſoure good lytell hadde berafte ladde fewe left lyue toke put pryſon blyue thus hath fortune lad hir daunce lytell ioye plente myſchaunce whoſe daunger lernyd experte fall mychefe pouerte great dole ſorowe full breeſt ſee londe southe nat eeſt come vnto preſence haue declaryd playnely ſentence myn auentures worthyneſſe truſte oonly faythfulneſſe haue ſpecyall haue reherſyd tolde hyghneſſe beſte wyſe without dothe ſuffyſe though hert conſtrayned ſore thylke tyme vlixes ſpake helde pea full heuy lokynge ydumeus lyke gentyll kynge comforted hym euer myght beſy herte lyght hym beſought heuyneſſe lete longe hym lyſte crete hym abyde made hym ſuerte ſhulde fare alſo well nat wante may hym eaſe whan ſorowe ſome gan apeaſe cage drewe vnto ende leue toke ſayde wolde wende tha • londe home countre firſte kynge fredome bounte gaue vnto hym great rycheſſe array ſo euer pay golde treaſour many thynges partynge thyſe two kynges ſhyppes whan hym lyſte ſayle redy ſtuffyd meyne vytayle thus vlixes gan hym redy make whan hath leue fully take haſted hym toke anone ſee gan ſayle towarde countree firſte wente kynge alphenon whiche paſſyngly hadde affeccyon ſe vlixes home comynge deſyrous ouer thynge haue hym newely aqueyntaunce vnto hym inly great pleſaunce hym talke eloquence wyſdome hye prudence ſmerte receyued playnely glad herte euer yet maner man sythen tyme worlde began encreaſe felycytee herde firſte penolopee trewe wyfe without ſpot blame yet grene noble fame whiche hir lorde longe abſence thought dede neuer dyde offence ſothly bothe chere dede thorugh grece exaumple womanhede yet ſhe bokes lyſte expreſſe thorugh world myrour fayreneſſe amonge grekes borne hyeſt blode called auctours bothe fayre gode yet ſay bookes hir doutlees neuer none hadde ſo great prees ſhe hir kept chaungynge newe vnto hir lorde euer ylyke trewe herte aye one nat parted twayne ſhe called quene ſouerayne wyfely trouthe bokes olde ofte fynde hir herte wolde colde tourne pale fro hir lorde ſo ferre hir cloſet werre drede ſhe hadde fro fere eke quake fantaſyes hir lordes ſake abſence bothe eue morowe deth vnto hir importable ſorowe aye ſothe ioye game whan fyll ſhe herde ectors name place anone ſhe fylle ſwowne gan hir ſelfe teres drowne womanhede ſo ſhe ferde ſlaughter mortall ſwerde lyſte hir lorde knyghtly ſurquedye hadde fortune falle ieopardye hap ſorte mette y• worthy knyght ſelde neuer ſhe felte hir herte lyght many dreme nyghtes dyde hir gaſte whyle ſege laſte euery play venym hir ſyght whan ſhe hir owne knyght worlde ioye hadde ſhe none hye lowe playnely one whoſe ſake myrthe ſhe refuſeth ſo herte muſeth woman thynge gode melancolye meuyd blode let hym aduerte wyſdome yſee remembre penolopee decert lyſte blamyd guydo thou ſhuldeſt aſhamyd ſay wyues thynge wele good fayth ferre fele though one two amonge offence good thorugh hir prouydence therof thynge wyte thoughe guydo boke endyte varyaunce eleyne creſeyde medea ſorowe deyde let agayne right equytee wyfely trouthe penolopee maydenhode yonge polycene goodneſſe eccuba quene caſſandra eke ſtedefaſtneſſe take kyndeneſſe pantaſylle without varyaunce put togydre balaunce ye ſhall fynde ye lyſte accounte maugre grutcheth trouth ſhal ſurmoūte dare afferme bere away pryſe wyll man replye wyſe feble oppynyon whyle vlixes alphenon hym made relacyon hatefull conſpiracyon certayne lordes enuyron countree bauyſſhe wold • quene penolopee maugre tho agayne albe ſhe euer ylyke playne hir trouthe ſtedfaſte wall yet haue caſte platly ſhe ſhall take force may nat eſchewed ſo haſte ſhe reſkewed caſte tyme nat aiourne day nyght hir ſoiourne inly herte loue diſamayde wyſedome ſhe hath ſo delayde none ſo manly ſo ſage coude hir gette auauntage auyſe ſhe hir werkynge whan vlixes conceyueth thynge fully knewe open euydence hadde alſo ſpecyall credence sent vnto hym fro penolopee mater hole declarynge ſecretee owne ſone thelamonyus wexe herte wood furyous wolde make dylacyon haſte beſoughte alphenon myghty kynge hye bounte releue hym aduerſyte wolde thorugh myghty honde gentylleſſe conueye hym londe graunteth hym ſay nat one nay bothe two full great array toke ſee whan wynde gode well fortuned thynge withſtode aryued hadde lettynge vlixes ye haue herde kynge ſecretely nyght conueyed haue lygaunce diſobeyed mercyles myght awake theyr beddes haue take makynge prolongynge tyll morowe haſt wyght durſt thē borowe smette theyr hedes jugement fynall ſette vpon caſtell wall eueryche endelonge rowe vpon toure whan kocke gan crowe thus nyght kept ſelfe cloſe tyll phebus meryly aroſe oryent whan larke ſonge tho theſe kyngꝭ meyne ſtronge freſſhely beſene entre cytee ¶who tho glad penolopee made ioye goodly quene full deſyrous hir owne lorde ſene ſhulde ordre ſette great myrthe made whan mette make reherſayle complayntes olde gan theyr hertes vnfolde eche lyſte thynge concele gladneſſe inly fele ſhulde put memorye reioyſynge hertely glorye lyeges made comynge coſtes eke hadde metynge gyftes great preſentes ryche worlde cowe none ylyche longe tariynge boke newe aſſuraunce toke lordes lyeges alle grace falle chere made eke alphenowne gentylleſſe thorugh hye renowne doughter inly debonayre alphenon nauſica fayre vlixes medyacyon yweddyd vnto thelamon borne diſcent may man ſay nay reioyſe crowne day thus came purueaunce two reygnes myghty allyaunce brought knotte men wolde deme playnely ſotte preſume oppynyon delate deſcripcyon sythen guydo touchynge chefe mater ſtyle brefe shortly reherſynge kynge alphenon repeyred home regyon vlixes chefe cytee abode ſtylle penolopee hym leue ioye ſolace tyll antropos lyketh purchace fychche fynally date threde vntwyne lyues fate ¶how tranſlatoure wryteth ſtocke pyrrus lyncall dyſcent fader hyght pelleus graunmoder called thetydes capitulo xxxvij muſte full beſy whyle directe tracy ſtyle deſcryuynge ſhortly entent ſtocke py •• u lyneal diſcēt myn auctour folowe compendyous ¶whoſe olde fader hyght pelleus graunmoder called therydes whiche two came worthy achylles troye treaſon loſte lyfe dardanyca called wyfe pyrrus moder doughter rede vnto kynge called lychomede hauynge fader acaſtus hyght whiche ſothneſſe euer myght bare heuy herte kynge pelleus achylles alſo pyrrus kyn playnely ſyde malyce rancoure pryde enuye hatefull rage ¶whan pelleus ſalie age berafte hym bothe ſceptre crowne ſee lowe lyght hym downe exyle auayle way ſtryfe made hym go thetydes wyfe hye diſdeyne gayne may grace herte gan day nyght compace deth pyrrus kepe hym therupon malycyouſly began ſhape away awayte lyinge hym ſle home comynge ¶but pyrrus treynes free many daunger eſcaped ſee many wawe many tempeſt wode great loſſe bothe men gode malaſus alder firſte gan londe ſtronge cyte lytell fro ſtronde refreſſhed wonder wele knewe grounde euerydele firſte thexyle lyke men hym tolde therydes pelleus olde ataſtus bare hym hatrede vnto deth wherof gan drede thought wolde y• right wyſe ſome engyne eſchewe malyſe therupon beſy payne nowhadde ataſtus ſones twayne menalyppus polyſtenes adoughter ycalled thetydes whyle wofull pelleus caſtell olde ruynous thetydes full ſorowe care drede deth day nyght gan dare diſeſpeyred vnweldy age recure fynde mortall rage except hadde hope yore pyrrus ſhulde helpe hym reſtore repeyre whan ſo falle whoſe comynge often gan calle tyme curſe ſo longe abode whan pyrrus vnderſtode malaſus relacyowne full faſte gan haſte towne toke ſee faſte gan hym hye towarde londe called theſalye ofentent make ordynaunce ataſtus vengaunce alderfirſte pyrrus full prudent eſpyes twayne tofore hath ſent theſalye forth togydre gone crylyppus called tone adaſtrus named fere expert nedeth nat lere whoſe expleyte auauntage pyrrus hath direct maſſage theſalye cyteſeyne called aſſandrus maner chaumberleyne pelleus whylom full ſecree whyle flourynge felycytee whan pyrrus concluſyon knewe ſothe relacyon ſee londe hym ne lyſte tarye albe founde wynde contrarye ¶but •• caped many dredefull ſtoundes theſalye aprocheth boundes eolus luſte obeyed fortune • erly con • eyed dryuen grace aryue ſame place pelleus dolefull caue drede deth lay hym ſelfe ſaue sool ſaue wyfe withouten ferys encloſyd huſſhes brerys pyrrus went vp firſte ſonde sool hym ſelfe walkynge ſtronde penſyfe tryſte way toke ¶where pelleus caue quoke hauynge hym tho none guyde saue ſwerde hangynge ſyde vn warely dredefull herte pelleus caue ſterte diſamayde lyfe doute whan behelde knyght walke aboute aſtoned abode ſtode full ſtylle ymagynynge ſawe achylle ¶by pyrrus ſtondynge place ſygnes ſhewed face nature without varyaunce made ſo lyke chere countenaunce forme ſhape lymmes euerychone difference effect none pelleus without longer ſpace gan anone pyrrus enbrace abrayde deedly
