thought ioye ſette ſorowe nought gan hym declare bothe exyle euyll fare pyteous lyfe pouerte myſchaunce fortune falſe varyaunce ataſtus feruent hoote enuye cruelte tyrannye ceryouſly tolde pyrrus alle full ſobre ſtode ſtylle walle face pale herte wrothe specheles ſhyp agayne gothe enformed douteles menalyppus polyſtenes ataſtus togydre thre huge array great meyne ſame day full ſurquedous pryde hunte foreſt lytell beſyde whan pyrrus therof toke good hede without abode chaunge gan wede full porely rent diſarayed lyke man thought diſmayed gyrte ſwerde made delay foreſt toke ryght way sool hym ſelfe without companye ſecretely man myght eſpye drowghe many dyuerſe boundes herde horne vncouplynge houndes lyke man lyſt make mone fro ſyght folke drewe hym aye alone caſuelly diſſeueryd fro prees firſte mette polyſtenes menalyppus rydynge ſyde bothe two pyrrus gan abyde boyſtouſly hym enquere fro ſe came alſo febly cladde ſo pore eſtate walkynge deſolate lowly chere countenaunce styll humble dalyaunce anſwerde agayne ſayde fordyuen myſchefe ſee affermed pale thynge rede felowſhyp drowned dede fyue hondred wawes ſo rage olde yonge medell age eſcaped tempeſt ſo ryfe tolde vnneth lyfe ouer tolde platly eke touchynge byrthe greke went deſtytur ioye late come fro ſege troye beſought towarde lyuynge helpe hym ſome refreſſhynge hym hadde catell loſte gode lyke ſawe naked ſtode prayinge alſo hope ſhulde auayle hym releue clothynge vytayle refute ſomewhat prouyde hym ſhulde abyde wyll wyt playnely whyle beſyde ran full great harte downe ryuer menalyppus prycked courſer ſempte hym dewe thorugh thynne thycke onely purſewe ſpareth nat alway rode brother pyrrus ſtylle abode polyſtenes toke hede haſte alyght fro ſtede grene reſte hym beſyde wery ryde without meyne beynge hym ſelfe ſool lyſ • ynge pyrrus complaynte y• dool ſodaynely myght aduerte cruell pyrrus ran hym herte lefte hym dede lyinge playne whan menalyppus repeyred agayne seynge brother baſkyn blode pyrrus efte furyous wode face coloure pale wan menalyppus yre ran ſlewe hym eke toke hede thus lay grounde blede bretherne two pyrrus ſwerd yſlawe anone aſyde gan hym drawe metynge aknyght ſorte caas ſayth ſtorye called cynara pyrrus gan haſte enquere whoſe man dyd anſwerde made tariynge ſeruaunt myghty kynge called ataſtus lorde countre pyrrus tho dedely enmyte cruell ſwerde freſſhe rede blode ran hym thorugh lyon wode foreſt forſoke haſte right way toke ſhyppe agayne pale blacke hewe gan anone array hym newe purpyll whiche clerkes telles kynges wyght elles pyrrus freſſhe well deſeyne foreſt repeyred ageyne ſodaynely hap walkynge ſhorte whyle mette kynge olde ataſtus aſked pyrrus man art thou thy ſelfe thus walkyſt thus day fro certes quod pyrrus full ſorowe wo inly ſuppryſed hertely complaynynge one ſones pryamus kynge whylom nowe put memorye whan troye flouryd glorye refutles myſchefe brought walke ſool full care thought exyle troye towne cruell pyrrus lyue pryſowne bounde vnto hym though full lothe honde aſſured many full great othe obeye luſte captyuyte loo thus ſtandeth ataſtus tho entencyon many queſtyon enqueryd hym dalyaunce knewe ought pyrrus gouernaunce coude ought vnderſtonde hym kept ſythe came londe ywyſſe quod ye lyſte hym haue kepeth hym cloſe yonder caue amonge bruſkayle ſhrowded face makynge ſygne ſame place done ydell maſe whyle kynge thyderwarde gan gaſe haſty pyrrus gan ſwerde drawe purpoſe fully ataſtus haue ſlawe wonderly ſtorye lere quene thetydes dyde anone appere rayned teres hir face gan ſwerde pyrrus enbrace prayinge hym deedly honde reſtrayne haſt yu nat ſlayne yonge brother twayne ala fader hore gray mercyles fro wylt take away put vp ſwerde blode ne ſhede haue pyte vpon thy kynrede aduerte clerely fyne thou arte come ſame lyne hatefull loke ryght vnkynde blode euery mannes ſyght pyrrus tho tygre wrothe gan afferme many full great othe ſo grutche agaynſt playne ſhall hym ſle hondes twayne hath nat falſe extorſyon put pelleus regyon whiche lorde ye trewe wyfe fynally ſhall leſe lyfe anone myn handes deye matere ſeye pelleus darynge caue grace oonly lyſte lyfe ſaue helpe platly nought pelleus anone forth brought croked olde vnweldy eke ſe tofore pyrrus fyll downe kn • beſechynge hym apyteous face requeſte take hym grace wolde manly herte goodly conſydre deedly wo ſmerte ataſtus mortall payne hadde ſones twayne whiche lay deed tofore hym grene slayne ſwerde y• ſo ſharpe kene whiche ne may recure wyſe ſorowe whiche ought ynough ſuffyſe though ye hym vengaunce peyſyd iuſtly balaunce syth hoolly ſubmyttyd myght take hym mercy anone ryght let ſwerde age nat conſume requeſt dare preſume pyrrus ſhortly ſayne whā put vp ſwerde agayue seynge mercy myght mooſt auayle without wordes reherſayle firſte tofore euerychone kynges made accorde one wyſdome concludynge vp dede eche ſhulde right poſſede theſalye partyd twayne neyther hadde mater complayne eueryche reygne dewe ſee whyle togydre thre preſence man ataſtus firſte thus tale began syres quod nat vnknowe thorugh age brought lowe thorugh nature kyndely mocyon wexed feble wyt reſon beynge vnweldy lymmes alle many yeres vpon falle vnneth thynge diſcerne feble ſothe kyngdome gouerne lyfe deth takynge hede syth ſones ſlayne dede ſool lefte without heyre worldly luſte fully diſpeyre tyme paſſyd felycyte fortune tourne mutabylyte hath taught playnly dare wel expreſſe worldly ioye ſykerneſſe truſte whyle abyde wyll ſelfe prouyde haſte prudent purueaunce diſcharge gouernaunce agayne ſort lyſte nat malygne ſceptre crowne frely reſygne theſalye lorſhyp eke londe fre wyll hole thy honde ſhall man reclayme ſay nay interupte make delay touchynge thynge colluſyon put poſſeſſyon hereupon euer ſayde makynge full fayth honde layde quene thetydes ſyttynge preſent pelleus ſame entent vnto pyrrus purpartye reſygned eke right theſalye fully affermynge yore ago full deſyre ioye alſo euer one neuewe ſuccede rightfull heyre kyngdome poſſede vtterly without repentaunce longeth vnto lygeaunce sceptre ſwerde crowne dyademe kynge lyfe deth deme thy hande without longer date ſame houre hooly tranſlate whan knot conuencyon fully brought concluſyon perfourmed vp hole vnyte euermore atwene theſe kynges thre ataſtus knyghtes diſſeueryd enuyrowne foreſt deſcendyd downe byddynge platly theyr lorde echone ſworne accorde attones luſty companye theſalye faſte gan hye pyrrus folke lyinge ſee ſayled forthe ſtreyght cytee ataſtus doth ſette parlement openly gaue cōmaundement lyeges hye lowe eſtate without ſtryfe debate specyally gentyll blode yborne ſame daye pyrrus ſworne lyke theyr degree royall halle perſeuere trewe lyeges alle durynge theyr lyfe erneſt game pelleus cōmaundeth hath ſame partye without fraude thus ioye ſolempne laude pyrrus euery maner age gladly accepted herytage day fortunat gode glad aſpectis whan heuen ſtode well accordynge ſuche maner thynge worthy pyrrus ycrowned kynge theſalye ryche regyon vayne make mencyon theyr reuell theyr great array feſte made ſame day eke ſtorye fynde nat ſothe wyll paſſe ouer myn auctour dothe saue boke ſpecefyed kyngdome fer magnefyed theſalye great myght pyrrus whylom ſo gode knght ſe hym royall ſee tournynge agayne kynge ydumee whiche whyle graue vnder ſtone hym ſone meryone ſtorye ſayth crowned kynge crete whyle reygnynge equyte deyed alſo wolde none haſte leorica brother rightfull heyre ſucceſſyon crowned kynge regyon whiche tyme ataſtus drede aſſent pyrrus rede full beſy make ſpecyall ryche toumbe paſſyngly royall buryed full huge prees menalyppus polyſtenes bothe two foreſt ſlawe thorugh pyrrus ſwerde full cruell lawe none proceſſe make euen fully tale take bothe alſo eke yfere ataſtus theyr owne fader dere ſothly locke hore troye boke rede ¶but muſt agayne pyrrus wende wryte hym ſory wofull ende whiche whan ſat hyeſt ſee made full blynde vayne proſperyte gouernynge londe theſalye falſly fyll fantaſye ſette loue hermyon quene horeſtes wyfe reygnynge methene brent hote fyre fulfyllynge foule deſyre purpoſe hole thus brought aboute hir rauyſſhynge whyle hir lorde oute ladde hir home helde hir wyfe semynge hym blyſfull lyfe full releſe paynes ſmerte whiche horeſtes bare full heuy herte caſte hym playnely auengyd whan may haue opportunyte tyme though hadde wronge feble pyrrus ſtronge ¶whiche helde alſo ſtorye tolde andronomecha hym houſholde ectors wyfe whylom ſhe hadde alytell childe whiche hir ſhe ladde ſege complete deſtruccyowne whan ſhe brought troye towne lamedouta fynde name encreaſynge full worthy fame pyrrus ſhe hadde ſone alſo called achylleydos ſo wryt guydo theſe woman theyr great eſtate atwene ſelfe amonge debate hermyone hir yre hote complaynynge hir fader wrote hir fere hir hye degree andronomecha cheriſſhed better thā ſhe kynge pyrrus beſechynge menelay enhaſte hym euer may come hym ſelfe anone ſle woman hir childe alſo abode nat faſte gan hym hye hete towarde theſalye venged ſwerde ſtele vpon hir treſpaſſeth neuer adele maugre hym cruelte reſkewed amyd cyte thynge whiche hath nat herde woman kynge drawe ſwerde wyll mater dwelle maner ſhamed wryte telle done whyle pyrrus courage delos gone pylgrymage hauynge hym lytell route appollo knele loute ſoule praye achylle vowes alſo fulfylle thanke hym humble affeccyon god exployte hadde troye towne wreche alſo take cyte faders ſake ¶but thynge yſpecefyed kynge horeſtes warely hath eſpyed delos gan haſte hym full ryght ledynge hym many luſty knyght vnwarely pyrrus mette vengeably vpon hym ſette fynally ſtraunge londe horeſtes ſlewe hym owne honde fynde ſothe made defence ſodayne mortall vyolence enmye coude nat aſterte myght ſwerde aduerte hym enuyron deſet thylke tyme myght bet nouther ſocoure declyne thus pyrrus brought vnto fyne late crowned kynge theſalye loo guerdon anoutrye lo mede rewarde full ryfe myſſe vſe another mannes wyfe drede folowe ſhall vengaunce sodayne deth vnware myſchaunce whiche euery man greatly ought charge delos temple large kynge pyrrus locked vnder ſtone horeſtes forth way gone force gat wyfe agayne wyght durſt hym tho wtſayne methene proudely repeyred theſalye pyteouſly diſpeyred deſtytute rede whan wyſte worthy kyng dede heyre none ſucceſſyon gouerne noble regyon saue achylleydos iytell aforne pyrrus abſence grece borne fully age nat quarter clene youthe ſothly grene lyſte conſydre rendre myght full many day reioyſe ryght gouerne sceptre honde large boundes ſo great londe yet childe lykely right feyre ſoth borne heyre pyrrus trouthe playne man lyſte withſayne ¶but fynde whan came age reſygned hole herytage brother frely ryght lamedoute wonder manly knyght deſcended troy anyſſhe blode downe fro ſtocke hym ſo gode floure knyghthode diffence frigya hym begat andromecha ordeyned nowe ſo gru • che frowne theſalye bere crowne whan made lorde londe frely reſygned honde hath cōmaunded man dare replye thorugh kyngome theſalye captyuyte pryſoners troye cyte loue hate excepcyon none ſhulde theyr large gone ¶by full aſſent achylleydos ſuche eke pryſon cloos without raunſon ſhall belyuered reioyſe full lyberte cuſtome vſed bothe borugh towne lyeges great regyon thus folke y• came thralle fro troye reſtored ſodaynely ioye ¶by lamedoute ymade free eke reygneth royall ſee full myghtely haue made mynde troye boke hym fynde pyrrus kynrede fro henſforth proceſſe rede ¶but incydentes bere ſubſtaunce whiche vayne put remēbraūce except myn auctor note entent impeth lytell incydent ywrought done full yore agon touchynge deth kynge menon whiche enuye cruell achylles ſlayne ſothe amonge myrundones proudely gan purſewe vpon achylles troylus reſkewe ¶whom kynge pryam made buryed beſyde troylus troye cyte temple ybylte marbyll olde fyne tale tolde chapitle ſhall reherſe anon noble quene kynge menon tyme longe many day ſhe dede grauen vnder clay toumbe heuenly gan appere beſet bryght ſterres clere whoſe ſymylytude reken lyke thynge immortall man myght vtterly ſuſtene beholde loke ſhe ſo ſhene downe deſcendynge fro fyrmament full many man beynge preſent clade mantell full celeſtyall hir porte paſſyngly royall ſwetneſſe freſſhe roſe made haſte toumbe vncloſe hir lorde taketh bone cheſte made golde ſtones couched faſte euer ſhe may diſapered went anone hir way tofore certayne place ſhe neuer ſayne affermynge lyklyneſſe outher aungell goodeſſe ſoule fate ſame kynge nat deme ſuche heuenly thynge therm holde none oppynyon tranſcendeth ſhortly reſon lyſte nat ſuche mater diffyne reſorte right lyne vlixes whyle dwelle ende ſurplus telle myght nat eſcape parodye hym ſhape parchas haue laſte terme ſette antropoſe meſured mette lyues threde rocke ſponne diffende thy ſelfe vlixes thou konne shewe thy manhode nat aferde welfare thy ſones ſwerde ſhall lyke wonte sha • pe penne bothe rude blonte deſcryue fyne thy ſoioure vpon boundes ſet laboure almoſt wery feynt weyke ynough veſtes ox plough longe day agayne hylle wende almoſt londes ende troye boke fychche wyll ſtake saue muſt ſpende fewe lynes blake laſte chapitre ſhortly tranſlate werke ympen date day deth ſette hym areſt full execute hym loued beſt lowe knee muſt loute god y• maketh men route cauſeth folke haue glad ſweuenes bothe morowe luſty euenes whan mortheus ſlepy wonde whiche holdeth alway honde hath marked agayne derke nyght make men bothe mery lyght ſome whyle haue gladneſſe ſodaynely falle heuyneſſe lyke gyueth euydence ſondry ſygnes apparence vnto lorde muſt mekely preye tyme ſtyle conueye vlixes dreme deſcryue laſte hadde lyue declarynge hym token full notable ſygnes demonſtrable ſlepte agayne pale moone fatall day ſhulde folowe ſoone fy • l thus bedde lay onyght tofore morowe gray hym thought ſawe appere creature ſyght celeſtyall fygure none erthly thynge veryly dyuyne porte chere wonder femynyne hym ſempte fantaſye lyke thynge ſent fayrye beaute hir goodly face recomforted playnely place moſt ſurmountynge moſte ſouerayne clereneſſe hir eyen twayne ſodaynely men myght aduerte perce wolde euen herte diffence none myght deuyſed vlixes hir loke ſuppryſed gan hir beholde alway ſlepe ſyghe ſore perſynge aye full beſy payne hir enbrace armes twayne aye gan purſewe agaynewarde gan hym eſchewe aye preſed hir ſe aye hym ſhe gan flee contrayre hym fortune whan ſhe ſawe importune axed hym ſhortly wolde hir platte trouthe tolde certys quod lyues empereſſe ye woman goddeſſe nat deme iuge halfe ryght ſo derked blynded ſyght dare well afferme place lyfe deth ſtande hoolly grace mercy requerynge ryght rewe whiche owne knyght pyte compaſſyon goodly ſe ſauacyon deſyre may fulfylle ſame nyght haue wylle recure remedye lacke rouche muſt dye nowe haue atwyxe hope drede ſelfe declaryd womanhede ſhe kepte hir cloſe whyle full ſadly gan hym ſmyle put remembraunce sayde vnto hym ſobre countenaunce sothly quod ſhe thyne affeccyon wolde fully tourne confuſyon v bothe ſo peryllous inly mortall contagyous vtterly gayne may rede one v muſt one dede fyne hatefull chaunce ſhulde folowe pleſaunce vlixes gan nyghe nere beholdynge aye hir heuenly chere ſhe ſtode vpryght grounde ſawe hir holde ſpere longe rounde hede therof borned ſtele forged newe grounde wonder wele therupon vyſyowne ſawe baner blaſynge vp downe felde therof coloure ynde full fyſſhes beten fynde ſome bokes lyke tolde myddes large crowne golde ſhe tourne gan hir face lykely anone parte place ſpake hym ſayde wordes playne full token partynge v twayne euermore nouther ſoure ſwete daye neuer agayne mete diſaperynge anone hir leue ſhe toke ſodaynely woke gan muſe fantalye thynge dreme myght ſygnefye mente outher euell gode ſecretneſſe nat vnderſtode ſurmounted ſothly reaſon therfore ſente thorugh regyon ſuche ſotell expoſytours fate ſorte crafty dyuynours clerkes ſoget crowne aſſemble one ſweuen expowne whan knewe informacyon maner hole vyſyon concluded accordynge one tyme approcheth ſhall come anone one next kynrede ſpere ſhulde make hym blede let ſe fate remewe syth harde deſtynero eſchewe ſay tho folke theyr oppynyon werke truſte conſtellacyon vlixes muſynge tale chaungeth coloure gan wexe pale wonder dredefull full fantaſyes gan hym ſelfe ſeke remedyes voyde away thynge wyll nat ſtareth brode may nat ſe warde loke cloude ſhent wenynge prudent made calle ſone thelamon take ſhet vp pryſon ſuppoſynge fully wytte myſchefe therby go quyte nat aduerteth ne toke none hede ſharpneſſe ſperes hede fyſſhes baner beete ſee ſwymme flete quene called circe ſygnes brought werre nat pee crowne token dignytee one ſhall holde royall ſee myd wawes bothe felle wode amonge fyſſhes large flode ſhall make dyuyſyon tofore remembred auyſyon agayne wyll ignoraunce execute fatall puruyaunce vp dreme ſpere ſtele whiche vlixes conſydreth neuer adele wyght hath ſuſpecyon ſone called thelamon cloſed ſhet vp toure vlixes coſte great laboure fro day day doth beſyneſſe hym ſelfe make fortereſſe bylte rocke lyme ſquare ſtones depe dyched aboute none man may entre ſyde caſteth lyfe abyde 〈◊〉 certayne men choſen ſpecyall nyght day watche vpon wall wyght ſhulde haue none entree ſo falle ſecree knowen olde counſayle ſworne ſtorye reherſed hath forne olde fole dotarde vlixes ſone hadde begoten cyrces freſſhe luſty yonge coragyous called thelagonyus borne ſee amonge floddes rage alſo reken age fyue twenty yere aboute fader aye doute man myght beynge therof ſeurte tyll day deſyrous knowe moder fyll knee lowe beſechynge hir goodly nat ſpare fader trouthe declare ſhulde dwelle beſought ſhe wolde telle ſothly ſhe longe many dayes prudence put hym delayes tyll ſhe ſawe ſhe myght haue reſte importune requeſte whā ſhe knewe none bote fro poynt poynt ſhe tolde crop rote vlixes kynge anone made lettynge toke leue may none ſayde playnely wolde fader ſe ¶wherof quene gan herte colde whan ſhe ſaide ſhe myght hȳ nat wtholde hym beſought chere debonayre wolde ſoone agayne repayre forthe ſayleth onwarde way without abode ſelfe ſame day many porte many fer countre tyll brought wolde achaya londe great renowne gan ſerche thorugh regyon place paleys pryncypall kynge helde ſee royall ſo longe countre rode tyll taught kynge abode vlixes ſhytte vp mewe whiche place haſte gan purſewe great party releuyd ſorowe monday erely morowe vnto brydge ryght way toke founde porter deynous loke lowely firſte gan hym praye wolde goodly hym conueye courte make tariynge meſſage hadde kynge proudely denyed hym gate ſhortly ſayde came late entre maner wyſe vngoodly gan hym deſpyſe frowarde ſpeche malycyous haſte thelagonyus herte nat aferde proude porter hente berde fyſte rofe chawe bone fyll deed muet ſtone eke hym tho withſtode made proudely lepe ye flode whan mo came make reſyſtence hente ſwerde manly vyolence furyouſly irous tene ſtorye ſayth ſlewe fyftene hym ſelfe almoſte wounded deth gan wery ſothly fayle breth vlixes noyſe ſowne brydge deſcendyd downe fyndynge men entre gate deed ſlayne full mortall hate full irous hente anone darte auenture ſtondynge tho parte cruelly caſte thelagon ſtroke conclucyon damageth nat glode aſyde haſte lenger wolde abyde hent vp darte without reſt ſmote kynge lowe vnder breſt thorugh rybbes ſhortly ſeye wounde muſt deye hauynge tho none oppynyon kynge ſuſpecyon hadde owne fader ſlawe whiche faſte gan ende drawe wounde ſo deedly ſo kene myght hym ſelfe nat ſuſtene pale wan grounde gan glyde men aboute vpon euery ſyde beſy helpe hym releue ſore gan ſo ake greue well felte muſt dede abraydynge lyfte vp hede hauynge yet mynde good reaſon remembre gan auyſyon tolde hym drede one next kynrede deſcendyd downe owne lyne ſweuene ſhall parfourme fyne accomplyſſhe darte ſtele coude nat conceyue wele ſhulde badde anone vnto meyne without harme vyolence fette anone vnto preſence yonge man whiche gate ſtode hath day ſhad ſo moche blode whan afore vlixes brought hym hath enqueryd ſought firſte kyn nexte countree certes quod borne ſee amonge fyſſhes myd wawes grene ſayde alſo moder quene called circe name kouthe bothe eſt weſt right fer ſouthe tolde alſo fader kynge hym begat home comynge fro troye towne towarde countre moder cyrces tolde secretely vlixes hyghte deſyrous haue ſyghte entred myghty regyon haue purſewed vnto dongeon oonly hope fader haue ſeyne ſe well labour veyne ſythe ſothe loſt trauayle may ſyde auayle foly lenger dwelle lo telle kynred axe ¶with vlixes gan ſyghe ſore lacke blode full pale ſayde anone whan herde tale wot well wofull deſtyne fulfylled may none wot well late grutche ſtryue agayne pyteous fate ſone clerkes whylom tolde hath made ende dayes olde theron expectant paynes full greuous worde thelagonyus whan wyſte agayne nature lawe ala fader ſlawe whiche londe longe bare crowne without abode fylle anone ſwowne clothes rent yelowe heer torne ala quod euer borne curſed wofull deſtyne fortune whiche may nat fle curſed ſort curſed myn auenture refuſe euery creature forwaryed eke diſpoſycyon curſed conſtellacyon curſed alſo infortunat houre whiche fader begat wolde god without lenger rede aquyte hym anone dede lay lyfe deth borowe whan kynge ſawe great ſorowe wyſte ſone cyrces borne many ſygnes reherſed toforne vnto hym anone forgaue deth myght lacke want breth importable paſſyon ſone called thelagon whiche hath pryſon ſo many daye ſhet preſence haſte fet whiche whan ſawe fader ſuche poynt vpon deth ſtondynge diſioynt knewe alſo trouth hath founde hadde laſte deedly wounde ſwerde hente mortally irous wolde haue ronne thelagonyus hye deſpyte auenged vlixes faderly pyte made men holde hym reſtrayne amyd greuous payne prudence done anone made ſones one gaue charge vnto thelamon enteerneſſe affeccyon hole herte fayned neuer adele lyfe loue brother wele parte hym treaſour golde gode nexte borne blode tho ſothe lenger taryed vlixes royally caryed achaya chefe cyte lyued dayes thre without tho gaue vp goſt nat ſay playnely coſt lyfe ſoule gone atoumbe metall ſtone body cloſed yſhet made let thelamon great ſolempnytee ȳcrowned fadres ſee swerde ſceptre delyueryd honde achaya full worthy londe ryght habundaunt treaſour gode thelagon hym abode yere complet well cheryſſhed ſyght brother toke ordre knyght hym lyſte lenger abyde kynge hym wyſely gan prouyde golde great treaſour plente repeyred home countre moder age wexe ſad repeyre paſſyngly glad ſhe ſawe hir sorcerye ſcapyd many iupardye many pereyll many great diſtreſſ • ſhe fylle ſykeneſſe hir dette yelde vnto nature whiche eſcape may creature wolde lyuynge whoſe deth hir ſone made kynge anlydos meruayllous countre haue tolde encloſed ſee amonge rockes many ſhyppes drowne ſyxty yere bare crowne manly man thelagonyus brother thelamonyus reygned alſo regyon seuenty wynter made mencyon made royall ende bothe two iubyter wende reygne amonge ſterres bryght bvt lanterne clere lyght waſted frygyus darete whylom troye wryter poyete guyde haue none ferther paſſe euen ſelfe place fychched hath boundes ſtyle ſege preſent whyle aye one dyde abyde dytes greke tother ſyde bothe two theyr wrytynge ne vary nat lytell thynge touchynge matere ſpecyall notable hyſtoryall force incydentis ſmale whiche ſothe lytell tale saue dytes maketh mencyowne nombre ſlayne towne laſtynge ſege affermynge drede eyght hondred thouſāde ſyx dede grekes ſyde vp right felde dare alſo behelde troye partye werre kene syxe hondred thouſande ſeuenty ſyxtene ſlayne guydo ye may ſe came helpe cyte fro many coſte many regyowne diffence reſkus towne full ten yere ſo caſte ſyxe monthes myghty ſege laſte gette dare wryte hym ſelfe ouer complet dayes twelue grekes hadde full poſſeſſyon falſe engyne greke synon lyke tofore reherſyd late haue latyn tranſlate dytes dare guydo adde therto myn auctours ſpecefye ſeyn • occupacyon ſothly veyne lyke maner preſumpcyon tyme complet tranſlacyon iuſte rekenynge countis clere thouſande foure hondred yere twenty nere knowe drede criſte receyued manhede hir empereſſe quene heuen helle mayde clene eyghte yere computacyon suynge coronacyon hym moſt gracyous werkynge herry fyfthe noble worthy kynge protectoure brutys albyowne called thorugh hyerenowne thorugh proweſſe chyualrye alſo fer paſſeth cloude ſkye normadye myghty conquerour thorugh knyghthod dilygent labour maugre tho lyſte hym withſeyne hath conqueryd herytage ageyne myghty prudent gouernaunce recuryd eke trewe tytle fraunce ſo lyſte loke vnfolde pee de grewe cronycles olde ſercheth bokes ywryt longe aforne ſhall fynde iuſtly borne reygne fraunce lyneall diſcent onwarde made regent thylke londe durynge faders lyfe goodneſſe voyde werre ſtryfe reioyſe without delay sceptre crowne kynges day clerely concluſyon enrolled vp conuencyon hope tyme fortunat olde worlde called aureat reſorte ſhall influence grace cruell mar ſhall manace lookes furyous wode falſe aſpectes ſhede blode atwene folkes thyſe realmes twayne whiche euery wyght ought complayne truſte myn oppynyon worthy kynge wyſedome reſon knyghthode ſhall ſo payne make one longe hath twayne mene thus englonde fraunce may one without varyaunce hertes olde rancour enchace influence myghty grace called clerkes douteles ſoueraygne lorde prynce pee hope grace ſhall reygne ſet reſte atwene thyſe realmes twayne power ſothly ſtondeth allyaunce blode royall knet vp bonde maryage werre ſhall voyde away rage make pea bryght bemes ſhyne one called katheryne named right good fayre alſo shalbe mene atwyxe bothe two grace emprynted hir womanhede complayne ſhall haue nede hope hir gracyous aryuaylle londe ſhall ſo moche auaylle ioye honour proſperyte without trouble aduerſyte repeyre ſhall hertely pleſaunce plente welfare fulſome habundaunce pea quyete bothe nyghe ferre without ſtryfe debate werre myſchefe pouert nede indigence full ceſſynge deth peſtylence sothly hope ye ſhall ſene come londe noble quene ſhall ſay herte feyne nought bleſſyd ſhe hath v brought y• hath thorugh myght werkȳg knyghthode concludyd thyng ſuche meruayles ī armes done wrought purpoſe fully aboute brought hye wyſedome ſet inwarde ſyght reioyſynge longeth ryght hyeſt ſyt worthyneſſe glorye sceptre conqueſt victorye praye god oonly beſte ¶whan hath ſet pea reſte full put clere poſſeſſyon longeth ſubieccyon ſende hym home great honour euer yet hadde conquerour longe ioye quyete reygne royall ſete thus ſhall aye ſaye daye nyght expleyt praye faythfull herte hole entent whylom gaue cōmaundement nat yore ago faders tyme ſege troye maner ryme moſt ſake ſpeke ſpecyall though boyſtous rurall gaue charge ſtorye tranſlate rude connynge called iohn̄ lydgate • onke burye profeſſyon vſynge habyte perfeccyon albe lyfe accorde nat therto feyne nat wot well ſo nedeth nat wytneſſe calle recorde take brother alle wyll nat fayle ſo great nede ſhall noble ſtorye rede beſeche ſupporte grace offende maner place ſo euer fynde errour gentylleſſe ſhewe fauour benyngnely theyr payne correcte rather diſdayne well wot moche thynge wronge falſely metryd bothe ſhort longe ſhulde haue diſdayne drede labour vayne let ignoraunce rudeneſſe excuſe ye platly refuſe certayne fautes whiche ye ſhall fynde doute nat thanke ſet behynde metrynge though ignoraunce yet ſtorye ye fynde may pleſaunce touchynge ſubſtaūce y• myn auctour wryt though ſo worde myſſe ſyt amende chere debonayre errour hyndre appayre nat ſayde purpoſe malyce worſhyp hym wyſe wyght gladly ſo ſoon demeth lacke specyally behynde backe ſoth ſkylle gothe full hole neuer hadde fall nat fynde newe olde deme none ſo bolde yblent vnconnynge blynde bayarde caſte pereyll thynge tyll ſtumble myddes lake none ſo redy vndertake ſothe bolder ſay werſe ſkylle proſe verſe ſuche nat ſtylle lytell forſe ſay good ylle vnto boke nat dyrect ſuche haue effect ſymple folke full compaſſyon goodly correccyon amende thynge hyndre neuer adele cuſtome aye redy ſay wele groūde well ſayinge lyfe hyndred makynge mayſter chaucer y• founde full many ſpot hym lyſt nat pynche grutche euery blot meue hym ſelfe parturbe reſte haue herde tolde ſayde alway beſte suffrynge goodly gentylleſſe full many thynge embraced rudeneſſe ſhall ſhortly hym deſcryue neuer none daye alyue reken bothe yonge olde worthy ynkehorne holde londe borugh towne vyllage cyte connynge hath tracy ſewe go brode ſhet mewe hym make dyreccyon boke haue inſpeccyon beſechynge theyr prudent loke race ſcrape thorugh bok • voyde adde ſemeth nede though ſo nat ne rede boke rethorykes newe ¶y•et hope ſhall fynde trewe ſtorye playne clefly ſubſtaunce ſo lyſte ſe varyaunce worldly thynge wrought dayes olde boke may full well beholde chaunge fortune hir courſe mutable selde nat faythfull outher ſtable lordes prynces sfrom hir royalte sodaynely brought aduerſyte kynges eke plounged pouerte drede darynge deſerte vnware ſlaunghtre compaſſed enuy • murdre execute conſpyracye awayt leyinge falſhede treaſon kyngdome ſodayne euerſyon bauyſſhynge woman delyte rote werre mortall deſpyte falſe mayntenaunce auoutrye many worthy cauſynge dye synne aye concludynge ſo taketh hede vengaunce vnware fynall mede vo declare worldly luſte loke right lytell truſte boke exaumple ye ſhall fynde ye lyſte enprente mynde paſſeth halt ſoiour waſtynge away doth ſomer floure ryche pore euery maner age lyfe pylgrymage meynt labour moche woo men wolde take hede therto tofore prudently aduerte lytell ioye ſhulde haue theyr herte ſet theyr truſte worldly thynge nouther prynce lorde kynge example troye lyke ye may ſe lyfe may haue full ſeurte therfore hym ſtarfe vpon rode suffrynge deth aller gode lyfte vp hertꝭ thynke hym amonge ye neuer ſo myghty ſo ſtronge without hym may nat auayle gyue victorye batayle holde felde ſhortly conclude fewe agayne great multytude grace maketh prynces ſtronge worthy kynges reygne longe tyrantes ſodaynely oppreſſe thorwe thē downe theyr great rycheſſe honde power reſerueth eche aquyte lyke diſſerueth praye deuocyon myn herte hole affeccyon lyſte graunte longe contynaunce proſperyte good perſeueraunce helthe welfare victorye honoure vnto noble myghty conqueroure herry fyfther tofore yſpecefyed name may magnefyed herein lyfe vp ſterrys clere afterwarde aboue nynthe ſpere whan deed haue place praye god ſende hym grace whoſe byddynge tolde late firſte began ſege tranſlate haue hoolly honoure executed fyne laboure vnto ſhall ſtorye ſe humble herte humylyte lytell booke lowely betake ſupporte thus ende make ¶laus deo ¶of mooſt noble excellent prynce kynge henry fyfthe mooſt worthy prynce knyghthode ſoures welle whoſe hye renowne thorugh worlde dothe ſhyne manhode doeſt excelle egall meryt worthy nyne borne alſo diſcent lyne rightfull heyre tytle attayne bere y• crowne worthy realme twayne alſo fer phebus ſpere eeſt weſt ſhedyth bemys bryght lucyna aſhrouded chere gothe compaſſe rounde hir pale lyght thou art yrekened beſt knyght regiſtred worthy name hyeſt place houſe fame holde palme knyghthod thy honde worthyneſſe hye victorye thou art drade ſee londe euermore laude honoure glorye iuſte conqueſt put memorye crowne made laurer grene vpon thy heed tofore famous quene whylom ordeyned oonly conquerours stable herte longe perſeueraunce gaue nat vp tyll victours empryſes take ſodayne chaunce whoſe name ay floureth wt newe remēbraūce fadeth nat yeres yore agone amonges whiche thou mayſte ſet one thorugh worlde many regyon reported fame flyeth wyde naturelly thy condycyon thynge begonne knyghtly abyde tyme manly ſet aſyde reſt eaſe coſt theron ſpente tyll thou haue cheued fyne thyn entente moſte circumſpect paſſynge auyſee thy werkes conueyed prudence sad demure lyke ioſuee agayne whoſe ſwerde reſyſtence haſt alſo heuenly influence salamon wyſely diſcerne oonly grace thy people gouerne mercy eke meynt thy magnyfycence oppreſſed haue pyte rebelles manly vyolence abate canſte great cruelte ſo dauyd thou haſte kyngly pyt • hye proweſſe seſar iulyus tyme mooſt victoryous manly holdeſt thy hondes two beholde clere inſpeccyon ſwerde knyghthode thy scepture alſo tone brynge ſubieccyon hertes made proude falſe rebellyon sceptre rewle beſt thy trewe people lyue reſt thou y• haſte manhode vertue grace attemperaunce fredome bounte lowly praye dredefull face diſdayne nat benyngely ſe vpon boke rudely made fyne oonly agrene thyne hyghneſſe rewe mercy vpon ſympleſſe thy noble kyngly aduertence conſydre ſe ſoueraygne lorde moſt dere thyne inuat famous ſapyence criſte iheſu receyued good chere twey munytys herte entere wydowe whiche wyl thought gaue hir good kept hir ſelfe right nought whiche enſaumple ſo nat offende thorugh myn vnconnyng thy hye nobleſſe let good wyll lytell gyfte amende thy mercy renowmed goodneſſe haue diſdayne bareyne rudeneſſe makynge though haue muſe let trewe menynge ſurplus excuſe good herte hath maner wyght preſent nouther god man parte ryght gyue hole ferforth aye perſeuere fro tyme gan wyll thought thyne eſtate praye whiche conſerue thus fynally ſaye firſte almyghty god queme may pleſaunce thy crowne thy dyademe grace good eure wt longe contynuaunce thy lyeges faythfull obeyſſaunce eche vertue man may ſpecefye praye god graunte vnto thy regalye ¶explicit liber quintus vltimus ¶lenuoye • oo lytell boke put grace hym moſte excellence nat hardy appere place without ſupporte magnyfycence ſo euer fynde offence nat bolde preſumpcyon thy ſelfe enarme aye pacyence ſubmytte theyr correccyon ¶verba tranſlatoris ad librum ſuum thou art enlymned flowres retoryke whyte blacke therfore thou muſte abyde ſhowres lyſte ſet alacke whan thou art moſt lykely go wracke agaynſt thyne errour nat diffende humbly drawe go backe requerynge y• amyſſe amende endeth troye booke otherwyſe called sege troye tranſlated iohn̄ lydgate monke monaſtery bery emprynted yere oure lorde mccccc xiij richard pynſon prynter vnto kyngꝭ noble grace
